`crates/vigil-common/src/http.rs`:

```rs
// zero-dep HTTP client — shared between daemon and GUI
// TLS is not included here (daemon adds it via feature flag)

use std::io::{BufRead, BufReader, Read, Write};
use std::net::TcpStream;
use std::time::Duration;

pub struct HttpResponse {
    pub status: u16,
    pub body: String,
}

// GET with optional Bearer token
pub fn get(url: &str, token: Option<&str>) -> Result<HttpResponse, String> {
    let (_tls, host, port, path) = parse_url(url)?;

    let stream = TcpStream::connect(format!("{}:{}", host, port))
        .map_err(|e| format!("connect failed: {}", e))?;

    stream.set_read_timeout(Some(Duration::from_secs(10)))
        .map_err(|e| format!("set_read_timeout failed: {}", e))?;

    let mut req = format!("GET {} HTTP/1.1\r\nHost: {}\r\n", path, host);
    if let Some(t) = token {
        req.push_str(&format!("Authorization: Bearer {}\r\n", t));
    }
    req.push_str("Connection: close\r\n\r\n");

    let mut stream = stream;
    stream.write_all(req.as_bytes()).map_err(|e| format!("write failed: {}", e))?;
    read_response(&mut stream)
}

// POST with JSON body and optional Bearer token
pub fn post(url: &str, body: &str, token: Option<&str>) -> Result<HttpResponse, String> {
    let (_tls, host, port, path) = parse_url(url)?;

    let stream = TcpStream::connect(format!("{}:{}", host, port))
        .map_err(|e| format!("connect failed: {}", e))?;

    stream.set_read_timeout(Some(Duration::from_secs(10)))
        .map_err(|e| format!("set_read_timeout failed: {}", e))?;

    let mut req = format!(
        "POST {} HTTP/1.1\r\nHost: {}\r\nContent-Type: application/json\r\nContent-Length: {}\r\n",
        path, host, body.len()
    );
    if let Some(t) = token {
        req.push_str(&format!("Authorization: Bearer {}\r\n", t));
    }
    req.push_str("Connection: close\r\n\r\n");
    req.push_str(body);

    let mut stream = stream;
    stream.write_all(req.as_bytes()).map_err(|e| format!("write failed: {}", e))?;
    read_response(&mut stream)
}

// parse http:// or https:// url into (is_tls, host, port, path)
pub fn parse_url(url: &str) -> Result<(bool, String, u16, String), String> {
    let (tls, rest) = if let Some(r) = url.strip_prefix("https://") {
        (true, r)
    } else if let Some(r) = url.strip_prefix("http://") {
        (false, r)
    } else {
        return Err(format!("unsupported scheme in url: {}", url));
    };

    let (authority, path) = match rest.find('/') {
        Some(i) => (&rest[..i], rest[i..].to_string()),
        None => (rest, "/".to_string()),
    };

    let default_port = if tls { 443 } else { 80 };
    let (host, port) = match authority.find(':') {
        Some(i) => {
            let p = authority[i + 1..].parse::<u16>()
                .map_err(|_| format!("invalid port in url: {}", url))?;
            (authority[..i].to_string(), p)
        }
        None => (authority.to_string(), default_port),
    };

    Ok((tls, host, port, path))
}

fn read_response(stream: &mut TcpStream) -> Result<HttpResponse, String> {
    let mut reader = BufReader::new(stream);

    let mut status_line = String::new();
    reader.read_line(&mut status_line)
        .map_err(|e| format!("read status line failed: {}", e))?;

    let status = parse_status_line(&status_line)?;

    let mut content_length: Option<usize> = None;
    loop {
        let mut line = String::new();
        reader.read_line(&mut line)
            .map_err(|e| format!("read header failed: {}", e))?;
        let trimmed = line.trim();
        if trimmed.is_empty() { break; }
        let lower = trimmed.to_ascii_lowercase();
        if let Some(val) = lower.strip_prefix("content-length:") {
            content_length = val.trim().parse::<usize>().ok();
        }
    }

    let body = if let Some(n) = content_length {
        let mut buf = vec![0u8; n];
        reader.read_exact(&mut buf)
            .map_err(|e| format!("read body failed: {}", e))?;
        String::from_utf8_lossy(&buf).into_owned()
    } else {
        let mut buf = Vec::new();
        let _ = reader.read_to_end(&mut buf);
        String::from_utf8_lossy(&buf).into_owned()
    };

    Ok(HttpResponse { status, body })
}

fn parse_status_line(line: &str) -> Result<u16, String> {
    let mut parts = line.splitn(3, ' ');
    let _version = parts.next().ok_or("empty status line")?;
    parts.next()
        .ok_or("missing status code")?
        .trim()
        .parse::<u16>()
        .map_err(|_| format!("invalid status code in: {}", line.trim()))
}

// true for network-level failures worth retrying; HTTP 4xx/5xx are not connection errors
pub fn is_connection_error(err: &str) -> bool {
    let lower = err.to_ascii_lowercase();
    lower.contains("connect")
        || lower.contains("timeout")
        || lower.contains("refused")
        || lower.contains("reset")
        || lower.contains("broken pipe")
        || lower.contains("no route")
        || lower.contains("network")
}

const RETRY_ATTEMPTS: u32 = 3;
const RETRY_DELAY_MS: u64 = 500;

// get with up to 3 retries on connection errors; HTTP 4xx/5xx returned immediately
pub fn get_with_retry(url: &str, token: Option<&str>) -> Result<HttpResponse, String> {
    let mut last_err = String::new();
    for attempt in 0..RETRY_ATTEMPTS {
        if attempt > 0 {
            std::thread::sleep(std::time::Duration::from_millis(RETRY_DELAY_MS));
        }
        match get(url, token) {
            Ok(resp) => return Ok(resp),
            Err(e) => {
                if is_connection_error(&e) {
                    last_err = e;
                    // loop and retry
                } else {
                    return Err(e);
                }
            }
        }
    }
    Err(last_err)
}

// post with up to 3 retries on connection errors; HTTP 4xx/5xx returned immediately
pub fn post_with_retry(url: &str, body: &str, token: Option<&str>) -> Result<HttpResponse, String> {
    let mut last_err = String::new();
    for attempt in 0..RETRY_ATTEMPTS {
        if attempt > 0 {
            std::thread::sleep(std::time::Duration::from_millis(RETRY_DELAY_MS));
        }
        match post(url, body, token) {
            Ok(resp) => return Ok(resp),
            Err(e) => {
                if is_connection_error(&e) {
                    last_err = e;
                    // loop and retry
                } else {
                    return Err(e);
                }
            }
        }
    }
    Err(last_err)
}

```

`crates/vigil-common/src/json.rs`:

```rs
// zero-dep json serializer/deserializer
// only uses std, no serde, no external crates

use std::fmt;

// represents any json value
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub enum JsonValue {
    Null,
    Bool(bool),
    Number(f64),
    String(String),
    Array(Vec<JsonValue>),
    Object(Vec<(String, JsonValue)>), // preserves insertion order
}

// max nesting depth to prevent stack overflow on malicious input
pub const MAX_DEPTH: usize = 128;

// parser state - tracks position and nesting depth
struct Parser {
    chars: Vec<char>,
    pos: usize,
    depth: usize,
}

impl Parser {
    fn new(input: &str) -> Self {
        Parser {
            chars: input.chars().collect(),
            depth: 0,
            pos: 0,
        }
    }

    // where we are in the input, for error messages
    fn location(&self) -> String {
        let consumed = &self.chars[..self.pos];
        let line = consumed.iter().filter(|&&c| c == '\n').count() + 1;
        let col = consumed.iter().rev().take_while(|&&c| c != '\n').count() + 1;
        format!("line {}, col {}", line, col)
    }

    fn err<T>(&self, msg: &str) -> Result<T, String> {
        Err(format!("{} at {}", msg, self.location()))
    }

    fn peek(&self) -> Option<char> {
        self.chars.get(self.pos).copied()
    }

    fn next(&mut self) -> Option<char> {
        let ch = self.chars.get(self.pos).copied();
        if ch.is_some() {
            self.pos += 1;
        }
        ch
    }

    fn skip_ws(&mut self) {
        while let Some(ch) = self.peek() {
            if ch == ' ' || ch == '\t' || ch == '\n' || ch == '\r' {
                self.pos += 1;
            } else {
                break;
            }
        }
    }

    // expect a specific character, error if not found
    fn expect(&mut self, expected: char) -> Result<(), String> {
        self.skip_ws();
        match self.next() {
            Some(ch) if ch == expected => Ok(()),
            Some(ch) => self.err(&format!("expected '{}', got '{}'", expected, ch)),
            None => self.err(&format!("expected '{}', got end of input", expected)),
        }
    }

    // try to consume a specific string literal (like "true", "false", "null")
    fn expect_str(&mut self, s: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
        for expected in s.chars() {
            match self.next() {
                Some(ch) if ch == expected => {}
                Some(ch) => return self.err(&format!("expected '{}' in '{}', got '{}'", expected, s, ch)),
                None => return self.err(&format!("unexpected end of input while parsing '{}'", s)),
            }
        }
        Ok(())
    }

    // main entry - parse a single json value
    fn parse_value(&mut self) -> Result<JsonValue, String> {
        self.skip_ws();
        match self.peek() {
            Some('"') => self.parse_string().map(JsonValue::String),
            Some('{') => self.parse_object(),
            Some('[') => self.parse_array(),
            Some('t') => {
                self.expect_str("true")?;
                Ok(JsonValue::Bool(true))
            }
            Some('f') => {
                self.expect_str("false")?;
                Ok(JsonValue::Bool(false))
            }
            Some('n') => {
                self.expect_str("null")?;
                Ok(JsonValue::Null)
            }
            Some(ch) if ch == '-' || ch.is_ascii_digit() => self.parse_number(),
            Some(ch) => self.err(&format!("unexpected character '{}'", ch)),
            None => self.err("unexpected end of input"),
        }
    }

    // parse a json string (consumes opening and closing quotes)
    fn parse_string(&mut self) -> Result<String, String> {
        self.expect('"')?;
        let mut res = String::new();

        loop {
            match self.next() {
                Some('"') => return Ok(res),
                Some('\\') => {
                    // escape sequence
                    match self.next() {
                        Some('"') => res.push('"'),
                        Some('\\') => res.push('\\'),
                        Some('/') => res.push('/'),
                        Some('n') => res.push('\n'),
                        Some('t') => res.push('\t'),
                        Some('r') => res.push('\r'),
                        Some('b') => res.push('\u{0008}'),
                        Some('f') => res.push('\u{000C}'),
                        Some('u') => {
                            let cp = self.parse_unicode_escape()?;
                            // handle surrogate pairs
                            if (0xD800..=0xDBFF).contains(&cp) {
                                // high surrogate - expect \uXXXX low surrogate
                                match (self.next(), self.next()) {
                                    (Some('\\'), Some('u')) => {
                                        let low = self.parse_unicode_escape()?;
                                        if !(0xDC00..=0xDFFF).contains(&low) {
                                            return self.err("expected low surrogate after high surrogate");
                                        }
                                        let full = 0x10000 + ((cp - 0xD800) << 10) + (low - 0xDC00);
                                        match char::from_u32(full as u32) {
                                            Some(c) => res.push(c),
                                            None => return self.err("invalid surrogate pair"),
                                        }
                                    }
                                    _ => return self.err("expected low surrogate pair (\\uXXXX) after high surrogate"),
                                }
                            } else {
                                match char::from_u32(cp as u32) {
                                    Some(c) => res.push(c),
                                    None => return self.err(&format!("invalid unicode codepoint: {:04X}", cp)),
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        Some(ch) => return self.err(&format!("invalid escape sequence '\\{}'", ch)),
                        None => return self.err("unexpected end of input in escape sequence"),
                    }
                }
                Some(ch) => {
                    // control characters (U+0000 through U+001F) must be escaped per spec
                    if ch < '\u{0020}' {
                        return self.err(&format!("unescaped control character U+{:04X} in string", ch as u32));
                    }
                    res.push(ch);
                }
                None => return self.err("unterminated string"),
            }
        }
    }

    // parse 4 hex digits for \uXXXX escapes, returns the codepoint as usize
    fn parse_unicode_escape(&mut self) -> Result<usize, String> {
        let mut val = 0usize;
        for _ in 0..4 {
            match self.next() {
                Some(ch) => {
                    let digit = match ch {
                        '0'..='9' => ch as usize - '0' as usize,
                        'a'..='f' => ch as usize - 'a' as usize + 10,
                        'A'..='F' => ch as usize - 'A' as usize + 10,
                        _ => return self.err(&format!("invalid hex digit '{}' in \\u escape", ch)),
                    };
                    val = val * 16 + digit;
                }
                None => return self.err("unexpected end of input in \\u escape"),
            }
        }
        Ok(val)
    }

    // parse a json number
    fn parse_number(&mut self) -> Result<JsonValue, String> {
        let start = self.pos;

        // optional minus
        if self.peek() == Some('-') {
            self.pos += 1;
        }

        // integer part
        match self.peek() {
            Some('0') => {
                self.pos += 1;
                // after leading 0, next char must not be a digit (no 007 style)
            }
            Some(ch) if ch.is_ascii_digit() => {
                while let Some(ch) = self.peek() {
                    if ch.is_ascii_digit() {
                        self.pos += 1;
                    } else {
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            _ => return self.err("expected digit in number"),
        }

        // fractional part
        if self.peek() == Some('.') {
            self.pos += 1;
            let frac_start = self.pos;
            while let Some(ch) = self.peek() {
                if ch.is_ascii_digit() {
                    self.pos += 1;
                } else {
                    break;
                }
            }
            if self.pos == frac_start {
                return self.err("expected digit after decimal point");
            }
        }

        // exponent part
        if let Some('e' | 'E') = self.peek() {
            self.pos += 1;
            // optional sign
            if let Some('+' | '-') = self.peek() {
                self.pos += 1;
            }
            let exp_start = self.pos;
            while let Some(ch) = self.peek() {
                if ch.is_ascii_digit() {
                    self.pos += 1;
                } else {
                    break;
                }
            }
            if self.pos == exp_start {
                return self.err("expected digit in exponent");
            }
        }

        let num_str: String = self.chars[start..self.pos].iter().collect();
        match num_str.parse::<f64>() {
            Ok(n) => Ok(JsonValue::Number(n)),
            Err(_) => self.err(&format!("invalid number '{}'", num_str)),
        }
    }

    // parse a json object: { "key": value, ... }
    fn parse_object(&mut self) -> Result<JsonValue, String> {
        self.depth += 1;
        if self.depth > MAX_DEPTH {
            return self.err("maximum nesting depth exceeded");
        }
        self.expect('{')?;
        let mut pairs: Vec<(String, JsonValue)> = Vec::new();

        self.skip_ws();
        if self.peek() == Some('}') {
            self.pos += 1;
            self.depth -= 1;
            return Ok(JsonValue::Object(pairs));
        }

        loop {
            self.skip_ws();
            // key must be a string
            if self.peek() != Some('"') {
                return self.err("expected string key in object");
            }
            let key = self.parse_string()?;
            self.expect(':')?;
            let val = self.parse_value()?;
            pairs.push((key, val));

            self.skip_ws();
            match self.peek() {
                Some(',') => {
                    self.pos += 1;
                }
                Some('}') => {
                    self.pos += 1;
                    self.depth -= 1;
                    return Ok(JsonValue::Object(pairs));
                }
                _ => return self.err("expected ',' or '}' in object"),
            }
        }
    }

    // parse a json array: [ value, ... ]
    fn parse_array(&mut self) -> Result<JsonValue, String> {
        self.depth += 1;
        if self.depth > MAX_DEPTH {
            return self.err("maximum nesting depth exceeded");
        }
        self.expect('[')?;
        let mut items: Vec<JsonValue> = Vec::new();

        self.skip_ws();
        if self.peek() == Some(']') {
            self.pos += 1;
            self.depth -= 1;
            return Ok(JsonValue::Array(items));
        }

        loop {
            let val = self.parse_value()?;
            items.push(val);

            self.skip_ws();
            match self.peek() {
                Some(',') => {
                    self.pos += 1;
                }
                Some(']') => {
                    self.pos += 1;
                    self.depth -= 1;
                    return Ok(JsonValue::Array(items));
                }
                _ => return self.err("expected ',' or ']' in array"),
            }
        }
    }
}

// parse a json string into a JsonValue
pub fn parse(input: &str) -> Result<JsonValue, String> {
    let mut parser = Parser::new(input);
    let val = parser.parse_value()?;
    parser.skip_ws();
    if parser.pos != parser.chars.len() {
        return parser.err("trailing data after json value");
    }
    Ok(val)
}

// serialize a JsonValue to a compact json string
pub fn stringify(val: &JsonValue) -> String {
    let mut out = String::new();
    write_value(val, &mut out);
    out
}

// recursive serializer
fn write_value(val: &JsonValue, out: &mut String) {
    match val {
        JsonValue::Null => out.push_str("null"),
        JsonValue::Bool(true) => out.push_str("true"),
        JsonValue::Bool(false) => out.push_str("false"),
        JsonValue::Number(n) => {
            // if the number is a whole integer, skip the decimal point
            if n.fract() == 0.0 && n.is_finite() && n.abs() < (i64::MAX as f64) {
                out.push_str(&(*n as i64).to_string());
            } else {
                out.push_str(&n.to_string());
            }
        }
        JsonValue::String(s) => {
            out.push('"');
            write_escaped(s, out);
            out.push('"');
        }
        JsonValue::Array(items) => {
            out.push('[');
            for (i, item) in items.iter().enumerate() {
                if i > 0 {
                    out.push(',');
                }
                write_value(item, out);
            }
            out.push(']');
        }
        JsonValue::Object(pairs) => {
            out.push('{');
            for (i, (key, val)) in pairs.iter().enumerate() {
                if i > 0 {
                    out.push(',');
                }
                out.push('"');
                write_escaped(key, out);
                out.push('"');
                out.push(':');
                write_value(val, out);
            }
            out.push('}');
        }
    }
}

// escape a string for json output
fn write_escaped(s: &str, out: &mut String) {
    for ch in s.chars() {
        match ch {
            '"' => out.push_str("\\\""),
            '\\' => out.push_str("\\\\"),
            '\n' => out.push_str("\\n"),
            '\r' => out.push_str("\\r"),
            '\t' => out.push_str("\\t"),
            '\u{0008}' => out.push_str("\\b"),
            '\u{000C}' => out.push_str("\\f"),
            c if c < '\u{0020}' => {
                // other control chars get \u00XX treatment
                out.push_str(&format!("\\u{:04x}", c as u32));
            }
            c => out.push(c),
        }
    }
}

impl JsonValue {
    pub fn get(&self, key: &str) -> Option<&JsonValue> {
        match self {
            JsonValue::Object(pairs) => {
                pairs.iter().find(|(k, _)| k == key).map(|(_, v)| v)
            }
            _ => None,
        }
    }

    pub fn as_str(&self) -> Option<&str> {
        match self {
            JsonValue::String(s) => Some(s.as_str()),
            _ => None,
        }
    }

    #[allow(dead_code)]
    pub fn as_f64(&self) -> Option<f64> {
        match self {
            JsonValue::Number(n) => Some(*n),
            _ => None,
        }
    }

    // truncates to i64
    pub fn as_i64(&self) -> Option<i64> {
        match self {
            JsonValue::Number(n) => Some(*n as i64),
            _ => None,
        }
    }

    pub fn as_bool(&self) -> Option<bool> {
        match self {
            JsonValue::Bool(b) => Some(*b),
            _ => None,
        }
    }

    pub fn as_array(&self) -> Option<&Vec<JsonValue>> {
        match self {
            JsonValue::Array(items) => Some(items),
            _ => None,
        }
    }

    #[allow(dead_code)]
    pub fn as_object(&self) -> Option<&Vec<(String, JsonValue)>> {
        match self {
            JsonValue::Object(pairs) => Some(pairs),
            _ => None,
        }
    }

    #[allow(dead_code)]
    pub fn is_null(&self) -> bool {
        matches!(self, JsonValue::Null)
    }
}

pub fn json_obj(pairs: Vec<(&str, JsonValue)>) -> JsonValue {
    JsonValue::Object(
        pairs.into_iter().map(|(k, v)| (k.to_string(), v)).collect(),
    )
}

pub fn json_arr(items: Vec<JsonValue>) -> JsonValue {
    JsonValue::Array(items)
}

pub fn json_str(s: &str) -> JsonValue {
    JsonValue::String(s.to_string())
}

pub fn json_num(n: f64) -> JsonValue {
    JsonValue::Number(n)
}

pub fn json_bool(b: bool) -> JsonValue {
    JsonValue::Bool(b)
}

pub fn json_null() -> JsonValue {
    JsonValue::Null
}

// Display just calls stringify
impl fmt::Display for JsonValue {
    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {
        write!(f, "{}", stringify(self))
    }
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn test_primitives() {
        assert!(parse("null").unwrap().is_null());
        assert_eq!(parse("true").unwrap().as_bool(), Some(true));
        assert_eq!(parse("false").unwrap().as_bool(), Some(false));
        assert_eq!(parse("42").unwrap().as_f64(), Some(42.0));
        assert_eq!(parse("-3.14").unwrap().as_f64(), Some(-3.14));
        assert_eq!(parse("1e10").unwrap().as_f64(), Some(1e10));
        assert_eq!(parse("\"hello\"").unwrap().as_str(), Some("hello"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_string_escapes() {
        let val = parse(r#""hello\nworld""#).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(val.as_str(), Some("hello\nworld"));

        let val = parse(r#""tab\there""#).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(val.as_str(), Some("tab\there"));

        let val = parse(r#""quote\"inside""#).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(val.as_str(), Some("quote\"inside"));

        let val = parse(r#""back\\slash""#).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(val.as_str(), Some("back\\slash"));

        let val = parse(r#""slash\/ok""#).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(val.as_str(), Some("slash/ok"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_unicode_escape() {
        // basic unicode
        let val = parse(r#""\u0041""#).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(val.as_str(), Some("A"));

        // surrogate pair for emoji (U+1F600 = grinning face)
        let val = parse(r#""\uD83D\uDE00""#).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(val.as_str(), Some("\u{1F600}"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_array() {
        let val = parse("[1, 2, 3]").unwrap();
        let arr = val.as_array().unwrap();
        assert_eq!(arr.len(), 3);
        assert_eq!(arr[0].as_f64(), Some(1.0));
        assert_eq!(arr[2].as_f64(), Some(3.0));

        // empty array
        let val = parse("[]").unwrap();
        assert_eq!(val.as_array().unwrap().len(), 0);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_object() {
        let val = parse(r#"{"name": "vigil", "version": 1}"#).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(val.get("name").unwrap().as_str(), Some("vigil"));
        assert_eq!(val.get("version").unwrap().as_f64(), Some(1.0));
        assert!(val.get("missing").is_none());

        // empty object
        let val = parse("{}").unwrap();
        assert_eq!(val.as_object().unwrap().len(), 0);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_nested() {
        let input = r#"{"players": [{"id": 1, "name": "test"}], "count": 1}"#;
        let val = parse(input).unwrap();
        let players = val.get("players").unwrap().as_array().unwrap();
        assert_eq!(players.len(), 1);
        assert_eq!(players[0].get("name").unwrap().as_str(), Some("test"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_stringify_roundtrip() {
        let input = r#"{"a":1,"b":"hello","c":[true,null,3.14],"d":{"nested":false}}"#;
        let val = parse(input).unwrap();
        let output = stringify(&val);
        assert_eq!(output, input);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_builder_helpers() {
        let val = json_obj(vec![
            ("status", json_str("ok")),
            ("code", json_num(200.0)),
            ("data", json_arr(vec![json_bool(true), json_null()])),
        ]);
        let s = stringify(&val);
        assert_eq!(s, r#"{"status":"ok","code":200,"data":[true,null]}"#);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_display() {
        let val = json_str("test");
        assert_eq!(format!("{}", val), "\"test\"");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_as_i64() {
        let val = parse("42").unwrap();
        assert_eq!(val.as_i64(), Some(42));

        let val = parse("3.9").unwrap();
        assert_eq!(val.as_i64(), Some(3)); // truncates
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_error_messages() {
        let res = parse("{bad}");
        assert!(res.is_err());
        assert!(res.unwrap_err().contains("line"));

        let res = parse("[1, 2,]");
        assert!(res.is_err());

        let res = parse("");
        assert!(res.is_err());
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_whitespace_handling() {
        let val = parse("  {  \"a\"  :  1  }  ").unwrap();
        assert_eq!(val.get("a").unwrap().as_f64(), Some(1.0));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_string_escape_output() {
        let val = JsonValue::String("line1\nline2\ttab".to_string());
        assert_eq!(stringify(&val), r#""line1\nline2\ttab""#);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_number_formats() {
        // leading zero not allowed for multi-digit
        assert_eq!(parse("0").unwrap().as_f64(), Some(0.0));
        assert_eq!(parse("-0").unwrap().as_f64(), Some(-0.0));
        assert_eq!(parse("1.5e2").unwrap().as_f64(), Some(150.0));
        assert_eq!(parse("1.5E-2").unwrap().as_f64(), Some(0.015));
        assert_eq!(parse("1e+3").unwrap().as_f64(), Some(1000.0));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_insertion_order_preserved() {
        let input = r#"{"z":1,"a":2,"m":3}"#;
        let val = parse(input).unwrap();
        let pairs = val.as_object().unwrap();
        assert_eq!(pairs[0].0, "z");
        assert_eq!(pairs[1].0, "a");
        assert_eq!(pairs[2].0, "m");
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil-common/src/lib.rs`:

```rs
#![cfg_attr(not(feature = "std"), no_std)]

// shared between BPF kernel program and userspace vigil

#[cfg(feature = "std")]
pub mod json;

#[cfg(feature = "std")]
pub mod crypto;

pub mod sha512;
pub mod ed25519;

#[cfg(feature = "std")]
pub mod http;

#[cfg(feature = "std")]
pub mod runtime;

#[cfg(feature = "std")]
pub mod ws;

#[cfg(feature = "std")]
pub mod timestamp;

#[cfg(feature = "std")]
pub mod log;

// repr(C) = C-compatible memory layout so bytes can be safely cast between BPF and Rust
// no_std required because BPF target has no standard library
// Clone + Copy for BPF (stack values), Debug for println in userspace
//
// syscall_type values:
//   0 = process_vm_readv
//   1 = process_vm_writev
//   2 = ptrace
//   3 = memfd_create
//   4 = mem_write (kprobe)
//   5 = module_load (kprobe do_init_module)
//   6 = mprotect_rwx (PROT_READ|PROT_WRITE|PROT_EXEC)
//   7 = connect (kprobe __sys_connect)

// suspicious syscall event captured by BPF and forwarded to userspace
// repr(C) so bytes can be cast directly from the BPF perf buffer
#[repr(C)]
#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug)]
pub struct SyscallEvent {
    pub pid_caller: i32,
    pub pid_target: i32,   // meaningful for cross-process operations
    pub syscall_type: u8,  // see module-level comment for values
}
```

`crates/vigil-common/src/log.rs`:

```rs
use std::io::Write;
use std::sync::atomic::{AtomicBool, AtomicU8, Ordering};

use crate::timestamp::now_rfc3339;

#[repr(u8)]
#[derive(Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, PartialOrd, Ord, Debug)]
pub enum Level {
    Error = 0,
    Warn  = 1,
    Info  = 2,
    Debug = 3,
}

static LOG_LEVEL: AtomicU8  = AtomicU8::new(2);   // default: Info
static USE_COLOR: AtomicBool = AtomicBool::new(true);

pub fn set_level(level: Level) {
    LOG_LEVEL.store(level as u8, Ordering::Relaxed);
}

pub fn set_color(enabled: bool) {
    USE_COLOR.store(enabled, Ordering::Relaxed);
}

/// Write a log line to stderr.  The call is a no-op when `level` is above the
/// currently configured maximum level.
pub fn log(level: Level, msg: &str) {
    if level as u8 > LOG_LEVEL.load(Ordering::Relaxed) {
        return;
    }

    let color = USE_COLOR.load(Ordering::Relaxed);
    let ts    = now_rfc3339();

    let (label, ansi) = match level {
        Level::Error => ("ERROR", "\x1b[31m"),   // red
        Level::Warn  => ("WARN ", "\x1b[33m"),   // yellow
        Level::Info  => ("INFO ", "\x1b[32m"),   // green
        Level::Debug => ("DEBUG", "\x1b[36m"),   // cyan
    };

    let stderr = std::io::stderr();
    let mut out = stderr.lock();

    if color {
        let _ = writeln!(out, "{} {}{}\x1b[0m {}", ts, ansi, label, msg);
    } else {
        let _ = writeln!(out, "{} {} {}", ts, label, msg);
    }
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Macros
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

#[macro_export]
macro_rules! log_error {
    ($($arg:tt)*) => {
        $crate::log::log($crate::log::Level::Error, &format!($($arg)*))
    };
}

#[macro_export]
macro_rules! log_warn {
    ($($arg:tt)*) => {
        $crate::log::log($crate::log::Level::Warn, &format!($($arg)*))
    };
}

#[macro_export]
macro_rules! log_info {
    ($($arg:tt)*) => {
        $crate::log::log($crate::log::Level::Info, &format!($($arg)*))
    };
}

#[macro_export]
macro_rules! log_debug {
    ($($arg:tt)*) => {
        $crate::log::log($crate::log::Level::Debug, &format!($($arg)*))
    };
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Tests
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn level_ordering() {
        assert!(Level::Error < Level::Warn);
        assert!(Level::Warn  < Level::Info);
        assert!(Level::Info  < Level::Debug);
    }

    #[test]
    fn set_and_get_level() {
        set_level(Level::Debug);
        assert_eq!(LOG_LEVEL.load(Ordering::Relaxed), Level::Debug as u8);

        set_level(Level::Error);
        assert_eq!(LOG_LEVEL.load(Ordering::Relaxed), Level::Error as u8);

        // restore default so other tests are unaffected
        set_level(Level::Info);
    }

    #[test]
    fn set_color_toggle() {
        set_color(false);
        assert!(!USE_COLOR.load(Ordering::Relaxed));

        set_color(true);
        assert!(USE_COLOR.load(Ordering::Relaxed));
    }

    /// Smoke-test: log() must not panic at any level.
    #[test]
    fn log_does_not_panic() {
        set_color(false);
        set_level(Level::Debug);
        log(Level::Error, "error message");
        log(Level::Warn,  "warn message");
        log(Level::Info,  "info message");
        log(Level::Debug, "debug message");
        set_level(Level::Info); // restore
    }

    /// Messages above the configured level must be silently dropped.
    #[test]
    fn level_filter_suppresses_debug() {
        set_level(Level::Info);
        // This must not panic — we cannot easily capture stderr in a unit test,
        // but at minimum it must be a no-op without crashing.
        log(Level::Debug, "this should be filtered out");
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil-common/src/runtime/executor.rs`:

```rs
use std::cell::RefCell;
use std::future::Future;
use std::pin::Pin;
use std::sync::atomic::{AtomicBool, Ordering};
use std::sync::Arc;
use std::task::{Context, Poll};

use crate::runtime::waker::create_waker;

// IO reactor trait — daemon uses epoll, GUI uses SleepReactor
pub trait Reactor {
    // wait for IO events and wake tasks; timeout_ms=0 for non-blocking
    fn poll(&mut self, timeout_ms: i32) -> usize;
}

// no-op reactor that just sleeps — suitable for thread-based async (GUI)
pub struct SleepReactor;

impl Reactor for SleepReactor {
    fn poll(&mut self, timeout_ms: i32) -> usize {
        if timeout_ms > 0 {
            std::thread::sleep(std::time::Duration::from_millis(timeout_ms as u64));
        }
        0
    }
}

struct Task {
    future: Pin<Box<dyn Future<Output = ()>>>,
    ready: Arc<AtomicBool>,
}

struct Runtime {
    tasks: Vec<Option<Task>>,
}

thread_local! {
    static RT: RefCell<Option<Runtime>> = const { RefCell::new(None) };
}

// spawn a task onto the current executor
pub fn spawn<F>(future: F)
where
    F: Future<Output = ()> + 'static,
{
    let ready = Arc::new(AtomicBool::new(true));
    let task = Task {
        future: Box::pin(future),
        ready,
    };
    RT.with(|rt| {
        let mut borrow = rt.borrow_mut();
        let runtime = borrow.as_mut().expect("no runtime active");
        runtime.tasks.push(Some(task));
    });
}

// run the main future and all spawned tasks to completion using SleepReactor
pub fn block_on<F>(main: F)
where
    F: Future<Output = ()>,
{
    block_on_with_reactor(main, SleepReactor);
}

// run the main future with a custom reactor (e.g. epoll for daemon)
pub fn block_on_with_reactor<F, R>(main: F, mut reactor: R)
where
    F: Future<Output = ()>,
    R: Reactor,
{
    RT.with(|rt| {
        *rt.borrow_mut() = Some(Runtime { tasks: vec![] });
    });

    let main_ready = Arc::new(AtomicBool::new(true));
    let mut main_future = Box::pin(main);
    let mut main_done = false;

    loop {
        let mut made_progress = false;
        let mut all_done = true;

        // poll main future
        if !main_done {
            if main_ready.load(Ordering::SeqCst) {
                main_ready.store(false, Ordering::SeqCst);
                let waker = create_waker(&main_ready);
                let mut cx = Context::from_waker(&waker);

                match main_future.as_mut().poll(&mut cx) {
                    Poll::Ready(()) => { main_done = true; made_progress = true; }
                    Poll::Pending => { made_progress = true; }
                }
            }
            if !main_done { all_done = false; }
        }

        // poll spawned tasks
        let task_count = RT.with(|rt| {
            rt.borrow().as_ref().map(|r| r.tasks.len()).unwrap_or(0)
        });

        for i in 0..task_count {
            let is_ready = RT.with(|rt| {
                let borrow = rt.borrow();
                let runtime = borrow.as_ref().unwrap();
                if let Some(Some(task)) = runtime.tasks.get(i) {
                    task.ready.load(Ordering::SeqCst)
                } else {
                    false
                }
            });

            if !is_ready {
                let has_task = RT.with(|rt| {
                    rt.borrow().as_ref().unwrap().tasks.get(i).map(|t| t.is_some()).unwrap_or(false)
                });
                if has_task { all_done = false; }
                continue;
            }

            let mut task = RT.with(|rt| {
                let mut borrow = rt.borrow_mut();
                let runtime = borrow.as_mut().unwrap();
                runtime.tasks[i].take()
            });

            if let Some(ref mut t) = task {
                t.ready.store(false, Ordering::SeqCst);
                let waker = create_waker(&t.ready);
                let mut cx = Context::from_waker(&waker);

                match t.future.as_mut().poll(&mut cx) {
                    Poll::Ready(()) => { made_progress = true; continue; }
                    Poll::Pending => { made_progress = true; all_done = false; }
                }
            }

            RT.with(|rt| {
                let mut borrow = rt.borrow_mut();
                let runtime = borrow.as_mut().unwrap();
                while runtime.tasks.len() <= i { runtime.tasks.push(None); }
                runtime.tasks[i] = task;
            });
        }

        if all_done { break; }

        if !made_progress {
            reactor.poll(100);
        }
    }

    RT.with(|rt| { *rt.borrow_mut() = None; });
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;
    use std::cell::Cell;
    use std::rc::Rc;

    #[test]
    fn block_on_immediate() {
        let ran = Rc::new(Cell::new(false));
        let ran2 = ran.clone();
        block_on(async move { ran2.set(true); });
        assert!(ran.get());
    }

    #[test]
    fn spawn_runs() {
        let flag = Rc::new(Cell::new(false));
        let flag2 = flag.clone();
        block_on(async move {
            spawn(async move { flag2.set(true); });
        });
        assert!(flag.get());
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil-common/src/runtime/waker.rs`:

```rs
use std::sync::atomic::{AtomicBool, Ordering};
use std::sync::Arc;
use std::task::{RawWaker, RawWakerVTable, Waker};

const VTABLE: RawWakerVTable = RawWakerVTable::new(clone_fn, wake_fn, wake_by_ref_fn, drop_fn);

pub fn create_waker(ready: &Arc<AtomicBool>) -> Waker {
    let ptr = Arc::into_raw(ready.clone()) as *const ();
    unsafe { Waker::from_raw(RawWaker::new(ptr, &VTABLE)) }
}

unsafe fn clone_fn(ptr: *const ()) -> RawWaker {
    let arc = unsafe { Arc::from_raw(ptr as *const AtomicBool) };
    let cloned = arc.clone();
    std::mem::forget(arc);
    RawWaker::new(Arc::into_raw(cloned) as *const (), &VTABLE)
}

unsafe fn wake_fn(ptr: *const ()) {
    let arc = unsafe { Arc::from_raw(ptr as *const AtomicBool) };
    arc.store(true, Ordering::SeqCst);
}

unsafe fn wake_by_ref_fn(ptr: *const ()) {
    let arc = unsafe { Arc::from_raw(ptr as *const AtomicBool) };
    arc.store(true, Ordering::SeqCst);
    std::mem::forget(arc);
}

unsafe fn drop_fn(ptr: *const ()) {
    unsafe { drop(Arc::from_raw(ptr as *const AtomicBool)); }
}
```

```rs
    0x748f82ee5defb2fc, 0x78a5636f43172f60, 0x84c87814a1f0ab72, 0x8cc702081a6439ec,
    0x90befffa23631e28, 0xa4506cebde82bde9, 0xbef9a3f7b2c67915, 0xc67178f2e372532b,
    0xca273eceea26619c, 0xd186b8c721c0c207, 0xeada7dd6cde0eb1e, 0xf57d4f7fee6ed178,
    0x06f067aa72176fba, 0x0a637dc5a2c898a6, 0x113f9804bef90dae, 0x1b710b35131c471b,
    0x28db77f523047d84, 0x32caab7b40c72493, 0x3c9ebe0a15c9bebc, 0x431d67c49c100d4c,
    0x4cc5d4becb3e42b6, 0x597f299cfc657e2a, 0x5fcb6fab3ad6faec, 0x6c44198c4a475817,
];

// initial hash values - first 64 bits of the fractional parts of the square roots of the first 8 primes
const H_INIT: [u64; 8] = [
    0x6a09e667f3bcc908, 0xbb67ae8584caa73b, 0x3c6ef372fe94f82b, 0xa54ff53a5f1d36f1,
    0x510e527fade682d1, 0x9b05688c2b3e6c1f, 0x1f83d9abfb41bd6b, 0x5be0cd19137e2179,
];

fn compress(h: &mut [u64; 8], block: &[u8; 128]) {
    let mut w = [0u64; 80];

    for i in 0..16 {
        w[i] = u64::from_be_bytes([
            block[i * 8],     block[i * 8 + 1], block[i * 8 + 2], block[i * 8 + 3],
            block[i * 8 + 4], block[i * 8 + 5], block[i * 8 + 6], block[i * 8 + 7],
        ]);
    }

    for i in 16..80 {
        let s0 = w[i - 15].rotate_right(1) ^ w[i - 15].rotate_right(8) ^ (w[i - 15] >> 7);
        let s1 = w[i - 2].rotate_right(19) ^ w[i - 2].rotate_right(61) ^ (w[i - 2] >> 6);
        w[i] = w[i - 16].wrapping_add(s0).wrapping_add(w[i - 7]).wrapping_add(s1);
    }

    let mut a = h[0];
    let mut b = h[1];
    let mut c = h[2];
    let mut d = h[3];
    let mut e = h[4];
    let mut f = h[5];
    let mut g = h[6];
    let mut hh = h[7];

    for i in 0..80 {
        let s1 = e.rotate_right(14) ^ e.rotate_right(18) ^ e.rotate_right(41);
        let ch = (e & f) ^ ((!e) & g);
        let t1 = hh.wrapping_add(s1).wrapping_add(ch).wrapping_add(K[i]).wrapping_add(w[i]);
        let s0 = a.rotate_right(28) ^ a.rotate_right(34) ^ a.rotate_right(39);
        let maj = (a & b) ^ (a & c) ^ (b & c);
        let t2 = s0.wrapping_add(maj);

        hh = g; g = f; f = e;
        e = d.wrapping_add(t1);
        d = c; c = b; b = a;
        a = t1.wrapping_add(t2);
    }

    h[0] = h[0].wrapping_add(a);
    h[1] = h[1].wrapping_add(b);
    h[2] = h[2].wrapping_add(c);
    h[3] = h[3].wrapping_add(d);
    h[4] = h[4].wrapping_add(e);
    h[5] = h[5].wrapping_add(f);
    h[6] = h[6].wrapping_add(g);
    h[7] = h[7].wrapping_add(hh);
}

// returns the raw 64-byte sha-512 hash
pub fn sha512(data: &[u8]) -> [u8; 64] {
    let bit_len = (data.len() as u128) * 8;
    let mut h = H_INIT;

    let full_blocks = data.len() / 128;
    for i in 0..full_blocks {
        let mut block = [0u8; 128];
        block.copy_from_slice(&data[i * 128..(i + 1) * 128]);
        compress(&mut h, &block);
    }

    // padding block(s): remainder + 0x80 + zeros + 128-bit big-endian length
    let remainder = &data[full_blocks * 128..];
    let mut pad = [0u8; 256];
    pad[..remainder.len()].copy_from_slice(remainder);
    pad[remainder.len()] = 0x80;

    // if remainder fits in 112 bytes, one pad block suffices; otherwise two
    let pad_blocks = if remainder.len() < 112 { 1 } else { 2 };
    let len_offset = pad_blocks * 128 - 16;
    pad[len_offset..len_offset + 16].copy_from_slice(&bit_len.to_be_bytes());

    for i in 0..pad_blocks {
        let mut block = [0u8; 128];
        block.copy_from_slice(&pad[i * 128..(i + 1) * 128]);
        compress(&mut h, &block);
    }

    let mut res = [0u8; 64];
    for i in 0..8 {
        res[i * 8..i * 8 + 8].copy_from_slice(&h[i].to_be_bytes());
    }
    res
}

#[allow(dead_code)]
const HEX_CHARS: &[u8] = b"0123456789abcdef";

// sha-512 digest as lowercase hex string
#[cfg(feature = "std")]
pub fn sha512_hex(data: &[u8]) -> String {
    let hash = sha512(data);
    let mut res = String::with_capacity(128);
    for b in &hash {
        res.push(HEX_CHARS[(b >> 4) as usize] as char);
        res.push(HEX_CHARS[(b & 0x0f) as usize] as char);
    }
    res
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    fn to_hex(bytes: &[u8]) -> [u8; 128] {
        let mut out = [0u8; 128];
        for (i, b) in bytes.iter().enumerate() {
            out[i * 2]     = HEX_CHARS[(b >> 4) as usize];
            out[i * 2 + 1] = HEX_CHARS[(b & 0x0f) as usize];
        }
        out
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_sha512_empty() {
        let hash = to_hex(&sha512(b""));
        assert_eq!(
            &hash,
            b"cf83e1357eefb8bdf1542850d66d8007d620e4050b5715dc83f4a921d36ce9ce47d0d13c5d85f2b0ff8318d2877eec2f63b931bd47417a81a538327af927da3e"
        );
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_sha512_abc() {
        let hash = to_hex(&sha512(b"abc"));
        assert_eq!(
            &hash,
            b"ddaf35a193617abacc417349ae20413112e6fa4e89a97ea20a9eeee64b55d39a2192992a274fc1a836ba3c23a3feebbd454d4423643ce80e2a9ac94fa54ca49f"
        );
    }

    #[test]

        let hash = to_hex(&sha512(data));

        );
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil-common/src/timestamp.rs`:

```rs
use std::time::{SystemTime, UNIX_EPOCH};

/// Returns the current time as an RFC3339 UTC string: "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z"
pub fn now_rfc3339() -> String {
    secs_to_rfc3339(now_secs())
}

/// Converts a unix timestamp (seconds since epoch) to an RFC3339 UTC string.
pub fn secs_to_rfc3339(secs: u64) -> String {
    let (y, mo, d, h, mi, s) = unix_to_datetime(secs);
    format!("{:04}-{:02}-{:02}T{:02}:{:02}:{:02}Z", y, mo, d, h, mi, s)
}

/// Returns the current unix timestamp in seconds.
pub fn now_secs() -> u64 {
    SystemTime::now()
        .duration_since(UNIX_EPOCH)
        .unwrap_or_default()
        .as_secs()
}

/// Parses an RFC3339 UTC string to unix seconds.  Returns `None` on parse
/// failure.  Accepts "Z" and "+00:00" suffixes; fractional seconds are
/// silently ignored.
pub fn rfc3339_to_secs(s: &str) -> Option<u64> {
    // Strip trailing 'Z' or '+00:00'
    let s = if let Some(stripped) = s.strip_suffix("+00:00") {
        stripped
    } else {
        s.trim_end_matches('Z')
    };
    // Strip fractional seconds if present
    let s = if let Some(dot) = s.find('.') { &s[..dot] } else { s };
    if s.len() < 19 {
        return None;
    }
    let year: u64 = s[..4].parse().ok()?;
    let month: u64 = s[5..7].parse().ok()?;
    let day: u64 = s[8..10].parse().ok()?;
    let hour: u64 = s[11..13].parse().ok()?;
    let min: u64 = s[14..16].parse().ok()?;
    let sec: u64 = s[17..19].parse().ok()?;

    // Civil date to days since unix epoch (Gregorian algorithm)
    let y = if month <= 2 { year - 1 } else { year };
    let m = if month <= 2 { month + 9 } else { month - 3 };
    let era = y / 400;
    let yoe = y % 400;
    let doy = (153 * m + 2) / 5 + day - 1;
    let doe = yoe * 365 + yoe / 4 - yoe / 100 + doy;
    let days = era * 146097 + doe;
    let epoch_days = days.checked_sub(719468)?;
    Some(epoch_days * 86400 + hour * 3600 + min * 60 + sec)
}

fn unix_to_datetime(secs: u64) -> (u64, u64, u64, u64, u64, u64) {
    let s = secs % 60;
    let mi = (secs / 60) % 60;
    let h = (secs / 3600) % 24;
    let mut days = secs / 86400;

    let mut y = 1970u64;
    loop {
        let dy = if is_leap(y) { 366 } else { 365 };
        if days < dy {
            break;
        }
        days -= dy;
        y += 1;
    }

    let mdays = month_days(y);
    let mut mo = 1u64;
    for (i, &md) in mdays.iter().enumerate() {
        if days < md as u64 {
            mo = i as u64 + 1;
            break;
        }
        days -= md as u64;
    }

    let d = days + 1;
    (y, mo, d, h, mi, s)
}

fn is_leap(y: u64) -> bool {
    (y.is_multiple_of(4) && !y.is_multiple_of(100)) || y.is_multiple_of(400)
}

fn month_days(y: u64) -> [u8; 12] {
    [
        31,
        if is_leap(y) { 29 } else { 28 },
        31,
        30,
        31,
        30,
        31,
        31,
        30,
        31,
        30,
        31,
    ]
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn test_epoch() {
        assert_eq!(secs_to_rfc3339(0), "1970-01-01T00:00:00Z");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_known_date() {
        // 2024-01-01T00:00:00Z = 1704067200
        assert_eq!(secs_to_rfc3339(1704067200), "2024-01-01T00:00:00Z");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_known_datetime() {
        // 2024-01-15T10:30:00Z = 1705314600
        assert_eq!(secs_to_rfc3339(1705314600), "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_leap_year_feb29() {
        // 2024 is a leap year: 2024-02-29T00:00:00Z = 1709164800
        assert_eq!(secs_to_rfc3339(1709164800), "2024-02-29T00:00:00Z");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_non_leap_century() {
        assert!(!is_leap(1900));
        assert!(!is_leap(2100));
        assert!(is_leap(2000));
        assert!(is_leap(2024));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_roundtrip() {
        let ts = 1704067200u64;
        let s = secs_to_rfc3339(ts);
        assert_eq!(rfc3339_to_secs(&s).unwrap(), ts);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_rfc3339_plus_offset() {
        assert_eq!(
            rfc3339_to_secs("2024-01-01T00:00:00+00:00").unwrap(),
            1704067200
        );
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_rfc3339_z() {
        assert_eq!(rfc3339_to_secs("2024-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap(), 1704067200);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_fractional_seconds() {
        assert_eq!(
            rfc3339_to_secs("2024-01-01T00:00:00.123Z").unwrap(),
            1704067200
        );
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil-common/src/ws.rs`:

```rs
// zero-dep WebSocket client (RFC 6455) — connects to vigil-server WS endpoint
// Receives push events: trust_update, banned, party_invite, match_found

use std::io::{Read, Write};
use std::net::TcpStream;
use std::time::Duration;

// WebSocket client (RFC 6455) for ws:// endpoints
pub struct WsClient {
    stream: TcpStream,
    recv_buf: Vec<u8>,
}

// text-frame message received from the server
pub struct WsMessage {
    pub text: String,
}

impl WsClient {
    // connect with WebSocket upgrade handshake
    pub fn connect(url: &str, token: Option<&str>) -> Result<Self, String> {
        let (host, port, path) = parse_ws_url(url)?;

        let mut stream = TcpStream::connect(format!("{}:{}", host, port))
            .map_err(|e| format!("ws connect: {}", e))?;

        stream.set_read_timeout(Some(Duration::from_millis(100))).ok();
        stream.set_write_timeout(Some(Duration::from_secs(5))).ok();

        // WebSocket upgrade request
        let key = generate_ws_key();
        let mut req = format!(
            "GET {} HTTP/1.1\r\n\
             Host: {}\r\n\
             Upgrade: websocket\r\n\
             Connection: Upgrade\r\n\
             Sec-WebSocket-Key: {}\r\n\
             Sec-WebSocket-Version: 13\r\n",
            path, host, key
        );
        if let Some(t) = token {
            req.push_str(&format!("Authorization: Bearer {}\r\n", t));
        }
        req.push_str("\r\n");

        stream.write_all(req.as_bytes())
            .map_err(|e| format!("ws write upgrade: {}", e))?;

        // Read upgrade response — just check for 101
        let mut buf = [0u8; 1024];
        let n = stream.read(&mut buf).map_err(|e| format!("ws read upgrade: {}", e))?;
        let resp = String::from_utf8_lossy(&buf[..n]);

        if !resp.contains("101") {
            return Err(format!("ws upgrade failed: {}", resp.lines().next().unwrap_or("")));
        }

        // Switch to blocking with longer timeout for message reads
        stream.set_read_timeout(Some(Duration::from_millis(50))).ok();

        Ok(WsClient { stream, recv_buf: Vec::new() })
    }

    // non-blocking receive; buffers partial reads across calls
    pub fn try_recv(&mut self) -> Option<WsMessage> {
        // Append any newly available bytes to the persistent buffer.
        let mut tmp = [0u8; 4096];
        match self.stream.read(&mut tmp) {
            Ok(0) | Err(_) => {} // timeout, WouldBlock, or EOF — try decoding what we have
            Ok(n) => self.recv_buf.extend_from_slice(&tmp[..n]),
        }

        // Try to decode a complete frame from whatever is buffered.
        match try_decode_text_frame(&self.recv_buf) {
            Some((text, consumed)) => {
                // Remove exactly the bytes that formed this frame.
                self.recv_buf.drain(..consumed);
                Some(WsMessage { text })
            }
            None => None,
        }
    }

    // send a text frame (masked per RFC 6455)
    pub fn send(&mut self, msg: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
        let data = msg.as_bytes();
        let mask_key = generate_mask_key();

        let mut frame = vec![0x81u8]; // FIN + text opcode

        if data.len() < 126 {
            frame.push(0x80 | data.len() as u8); // masked bit + length
        } else {
            frame.push(0x80 | 126);
            frame.push((data.len() >> 8) as u8);
            frame.push(data.len() as u8);
        }

        frame.extend_from_slice(&mask_key);

        // mask the payload
        for (i, &byte) in data.iter().enumerate() {
            frame.push(byte ^ mask_key[i % 4]);
        }

        self.stream.write_all(&frame).map_err(|e| format!("ws send: {}", e))
    }

    // send a close frame
    pub fn close(&mut self) {
        let frame = [0x88, 0x80, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00, 0x00]; // masked close
        let _ = self.stream.write_all(&frame);
    }
}

impl Drop for WsClient {
    fn drop(&mut self) {
        self.close();
    }
}

// decode one text frame from buf; returns (text, bytes_consumed) or None if incomplete
fn try_decode_text_frame(buf: &[u8]) -> Option<(String, usize)> {
    if buf.len() < 2 { return None; }
    let opcode = buf[0] & 0x0F;

    // only handle text frames (0x1); silently skip ping/pong/close by consuming them
    // without returning a message so the caller can loop if needed
    if opcode != 0x1 { return None; }

    let masked = buf[1] & 0x80 != 0;
    let mut payload_len = (buf[1] & 0x7F) as usize;
    let mut offset = 2;

    if payload_len == 126 {
        if buf.len() < 4 { return None; }
        payload_len = ((buf[2] as usize) << 8) | buf[3] as usize;
        offset = 4;
    } else if payload_len == 127 {
        // 8-byte extended length — require at least the header before deciding
        if buf.len() < 10 { return None; }
        // frames this large are not expected; skip by returning None
        return None;
    }

    let mask_key = if masked {
        if buf.len() < offset + 4 { return None; }
        let key = [buf[offset], buf[offset+1], buf[offset+2], buf[offset+3]];
        offset += 4;
        Some(key)
    } else {
        None
    };

    // Not enough data buffered yet — wait for more reads
    if buf.len() < offset + payload_len { return None; }

    let mut data = buf[offset..offset + payload_len].to_vec();
    let total_consumed = offset + payload_len;

    if let Some(key) = mask_key {
        for (i, byte) in data.iter_mut().enumerate() {
            *byte ^= key[i % 4];
        }
    }

    let text = String::from_utf8(data).ok()?;
    Some((text, total_consumed))
}

fn parse_ws_url(url: &str) -> Result<(String, u16, String), String> {
    let rest = url.strip_prefix("ws://")
        .or_else(|| url.strip_prefix("http://"))
        .ok_or_else(|| format!("unsupported ws scheme: {}", url))?;

    let (authority, path) = match rest.find('/') {
        Some(i) => (&rest[..i], rest[i..].to_string()),
        None => (rest, "/ws".to_string()),
    };

    let (host, port) = match authority.find(':') {
        Some(i) => {
            let p = authority[i+1..].parse::<u16>().map_err(|_| "invalid port")?;
            (authority[..i].to_string(), p)
        }
        None => (authority.to_string(), 80),
    };

    Ok((host, port, path))
}

fn generate_mask_key() -> [u8; 4] {
    // Simple pseudo-random mask using time nanos + thread id (no external RNG needed)
    use std::time::SystemTime;
    let nanos = SystemTime::now()
        .duration_since(SystemTime::UNIX_EPOCH)
        .map(|d| d.as_nanos() as u64)
        .unwrap_or(0x1234_5678);
    let tid = std::thread::current().id();
    let mix = nanos.wrapping_mul(6364136223846793005).wrapping_add(format!("{:?}", tid).len() as u64);
    [
        (mix >> 24) as u8,
        (mix >> 16) as u8,
        (mix >> 8) as u8,
        mix as u8,
    ]
}

fn generate_ws_key() -> String {
    // Simple deterministic key — server doesn't validate the randomness
    base64_encode(b"vigil-gui-ws-key")
}

fn base64_encode(data: &[u8]) -> String {
    const CHARS: &[u8] = b"ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/";
    let mut result = String::new();
    for chunk in data.chunks(3) {
        let b0 = chunk[0] as u32;
        let b1 = if chunk.len() > 1 { chunk[1] as u32 } else { 0 };
        let b2 = if chunk.len() > 2 { chunk[2] as u32 } else { 0 };
        let triple = (b0 << 16) | (b1 << 8) | b2;
        result.push(CHARS[((triple >> 18) & 0x3F) as usize] as char);
        result.push(CHARS[((triple >> 12) & 0x3F) as usize] as char);
        if chunk.len() > 1 { result.push(CHARS[((triple >> 6) & 0x3F) as usize] as char); } else { result.push('='); }
        if chunk.len() > 2 { result.push(CHARS[(triple & 0x3F) as usize] as char); } else { result.push('='); }
    }
    result
}
```

`crates/vigil-gui/Cargo.toml`:

```toml
[package]
name = "vigil-gui"
version.workspace = true
edition.workspace = true
authors.workspace = true
license.workspace = true
repository.workspace = true
description = "Vigil anti-cheat GUI client"

[dependencies]
slint = "1.12"
vigil-common = { path = "../vigil-common", features = ["std"] }

[build-dependencies]
slint-build = "1.12"

```

`crates/vigil-gui/build.rs`:

```rs
fn main() {
    slint_build::compile("ui/main.slint").unwrap();
}

```

`crates/vigil-gui/src/api.rs`:

```rs
// vigil-server API client — zero-dep, uses vigil-common::json

use crate::http;
use crate::json;
use vigil_common::json::{JsonValue, json_obj, json_str, stringify};

pub struct Friend {
    pub name: String,
    pub trust_score: i64,
    pub is_clean: bool,
    pub banned: bool,
}

pub struct Server {
    pub name: String,
    pub game: String,
    pub max_players: i64,
    pub current_players: i64,
    pub address: String,
}

pub struct Match {
    pub id: String,
    pub created_at: String,
    #[allow(dead_code)]
    pub ended_at: Option<String>,
    pub game: Option<String>,
    pub map: Option<String>,
    pub result: Option<String>,
    pub duration: Option<String>,
}

pub struct QueueResponse {
    pub status: String,
    pub position: Option<i32>,
}

pub struct Client {
    pub base_url: String,
    pub token: Option<String>,
    pub player_id: Option<String>,
}

impl Client {
    pub fn new(base_url: &str) -> Self {
        Client {
            base_url: base_url.trim_end_matches('/').to_string(),
            token: None,
            player_id: None,
        }
    }

    fn tok(&self) -> Option<&str> {
        self.token.as_deref()
    }

    pub fn login(&mut self, name: &str, password: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
        let body = stringify(&json_obj(vec![
            ("name", json_str(name)),
            ("password", json_str(password)),
        ]));
        let resp = http::post(&format!("{}/api/player/login", self.base_url), &body, None)?;
        let data = json::parse_response(&resp.body)?;
        self.token = Some(get_str(&data, "token")?);
        let player = data.get("player").ok_or("missing player")?;
        self.player_id = Some(get_str(player, "id")?);
        Ok(())
    }

    pub fn register(&mut self, name: &str, password: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
        let body = stringify(&json_obj(vec![
            ("name", json_str(name)),
            ("password", json_str(password)),
        ]));
        let resp = http::post(&format!("{}/api/player/register", self.base_url), &body, None)?;
        let data = json::parse_response(&resp.body)?;
        self.token = Some(get_str(&data, "token")?);
        let player = data.get("player").ok_or("missing player")?;
        self.player_id = Some(get_str(player, "id")?);
        Ok(())
    }

    pub fn get_friends(&self) -> Result<Vec<Friend>, String> {
        let resp = http::get(&format!("{}/api/friends", self.base_url), self.tok())?;
        let data = json::parse_response(&resp.body)?;
        let arr = data.as_array().ok_or("expected array")?;
        Ok(arr.iter().map(|v| Friend {
            name: v.get("name").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("").to_string(),
            trust_score: v.get("trust_score").and_then(|x| x.as_i64()).unwrap_or(0),
            is_clean: v.get("is_clean").and_then(|x| x.as_bool()).unwrap_or(true),
            banned: v.get("banned").and_then(|x| x.as_bool()).unwrap_or(false),
        }).collect())
    }

    pub fn add_friend(&self, name: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
        let body = stringify(&json_obj(vec![("friend_name", json_str(name))]));
        let resp = http::post(&format!("{}/api/friends/add", self.base_url), &body, self.tok())?;
        let _ = json::parse_response(&resp.body)?;
        Ok(())
    }

    pub fn remove_friend(&self, id: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
        let body = stringify(&json_obj(vec![("friend_id", json_str(id))]));
        http::post(&format!("{}/api/friends/remove", self.base_url), &body, self.tok())?;
        Ok(())
    }

    pub fn create_party(&self) -> Result<String, String> {
        let resp = http::post(&format!("{}/api/party/create", self.base_url), "{}", self.tok())?;
        let data = json::parse_response(&resp.body)?;
        get_str(&data, "id")
    }

    pub fn leave_party(&self) -> Result<(), String> {
        http::post(&format!("{}/api/party/leave", self.base_url), "{}", self.tok())?;
        Ok(())
    }

    pub fn invite_to_party(&self, player_id: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
        let body = stringify(&json_obj(vec![("player_id", json_str(player_id))]));
        http::post(&format!("{}/api/party/invite", self.base_url), &body, self.tok())?;
        Ok(())
    }

    pub fn join_queue(&self, game: &str) -> Result<QueueResponse, String> {
        let body = stringify(&json_obj(vec![("game", json_str(game))]));
        let resp = http::post(&format!("{}/api/queue/join", self.base_url), &body, self.tok())?;
        let data = json::parse_response(&resp.body)?;
        Ok(QueueResponse {
            status: data.get("status").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("queued").to_string(),
            position: data.get("position").and_then(|x| x.as_i64()).map(|n| n as i32),
        })
    }

    pub fn leave_queue(&self) -> Result<(), String> {
        http::post(&format!("{}/api/queue/leave", self.base_url), "{}", self.tok())?;
        Ok(())
    }

    pub fn get_servers(&self) -> Result<Vec<Server>, String> {
        let resp = http::get(&format!("{}/api/servers", self.base_url), self.tok())?;
        let data = json::parse_response(&resp.body)?;
        let arr = data.as_array().ok_or("expected array")?;
        Ok(arr.iter().map(|v| Server {
            name: v.get("name").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("").to_string(),
            game: v.get("game").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("").to_string(),
            max_players: v.get("max_players").and_then(|x| x.as_i64()).unwrap_or(0),
            current_players: v.get("current_players").and_then(|x| x.as_i64()).unwrap_or(0),
            address: v.get("address").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("").to_string(),
        }).collect())
    }

    pub fn get_matches(&self) -> Result<Vec<Match>, String> {
        let pid = self.player_id.as_deref().unwrap_or("");
        let resp = http::get(&format!("{}/api/player/{}/matches", self.base_url, pid), self.tok())?;
        let data = json::parse_response(&resp.body)?;
        let arr = data.as_array().ok_or("expected array")?;
        Ok(arr.iter().map(|v| Match {
            id: v.get("id").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("").to_string(),
            created_at: v.get("created_at").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("").to_string(),
            ended_at: v.get("ended_at").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).map(|s| s.to_string()),
            game: v.get("game").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).map(|s| s.to_string()),
            map: v.get("map").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).map(|s| s.to_string()),
            result: v.get("result").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).map(|s| s.to_string()),
            duration: v.get("duration").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).map(|s| s.to_string()),
        }).collect())
    }
}

fn get_str(val: &JsonValue, key: &str) -> Result<String, String> {
    val.get(key)
        .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
        .map(|s| s.to_string())
        .ok_or_else(|| format!("missing field: {}", key))
}
```

`crates/vigil-gui/src/config.rs`:

```rs
// Config persistence for vigil-gui
// Reads/writes ~/.config/vigil/gui.json using vigil_common::json (zero external deps)

use crate::json::{parse, stringify, json_obj, json_str, JsonValue};
use std::fs;
use std::path::PathBuf;

/// All persisted GUI settings.
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct Config {
    // Kernel module toggles
    pub ebpf_monitoring: bool,
    pub process_integrity: bool,
    pub network_analysis: bool,
    pub memory_scanner: bool,
    pub auto_update: bool,
    // Game profile toggles
    pub auto_detect_game: bool,
    pub overlay_hud: bool,
    // Network toggles
    pub tls_enabled: bool,
    pub auto_reconnect: bool,
    // Connection
    pub server_url: String,
    // Active profile
    pub active_profile: String,
}

impl Default for Config {
    fn default() -> Self {
        Config {
            ebpf_monitoring: true,
            process_integrity: true,
            network_analysis: true,
            memory_scanner: false,
            auto_update: true,
            auto_detect_game: true,
            overlay_hud: false,
            tls_enabled: true,
            auto_reconnect: true,
            server_url: "http://localhost:3000".to_string(),
            active_profile: "none".to_string(),
        }
    }
}

/// Returns the path to the config file: ~/.config/vigil/gui.json
fn config_path() -> Option<PathBuf> {
    // $HOME is the most reliable on Linux
    let home = std::env::var("HOME").ok()?;
    Some(PathBuf::from(home).join(".config").join("vigil").join("gui.json"))
}

impl Config {
    /// Load config from disk. Falls back to defaults if the file is missing or malformed.
    pub fn load() -> Self {
        let defaults = Config::default();
        let path = match config_path() {
            Some(p) => p,
            None => return defaults,
        };

        let text = match fs::read_to_string(&path) {
            Ok(t) => t,
            Err(_) => return defaults,
        };

        let root = match parse(&text) {
            Ok(v) => v,
            Err(e) => {
                eprintln!("vigil-gui: failed to parse config: {}", e);
                return defaults;
            }
        };

        // Helper: pull a bool out of the parsed object, falling back to the default value.
        let get_bool = |key: &str, fallback: bool| -> bool {
            root.get(key).and_then(|v| v.as_bool()).unwrap_or(fallback)
        };
        let get_str = |key: &str, fallback: &str| -> String {
            root.get(key).and_then(|v| v.as_str()).unwrap_or(fallback).to_string()
        };

        Config {
            ebpf_monitoring:  get_bool("ebpf_monitoring",  defaults.ebpf_monitoring),
            process_integrity: get_bool("process_integrity", defaults.process_integrity),
            network_analysis: get_bool("network_analysis",  defaults.network_analysis),
            memory_scanner:   get_bool("memory_scanner",    defaults.memory_scanner),
            auto_update:      get_bool("auto_update",       defaults.auto_update),
            auto_detect_game: get_bool("auto_detect_game",  defaults.auto_detect_game),
            overlay_hud:      get_bool("overlay_hud",       defaults.overlay_hud),
            tls_enabled:      get_bool("tls_enabled",       defaults.tls_enabled),
            auto_reconnect:   get_bool("auto_reconnect",    defaults.auto_reconnect),
            server_url:       get_str("server_url",         &defaults.server_url),
            active_profile:   get_str("active_profile",     &defaults.active_profile),
        }
    }

    /// Serialize the config and write it to ~/.config/vigil/gui.json.
    /// Creates the directory if it does not exist. Errors are logged to stderr.
    pub fn save(&self) {
        let path = match config_path() {
            Some(p) => p,
            None => {
                eprintln!("vigil-gui: cannot determine config path (HOME not set)");
                return;
            }
        };

        // Create parent directory (~/.config/vigil/) if needed.
        if let Some(dir) = path.parent() && let Err(e) = fs::create_dir_all(dir) {
                eprintln!("vigil-gui: failed to create config dir {:?}: {}", dir, e);
                return;
        }

        let json = json_obj(vec![
            ("ebpf_monitoring",  JsonValue::Bool(self.ebpf_monitoring)),
            ("process_integrity", JsonValue::Bool(self.process_integrity)),
            ("network_analysis", JsonValue::Bool(self.network_analysis)),
            ("memory_scanner",   JsonValue::Bool(self.memory_scanner)),
            ("auto_update",      JsonValue::Bool(self.auto_update)),
            ("auto_detect_game", JsonValue::Bool(self.auto_detect_game)),
            ("overlay_hud",      JsonValue::Bool(self.overlay_hud)),
            ("tls_enabled",      JsonValue::Bool(self.tls_enabled)),
            ("auto_reconnect",   JsonValue::Bool(self.auto_reconnect)),
            ("server_url",       json_str(&self.server_url)),
            ("active_profile",   json_str(&self.active_profile)),
        ]);

        let text = stringify(&json);
        if let Err(e) = fs::write(&path, text) {
            eprintln!("vigil-gui: failed to write config to {:?}: {}", path, e);
        }
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil-gui/src/ipc.rs`:

```rs
// IPC client - talks to vigil daemon via /run/vigil.sock
// Uses vigil-common::json instead of regex-based parsing

use std::io::{Read, Write};
use std::os::unix::net::UnixStream;
use std::time::Duration;
use vigil_common::json::{parse, stringify, json_obj, json_str};

const SOCK_PATH: &str = "/run/vigil.sock";

pub fn send_command(cmd: &str) -> Result<String, String> {
    let mut stream = UnixStream::connect(SOCK_PATH)
        .map_err(|e| format!("ipc connect: {}", e))?;
    stream.set_read_timeout(Some(Duration::from_secs(2))).ok();
    stream.set_write_timeout(Some(Duration::from_secs(2))).ok();

    stream.write_all(cmd.as_bytes())
        .map_err(|e| format!("ipc write: {}", e))?;

    let mut buf = [0u8; 4096];
    let n = stream.read(&mut buf)
        .map_err(|e| format!("ipc read: {}", e))?;

    Ok(String::from_utf8_lossy(&buf[..n]).trim().to_string())
}

pub fn get_status() -> Result<DaemonStatus, String> {
    let resp = send_command(&stringify(&json_obj(vec![("cmd", json_str("status"))])))?;
    let val = parse(&resp).map_err(|e| format!("ipc json: {}", e))?;

    Ok(DaemonStatus {
        running: val.get("running").and_then(|v| v.as_bool()).unwrap_or(false),
        trust_score: val.get("trust_score").and_then(|v| v.as_i64()).unwrap_or(0) as i32,
        ebpf: val.get("ebpf").and_then(|v| v.as_bool()).unwrap_or(false),
        profile: val.get("profile").and_then(|v| v.as_str()).unwrap_or("").to_string(),
        scan_count: val.get("scan_count").and_then(|v| v.as_i64()).unwrap_or(0),
        banned: val.get("banned").and_then(|v| v.as_bool()).unwrap_or(false),
    })
}

pub fn set_profile(name: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
    let cmd = stringify(&json_obj(vec![
        ("cmd", json_str("set_profile")),
        ("profile", json_str(name)),
    ]));
    let resp = send_command(&cmd)?;
    let val = parse(&resp).map_err(|e| format!("ipc json: {}", e))?;

    if val.get("status").and_then(|v| v.as_str()) == Some("ok") {
        Ok(())
    } else {
        Err(resp)
    }
}

pub struct DaemonStatus {
    pub running: bool,
    pub trust_score: i32,
    pub ebpf: bool,
    pub profile: String,
    pub scan_count: i64,
    pub banned: bool,
}

```

`crates/vigil-gui/src/json.rs`:

```rs
// zero-dep json helpers for GUI — uses vigil-common::json
pub use vigil_common::json::{parse, stringify, JsonValue, json_obj, json_str};

/// Parse a server response that wraps data in {"success":true,"data":...,"error":"..."}
pub fn parse_response(body: &str) -> Result<JsonValue, String> {
    if body.trim().is_empty() {
        return Err("empty response".to_string());
    }

    let root = parse(body)?;

    let success = root.get("success")
        .and_then(|v| v.as_bool())
        .unwrap_or(false);

    if success {
        match root.get("data") {
            Some(data) => Ok(data.clone()),
            None => Err("missing data in response".to_string()),
        }
    } else {
        let msg = root.get("error")
            .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
            .unwrap_or("unknown server error");
        Err(msg.to_string())
    }
}
```
