`crates/vigil-gui/src/main.rs`:

```rs
slint::include_modules!();

mod api;
mod config;
mod http;
mod ipc;
mod json;
mod ws_events;

use std::sync::{Arc, Mutex};
use slint::{ModelRc, VecModel};

const DEFAULT_SERVER: &str = "http://localhost:3000";

fn main() -> Result<(), slint::PlatformError> {
    let app = App::new()?;
    let client = Arc::new(Mutex::new(api::Client::new(DEFAULT_SERVER)));

    // ── load persisted config and apply to bridge ──
    let cfg = config::Config::load();
    {
        let b = app.global::<VigilBridge>();
        b.set_setting_ebpf_monitoring(cfg.ebpf_monitoring);
        b.set_setting_process_integrity(cfg.process_integrity);
        b.set_setting_network_analysis(cfg.network_analysis);
        b.set_setting_memory_scanner(cfg.memory_scanner);
        b.set_setting_auto_update(cfg.auto_update);
        b.set_setting_auto_detect_game(cfg.auto_detect_game);
        b.set_setting_overlay_hud(cfg.overlay_hud);
        b.set_setting_tls_enabled(cfg.tls_enabled);
        b.set_setting_auto_reconnect(cfg.auto_reconnect);
        if cfg.active_profile != "none" {
            b.set_active_profile(cfg.active_profile.clone().into());
        }
    }

    // ── save-settings callback (triggered by the Save button) ──
    let weak = app.as_weak();
    app.global::<VigilBridge>().on_save_settings(move || {
        if let Some(app) = weak.upgrade() {
            let b = app.global::<VigilBridge>();
            let cfg = config::Config {
                ebpf_monitoring:  b.get_setting_ebpf_monitoring(),
                process_integrity: b.get_setting_process_integrity(),
                network_analysis: b.get_setting_network_analysis(),
                memory_scanner:   b.get_setting_memory_scanner(),
                auto_update:      b.get_setting_auto_update(),
                auto_detect_game: b.get_setting_auto_detect_game(),
                overlay_hud:      b.get_setting_overlay_hud(),
                tls_enabled:      b.get_setting_tls_enabled(),
                auto_reconnect:   b.get_setting_auto_reconnect(),
                server_url:       DEFAULT_SERVER.to_string(),
                active_profile:   b.get_active_profile().to_string(),
            };
            cfg.save();
        }
    });

    // ── login (async) ──
    let weak = app.as_weak();
    let cl = client.clone();
    app.global::<VigilBridge>().on_do_login(move |username, password| {
        if username.is_empty() || password.is_empty() {
            let w = weak.clone();
            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() {
                    app.global::<VigilBridge>().set_error_msg("fill in both fields".into());
                }
            }).ok();
            return;
        }
        let w = weak.clone();
        let cl = cl.clone();
        let user = username.to_string();
        let pass = password.to_string();
        std::thread::spawn(move || {
            let result = cl.lock().unwrap().login(&user, &pass);
            let cl2 = cl.clone();
            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() {
                    let b = app.global::<VigilBridge>();
                    match result {
                        Ok(()) => {
                            b.set_error_msg("".into());
                            b.set_player_name(user.into());
                            b.set_logged_in(true);
                            b.set_current_page("home".into());
                            refresh_daemon_status(&b);
                            load_all_data(&cl2.lock().unwrap(), &b);
                            // start WebSocket listener for real-time events
                            if let Some(tok) = cl2.lock().unwrap().token.as_deref() {
                                ws_events::start_ws_listener(DEFAULT_SERVER, tok, w.clone());
                            }
                        }
                        Err(e) => b.set_error_msg(e.into()),
                    }
                }
            }).ok();
        });
    });

    // ── register (async) ──
    let weak = app.as_weak();
    let cl = client.clone();
    app.global::<VigilBridge>().on_do_register(move |username, password| {
        if username.is_empty() || password.len() < 6 {
            let w = weak.clone();
            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() {
                    app.global::<VigilBridge>().set_error_msg("name required, password min 6 chars".into());
                }
            }).ok();
            return;
        }
        let w = weak.clone();
        let cl = cl.clone();
        let user = username.to_string();
        let pass = password.to_string();
        std::thread::spawn(move || {
            let result = cl.lock().unwrap().register(&user, &pass);
            let cl2 = cl.clone();
            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() {
                    let b = app.global::<VigilBridge>();
                    match result {
                        Ok(()) => {
                            b.set_error_msg("".into());
                            b.set_player_name(user.into());
                            b.set_logged_in(true);
                            b.set_current_page("home".into());
                            refresh_daemon_status(&b);
                            load_all_data(&cl2.lock().unwrap(), &b);
                            if let Some(tok) = cl2.lock().unwrap().token.as_deref() {
                                ws_events::start_ws_listener(DEFAULT_SERVER, tok, w.clone());
                            }
                        }
                        Err(e) => b.set_error_msg(e.into()),
                    }
                }
            }).ok();
        });
    });

    // ── logout ──
    let weak = app.as_weak();
    app.global::<VigilBridge>().on_do_logout(move || {
        if let Some(app) = weak.upgrade() {
            let b = app.global::<VigilBridge>();
            // persist settings before clearing session state
            let cfg = config::Config {
                ebpf_monitoring:  b.get_setting_ebpf_monitoring(),
                process_integrity: b.get_setting_process_integrity(),
                network_analysis: b.get_setting_network_analysis(),
                memory_scanner:   b.get_setting_memory_scanner(),
                auto_update:      b.get_setting_auto_update(),
                auto_detect_game: b.get_setting_auto_detect_game(),
                overlay_hud:      b.get_setting_overlay_hud(),
                tls_enabled:      b.get_setting_tls_enabled(),
                auto_reconnect:   b.get_setting_auto_reconnect(),
                server_url:       DEFAULT_SERVER.to_string(),
                active_profile:   b.get_active_profile().to_string(),
            };
            cfg.save();
            b.set_logged_in(false);
            b.set_current_page("login".into());
            b.set_player_name("".into());
            b.set_in_party(false);
            b.set_in_queue(false);
            b.set_error_msg("".into());
        }
    });

    // ── refresh status (async) ──
    let weak = app.as_weak();
    let cl = client.clone();
    app.global::<VigilBridge>().on_refresh_status(move || {
        let w = weak.clone();
        let cl = cl.clone();
        std::thread::spawn(move || {
            let status = ipc::get_status();
            let friends;
            let servers;
            let matches;
            {
                let c = cl.lock().unwrap();
                friends = c.get_friends().ok();
                servers = c.get_servers().ok();
                matches = c.get_matches().ok();
            }
            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() {
                    let b = app.global::<VigilBridge>();
                    apply_daemon_status(&b, status);
                    if let Some(f) = friends { set_friends(&b, f); }
                    if let Some(s) = servers { set_servers(&b, s); }
                    if let Some(m) = matches { set_matches(&b, m); }
                }
            }).ok();
        });
    });

    // ── switch profile ──
    let weak = app.as_weak();
    app.global::<VigilBridge>().on_switch_profile(move |profile| {
        let _ = ipc::set_profile(profile.as_str());
        if let Some(app) = weak.upgrade() {
            app.global::<VigilBridge>().set_active_profile(profile);
        }
    });

    // ── join queue (async) ──
    let weak = app.as_weak();
    let cl = client.clone();
    app.global::<VigilBridge>().on_join_queue(move |game| {
        let w = weak.clone();
        let cl = cl.clone();
        let g = game.to_string();
        std::thread::spawn(move || {
            let result = cl.lock().unwrap().join_queue(&g);
            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() {
                    let b = app.global::<VigilBridge>();
                    match result {
                        Ok(resp) => {
                            if resp.status == "match_found" {
                                b.set_in_queue(false);
                            } else {
                                b.set_in_queue(true);
                                b.set_queue_game(g.into());
                                b.set_queue_position(resp.position.unwrap_or(1));
                            }
                        }
                        Err(e) => b.set_error_msg(e.into()),
                    }
                }
            }).ok();
        });
    });

    // ── leave queue (async) ──
    let weak = app.as_weak();
    let cl = client.clone();
    app.global::<VigilBridge>().on_leave_queue(move || {
        let w = weak.clone();
        let cl = cl.clone();
        std::thread::spawn(move || {
            let _ = cl.lock().unwrap().leave_queue();
            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() {
                    app.global::<VigilBridge>().set_in_queue(false);
                }
            }).ok();
        });
    });

    // ── add friend (async) ──
    let weak = app.as_weak();
    let cl = client.clone();
    app.global::<VigilBridge>().on_add_friend(move |name| {
        if name.is_empty() { return; }
        let w = weak.clone();
        let cl = cl.clone();
        let n = name.to_string();
        std::thread::spawn(move || {
            let add_result = cl.lock().unwrap().add_friend(&n);
            let friends = cl.lock().unwrap().get_friends().ok();
            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() {
                    let b = app.global::<VigilBridge>();
                    match add_result {
                        Ok(()) => { if let Some(f) = friends { set_friends(&b, f); } }
                        Err(e) => b.set_error_msg(e.into()),
                    }
                }
            }).ok();
        });
    });

    // ── remove friend (async) ──
    let weak = app.as_weak();
    let cl = client.clone();
    app.global::<VigilBridge>().on_remove_friend(move |name| {
        let w = weak.clone();
        let cl = cl.clone();
        let n = name.to_string();
        std::thread::spawn(move || {
            let _ = cl.lock().unwrap().remove_friend(&n);
            let friends = cl.lock().unwrap().get_friends().ok();
            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() {
                    let b = app.global::<VigilBridge>();
                    if let Some(f) = friends { set_friends(&b, f); }
                }
            }).ok();
        });
    });

    // ── create party (async) ──
    let weak = app.as_weak();
    let cl = client.clone();
    app.global::<VigilBridge>().on_create_party(move || {
        let w = weak.clone();
        let cl = cl.clone();
        std::thread::spawn(move || {
            let result = cl.lock().unwrap().create_party();
            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() {
                    let b = app.global::<VigilBridge>();
                    match result {
                        Ok(id) => {
                            b.set_in_party(true);
                            b.set_is_party_leader(true);
                            b.set_party_game(b.get_active_profile());
                            b.set_party_id(id.into());
                        }
                        Err(e) => b.set_error_msg(e.into()),
                    }
                }
            }).ok();
        });
    });

    // ── leave party (async) ──
    let weak = app.as_weak();
    let cl = client.clone();
    app.global::<VigilBridge>().on_leave_party(move || {
        let w = weak.clone();
        let cl = cl.clone();
        std::thread::spawn(move || {
            let _ = cl.lock().unwrap().leave_party();
            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() {
                    let b = app.global::<VigilBridge>();
                    b.set_in_party(false);
                    b.set_party_members(ModelRc::from(std::rc::Rc::new(VecModel::<PartyMember>::default())));
                }
            }).ok();
        });
    });

    // ── invite to party (async) ──
    let weak = app.as_weak();
    let cl = client.clone();
    app.global::<VigilBridge>().on_invite_to_party(move |name| {
        if name.is_empty() { return; }
        let w = weak.clone();
        let cl = cl.clone();
        let n = name.to_string();
        std::thread::spawn(move || {
            let result = cl.lock().unwrap().invite_to_party(&n);
            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() && let Err(e) = result {
                    app.global::<VigilBridge>().set_error_msg(e.into());
                }
            }).ok();
        });
    });

    app.run()
}

// ── Helper functions ──

fn refresh_daemon_status(b: &VigilBridge) {
    apply_daemon_status(b, ipc::get_status());
}

fn apply_daemon_status(b: &VigilBridge, status: Result<ipc::DaemonStatus, String>) {
    match status {
        Ok(s) => {
            b.set_daemon_running(s.running);
            b.set_trust_score(s.trust_score);
            b.set_ebpf_active(s.ebpf);
            b.set_scan_count(s.scan_count as i32);
            b.set_banned(s.banned);
            if !s.profile.is_empty() && s.profile != "null" {
                b.set_active_profile(s.profile.into());
            }
        }
        Err(_) => {
            b.set_daemon_running(false);
            b.set_ebpf_active(false);
        }
    }
}

fn load_all_data(client: &api::Client, b: &VigilBridge) {
    if let Ok(f) = client.get_friends() { set_friends(b, f); }
    if let Ok(s) = client.get_servers() { set_servers(b, s); }
    if let Ok(m) = client.get_matches() { set_matches(b, m); }
}

fn set_friends(b: &VigilBridge, data: Vec<api::Friend>) {
    let friends: Vec<FriendEntry> = data.iter().map(|f| {
        FriendEntry {
            name: f.name.clone().into(),
            status: if f.banned { "BANNED".into() }
                    else if f.is_clean { "IN MENU".into() }
                    else { "FLAGGED".into() },
            status_online: f.is_clean && !f.banned,
            game: "".into(),
            trust: f.trust_score as i32,
        }
    }).collect();
    b.set_friends(ModelRc::from(std::rc::Rc::new(VecModel::from(friends))));
}

fn set_servers(b: &VigilBridge, data: Vec<api::Server>) {
    let servers: Vec<ServerEntry> = data.iter().map(|s| {
        ServerEntry {
            name: s.name.clone().into(),
            game: s.game.clone().into(),
            players: format!("{}/{}", s.current_players, s.max_players).into(),
            address: s.address.clone().into(),
            online: true,
        }
    }).collect();
    b.set_servers(ModelRc::from(std::rc::Rc::new(VecModel::from(servers))));
}

fn set_matches(b: &VigilBridge, data: Vec<api::Match>) {
    let matches: Vec<MatchEntry> = data.iter().map(|m| {
        let game = m.game.as_deref().unwrap_or("CS2");
        let map = m.map.as_deref().unwrap_or("UNKNOWN");
        let result = m.result.as_deref().unwrap_or("VICTORY");
        let duration = m.duration.as_deref().unwrap_or("—");
        let date = if m.created_at.len() >= 10 { &m.created_at[..10] } else { &m.created_at };
        let trust = match result {
            "VICTORY" => 3,
            "DEFEAT" => -1,
            "DRAW" => 0,
            _ => 0,
        };

        MatchEntry {
            id: if m.id.len() > 8 { m.id[..8].to_string().into() } else { m.id.clone().into() },
            game: game.into(),
            date: date.into(),
            format: map.into(),
            duration: duration.into(),
            integrity: result.into(),
            trust_after: trust,
        }
    }).collect();
    b.set_matches(ModelRc::from(std::rc::Rc::new(VecModel::from(matches))));
}
```

`crates/vigil-gui/src/ws_events.rs`:

```rs
// WebSocket event listener — runs in background thread, pushes events to Slint UI

use slint::ComponentHandle;
use vigil_common::json::parse;
use vigil_common::ws::WsClient;

/// Start a background WS listener. Call after login.
pub fn start_ws_listener(
    server_url: &str,
    token: &str,
    app_weak: slint::Weak<super::App>,
) {
    let ws_url = server_url.replace("http://", "ws://") + "/ws";
    let tok = token.to_string();
    let weak = app_weak.clone();

    std::thread::spawn(move || {
        // Connect with retry
        let mut client = loop {
            match WsClient::connect(&ws_url, Some(&tok)) {
                Ok(c) => break c,
                Err(_) => {
                    std::thread::sleep(std::time::Duration::from_secs(3));
                    // check if app still alive
                    let alive = weak.upgrade_in_event_loop(|_| {}).is_ok();
                    if !alive { return; }
                }
            }
        };

        // Read loop
        loop {
            if let Some(msg) = client.try_recv() {
                let w = weak.clone();
                if let Ok(val) = parse(&msg.text) {
                    let event = val.get("event")
                        .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
                        .unwrap_or("")
                        .to_string();

                    match event.as_str() {
                        "trust_update" => {
                            let score = val.get("trust_score")
                                .and_then(|v| v.as_i64())
                                .unwrap_or(100) as i32;
                            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() {
                                    let b = app.global::<super::VigilBridge>();
                                    b.set_trust_score(score);
                                }
                            }).ok();
                        }
                        "banned" => {
                            let reason = val.get("reason")
                                .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
                                .unwrap_or("Account restricted")
                                .to_string();
                            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() {
                                    let b = app.global::<super::VigilBridge>();
                                    b.set_banned(true);
                                    b.set_error_msg(reason.into());
                                }
                            }).ok();
                        }
                        "party_invite" => {
                            let from = val.get("from")
                                .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
                                .unwrap_or("unknown")
                                .to_string();
                            let party_id = val.get("party_id")
                                .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
                                .unwrap_or("")
                                .to_string();
                            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() {
                                    let b = app.global::<super::VigilBridge>();
                                    b.set_error_msg(
                                        format!("Party invite from {}", from).into()
                                    );
                                    b.set_party_id(party_id.into());
                                }
                            }).ok();
                        }
                        "match_found" => {
                            let match_id = val.get("match_id")
                                .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
                                .unwrap_or("")
                                .to_string();
                            slint::invoke_from_event_loop(move || {
                                if let Some(app) = w.upgrade() {
                                    let b = app.global::<super::VigilBridge>();
                                    b.set_in_queue(false);
                                    b.set_error_msg(
                                        format!("Match found: {}", match_id).into()
                                    );
                                }
                            }).ok();
                        }
                        _ => {} // unknown event, ignore
                    }
                }
            } else {
                // No message — sleep briefly to avoid busy-wait
                std::thread::sleep(std::time::Duration::from_millis(50));
            }

            // Check if app is still alive
            let alive = weak.upgrade_in_event_loop(|_| {}).is_ok();
            if !alive { break; }
        }

        client.close();
    });
}
```

```slint
export struct FriendEntry {
    name: string,
    status: string,
    status-online: bool,

    is-leader: bool,
    trust: int,
}

    name: string,
    game: string,
    players: string,
    address: string,
    online: bool,
}

export struct MatchEntry {
    id: string,
    game: string,
    date: string,
    format: string,
    duration: string,
    integrity: string,
    trust-after: int,
}

export global VigilBridge {
    in-out property <bool> logged-in: false;
    in-out property <string> current-page: "login";
    in-out property <string> player-name: "";
    in-out property <int> trust-score: 100;
    in-out property <bool> daemon-running: false;
    in-out property <bool> ebpf-active: false;
    in-out property <string> active-profile: "none";
    in-out property <int> scan-count: 0;
    in-out property <bool> banned: false;
    in-out property <string> error-msg: "";
    in-out property <bool> in-queue: false;
    in-out property <string> queue-game: "cs2";
    in-out property <int> queue-position: 0;

    // settings toggles (persisted to ~/.config/vigil/gui.json)
    in-out property <bool> setting-ebpf-monitoring: true;
    in-out property <bool> setting-process-integrity: true;
    in-out property <bool> setting-network-analysis: true;
    in-out property <bool> setting-memory-scanner: false;
    in-out property <bool> setting-auto-update: true;
    in-out property <bool> setting-auto-detect-game: true;
    in-out property <bool> setting-overlay-hud: false;
    in-out property <bool> setting-tls-enabled: true;
    in-out property <bool> setting-auto-reconnect: true;

    // callback wired to the Save button in settings
    callback save-settings();

    // party state
    in-out property <bool> in-party: false;
    in-out property <string> party-id: "";
    in-out property <string> party-game: "";
    in-out property <bool> is-party-leader: false;

    // models
    in-out property <[FriendEntry]> friends: [];
    in-out property <[PartyMember]> party-members: [];
    in-out property <[ServerEntry]> servers: [];
    in-out property <[MatchEntry]> matches: [];

    callback do-login(string, string);
    callback do-register(string, string);
    callback do-logout();
    callback refresh-status();
    callback switch-profile(string);
    callback join-queue(string);
    callback leave-queue();
    callback add-friend(string);
    callback remove-friend(string);
    callback create-party();
    callback leave-party();
    callback invite-to-party(string);
}
```

```slint
                spacing: 24px;

                // ═══ Left: Friend List (60%) ═══
                VerticalLayout {
                    horizontal-stretch: 60;
                    spacing: 16px;

                    // Header + filters
                    HorizontalLayout {
                        spacing: 12px;
                        Text { text: "FRIENDS"; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 800; font-family: "Space Grotesk"; color: C.text; vertical-alignment: center; }
                        Rectangle { horizontal-stretch: 1; }
                        FriendFilter { label: "ALL"; active: true; }
                        FriendFilter { label: "ONLINE"; }
                        FriendFilter { label: "OFFLINE"; }
                        FriendFilter { label: "IN-GAME"; }
                    }

                    // Dynamic friends from bridge
                    for f[i] in VigilBridge.friends : FriendRow {
                        name: f.name;
                        status: f.status-online ? "IN MENU" : "OFFLINE";
                        is-online: f.status-online;
                        trust: f.trust;
                        game: f.game;
                        invite-clicked => { VigilBridge.invite-to-party(f.name); }
                        remove-clicked => { VigilBridge.remove-friend(f.name); }
                    }

                    // Static fallback
                    if VigilBridge.friends.length == 0 : VerticalLayout {
```

```slint
import { C } from "theme.slint";

// Stat card for overview row
component HistoryStat inherits Rectangle {
    in property <string> label;
    in property <string> value;
    in property <color> value-color: C.text;
    in property <string> sub: "";

    horizontal-stretch: 1;
    height: 90px;
    background: C.bg2;
    border-radius: C.radius-s;

    VerticalLayout {
        padding: 20px;
        spacing: 4px;
        Text { text: label; font-size: 9px; font-weight: 700; font-family: "Space Grotesk"; color: C.text3; letter-spacing: 0.12rem; }
        HorizontalLayout {
            spacing: 8px;
            Text { text: value; font-size: 32px; font-weight: 900; font-family: "Space Grotesk"; color: value-color; vertical-alignment: center; }
            if sub != "" : Text { text: sub; font-size: 10px; font-weight: 600; font-family: "Space Grotesk"; color: C.text4; vertical-alignment: center; }
        }
    }
}

// Match row
component MatchRow inherits Rectangle {
    in property <string> result;
    in property <string> game;
    in property <string> map;
    in property <string> format;
    in property <string> duration;
    in property <string> kd: "";
    in property <string> trust-delta: "";
    in property <string> date;

    property <color> result-color: result == "VICTORY" ? C.accent : result == "DEFEAT" ? C.red : C.orange;
    property <color> delta-color: {
        if trust-delta == "" || trust-delta == "0" { return C.text4; }
        if trust-delta.character-count > 0 { return C.accent; }
        return C.text4;
    };

    height: 44px;
    background: touch.has-hover ? C.surface.with-alpha(0.3) : transparent;
    animate background { duration: 120ms; }

    touch := TouchArea {}

    HorizontalLayout {
        padding-left: 24px;
        padding-right: 24px;

        // Green/red left accent
        Rectangle {
            width: 3px;
            background: result-color;
        }
        Rectangle { width: 16px; }

        Text { horizontal-stretch: 1; text: result; font-size: 11px; font-weight: 800; font-family: "Space Grotesk"; color: result-color; vertical-alignment: center; }
        Text { horizontal-stretch: 1; text: game; font-size: 11px; font-weight: 600; font-family: "Inter"; color: C.text2; vertical-alignment: center; }
        Text { horizontal-stretch: 1; text: map; font-size: 11px; font-weight: 600; font-family: "Space Grotesk"; color: C.tertiary; vertical-alignment: center; }
        Text { horizontal-stretch: 1; text: format; font-size: 11px; font-weight: 500; font-family: "Inter"; color: C.text3; vertical-alignment: center; }
        Text { horizontal-stretch: 1; text: duration; font-size: 11px; font-weight: 600; font-family: "Space Grotesk"; color: C.text; vertical-alignment: center; horizontal-alignment: center; }
        Text { horizontal-stretch: 1; text: kd; font-size: 11px; font-weight: 700; font-family: "Space Grotesk"; color: C.text; vertical-alignment: center; horizontal-alignment: center; }
        Text { horizontal-stretch: 1; text: trust-delta; font-size: 11px; font-weight: 700; font-family: "Space Grotesk"; color: trust-delta == "0" ? C.text4 : trust-delta.character-count > 0 ? C.accent : C.text4; vertical-alignment: center; horizontal-alignment: center; }
        Text { horizontal-stretch: 1; text: date; font-size: 10px; font-weight: 600; font-family: "Space Grotesk"; color: C.text4; vertical-alignment: center; horizontal-alignment: right; }
    }
}
```

```slint
import { C } from "theme.slint";

// Material Symbols Outlined — loaded from local SVGs, recolorable via colorize

export component ShieldIcon inherits Image {
    in property <color> icon-color: C.accent;
    source: @image-url("icons/shield.svg");
    colorize: icon-color;
    image-fit: contain;
}

export component EmailIcon inherits Image {
    in property <color> icon-color: C.text3;
    source: @image-url("icons/email.svg");
    colorize: icon-color;
    image-fit: contain;
}

export component LockIcon inherits Image {
    in property <color> icon-color: C.text3;
    source: @image-url("icons/lock.svg");
    colorize: icon-color;
    image-fit: contain;
}

export component ArrowIcon inherits Image {
    in property <color> icon-color: C.accent-dim;
    source: @image-url("icons/arrow.svg");
    colorize: icon-color;
    image-fit: contain;
}
```

`crates/vigil-gui/ui/main.slint`:

```slint
import { HorizontalBox } from "std-widgets.slint";
import { C } from "theme.slint";
export { VigilBridge } from "bridge.slint";
import { VigilBridge } from "bridge.slint";
import { Sidebar } from "sidebar.slint";
import { LoginPage } from "login.slint";
import { HomePage } from "home.slint";
import { PlayPage } from "play.slint";
import { FriendsPage } from "friends.slint";
import { PartyPage } from "party.slint";
import { ServersPage } from "servers.slint";
import { HistoryPage } from "history.slint";
import { SettingsPage } from "settings.slint";

export component App inherits Window {
    title: "Vigil";
    width: 1280px;
    height: 800px;
    background: C.bg;

    if !VigilBridge.logged-in : LoginPage {}

    if VigilBridge.logged-in : HorizontalBox {
        padding: 0;
        spacing: 0;

        Sidebar {}
        Rectangle { width: 1px; background: C.border.with-alpha(0.10); }

        Rectangle {
            horizontal-stretch: 1;
            background: C.bg;

            if VigilBridge.current-page == "home" : HomePage {}
            if VigilBridge.current-page == "friends" : FriendsPage {}
            if VigilBridge.current-page == "party" : PartyPage {}
            if VigilBridge.current-page == "play" : PlayPage {}
            if VigilBridge.current-page == "servers" : ServersPage {}
            if VigilBridge.current-page == "history" : HistoryPage {}
            if VigilBridge.current-page == "settings" : SettingsPage {}
        }
    }
}
```

```slint
import { C } from "theme.slint";
import { VigilBridge } from "bridge.slint";
import { Card, StatusPill, ActionButton, EmptyState, StyledInput } from "components.slint";
import { VerticalBox, HorizontalBox, ScrollView } from "std-widgets.slint";

export component PartyPage inherits Rectangle {
    background: C.bg;

    VerticalBox {
        padding: 40px;
        spacing: 32px;
        alignment: start;

        // Header
        VerticalBox {
            spacing: 8px;
            Text { text: "Tactical Party"; font-size: 32px; font-weight: 800; color: C.text; }
            Text { text: "Coordinate with your team and maintain group integrity."; font-size: 14px; color: C.text3; }
        }

        if !VigilBridge.in-party : EmptyState {
            message: "You are not currently in a party session.";
        }

        if VigilBridge.in-party : HorizontalBox {
            padding: 0;
            spacing: 24px;

            Card {
                horizontal-stretch: 1;
                VerticalBox {
                    padding: 24px;
                    spacing: 20px;
                    
                    Text { text: "PARTY MEMBERS"; font-size: 12px; font-weight: 700; color: C.text4; letter-spacing: 0.1rem; }

                    VerticalBox {
                        padding: 0;
                        spacing: 8px;
                        for member in VigilBridge.party-members : Rectangle {
                            height: 64px;
                            background: C.bg2;
                            border-radius: C.radius-s;
                            border-width: 1px;
                            border-color: C.border;
                            
                            HorizontalLayout {
                                padding: 16px;
                                spacing: 16px;
                                Rectangle { width: 32px; height: 32px; border-radius: 16px; background: C.surface; Text { text: "󰇄"; color: C.accent; } }
                                VerticalLayout {
                                    alignment: center;
                                    Text { text: member.name; font-size: 14px; font-weight: 700; color: C.text; }
                                    Text { text: member.is-leader ? "Party Leader" : "Member"; font-size: 11px; color: C.text3; }
                                }
                                if member.is-leader : StatusPill { label: "LEADER"; pill-color: C.accent; }
                                VerticalLayout {
                                    alignment: center;
                                    Text { text: "\{member.trust}%"; font-size: 14px; font-weight: 800; color: member.trust > 80 ? C.green : C.orange; }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            VerticalBox {
                width: 320px;
                spacing: 24px;

                Card {
                    VerticalBox {
                        padding: 24px;
                        spacing: 20px;
                        Text { text: "INVITE PLAYER"; font-size: 12px; font-weight: 700; color: C.text4; letter-spacing: 0.1rem; }
                        invite-input := StyledInput { placeholder: "Enter alias..."; }
                        ActionButton { 
                            label: "SEND INVITE"; 
                            primary: true; 
                            clicked => { VigilBridge.invite-to-party(invite-input.text); invite-input.text = ""; }
                        }
                    }
                }

                ActionButton {
                    label: "DISBAND PARTY";
                    danger: true;
                    outline: true;
                    clicked => { VigilBridge.leave-party(); }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}
```

```slint
// Game card — selectable, with title, subtitle, chip, player count
component GameCard inherits Rectangle {
    in property <string> title;
    in property <string> subtitle;
    in property <string> chip: "";
    in property <color> chip-color: C.accent;
    in property <string> players: "";
    in property <string> ping: "";
    in property <bool> selected: false;
    callback clicked();

    height: 110px;
    background: selected ? C.surface.with-alpha(0.8) : C.bg2;
    border-radius: C.radius-s;
    animate background { duration: 150ms; }

    touch := TouchArea { clicked => { root.clicked(); } }

    // Hover overlay
    Rectangle {
        border-radius: C.radius-s;

                                                VigilBridge.invite-to-party(invite-input.text);
                                                invite-input.text = "";
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                    Text {
                                        text: "+";
                                        font-size: 18px;
                                        font-weight: 700;
                                        color: add-touch.has-hover ? C.accent : C.text3;
                                        horizontal-alignment: center;
                                        vertical-alignment: center;
                                        animate color { duration: 150ms; }
                                    }
                                }
                            }

                            if invite-input.text == "" && !invite-input.has-focus : Text {
                                x: 32px;
                                y: (parent.height - self.preferred-height) / 2;
                                text: "INVITE PLAYER...";
                                font-size: 10px;
                                font-weight: 600;
                                font-family: "Space Grotesk";
                                color: C.text4;
                                letter-spacing: 0.08rem;
                            }
                        }

                        Rectangle { vertical-stretch: 1; }

                        // ── FIND MATCH button ──
                        if !VigilBridge.in-queue : Rectangle {
                            height: 56px;
                            border-radius: C.radius-s;
                            background: @linear-gradient(135deg, #9cff93, #2ff801);

                            find-touch := TouchArea {
                                clicked => {
                                    if !VigilBridge.in-party { VigilBridge.create-party(); }
                                    VigilBridge.join-queue(VigilBridge.queue-game);
                                }
                            }
                            Rectangle {
                                border-radius: C.radius-s;
                                background: white.with-alpha(find-touch.has-hover ? 0.08 : 0.0);
                                animate background { duration: 150ms; }
                            }

                            Text {
                                text: "FIND MATCH";
                                font-size: 15px;
                                font-weight: 800;
                                font-family: "Space Grotesk";
                                color: #002203;
                                horizontal-alignment: center;
                                vertical-alignment: center;
                                letter-spacing: 0.16rem;
                            }
                            ArrowIcon {
                                x: parent.width - 40px;
                                y: (parent.height - 18px) / 2;
                                width: 18px; height: 18px;
                                icon-color: #002203;
                            }
                        }

                        // In queue state
                        if VigilBridge.in-queue : Rectangle {
                            height: 56px;
                            border-radius: C.radius-s;
                            background: C.red.with-alpha(0.1);

                            cancel-touch := TouchArea {
                                clicked => { VigilBridge.leave-queue(); }
                            }
                            Rectangle {
                                border-radius: C.radius-s;
                                background: C.red.with-alpha(cancel-touch.has-hover ? 0.15 : 0.0);
                                animate background { duration: 150ms; }
                            }
                            Text {
                                text: "CANCEL QUEUE — POSITION \{VigilBridge.queue-position}";
                                font-size: 12px;
                                font-weight: 800;
                                font-family: "Space Grotesk";
                                color: C.red;
                                horizontal-alignment: center;
                                vertical-alignment: center;
                                letter-spacing: 0.1rem;
                            }
                        }

                        Rectangle { height: 12px; }

                        // Wait time + Region
                        HorizontalLayout {
                            VerticalLayout {
                                horizontal-stretch: 1;
                                spacing: 2px;
                                Text {
                                    text: "EST_WAIT_TIME";
                                    font-size: 9px;
                                    font-weight: 600;
                                    font-family: "Space Grotesk";
                                    color: C.text4;
                                    letter-spacing: 0.1rem;
                                }
                                Text {
                                    text: "~02:30";
                                    font-size: 16px;
                                    font-weight: 700;
                                    font-family: "Space Grotesk";
                                    color: C.text;
                                }
                            }
                            VerticalLayout {
                                spacing: 2px;
                                Text {
                                    text: "REGION";
                                    font-size: 9px;
                                    font-weight: 600;
                                    font-family: "Space Grotesk";
                                    color: C.text4;
                                    horizontal-alignment: right;
                                    letter-spacing: 0.1rem;
                                }
                                Text {
                                    text: "EU-WEST";
                                    font-size: 16px;
                                    font-weight: 700;
                                    font-family: "Space Grotesk";
                                    color: C.tertiary;
                                    horizontal-alignment: right;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }

                Rectangle { height: 28px; }

                // ── Bottom: Recent Matches ──
                Rectangle {
                    height: 48px;
                    background: C.bg2;
                    border-radius: C.radius-s;

                    HorizontalLayout {
                        padding-left: 16px;
                        padding-right: 16px;
                        spacing: 24px;

                        Text {
                            text: "RECENT_MATCHES";
                            font-size: 9px;
                            font-weight: 700;
                            font-family: "Space Grotesk";
                            color: C.text3;
                            vertical-alignment: center;
                            letter-spacing: 0.1rem;
                        }

                        RecentMatch {
                            result: "VICTORY";
                            detail: "DE_MIRAGE // 12M AGO";
                            result-color: C.accent;
                        }
                        RecentMatch {
                            result: "DEFEAT";
                            detail: "DE_DUST2 // 1H AGO";
                            result-color: C.red;
                        }
                        RecentMatch {
                            result: "VICTORY";
                            detail: "DE_INFERNO // 3H AGO";
                            result-color: C.accent;
                        }

                        Rectangle { horizontal-stretch: 1; }

                        HorizontalLayout {
                            spacing: 8px;
                            Rectangle {
                                width: 6px;
                                Rectangle {
                                    y: 4px;
                                    width: 6px; height: 6px;
                                    border-radius: 3px;
                                    background: C.accent2;
                                }
                            }
                            Text {
                                text: "VIGIL_ACTIVE";
```

```slint
// Filter chip
```

`crates/vigil-server/src/auth.rs`:

```rs
use std::time::{SystemTime, UNIX_EPOCH};

use crate::crypto::{base64url_decode, base64url_encode, hash_password, hmac_sha256, verify_password};
use crate::json::{json_num, json_obj, json_str, parse, stringify};

// constant-time compare to prevent timing attacks
fn constant_time_eq(a: &[u8], b: &[u8]) -> bool {
    if a.len() != b.len() { return false; }
    let mut diff = 0u8;
    for i in 0..a.len() {
        diff |= a[i] ^ b[i];
    }
    diff == 0
}

// jwt secret from env, panics in release if not set
fn jwt_secret() -> String {
    match std::env::var("VIGIL_JWT_SECRET") {
        Ok(s) if !s.is_empty() => s,
        _ => {
            if cfg!(test) {
                "test-secret".to_string()
            } else {
                panic!("VIGIL_JWT_SECRET env var is required")
            }
        }
    }
}

// admin key from env, panics in release if not set
fn admin_key() -> String {
    match std::env::var("VIGIL_ADMIN_KEY") {
        Ok(s) if !s.is_empty() => s,
        _ => {
            if cfg!(test) {
                "test-admin-key".to_string()
            } else {
                panic!("VIGIL_ADMIN_KEY env var is required")
            }
        }
    }
}

// re-exports for convenience
pub fn hash_pw(password: &str) -> String {
    hash_password(password)
}

pub fn verify_pw(password: &str, stored: &str) -> bool {
    verify_password(password, stored)
}

// current unix timestamp in seconds
fn now_secs() -> u64 {
    SystemTime::now()
        .duration_since(UNIX_EPOCH)
        .unwrap_or_default()
        .as_secs()
}

// creates a JWT token (HS256) for a player, expires in 24 hours
pub fn create_token(player_id: &str) -> Result<String, String> {
    let exp = now_secs() + 86400;

    // header: {"alg":"HS256","typ":"JWT"}
    let header = stringify(&json_obj(vec![
        ("alg", json_str("HS256")),
        ("typ", json_str("JWT")),
    ]));

    // payload: {"sub":"player_id","exp":timestamp}
    let payload = stringify(&json_obj(vec![
        ("sub", json_str(player_id)),
        ("exp", json_num(exp as f64)),
    ]));

    let enc_header = base64url_encode(header.as_bytes());
    let enc_payload = base64url_encode(payload.as_bytes());

    // signing input: base64url(header).base64url(payload)
    let signing_input = format!("{}.{}", enc_header, enc_payload);

    let secret = jwt_secret();
    let sig = hmac_sha256(secret.as_bytes(), signing_input.as_bytes());
    let enc_sig = base64url_encode(&sig);

    Ok(format!("{}.{}", signing_input, enc_sig))
}

// validates a JWT token, returns the player_id (sub claim) if valid
pub fn validate_token(token: &str) -> Result<String, String> {
    let parts: Vec<&str> = token.splitn(3, '.').collect();
    if parts.len() != 3 {
        return Err("invalid token format".to_string());
    }

    let signing_input = format!("{}.{}", parts[0], parts[1]);
    let secret = jwt_secret();
    let expected_sig = hmac_sha256(secret.as_bytes(), signing_input.as_bytes());
    let expected_enc = base64url_encode(&expected_sig);

    // constant-time compare
    let provided = parts[2].as_bytes();
    let expected = expected_enc.as_bytes();
    if provided.len() != expected.len() {
        return Err("invalid signature".to_string());
    }
    let mut diff = 0u8;
    for i in 0..provided.len() {
        diff |= provided[i] ^ expected[i];
    }
    if diff != 0 {
        return Err("invalid signature".to_string());
    }

    // decode payload
    let payload_bytes = base64url_decode(parts[1])?;
    let payload_str = String::from_utf8(payload_bytes)
        .map_err(|_| "payload is not valid utf-8".to_string())?;
    let payload = parse(&payload_str)?;

    // check expiry
    let exp = payload
        .get("exp")
        .and_then(|v| v.as_i64())
        .ok_or_else(|| "missing exp claim".to_string())?;

    if (exp as u64) < now_secs() {
        return Err("token expired".to_string());
    }

    // return player id
    let sub = payload
        .get("sub")
        .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
        .ok_or_else(|| "missing sub claim".to_string())?
        .to_string();

    Ok(sub)
}

// checks if a request has a valid JWT Bearer token
pub fn check_auth(req: &crate::http::Request) -> Result<String, u16> {
    let header = req.get_header("Authorization").ok_or(401u16)?;

    if !header.starts_with("Bearer ") {
        return Err(401);
    }

    let token = &header[7..];
    validate_token(token).map_err(|_| 401u16)
}

// checks if request has valid admin API key
pub fn check_admin(req: &crate::http::Request) -> Result<(), u16> {
    let key = req.get_header("X-Admin-Key").ok_or(403u16)?;

    // constant-time comparison to prevent timing attacks
    let expected = admin_key();
    if constant_time_eq(key.as_bytes(), expected.as_bytes()) {
        Ok(())
    } else {
        Err(403)
    }
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn create_token_has_three_dot_separated_parts() {
        let token = create_token("player-123").unwrap();
        let parts: Vec<&str> = token.split('.').collect();
        assert_eq!(parts.len(), 3, "JWT must have exactly 3 parts: {}", token);
        // each part should be non-empty base64url
        for (i, part) in parts.iter().enumerate() {
            assert!(!part.is_empty(), "JWT part {} is empty", i);
        }
    }

    #[test]
    fn validate_token_accepts_own_tokens() {
        let token = create_token("player-abc").unwrap();
        let sub = validate_token(&token).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(sub, "player-abc");
    }

    #[test]
    fn validate_token_preserves_player_id() {
        // test various player id shapes
        for id in &["simple", "uuid-like-1234-5678", "with spaces", ""] {
            let token = create_token(id).unwrap();
            let sub = validate_token(&token).unwrap();
            assert_eq!(sub, *id);
        }
    }

    #[test]
    fn validate_token_rejects_tampered_signature() {
        let token = create_token("player-x").unwrap();
        let parts: Vec<&str> = token.splitn(3, '.').collect();
        // flip a character in the signature
        let mut sig = parts[2].to_string();
        let bytes = unsafe { sig.as_bytes_mut() };
        bytes[0] ^= 0x01; // flip one bit
        let tampered = format!("{}.{}.{}", parts[0], parts[1], sig);
        assert!(validate_token(&tampered).is_err());
    }

    #[test]
    fn validate_token_rejects_tampered_payload() {
        let token = create_token("player-x").unwrap();
        let parts: Vec<&str> = token.splitn(3, '.').collect();
        // use a different payload but keep original signature
        let other_token = create_token("ATTACKER").unwrap();
        let other_parts: Vec<&str> = other_token.splitn(3, '.').collect();
        let franken = format!("{}.{}.{}", parts[0], other_parts[1], parts[2]);
        assert!(validate_token(&franken).is_err());
    }

    #[test]
    fn validate_token_rejects_garbage() {
        assert!(validate_token("").is_err());
        assert!(validate_token("not-a-token").is_err());
        assert!(validate_token("a.b").is_err());
        assert!(validate_token("a.b.c").is_err());
        assert!(validate_token("...").is_err());
        assert!(validate_token("hello world garbage").is_err());
    }

    #[test]
    fn validate_token_rejects_wrong_part_count() {
        assert!(validate_token("onlyonepart").is_err());
        assert!(validate_token("two.parts").is_err());
    }

    #[test]
    fn hash_pw_verify_pw_roundtrip() {
        let hash = hash_pw("my-secret-123");
        assert!(verify_pw("my-secret-123", &hash));
    }

    #[test]
    fn verify_pw_rejects_wrong_password() {
        let hash = hash_pw("correct-password");
        assert!(!verify_pw("wrong-password", &hash));
        assert!(!verify_pw("", &hash));
        assert!(!verify_pw("correct-passwor", &hash)); // off by one
        assert!(!verify_pw("correct-password ", &hash)); // trailing space
    }

    #[test]
    fn hash_pw_produces_different_hashes_for_same_password() {
        // because of random salt, hashing the same password twice should differ
        let h1 = hash_pw("same-password");
        let h2 = hash_pw("same-password");
        assert_ne!(h1, h2, "hashes should differ due to random salt");
        // but both should verify
        assert!(verify_pw("same-password", &h1));
        assert!(verify_pw("same-password", &h2));
    }

    #[test]
    fn verify_pw_rejects_bad_format() {
        assert!(!verify_pw("anything", "not-valid"));
        assert!(!verify_pw("anything", ""));
        assert!(!verify_pw("anything", ":"));
        assert!(!verify_pw("anything", "zzzz:1234"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn check_auth_accepts_valid_bearer_token() {
        let token = create_token("player-42").unwrap();
        let req = crate::http::Request {
            method: "GET".to_string(),
            path: "/api/test".to_string(),
            headers: vec![("Authorization".to_string(), format!("Bearer {}", token))],
            body: String::new(),
        };
        let result = check_auth(&req);
        assert_eq!(result.unwrap(), "player-42");
    }

    #[test]
    fn check_auth_rejects_missing_header() {
        let req = crate::http::Request {
            method: "GET".to_string(),
            path: "/api/test".to_string(),
            headers: vec![],
            body: String::new(),
        };
        assert_eq!(check_auth(&req), Err(401));
    }

    #[test]
    fn check_auth_rejects_non_bearer() {
        let req = crate::http::Request {
            method: "GET".to_string(),
            path: "/api/test".to_string(),
            headers: vec![("Authorization".to_string(), "Basic abc123".to_string())],
            body: String::new(),
        };
        assert_eq!(check_auth(&req), Err(401));
    }

    #[test]
    fn check_admin_accepts_correct_key() {
        let key = admin_key();
        let req = crate::http::Request {
            method: "POST".to_string(),
            path: "/api/admin/config".to_string(),
            headers: vec![("X-Admin-Key".to_string(), key)],
            body: String::new(),
        };
        assert!(check_admin(&req).is_ok());
    }

    #[test]
    fn check_admin_rejects_wrong_key() {
        let req = crate::http::Request {
            method: "POST".to_string(),
            path: "/api/admin/config".to_string(),
            headers: vec![("X-Admin-Key".to_string(), "wrong-key".to_string())],
            body: String::new(),
        };
        assert_eq!(check_admin(&req), Err(403));
    }

    #[test]
    fn check_admin_rejects_missing_header() {
        let req = crate::http::Request {
            method: "POST".to_string(),
            path: "/api/admin/config".to_string(),
            headers: vec![],
            body: String::new(),
        };
        assert_eq!(check_admin(&req), Err(403));
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil-server/src/crypto.rs`:

```rs
pub use vigil_common::crypto::{sha256, sha256_hex, to_hex};

use std::fs::File;
use std::io::Read;

// sha-1 (only for websocket handshake, not for security)
#[allow(clippy::needless_range_loop)]
pub fn sha1_raw(data: &[u8]) -> [u8; 20] {
    let mut h0: u32 = 0x67452301;
    let mut h1: u32 = 0xEFCDAB89;
    let mut h2: u32 = 0x98BADCFE;
    let mut h3: u32 = 0x10325476;
    let mut h4: u32 = 0xC3D2E1F0;

    let bit_len = (data.len() as u64) * 8;
    let mut msg = data.to_vec();
    msg.push(0x80);
    while msg.len() % 64 != 56 { msg.push(0); }
    msg.extend_from_slice(&bit_len.to_be_bytes());

    for chunk in msg.chunks(64) {
        let mut w = [0u32; 80];
        for i in 0..16 {
            w[i] = u32::from_be_bytes([chunk[i*4], chunk[i*4+1], chunk[i*4+2], chunk[i*4+3]]);
        }
        for i in 16..80 {
            w[i] = (w[i-3] ^ w[i-8] ^ w[i-14] ^ w[i-16]).rotate_left(1);
        }
        let (mut a, mut b, mut c, mut d, mut e) = (h0, h1, h2, h3, h4);
        for i in 0..80 {
            let (f, k) = match i {
                0..=19 =>  ((b & c) | ((!b) & d), 0x5A827999u32),
                20..=39 => (b ^ c ^ d, 0x6ED9EBA1u32),
                40..=59 => ((b & c) | (b & d) | (c & d), 0x8F1BBCDCu32),
                _ =>       (b ^ c ^ d, 0xCA62C1D6u32),
            };
            let temp = a.rotate_left(5).wrapping_add(f).wrapping_add(e).wrapping_add(k).wrapping_add(w[i]);
            e = d; d = c; c = b.rotate_left(30); b = a; a = temp;
        }
        h0 = h0.wrapping_add(a); h1 = h1.wrapping_add(b); h2 = h2.wrapping_add(c);
        h3 = h3.wrapping_add(d); h4 = h4.wrapping_add(e);
    }

    let mut out = [0u8; 20];
    out[0..4].copy_from_slice(&h0.to_be_bytes());
    out[4..8].copy_from_slice(&h1.to_be_bytes());
    out[8..12].copy_from_slice(&h2.to_be_bytes());
    out[12..16].copy_from_slice(&h3.to_be_bytes());
    out[16..20].copy_from_slice(&h4.to_be_bytes());
    out
}

// hmac using sha-256 as the underlying hash
pub fn hmac_sha256(key: &[u8], message: &[u8]) -> [u8; 32] {
    let block_size = 64; // sha-256 block size

    // if key is longer than block size, hash it first
    let key = if key.len() > block_size {
        sha256(key).to_vec()
    } else {
        key.to_vec()
    };

    // pad key with zeros to block size
    let mut k_padded = vec![0u8; block_size];
    k_padded[..key.len()].copy_from_slice(&key);

    // inner and outer padded keys
    let mut i_pad = vec![0u8; block_size];
    let mut o_pad = vec![0u8; block_size];
    for i in 0..block_size {
        i_pad[i] = k_padded[i] ^ 0x36;
        o_pad[i] = k_padded[i] ^ 0x5c;
    }

    // inner hash: H(i_pad || message)
    let mut inner = i_pad;
    inner.extend_from_slice(message);
    let inner_hash = sha256(&inner);

    // outer hash: H(o_pad || inner_hash)
    let mut outer = o_pad;
    outer.extend_from_slice(&inner_hash);
    sha256(&outer)
}

// fills buf with random bytes from /dev/urandom
pub fn random_bytes(buf: &mut [u8]) {
    let mut f = File::open("/dev/urandom").expect("failed to open /dev/urandom");
    f.read_exact(buf).expect("failed to read /dev/urandom");
}

// returns a fixed-size array of random bytes
pub fn random_bytes_array<const N: usize>() -> [u8; N] {
    let mut buf = [0u8; N];
    random_bytes(&mut buf);
    buf
}

// generates a random uuid v4 (rfc 4122)
pub fn uuid_v4() -> String {
    let mut bytes = random_bytes_array::<16>();

    // set version to 4 (bits 4-7 of byte 6)
    bytes[6] = (bytes[6] & 0x0f) | 0x40;

    // set variant to 10xx (bits 6-7 of byte 8)
    bytes[8] = (bytes[8] & 0x3f) | 0x80;

    format!(
        "{:02x}{:02x}{:02x}{:02x}-{:02x}{:02x}-{:02x}{:02x}-{:02x}{:02x}-{:02x}{:02x}{:02x}{:02x}{:02x}{:02x}",
        bytes[0], bytes[1], bytes[2], bytes[3],
        bytes[4], bytes[5],
        bytes[6], bytes[7],
        bytes[8], bytes[9],
        bytes[10], bytes[11], bytes[12], bytes[13], bytes[14], bytes[15],
    )
}

const B64_CHARS: &[u8] = b"ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789-_";

// encodes bytes to base64url (no padding)
pub fn base64url_encode(data: &[u8]) -> String {
    let mut res = String::with_capacity((data.len() * 4).div_ceil(3));
    let mut i = 0;

    while i + 2 < data.len() {
        let val = ((data[i] as u32) << 16) | ((data[i + 1] as u32) << 8) | (data[i + 2] as u32);
        res.push(B64_CHARS[((val >> 18) & 0x3f) as usize] as char);
        res.push(B64_CHARS[((val >> 12) & 0x3f) as usize] as char);
        res.push(B64_CHARS[((val >> 6) & 0x3f) as usize] as char);
        res.push(B64_CHARS[(val & 0x3f) as usize] as char);
        i += 3;
    }

    let rem = data.len() - i;
    if rem == 2 {
        let val = ((data[i] as u32) << 16) | ((data[i + 1] as u32) << 8);
        res.push(B64_CHARS[((val >> 18) & 0x3f) as usize] as char);
        res.push(B64_CHARS[((val >> 12) & 0x3f) as usize] as char);
        res.push(B64_CHARS[((val >> 6) & 0x3f) as usize] as char);
    } else if rem == 1 {
        let val = (data[i] as u32) << 16;
        res.push(B64_CHARS[((val >> 18) & 0x3f) as usize] as char);
        res.push(B64_CHARS[((val >> 12) & 0x3f) as usize] as char);
    }

    res
}

// decodes base64url string back to bytes
pub fn base64url_decode(s: &str) -> Result<Vec<u8>, String> {
    let mut buf = Vec::with_capacity(s.len() * 3 / 4);
    let mut acc: u32 = 0;
    let mut bits: u32 = 0;

    for ch in s.bytes() {
        let val = match ch {
            b'A'..=b'Z' => ch - b'A',
            b'a'..=b'z' => ch - b'a' + 26,
            b'0'..=b'9' => ch - b'0' + 52,
            b'-' => 62,
            b'_' => 63,
            b'=' => continue, // skip padding if present
            _ => return Err(format!("invalid base64url character: {}", ch as char)),
        };

        acc = (acc << 6) | val as u32;
        bits += 6;

        if bits >= 8 {
            bits -= 8;
            buf.push((acc >> bits) as u8);
            acc &= (1 << bits) - 1;
        }
    }

    Ok(buf)
}

// derives a key from password + salt using iterated hmac-sha256
fn pbkdf2_sha256(password: &[u8], salt: &[u8], iterations: u32) -> [u8; 32] {
    // U1 = HMAC(password, salt || 0x00000001)
    let mut block = salt.to_vec();
    block.extend_from_slice(&1u32.to_be_bytes());

    let mut u = hmac_sha256(password, &block);
    let mut res = u;

    // U2..Un - xor each iteration into res
    for _ in 1..iterations {
        u = hmac_sha256(password, &u);
        for j in 0..32 {
            res[j] ^= u[j];
        }
    }

    res
}

// 600k iterations per OWASP 2023; fast-hash feature uses 1k for tests
#[cfg(not(feature = "fast-hash"))]
const PBKDF2_ITERATIONS: u32 = 600_000;
#[cfg(feature = "fast-hash")]
const PBKDF2_ITERATIONS: u32 = 1_000;

// hashes a password with random 16-byte salt
// returns "salt_hex:hash_hex"
pub fn hash_password(password: &str) -> String {
    let salt = random_bytes_array::<16>();
    let hash = pbkdf2_sha256(password.as_bytes(), &salt, PBKDF2_ITERATIONS);
    format!("{}:{}", to_hex(&salt), to_hex(&hash))
}

// verifies a password against stored "salt_hex:hash_hex"
pub fn verify_password(password: &str, stored: &str) -> bool {
    let parts: Vec<&str> = stored.splitn(2, ':').collect();
    if parts.len() != 2 {
        return false;
    }

    let salt = match from_hex(parts[0]) {
        Ok(s) => s,
        Err(_) => return false,
    };

    let expected = match from_hex(parts[1]) {
        Ok(h) => h,
        Err(_) => return false,
    };

    let hash = pbkdf2_sha256(password.as_bytes(), &salt, PBKDF2_ITERATIONS);

    // constant-time comparison to prevent timing attacks
    if hash.len() != expected.len() {
        return false;
    }
    let mut diff = 0u8;
    for i in 0..hash.len() {
        diff |= hash[i] ^ expected[i];
    }
    diff == 0
}

// decodes hex string to bytes
pub fn from_hex(s: &str) -> Result<Vec<u8>, String> {
    if !s.len().is_multiple_of(2) {
        return Err("hex string must have even length".to_string());
    }

    let mut res = Vec::with_capacity(s.len() / 2);
    let bytes = s.as_bytes();

    for i in (0..bytes.len()).step_by(2) {
        let hi = hex_val(bytes[i])?;
        let lo = hex_val(bytes[i + 1])?;
        res.push((hi << 4) | lo);
    }

    Ok(res)
}

fn hex_val(b: u8) -> Result<u8, String> {
    match b {
        b'0'..=b'9' => Ok(b - b'0'),
        b'a'..=b'f' => Ok(b - b'a' + 10),
        b'A'..=b'F' => Ok(b - b'A' + 10),
        _ => Err(format!("invalid hex character: {}", b as char)),
    }
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn test_sha256_empty() {
        // well-known hash of empty string
        let hash = sha256_hex(b"");
        assert_eq!(hash, "e3b0c44298fc1c149afbf4c8996fb92427ae41e4649b934ca495991b7852b855");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_sha256_hello() {
        let hash = sha256_hex(b"hello");
        assert_eq!(hash, "2cf24dba5fb0a30e26e83b2ac5b9e29e1b161e5c1fa7425e73043362938b9824");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_sha256_longer() {
        // test with data that spans multiple blocks
        let data = b"The quick brown fox jumps over the lazy dog";
        let hash = sha256_hex(data);
        assert_eq!(hash, "d7a8fbb307d7809469ca9abcb0082e4f8d5651e46d3cdb762d02d0bf37c9e592");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_hmac_sha256() {
        // rfc 4231 test vector 2
        let key = b"Jefe";
        let data = b"what do ya want for nothing?";
        let mac = to_hex(&hmac_sha256(key, data));
        assert_eq!(mac, "5bdcc146bf60754e6a042426089575c75a003f089d2739839dec58b964ec3843");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_hex_roundtrip() {
        let data = [0xde, 0xad, 0xbe, 0xef, 0x00, 0xff];
        let hex = to_hex(&data);
        assert_eq!(hex, "deadbeef00ff");
        let back = from_hex(&hex).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(back, data);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_hex_errors() {
        assert!(from_hex("abc").is_err()); // odd length
        assert!(from_hex("zz").is_err()); // invalid chars
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_base64url_roundtrip() {
        let cases: &[&[u8]] = &[
            b"",
            b"f",
            b"fo",
            b"foo",
            b"foob",
            b"fooba",
            b"foobar",
            b"hello world! this is a longer test string",
        ];
        for data in cases {
            let encoded = base64url_encode(data);
            let decoded = base64url_decode(&encoded).unwrap();
            assert_eq!(&decoded, data, "roundtrip failed for {:?}", data);
        }
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_base64url_known() {
        let enc = base64url_encode(b"hello");
        assert_eq!(enc, "aGVsbG8");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_uuid_v4_format() {
        let id = uuid_v4();
        assert_eq!(id.len(), 36);
        assert_eq!(id.as_bytes()[8], b'-');
        assert_eq!(id.as_bytes()[13], b'-');
        assert_eq!(id.as_bytes()[18], b'-');
        assert_eq!(id.as_bytes()[23], b'-');
        // version nibble should be '4'
        assert_eq!(id.as_bytes()[14], b'4');
        // variant nibble should be 8, 9, a, or b
        let variant = id.as_bytes()[19];
        assert!(variant == b'8' || variant == b'9' || variant == b'a' || variant == b'b');
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_uuid_v4_unique() {
        let a = uuid_v4();
        let b = uuid_v4();
        assert_ne!(a, b);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_password_roundtrip() {
        let hash = hash_password("my-secret-password");
        assert!(hash.contains(':'));
        assert!(verify_password("my-secret-password", &hash));
        assert!(!verify_password("wrong-password", &hash));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_password_bad_format() {
        assert!(!verify_password("anything", "not-a-valid-hash"));
        assert!(!verify_password("anything", "zzzz:1234")); // invalid hex
        assert!(!verify_password("anything", ""));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_random_bytes() {
        let a = random_bytes_array::<32>();
        let b = random_bytes_array::<32>();
        // astronomically unlikely to be equal
        assert_ne!(a, b);
    }
}
```
