`crates/vigil-server/src/db.rs`:

```rs
use std::sync::Mutex;

use crate::sqlite::Db;
use vigil_common::timestamp::now_rfc3339;

// global connection pool for production use
// init_db stores the connection, open() reuses it if path matches
static POOL: Mutex<Option<(String, Db)>> = Mutex::new(None);

pub struct PlayerData {
    pub id: String,
    pub name: String,
    pub registered_at: String,
    pub last_report: Option<String>,
    pub is_clean: bool,
    pub config_hash: Option<String>,
    pub trust_score: u8,
    pub heartbeat_seq: u64,
    pub consecutive_clean: u32,
    pub banned: bool,
    pub banned_at: Option<String>,
    pub ban_reason: Option<String>,
}

pub struct MatchData {
    pub id: String,
    pub created_at: String,
    pub ended_at: Option<String>,
    pub player_ids: Vec<String>,
    pub game: Option<String>,
    pub map: Option<String>,
    pub result: Option<String>,
}

pub struct PartyData {
    pub id: String,
    pub leader: String,
    pub members: Vec<String>,
    pub invited: Vec<String>,
    pub game: Option<String>,
    pub created_at: String,
}

pub struct QueueEntry {
    pub player_id: String,
    pub party_id: Option<String>,
    pub game: String,
    pub joined_at: String,
}

pub struct ServerData {
    pub id: String,
    pub name: String,
    pub address: String,
    pub game: String,
    pub max_players: u32,
    pub created_at: String,
}

pub struct WhitelistEntry {
    pub pattern: String,
    pub reason: String,
    pub added_by: String,
    pub added_at: String,
}

pub struct AppealData {
    pub id: String,
    pub player_id: String,
    pub reason: String,
    pub status: String,
    pub created_at: String,
}

fn db_path(data_dir: &str) -> String {
    format!("{}/vigil.db", data_dir)
}

fn open(data_dir: &str) -> Result<PooledDb, String> {
    let path = db_path(data_dir);
    let guard = POOL.lock().map_err(|e| format!("db lock: {}", e))?;
    if let Some((ref cached_path, _)) = *guard
        && *cached_path == path {
            return Ok(PooledDb::Pooled(guard));
        }
    drop(guard);
    Ok(PooledDb::Owned(Db::open(&path)?))
}

// wraps either a pooled reference or an owned connection
// production uses pooled (from init_db), tests get owned
enum PooledDb {
    Pooled(std::sync::MutexGuard<'static, Option<(String, Db)>>),
    Owned(Db),
}

impl std::ops::Deref for PooledDb {
    type Target = Db;
    fn deref(&self) -> &Db {
        match self {
            PooledDb::Pooled(guard) => &guard.as_ref().unwrap().1,
            PooledDb::Owned(db) => db,
        }
    }
}

pub fn init_db(data_dir: &str) {
    std::fs::create_dir_all(data_dir).expect("failed to create data directory");
    let path = db_path(data_dir);

    // skip if already initialized for this path
    {
        let guard = POOL.lock().map_err(|e| format!("db lock: {}", e)).expect("db lock poisoned");
        if let Some((ref cached, _)) = *guard
            && *cached == path {
                return;
            }
    }

    let db_conn = Db::open(&path).expect("failed to open database");
    let db = &db_conn;

    // migration system
    db.execute("CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS schema_version (version INTEGER NOT NULL)").ok();
    let version = db.query("SELECT version FROM schema_version", &[])
        .ok()
        .and_then(|rows| rows.first().and_then(|r| r[0].parse::<u32>().ok()))
        .unwrap_or(0);

    if version == 0 {
        // initial schema - v1
        run_v1_schema(db);
        db.execute("DELETE FROM schema_version").ok();
        db.execute_params("INSERT INTO schema_version (version) VALUES (?1)", &["1"]).ok();
    }

    if version < 2 {
        // v2: add game, map, result columns to matches
        run_v2_migration(db);
        db.execute("DELETE FROM schema_version").ok();
        db.execute_params("INSERT INTO schema_version (version) VALUES (?1)", &["2"]).ok();
    }

    if version < 3 {
        // v3: audit log table
        run_v3_migration(db);
        db.execute("DELETE FROM schema_version").ok();
        db.execute_params("INSERT INTO schema_version (version) VALUES (?1)", &["3"]).ok();
    }

    if version < 4 {
        // v4: join tables for match_players, party_members, party_invites
        run_v4_migration(db);
        db.execute("DELETE FROM schema_version").ok();
        db.execute_params("INSERT INTO schema_version (version) VALUES (?1)", &["4"]).ok();
    }

    // indexes (idempotent, run every startup)
    run_indexes(db);

    // store in pool for reuse
    *POOL.lock().map_err(|e| format!("db lock: {}", e)).expect("db lock poisoned") = Some((path, db_conn));
}

fn run_v1_schema(db: &Db) {
    for sql in [
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS players (
            id TEXT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT UNIQUE NOT NULL, password_hash TEXT NOT NULL,
            registered_at TEXT NOT NULL, last_report TEXT, is_clean INTEGER DEFAULT 1,
            config_hash TEXT, trust_score INTEGER DEFAULT 100, heartbeat_seq INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
            consecutive_clean INTEGER DEFAULT 0, banned INTEGER DEFAULT 0, banned_at TEXT, ban_reason TEXT
        )",
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS reports (
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT, player_id TEXT NOT NULL,
            timestamp TEXT NOT NULL, data TEXT NOT NULL
        )",
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS matches (
            id TEXT PRIMARY KEY, created_at TEXT NOT NULL, ended_at TEXT, player_ids TEXT NOT NULL
        )",
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS config (key TEXT PRIMARY KEY, value TEXT NOT NULL)",
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS whitelist (
            pattern TEXT PRIMARY KEY, reason TEXT, added_by TEXT, added_at TEXT
        )",
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS friends (
            player_id TEXT NOT NULL, friend_id TEXT NOT NULL, PRIMARY KEY (player_id, friend_id)
        )",
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS parties (
            id TEXT PRIMARY KEY, leader TEXT NOT NULL, members TEXT NOT NULL,
            invited TEXT, game TEXT, created_at TEXT NOT NULL
        )",
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS servers (
            id TEXT PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT NOT NULL, address TEXT NOT NULL,
            game TEXT NOT NULL, max_players INTEGER NOT NULL, created_at TEXT NOT NULL
        )",
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS appeals (
            id TEXT PRIMARY KEY, player_id TEXT NOT NULL, reason TEXT NOT NULL,
            status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending', created_at TEXT NOT NULL
        )",
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS queue (
            player_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY, party_id TEXT, game TEXT NOT NULL, joined_at TEXT NOT NULL
        )",
    ] {
        db.execute(sql).expect("failed to create table");
    }
}

fn run_v2_migration(db: &Db) {
    // add enrichment columns to matches; ALTER TABLE ADD COLUMN is safe to run on existing DBs
    for sql in [
        "ALTER TABLE matches ADD COLUMN game TEXT",
        "ALTER TABLE matches ADD COLUMN map TEXT",
        "ALTER TABLE matches ADD COLUMN result TEXT",
    ] {
        // ignore errors — column may already exist if migration was partially applied
        db.execute(sql).ok();
    }
}

fn run_v3_migration(db: &Db) {
    db.execute(
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS audit_log (
            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
            timestamp TEXT NOT NULL,
            actor TEXT NOT NULL,
            action TEXT NOT NULL,
            target TEXT,
            detail TEXT,
            ip TEXT
        )",
    )
    .expect("failed to create audit_log table");
}

fn run_v4_migration(db: &Db) {
    // Create join tables — idempotent via IF NOT EXISTS
    for sql in [
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS match_players (
            match_id TEXT NOT NULL,
            player_id TEXT NOT NULL,
            PRIMARY KEY (match_id, player_id)
        )",
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS party_members (
            party_id TEXT NOT NULL,
            player_id TEXT NOT NULL,
            role TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'member',
            PRIMARY KEY (party_id, player_id)
        )",
        "CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS party_invites (
            party_id TEXT NOT NULL,
            player_id TEXT NOT NULL,
            PRIMARY KEY (party_id, player_id)
        )",
    ] {
        db.execute(sql).expect("failed to create join table");
    }

    // Migrate existing match CSV data into match_players
    // Use a transaction so a crash mid-migration leaves the DB at v3 (re-runnable)
    db.execute("BEGIN").ok();
    let match_rows = db
        .query("SELECT id, player_ids FROM matches WHERE player_ids != ''", &[])
        .unwrap_or_default();
    for row in &match_rows {
        let match_id = &row[0];
        let csv = &row[1];
        for pid in csv.split(',').filter(|s| !s.is_empty()) {
            // INSERT OR IGNORE: safe to re-run
            db.execute_params(
                "INSERT OR IGNORE INTO match_players (match_id, player_id) VALUES (?1, ?2)",
                &[match_id.as_str(), pid],
            )
            .ok();
        }
    }

    // Migrate existing party CSV data into party_members / party_invites
    let party_rows = db
        .query("SELECT id, leader, members, invited FROM parties", &[])
        .unwrap_or_default();
    for row in &party_rows {
        let party_id = &row[0];
        let leader = &row[1];
        let members_csv = &row[2];
        let invited_csv = &row[3];

        for mid in members_csv.split(',').filter(|s| !s.is_empty()) {
            let role = if mid == leader.as_str() { "leader" } else { "member" };
            db.execute_params(
                "INSERT OR IGNORE INTO party_members (party_id, player_id, role) VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3)",
                &[party_id.as_str(), mid, role],
            )
            .ok();
        }

        for iid in invited_csv.split(',').filter(|s| !s.is_empty()) {
            db.execute_params(
                "INSERT OR IGNORE INTO party_invites (party_id, player_id) VALUES (?1, ?2)",
                &[party_id.as_str(), iid],
            )
            .ok();
        }
    }

    db.execute("COMMIT").ok();
}

fn run_indexes(db: &Db) {
    for sql in [
        "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_players_name ON players(name)",
        "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_reports_player ON reports(player_id, timestamp)",
        "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_friends_player ON friends(player_id)",
        "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_parties_leader ON parties(leader)",
        "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_queue_game ON queue(game)",
        "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_appeals_player ON appeals(player_id)",
        "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_appeals_status ON appeals(status)",
        "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_audit_ts ON audit_log(timestamp)",
        "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_audit_actor ON audit_log(actor)",
        // v4 join-table indexes
        "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_match_players_player ON match_players(player_id)",
        "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_party_members_player ON party_members(player_id)",
        "CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_party_invites_player ON party_invites(player_id)",
    ] {
        db.execute(sql).ok();
    }
}


// --- helpers ---

fn opt(s: &str) -> Option<String> {
    if s.is_empty() { None } else { Some(s.to_string()) }
}

#[allow(dead_code)]
fn csv_to_vec(s: &str) -> Vec<String> {
    if s.is_empty() {
        vec![]
    } else {
        s.split(',').map(|x| x.to_string()).collect()
    }
}

fn vec_to_csv(v: &[String]) -> String {
    v.join(",")
}

fn bool_to_int(b: bool) -> String {
    if b { "1".to_string() } else { "0".to_string() }
}

fn row_to_player(row: &[String]) -> PlayerData {
    // columns: id, name, registered_at, last_report, is_clean, config_hash,
    //          trust_score, heartbeat_seq, consecutive_clean, banned, banned_at, ban_reason
    PlayerData {
        id: row[0].clone(),
        name: row[1].clone(),
        registered_at: row[2].clone(),
        last_report: opt(&row[3]),
        is_clean: row[4] != "0",
        config_hash: opt(&row[5]),
        trust_score: row[6].parse().unwrap_or(100),
        heartbeat_seq: row[7].parse().unwrap_or(0),
        consecutive_clean: row[8].parse().unwrap_or(0),
        banned: row[9] != "0",
        banned_at: opt(&row[10]),
        ban_reason: opt(&row[11]),
    }
}


// --- players ---

pub fn insert_player(
    data_dir: &str,
    id: &str,
    name: &str,
    password_hash: &str,
    registered_at: &str,
) -> Result<(), String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let existing = db.query("SELECT id FROM players WHERE id = ?1", &[id])?;
    if !existing.is_empty() {
        return Err(format!("player {} already exists", id));
    }
    db.execute_params(
        "INSERT INTO players (id, name, password_hash, registered_at) VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3, ?4)",
        &[id, name, password_hash, registered_at],
    )
}

pub fn get_player(data_dir: &str, id: &str) -> Result<Option<PlayerData>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT id, name, registered_at, last_report, is_clean, config_hash,
                trust_score, heartbeat_seq, consecutive_clean, banned, banned_at, ban_reason
         FROM players WHERE id = ?1",
        &[id],
    )?;
    if rows.is_empty() {
        return Ok(None);
    }
    Ok(Some(row_to_player(&rows[0])))
}

pub fn get_player_by_name(data_dir: &str, name: &str) -> Result<Option<(PlayerData, String)>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT id, name, registered_at, last_report, is_clean, config_hash,
                trust_score, heartbeat_seq, consecutive_clean, banned, banned_at, ban_reason,
                password_hash
         FROM players WHERE name = ?1",
        &[name],
    )?;
    if rows.is_empty() {
        return Ok(None);
    }
    let r = &rows[0];
    let player = row_to_player(r);
    let hash = r[12].clone();
    Ok(Some((player, hash)))
}

pub fn list_players(data_dir: &str) -> Result<Vec<PlayerData>, String> {
    list_players_paged(data_dir, 100, 0)
}

pub fn list_players_paged(data_dir: &str, limit: u32, offset: u32) -> Result<Vec<PlayerData>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let lim = limit.to_string();
    let off = offset.to_string();
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT id, name, registered_at, last_report, is_clean, config_hash,
                trust_score, heartbeat_seq, consecutive_clean, banned, banned_at, ban_reason
         FROM players LIMIT ?1 OFFSET ?2",
        &[&lim, &off],
    )?;
    Ok(rows.iter().map(|r| row_to_player(r)).collect())
}

#[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]
pub fn update_player_report(
    data_dir: &str,
    id: &str,
    last_report: &str,
    is_clean: bool,
    config_hash: &str,
    trust_score: u8,
    heartbeat_seq: u64,
    consecutive_clean: u32,
) -> Result<bool, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let clean_s = bool_to_int(is_clean);
    let trust_s = trust_score.to_string();
    let hb_s = heartbeat_seq.to_string();
    let cc_s = consecutive_clean.to_string();
    db.execute_params(
        "UPDATE players SET last_report = ?1, is_clean = ?2, config_hash = ?3,
                trust_score = ?4, heartbeat_seq = ?5, consecutive_clean = ?6
         WHERE id = ?7",
        &[last_report, &clean_s, config_hash, &trust_s, &hb_s, &cc_s, id],
    )?;
    Ok(db.changes() > 0)
}

pub fn mark_player_dirty(data_dir: &str, id: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    db.execute_params("UPDATE players SET is_clean = 0 WHERE id = ?1", &[id])?;
    if db.changes() == 0 {
        return Err(format!("player {} not found", id));
    }
    Ok(())
}

pub fn ban_player(data_dir: &str, id: &str, reason: &str) -> Result<bool, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let now = now_rfc3339();
    db.execute_params(
        "UPDATE players SET banned = 1, banned_at = ?1, ban_reason = ?2 WHERE id = ?3",
        &[&now, reason, id],
    )?;
    Ok(db.changes() > 0)
}

pub fn unban_player(data_dir: &str, id: &str) -> Result<bool, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    db.execute_params(
        "UPDATE players SET banned = 0, banned_at = NULL, ban_reason = NULL WHERE id = ?1",
        &[id],
    )?;
    Ok(db.changes() > 0)
}


// --- reports ---

pub fn insert_report(data_dir: &str, player_id: &str, timestamp: &str, data: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    db.execute_params(
        "INSERT INTO reports (player_id, timestamp, data) VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3)",
        &[player_id, timestamp, data],
    )
}

pub fn get_reports_in_range(
    data_dir: &str,
    player_id: &str,
    start: &str,
    end: &str,
) -> Result<Vec<String>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT data FROM reports WHERE player_id = ?1 AND timestamp >= ?2 AND timestamp <= ?3",
        &[player_id, start, end],
    )?;
    Ok(rows.into_iter().map(|r| r[0].clone()).collect())
}


// --- matches ---

pub fn insert_match(
    data_dir: &str,
    id: &str,
    created_at: &str,
    player_ids: &[String],
    game: Option<&str>,
    map: Option<&str>,
) -> Result<(), String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let existing = db.query("SELECT id FROM matches WHERE id = ?1", &[id])?;
    if !existing.is_empty() {
        return Err(format!("match {} already exists", id));
    }
    let pids = vec_to_csv(player_ids);
    let game_val = game.unwrap_or("");
    let map_val = map.unwrap_or("");
    db.execute_params(
        "INSERT INTO matches (id, created_at, player_ids, game, map) VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3, ?4, ?5)",
        &[id, created_at, &pids, game_val, map_val],
    )?;
    // also populate the join table
    for pid in player_ids {
        db.execute_params(
            "INSERT OR IGNORE INTO match_players (match_id, player_id) VALUES (?1, ?2)",
            &[id, pid.as_str()],
        )?;
    }
    Ok(())
}

pub fn get_match(data_dir: &str, id: &str) -> Result<Option<MatchData>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT id, created_at, ended_at, game, map, result FROM matches WHERE id = ?1",
        &[id],
    )?;
    if rows.is_empty() {
        return Ok(None);
    }
    let r = &rows[0];
    // read player_ids from join table
    let pid_rows = db.query(
        "SELECT player_id FROM match_players WHERE match_id = ?1",
        &[id],
    )?;
    let player_ids: Vec<String> = pid_rows.into_iter().map(|r| r[0].clone()).collect();
    Ok(Some(MatchData {
        id: r[0].clone(),
        created_at: r[1].clone(),
        ended_at: opt(&r[2]),
        player_ids,
        game: opt(&r[3]),
        map: opt(&r[4]),
        result: opt(&r[5]),
    }))
}

pub fn end_match(data_dir: &str, id: &str, ended_at: &str) -> Result<bool, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    db.execute_params(
        "UPDATE matches SET ended_at = ?1 WHERE id = ?2",
        &[ended_at, id],
    )?;
    Ok(db.changes() > 0)
}

pub fn list_matches(data_dir: &str) -> Result<Vec<MatchData>, String> {
    list_matches_paged(data_dir, 100, 0)
}

pub fn list_matches_paged(data_dir: &str, limit: u32, offset: u32) -> Result<Vec<MatchData>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let lim = limit.to_string();
    let off = offset.to_string();
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT id, created_at, ended_at, game, map, result FROM matches LIMIT ?1 OFFSET ?2",
        &[&lim, &off],
    )?;
    let mut result = Vec::with_capacity(rows.len());
    for r in &rows {
        let mid = &r[0];
        let pid_rows = db.query(
            "SELECT player_id FROM match_players WHERE match_id = ?1",
            &[mid.as_str()],
        )?;
        let player_ids: Vec<String> = pid_rows.into_iter().map(|pr| pr[0].clone()).collect();
        result.push(MatchData {
            id: r[0].clone(),
            created_at: r[1].clone(),
            ended_at: opt(&r[2]),
            player_ids,
            game: opt(&r[3]),
            map: opt(&r[4]),
            result: opt(&r[5]),
        });
    }
    Ok(result)
}

/// Returns matches for a specific player, ordered newest first. O(log n) via index.
pub fn get_player_matches(data_dir: &str, player_id: &str, limit: u32, offset: u32) -> Result<Vec<MatchData>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let lim = limit.to_string();
    let off = offset.to_string();
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT m.id, m.created_at, m.ended_at, m.game, m.map, m.result
         FROM matches m
         JOIN match_players mp ON m.id = mp.match_id
         WHERE mp.player_id = ?1
         ORDER BY m.created_at DESC
         LIMIT ?2 OFFSET ?3",
        &[player_id, &lim, &off],
    )?;
    let mut result = Vec::with_capacity(rows.len());
    for r in &rows {
        let mid = &r[0];
        let pid_rows = db.query(
            "SELECT player_id FROM match_players WHERE match_id = ?1",
            &[mid.as_str()],
        )?;
        let player_ids: Vec<String> = pid_rows.into_iter().map(|pr| pr[0].clone()).collect();
        result.push(MatchData {
            id: r[0].clone(),
            created_at: r[1].clone(),
            ended_at: opt(&r[2]),
            player_ids,
            game: opt(&r[3]),
            map: opt(&r[4]),
            result: opt(&r[5]),
        });
    }
    Ok(result)
}

/// Counts matches a player participated in. O(log n) via index.
pub fn count_player_matches(data_dir: &str, player_id: &str) -> Result<u64, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM match_players WHERE player_id = ?1",
        &[player_id],
    )?;
    Ok(rows.first().and_then(|r| r[0].parse().ok()).unwrap_or(0))
}

/// Counts distinct active players (in matches that have not ended). O(log n) via index.
pub fn count_active_players(data_dir: &str) -> Result<u32, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT mp.player_id)
         FROM match_players mp
         JOIN matches m ON mp.match_id = m.id
         WHERE m.ended_at IS NULL OR m.ended_at = ''",
        &[],
    )?;
    Ok(rows.first().and_then(|r| r[0].parse().ok()).unwrap_or(0))
}


// --- whitelist ---

pub fn get_whitelist(data_dir: &str) -> Result<Vec<WhitelistEntry>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let rows = db.query("SELECT pattern, reason, added_by, added_at FROM whitelist", &[])?;
    Ok(rows
        .iter()
        .map(|r| WhitelistEntry {
            pattern: r[0].clone(),
            reason: r[1].clone(),
            added_by: r[2].clone(),
            added_at: r[3].clone(),
        })
        .collect())
}

pub fn add_whitelist_entry(
    data_dir: &str,
    pattern: &str,
    reason: &str,
    added_by: &str,
    added_at: &str,
) -> Result<(), String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let existing = db.query("SELECT pattern FROM whitelist WHERE pattern = ?1", &[pattern])?;
    if !existing.is_empty() {
        return Err(format!("whitelist entry '{}' already exists", pattern));
    }
    db.execute_params(
        "INSERT INTO whitelist (pattern, reason, added_by, added_at) VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3, ?4)",
        &[pattern, reason, added_by, added_at],
    )
}

pub fn remove_whitelist_entry(data_dir: &str, pattern: &str) -> Result<bool, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    db.execute_params("DELETE FROM whitelist WHERE pattern = ?1", &[pattern])?;
    Ok(db.changes() > 0)
}

pub fn list_whitelist(data_dir: &str) -> Result<Vec<WhitelistEntry>, String> {
    get_whitelist(data_dir)
}


// --- friends ---

pub fn get_friends(data_dir: &str, player_id: &str) -> Result<Vec<String>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT friend_id FROM friends WHERE player_id = ?1",
        &[player_id],
    )?;
    Ok(rows.into_iter().map(|r| r[0].clone()).collect())
}

pub fn get_friends_paged(data_dir: &str, player_id: &str, limit: u32, offset: u32) -> Result<Vec<String>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let lim = limit.to_string();
    let off = offset.to_string();
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT friend_id FROM friends WHERE player_id = ?1 LIMIT ?2 OFFSET ?3",
        &[player_id, &lim, &off],
    )?;
    Ok(rows.into_iter().map(|r| r[0].clone()).collect())
}

pub fn add_friend(data_dir: &str, player_id: &str, friend_id: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    // add both directions, ignore if already exists
    let existing = db.query(
        "SELECT player_id FROM friends WHERE player_id = ?1 AND friend_id = ?2",
        &[player_id, friend_id],
    )?;
    if existing.is_empty() {
        db.execute_params(
            "INSERT INTO friends (player_id, friend_id) VALUES (?1, ?2)",
            &[player_id, friend_id],
        )?;
    }
    let existing = db.query(
        "SELECT player_id FROM friends WHERE player_id = ?1 AND friend_id = ?2",
        &[friend_id, player_id],
    )?;
    if existing.is_empty() {
        db.execute_params(
            "INSERT INTO friends (player_id, friend_id) VALUES (?1, ?2)",
            &[friend_id, player_id],
        )?;
    }
    Ok(())
}

pub fn remove_friend(data_dir: &str, player_id: &str, friend_id: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    db.execute_params(
        "DELETE FROM friends WHERE player_id = ?1 AND friend_id = ?2",
        &[player_id, friend_id],
    )?;
    db.execute_params(
        "DELETE FROM friends WHERE player_id = ?1 AND friend_id = ?2",
        &[friend_id, player_id],
    )?;
    Ok(())
}


// --- parties ---

pub fn create_party(data_dir: &str, leader_id: &str) -> Result<String, String> {
    let id = crate::crypto::uuid_v4();
    let now = now_rfc3339();
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    db.execute_params(
        "INSERT INTO parties (id, leader, members, invited, game, created_at)
         VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3, '', '', ?4)",
        &[&id, leader_id, leader_id, &now],
    )?;
    // populate join table: leader is first member with role 'leader'
    db.execute_params(
        "INSERT OR IGNORE INTO party_members (party_id, player_id, role) VALUES (?1, ?2, 'leader')",
        &[&id, leader_id],
    )?;
    Ok(id)
}

pub fn get_party(data_dir: &str, party_id: &str) -> Result<Option<PartyData>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT id, leader, game, created_at FROM parties WHERE id = ?1",
        &[party_id],
    )?;
    if rows.is_empty() {
        return Ok(None);
    }
    let r = &rows[0];
    let member_rows = db.query(
        "SELECT player_id FROM party_members WHERE party_id = ?1",
        &[party_id],
    )?;
    let members: Vec<String> = member_rows.into_iter().map(|r| r[0].clone()).collect();
    let invite_rows = db.query(
        "SELECT player_id FROM party_invites WHERE party_id = ?1",
        &[party_id],
    )?;
    let invited: Vec<String> = invite_rows.into_iter().map(|r| r[0].clone()).collect();
    Ok(Some(PartyData {
        id: r[0].clone(),
        leader: r[1].clone(),
        members,
        invited,
        game: opt(&r[2]),
        created_at: r[3].clone(),
    }))
}

pub fn get_player_party(data_dir: &str, player_id: &str) -> Result<Option<PartyData>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    // O(1) indexed lookup via join table instead of full scan
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT p.id, p.leader, p.game, p.created_at
         FROM parties p
         JOIN party_members pm ON p.id = pm.party_id
         WHERE pm.player_id = ?1
         LIMIT 1",
        &[player_id],
    )?;
    if rows.is_empty() {
        return Ok(None);
    }
    let r = &rows[0];
    let party_id = &r[0];
    let member_rows = db.query(
        "SELECT player_id FROM party_members WHERE party_id = ?1",
        &[party_id.as_str()],
    )?;
    let members: Vec<String> = member_rows.into_iter().map(|r| r[0].clone()).collect();
    let invite_rows = db.query(
        "SELECT player_id FROM party_invites WHERE party_id = ?1",
        &[party_id.as_str()],
    )?;
    let invited: Vec<String> = invite_rows.into_iter().map(|r| r[0].clone()).collect();
    Ok(Some(PartyData {
        id: r[0].clone(),
        leader: r[1].clone(),
        members,
        invited,
        game: opt(&r[2]),
        created_at: r[3].clone(),
    }))
}

pub fn invite_to_party(data_dir: &str, party_id: &str, player_id: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
    // Phase 1: validation reads
    {
        let db = open(data_dir)?;
        let exists = db.query("SELECT id FROM parties WHERE id = ?1", &[party_id])?;
        if exists.is_empty() {
            return Err("party not found".to_string());
        }
        let in_members = db.query(
            "SELECT player_id FROM party_members WHERE party_id = ?1 AND player_id = ?2",
            &[party_id, player_id],
        )?;
        if !in_members.is_empty() {
            return Err("player already invited or in party".to_string());
        }
        let in_invites = db.query(
            "SELECT player_id FROM party_invites WHERE party_id = ?1 AND player_id = ?2",
            &[party_id, player_id],
        )?;
        if !in_invites.is_empty() {
            return Err("player already invited or in party".to_string());
        }
    } // db dropped here

    // Phase 2: write to join table
    {
        let db = open(data_dir)?;
        db.execute_params(
            "INSERT INTO party_invites (party_id, player_id) VALUES (?1, ?2)",
            &[party_id, player_id],
        )?;
    } // db dropped here

    // Phase 3: sync legacy CSV (reads join table, writes parties)
    let party = get_party(data_dir, party_id)?
        .ok_or_else(|| "party not found".to_string())?;
    let csv = vec_to_csv(&party.invited);
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    db.execute_params(
        "UPDATE parties SET invited = ?1 WHERE id = ?2",
        &[&csv, party_id],
    )
}

pub fn join_party(data_dir: &str, party_id: &str, player_id: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
    // Phase 1: check invite exists
    {
        let db = open(data_dir)?;
        let invited_rows = db.query(
            "SELECT player_id FROM party_invites WHERE party_id = ?1 AND player_id = ?2",
            &[party_id, player_id],
        )?;
        if invited_rows.is_empty() {
            return Err("player not invited".to_string());
        }
    } // db dropped here

    // Phase 2: move from invites → members
    {
        let db = open(data_dir)?;
        db.execute_params(
            "DELETE FROM party_invites WHERE party_id = ?1 AND player_id = ?2",
            &[party_id, player_id],
        )?;
        db.execute_params(
            "INSERT OR IGNORE INTO party_members (party_id, player_id, role) VALUES (?1, ?2, 'member')",
            &[party_id, player_id],
        )?;
    } // db dropped here

    // Phase 3: sync legacy CSV
    let party = get_party(data_dir, party_id)?
        .ok_or_else(|| "party not found".to_string())?;
    let members_csv = vec_to_csv(&party.members);
    let invited_csv = vec_to_csv(&party.invited);
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    db.execute_params(
        "UPDATE parties SET members = ?1, invited = ?2 WHERE id = ?3",
        &[&members_csv, &invited_csv, party_id],
    )
}

pub fn leave_party(data_dir: &str, party_id: &str, player_id: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
    let party = get_party(data_dir, party_id)?
        .ok_or_else(|| "party not found".to_string())?;
    if party.leader == player_id {
        return delete_party(data_dir, party_id);
    }
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    db.execute_params(
        "DELETE FROM party_members WHERE party_id = ?1 AND player_id = ?2",
        &[party_id, player_id],
    )?;
    // keep legacy CSV in sync
    let remaining: Vec<String> = party.members.into_iter().filter(|m| m != player_id).collect();
    let members_csv = vec_to_csv(&remaining);
    db.execute_params(
        "UPDATE parties SET members = ?1 WHERE id = ?2",
        &[&members_csv, party_id],
    )
}

pub fn delete_party(data_dir: &str, party_id: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    db.execute_params("DELETE FROM party_members WHERE party_id = ?1", &[party_id])?;
    db.execute_params("DELETE FROM party_invites WHERE party_id = ?1", &[party_id])?;
    db.execute_params("DELETE FROM parties WHERE id = ?1", &[party_id])?;
    Ok(())
}


// --- queue ---

pub fn join_queue(data_dir: &str, player_id: &str, party_id: Option<&str>, game: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let existing = db.query("SELECT player_id FROM queue WHERE player_id = ?1", &[player_id])?;
    if !existing.is_empty() {
        return Err("already in queue".to_string());
    }
    let now = now_rfc3339();
    let pid = party_id.unwrap_or("");
    db.execute_params(
        "INSERT INTO queue (player_id, party_id, game, joined_at) VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3, ?4)",
        &[player_id, pid, game, &now],
    )
}

pub fn leave_queue(data_dir: &str, player_id: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    db.execute_params("DELETE FROM queue WHERE player_id = ?1", &[player_id])?;
    Ok(())
}

pub fn get_queue(data_dir: &str) -> Result<Vec<QueueEntry>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT player_id, party_id, game, joined_at FROM queue ORDER BY rowid",
        &[],
    )?;
    Ok(rows
        .iter()
        .map(|r| QueueEntry {
            player_id: r[0].clone(),
            party_id: opt(&r[1]),
            game: r[2].clone(),
            joined_at: r[3].clone(),
        })
        .collect())
}

pub fn get_queue_paged(data_dir: &str, limit: u32, offset: u32) -> Result<Vec<QueueEntry>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let lim = limit.to_string();
    let off = offset.to_string();
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT player_id, party_id, game, joined_at FROM queue ORDER BY rowid LIMIT ?1 OFFSET ?2",
        &[&lim, &off],
    )?;
    Ok(rows
        .iter()
        .map(|r| QueueEntry {
            player_id: r[0].clone(),
            party_id: opt(&r[1]),
            game: r[2].clone(),
            joined_at: r[3].clone(),
        })
        .collect())
}

pub fn get_queue_position(data_dir: &str, player_id: &str) -> Result<Option<usize>, String> {
    let entries = get_queue(data_dir)?;
    Ok(entries.iter().position(|e| e.player_id == player_id))
}

// tries to form a match from queued players for the same game
// match_size = number of players needed (e.g. 10)
// returns (match_id, player_ids) if formed, None if not enough players
// skill-based: groups players by trust_score within 20 points of each other
// also purges stale queue entries older than 5 minutes
pub fn try_matchmake(data_dir: &str, game: &str, match_size: usize) -> Result<Option<(String, Vec<String>)>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;

    db.execute("BEGIN")?;

    // queue timeout: delete entries older than 5 minutes
    let now = now_rfc3339();
    let cutoff = vigil_common::timestamp::secs_to_rfc3339(
        vigil_common::timestamp::now_secs().saturating_sub(300),
    );
    let _ = db.execute_params(
        "DELETE FROM queue WHERE joined_at < ?1",
        &[&cutoff],
    );

    // fetch queued players with their trust scores, sorted by trust_score
    let rows = match db.query(
        "SELECT q.player_id, COALESCE(p.trust_score, 100)
         FROM queue q LEFT JOIN players p ON q.player_id = p.id
         WHERE q.game = ?1
         ORDER BY CAST(COALESCE(p.trust_score, 100) AS INTEGER) DESC",
        &[game],
    ) {
        Ok(r) => r,
        Err(e) => {
            let _ = db.execute("ROLLBACK");
            return Err(e);
        }
    };

    if rows.len() < match_size {
        let _ = db.execute("ROLLBACK");
        return Ok(None);
    }

    // group players with similar trust scores (within 20 points)
    // find the first group that has enough players
    let mut best_group: Option<Vec<String>> = None;
    for (idx, anchor_row) in rows.iter().enumerate() {
        let anchor_score: i64 = anchor_row[1].parse().unwrap_or(100);
        let mut group = Vec::new();
        for row in rows.iter().skip(idx) {
            let score: i64 = row[1].parse().unwrap_or(100);
            if (anchor_score - score).abs() <= 20 {
                group.push(row[0].clone());
            }
            if group.len() == match_size {
                break;
            }
        }
        if group.len() >= match_size {
            best_group = Some(group);
            break;
        }
    }

    let player_ids = match best_group {
        Some(g) => g,
        None => {
            let _ = db.execute("ROLLBACK");
            return Ok(None);
        }
    };

    let match_id = crate::crypto::uuid_v4();
    let ids_csv = player_ids.join(",");

    if let Err(e) = db.execute_params(
        "INSERT INTO matches (id, created_at, player_ids, game, map) VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3, ?4, ?5)",
        &[&match_id, &now, &ids_csv, game, ""],
    ) {
        let _ = db.execute("ROLLBACK");
        return Err(e);
    }

    // populate join table for the new match
    for pid in &player_ids {
        if let Err(e) = db.execute_params(
            "INSERT OR IGNORE INTO match_players (match_id, player_id) VALUES (?1, ?2)",
            &[match_id.as_str(), pid.as_str()],
        ) {
            let _ = db.execute("ROLLBACK");
            return Err(e);
        }
    }

    // remove matched players from queue
    for pid in &player_ids {
        if let Err(e) = db.execute_params("DELETE FROM queue WHERE player_id = ?1", &[pid.as_str()]) {
            let _ = db.execute("ROLLBACK");
            return Err(e);
        }
    }

    db.execute("COMMIT")?;
    Ok(Some((match_id, player_ids)))
}

// --- servers ---

pub fn register_server(data_dir: &str, name: &str, address: &str, game: &str, max_players: u32) -> Result<String, String> {
    let id = crate::crypto::uuid_v4();
    let now = now_rfc3339();
    let mp = max_players.to_string();
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    db.execute_params(
        "INSERT INTO servers (id, name, address, game, max_players, created_at)
         VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3, ?4, ?5, ?6)",
        &[&id, name, address, game, &mp, &now],
    )?;
    Ok(id)
}

pub fn list_servers_paged(data_dir: &str, limit: u32, offset: u32) -> Result<Vec<ServerData>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let lim = limit.to_string();
    let off = offset.to_string();
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT id, name, address, game, max_players, created_at FROM servers LIMIT ?1 OFFSET ?2",
        &[&lim, &off],
    )?;
    Ok(rows
        .iter()
        .map(|r| ServerData {
            id: r[0].clone(),
            name: r[1].clone(),
            address: r[2].clone(),
            game: r[3].clone(),
            max_players: r[4].parse().unwrap_or(16),
            created_at: r[5].clone(),
        })
        .collect())
}


// --- config ---

pub fn get_config(data_dir: &str, key: &str) -> Result<Option<String>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let rows = db.query("SELECT value FROM config WHERE key = ?1", &[key])?;
    if rows.is_empty() {
        return Ok(None);
    }
    Ok(Some(rows[0][0].clone()))
}

pub fn set_config(data_dir: &str, key: &str, value: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let existing = db.query("SELECT key FROM config WHERE key = ?1", &[key])?;
    if existing.is_empty() {
        db.execute_params(
            "INSERT INTO config (key, value) VALUES (?1, ?2)",
            &[key, value],
        )
    } else {
        db.execute_params(
            "UPDATE config SET value = ?1 WHERE key = ?2",
            &[value, key],
        )
    }
}


// --- appeals ---

pub fn submit_appeal(data_dir: &str, player_id: &str, reason: &str) -> Result<String, String> {
    let id = crate::crypto::uuid_v4();
    let now = now_rfc3339();
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    db.execute_params(
        "INSERT INTO appeals (id, player_id, reason, status, created_at)
         VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3, 'pending', ?4)",
        &[&id, player_id, reason, &now],
    )?;
    Ok(id)
}

pub fn list_appeals(data_dir: &str) -> Result<Vec<AppealData>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT id, player_id, reason, status, created_at FROM appeals",
        &[],
    )?;
    Ok(rows
        .iter()
        .map(|r| AppealData {
            id: r[0].clone(),
            player_id: r[1].clone(),
            reason: r[2].clone(),
            status: r[3].clone(),
            created_at: r[4].clone(),
        })
        .collect())
}

pub fn list_appeals_paged(data_dir: &str, limit: u32, offset: u32) -> Result<Vec<AppealData>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let lim = limit.to_string();
    let off = offset.to_string();
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT id, player_id, reason, status, created_at FROM appeals LIMIT ?1 OFFSET ?2",
        &[&lim, &off],
    )?;
    Ok(rows
        .iter()
        .map(|r| AppealData {
            id: r[0].clone(),
            player_id: r[1].clone(),
            reason: r[2].clone(),
            status: r[3].clone(),
            created_at: r[4].clone(),
        })
        .collect())
}

pub fn resolve_appeal(data_dir: &str, appeal_id: &str, new_status: &str) -> Result<bool, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    db.execute_params(
        "UPDATE appeals SET status = ?1 WHERE id = ?2",
        &[new_status, appeal_id],
    )?;
    Ok(db.changes() > 0)
}


// --- audit log ---

pub struct AuditEntry {
    pub id: i64,
    pub timestamp: String,
    pub actor: String,
    pub action: String,
    pub target: Option<String>,
    pub detail: Option<String>,
    pub ip: Option<String>,
}

pub fn audit_log(
    data_dir: &str,
    actor: &str,
    action: &str,
    target: Option<&str>,
    detail: Option<&str>,
    ip: Option<&str>,
) -> Result<(), String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let ts = now_rfc3339();
    db.execute_params(
        "INSERT INTO audit_log (timestamp, actor, action, target, detail, ip) VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3, ?4, ?5, ?6)",
        &[&ts, actor, action, target.unwrap_or(""), detail.unwrap_or(""), ip.unwrap_or("")],
    )
}

pub fn list_audit_log(data_dir: &str, limit: u32, offset: u32) -> Result<Vec<AuditEntry>, String> {
    let db = open(data_dir)?;
    let lim = limit.to_string();
    let off = offset.to_string();
    let rows = db.query(
        "SELECT id, timestamp, actor, action, target, detail, ip FROM audit_log ORDER BY id DESC LIMIT ?1 OFFSET ?2",
        &[&lim, &off],
    )?;
    Ok(rows
        .iter()
        .map(|r| AuditEntry {
            id: r[0].parse().unwrap_or(0),
            timestamp: r[1].clone(),
            actor: r[2].clone(),
            action: r[3].clone(),
            target: opt(&r[4]),
            detail: opt(&r[5]),
            ip: opt(&r[6]),
        })
        .collect())
}


#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    fn tmp_db(label: &str) -> String {
        let dir = std::env::temp_dir()
            .join(format!("vigil_db_test_{}_{}", std::process::id(), label));
        let _ = std::fs::remove_dir_all(&dir);
        dir.to_string_lossy().to_string()
    }

    fn cleanup(dir: &str) {
        let _ = std::fs::remove_dir_all(dir);
    }


    #[test]
    fn init_db_creates_database() {
        let dir = tmp_db("init");
        init_db(&dir);

        assert!(std::path::Path::new(&format!("{}/vigil.db", dir)).exists());

        cleanup(&dir);
    }

    #[test]
    fn init_db_is_idempotent() {
        let dir = tmp_db("init_idem");
        init_db(&dir);
        init_db(&dir);
        assert!(std::path::Path::new(&format!("{}/vigil.db", dir)).exists());
        cleanup(&dir);
    }


    #[test]
    fn insert_and_get_player_roundtrip() {
        let dir = tmp_db("player_rt");
        init_db(&dir);

        insert_player(&dir, "p1", "alice", "hash123", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();

        let p = get_player(&dir, "p1").unwrap().expect("player should exist");
        assert_eq!(p.id, "p1");
        assert_eq!(p.name, "alice");
        assert_eq!(p.registered_at, "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z");
        assert!(p.last_report.is_none());
        assert!(p.is_clean);
        assert!(p.config_hash.is_none());

        cleanup(&dir);
    }

    #[test]
    fn get_player_returns_none_for_missing() {
        let dir = tmp_db("player_miss");
        init_db(&dir);

        assert!(get_player(&dir, "nonexistent").unwrap().is_none());

        cleanup(&dir);
    }

    #[test]
    fn insert_player_rejects_duplicate_id() {
        let dir = tmp_db("player_dup");
        init_db(&dir);

        insert_player(&dir, "p1", "alice", "h1", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();
        let result = insert_player(&dir, "p1", "bob", "h2", "2025-01-02T00:00:00Z");
        assert!(result.is_err());
        assert!(result.unwrap_err().contains("already exists"));

        cleanup(&dir);
    }

    #[test]
    fn get_player_by_name_finds_correct_player() {
        let dir = tmp_db("player_byname");
        init_db(&dir);

        insert_player(&dir, "p1", "alice", "h1", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();
        insert_player(&dir, "p2", "bob", "h2", "2025-01-02T00:00:00Z").unwrap();

        let (p, hash) = get_player_by_name(&dir, "bob").unwrap().expect("bob should exist");
        assert_eq!(p.id, "p2");
        assert_eq!(p.name, "bob");
        assert_eq!(hash, "h2");

        cleanup(&dir);
    }

    #[test]
    fn get_player_by_name_returns_none_for_missing() {
        let dir = tmp_db("player_byname_miss");
        init_db(&dir);

        assert!(get_player_by_name(&dir, "charlie").unwrap().is_none());

        cleanup(&dir);
    }

    #[test]
    fn list_players_returns_all() {
        let dir = tmp_db("player_list");
        init_db(&dir);

        insert_player(&dir, "p1", "alice", "h1", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();
        insert_player(&dir, "p2", "bob", "h2", "2025-01-02T00:00:00Z").unwrap();
        insert_player(&dir, "p3", "charlie", "h3", "2025-01-03T00:00:00Z").unwrap();

        let players = list_players(&dir).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(players.len(), 3);

        let mut names: Vec<&str> = players.iter().map(|p| p.name.as_str()).collect();
        names.sort();
        assert_eq!(names, vec!["alice", "bob", "charlie"]);

        cleanup(&dir);
    }

    #[test]
    fn list_players_returns_empty_when_no_players() {
        let dir = tmp_db("player_list_empty");
        init_db(&dir);

        let players = list_players(&dir).unwrap();
        assert!(players.is_empty());

        cleanup(&dir);
    }


    #[test]
    fn update_player_report_updates_fields() {
        let dir = tmp_db("player_update");
        init_db(&dir);

        insert_player(&dir, "p1", "alice", "h1", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();

        let updated = update_player_report(&dir, "p1", "2025-06-15T12:00:00Z", false, "abc123", 85, 5, 0)
            .unwrap();
        assert!(updated);

        let p = get_player(&dir, "p1").unwrap().unwrap();
        assert_eq!(p.last_report.as_deref(), Some("2025-06-15T12:00:00Z"));
        assert!(!p.is_clean);
        assert_eq!(p.config_hash.as_deref(), Some("abc123"));

        cleanup(&dir);
    }

    #[test]
    fn update_player_report_returns_false_for_missing() {
        let dir = tmp_db("player_update_miss");
        init_db(&dir);

        let result = update_player_report(&dir, "noone", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z", true, "h", 100, 1, 0)
            .unwrap();
        assert!(!result);

        cleanup(&dir);
    }

    #[test]
    fn update_player_report_preserves_password_hash() {
        let dir = tmp_db("player_update_pw");
        init_db(&dir);

        insert_player(&dir, "p1", "alice", "secret-hash-value", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();
        update_player_report(&dir, "p1", "2025-06-01T00:00:00Z", true, "cfg1", 100, 1, 0).unwrap();

        let (_, hash) = get_player_by_name(&dir, "alice").unwrap().unwrap();
        assert_eq!(hash, "secret-hash-value");

        cleanup(&dir);
    }


    #[test]
    fn mark_player_dirty_sets_is_clean_false() {
        let dir = tmp_db("player_dirty");
        init_db(&dir);

        insert_player(&dir, "p1", "alice", "h1", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();
        assert!(get_player(&dir, "p1").unwrap().unwrap().is_clean);

        mark_player_dirty(&dir, "p1").unwrap();
        assert!(!get_player(&dir, "p1").unwrap().unwrap().is_clean);

        cleanup(&dir);
    }

    #[test]
    fn mark_player_dirty_errors_for_missing() {
        let dir = tmp_db("player_dirty_miss");
        init_db(&dir);

        let result = mark_player_dirty(&dir, "noone");
        assert!(result.is_err());

        cleanup(&dir);
    }


    #[test]
    fn insert_and_get_reports_in_range() {
        let dir = tmp_db("report_range");
        init_db(&dir);

        insert_report(&dir, "p1", "2025-01-10T00:00:00Z", "data-a").unwrap();
        insert_report(&dir, "p1", "2025-01-15T00:00:00Z", "data-b").unwrap();
        insert_report(&dir, "p1", "2025-01-20T00:00:00Z", "data-c").unwrap();
        insert_report(&dir, "p2", "2025-01-15T00:00:00Z", "data-other").unwrap();

        let reports = get_reports_in_range(
            &dir, "p1", "2025-01-12T00:00:00Z", "2025-01-20T00:00:00Z",
        ).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(reports.len(), 2);
        assert!(reports.contains(&"data-b".to_string()));
        assert!(reports.contains(&"data-c".to_string()));

        cleanup(&dir);
    }

    #[test]
    fn get_reports_in_range_filters_by_player() {
        let dir = tmp_db("report_filter");
        init_db(&dir);

        insert_report(&dir, "p1", "2025-01-15T00:00:00Z", "p1-data").unwrap();
        insert_report(&dir, "p2", "2025-01-15T00:00:00Z", "p2-data").unwrap();

        let reports = get_reports_in_range(
            &dir, "p1", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z", "2025-12-31T00:00:00Z",
        ).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(reports.len(), 1);
        assert_eq!(reports[0], "p1-data");

        cleanup(&dir);
    }

        assert!(reports.is_empty());

        cleanup(&dir);
    }


    #[test]

        init_db(&dir);

        let m = get_match(&dir, "m1").unwrap().expect("match should exist");
        assert_eq!(m.id, "m1");
        assert_eq!(m.created_at, "2025-03-01T10:00:00Z");

        insert_match(&dir, "m2", "2025-03-02T10:00:00Z", &p2, None, None).unwrap();

        let matches = list_matches(&dir).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(matches.len(), 2);

        let mut ids: Vec<&str> = matches.iter().map(|m| m.id.as_str()).collect();
        ids.sort();
        assert_eq!(ids, vec!["m1", "m2"]);

        cleanup(&dir);

        assert_eq!(p.ban_reason.as_deref(), Some("trust score reached 0"));

        cleanup(&dir);
    }

    #[test]
    fn matchmake_not_enough_players() {
        let dir = tmp_db("mm_not_enough");
        init_db(&dir);

        insert_player(&dir, "p1", "a1", "h1", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();
        insert_player(&dir, "p2", "a2", "h2", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();

        join_queue(&dir, "p1", None, "cs2").unwrap();
        join_queue(&dir, "p2", None, "cs2").unwrap();

        let result = try_matchmake(&dir, "cs2", 3).unwrap();
        assert!(result.is_none());

        // players still in queue
        assert_eq!(get_queue(&dir).unwrap().len(), 2);
        cleanup(&dir);
    }

    #[test]
    fn matchmake_forms_match() {
        let dir = tmp_db("mm_form");
        init_db(&dir);

        insert_player(&dir, "p1", "a1", "h1", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();
        insert_player(&dir, "p2", "a2", "h2", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();
        insert_player(&dir, "p3", "a3", "h3", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();

        join_queue(&dir, "p1", None, "cs2").unwrap();
        join_queue(&dir, "p2", None, "cs2").unwrap();
        join_queue(&dir, "p3", None, "cs2").unwrap();

        let result = try_matchmake(&dir, "cs2", 3).unwrap();
        assert!(result.is_some());

        let (match_id, player_ids) = result.unwrap();

        // players removed from queue
        assert_eq!(get_queue(&dir).unwrap().len(), 0);

        // match created with correct players
        let m = get_match(&dir, &match_id).unwrap().unwrap();
        assert_eq!(m.player_ids.len(), 3);
        assert_eq!(player_ids.len(), 3);
        cleanup(&dir);
    }

    #[test]
    fn matchmake_different_games_dont_mix() {
        let dir = tmp_db("mm_games");
        init_db(&dir);

        insert_player(&dir, "p1", "a1", "h1", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();
        insert_player(&dir, "p2", "a2", "h2", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();
        insert_player(&dir, "p3", "a3", "h3", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();

        join_queue(&dir, "p1", None, "cs2").unwrap();
        join_queue(&dir, "p2", None, "deadlock").unwrap();
        join_queue(&dir, "p3", None, "cs2").unwrap();

        let result = try_matchmake(&dir, "cs2", 3).unwrap();
        assert!(result.is_none()); // only 2 cs2 players, need 3

        let result = try_matchmake(&dir, "deadlock", 2).unwrap();
        assert!(result.is_none()); // only 1 deadlock player

        cleanup(&dir);
    }
}
```
