`crates/vigil-server/src/error.rs`:

```rs
use std::fmt;

// TODO: migrate existing String errors to ServerError
#[derive(Debug)]
pub enum ServerError {
    BadRequest(String),
    Unauthorized,
    Forbidden,
    NotFound(String),
    Conflict(String),
    Internal(String),
    Db(String),
}

impl fmt::Display for ServerError {
    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {
        match self {
            Self::BadRequest(m) => write!(f, "bad request: {}", m),
            Self::Unauthorized => write!(f, "unauthorized"),
            Self::Forbidden => write!(f, "forbidden"),
            Self::NotFound(m) => write!(f, "not found: {}", m),
            Self::Conflict(m) => write!(f, "conflict: {}", m),
            Self::Internal(m) => write!(f, "internal: {}", m),
            Self::Db(m) => write!(f, "db error: {}", m),
        }
    }
}

impl From<String> for ServerError {
    fn from(s: String) -> Self {
        ServerError::Internal(s)
    }
}

```

`crates/vigil-server/src/handlers.rs`:

```rs
use std::collections::HashMap;
use std::sync::Mutex;

use vigil_common::timestamp::{now_secs, rfc3339_to_secs, secs_to_rfc3339};

use crate::auth::{check_admin, check_auth, create_token, hash_pw, verify_pw};
use crate::crypto::{sha256_hex, uuid_v4};
use crate::db::{self, MatchData, PartyData, PlayerData};
use crate::http::{Request, Response};
use crate::json::{
    json_arr, json_bool, json_null, json_num, json_obj, json_str, parse, stringify, JsonValue,
};
use crate::router::Params;
use crate::ws;

macro_rules! require_auth {
    ($req:expr) => {
        match check_auth($req) {
            Ok(id) => id,
            Err(code) => return err_response(code, "unauthorized"),
        }
    };
}

macro_rules! require_admin {
    ($req:expr) => {
        if let Err(code) = check_admin($req) {
            return err_response(code, "forbidden");
        }
    };
}

macro_rules! parse_body {
    ($req:expr) => {
        match parse(&$req.body) {
            Ok(v) => v,
            Err(_) => return err_response(400, "invalid json"),
        }
    };
}

// global data dir - set once at startup via init()
static DATA_DIR: std::sync::OnceLock<String> = std::sync::OnceLock::new();

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Replay protection — nonce tracking
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

// Maps nonce string → unix timestamp (secs) when it was first seen.
// The Option<_> wrapper lets us use Mutex::new(None) as a const expression,
// then lazily initialise the HashMap on first use without OnceLock.
static SEEN_NONCES: Mutex<Option<HashMap<String, u64>>> = Mutex::new(None);

/// Initialise the nonce store.  Safe to call multiple times; subsequent calls
/// are no-ops.  Must be called before the first request arrives.
pub fn init_nonces() {
    let mut guard = SEEN_NONCES.lock().unwrap_or_else(|e| e.into_inner());
    if guard.is_none() {
        *guard = Some(HashMap::new());
    }
    init_report_rate();
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Per-player report rate limiting
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

// Maps player_id → unix timestamp (secs) of their last accepted report.
static REPORT_RATE: Mutex<Option<HashMap<String, u64>>> = Mutex::new(None);

/// Initialise the report rate store.  Safe to call multiple times; subsequent
/// calls are no-ops.
fn init_report_rate() {
    let mut guard = REPORT_RATE.lock().unwrap_or_else(|e| e.into_inner());
    if guard.is_none() {
        *guard = Some(HashMap::new());
    }
}

/// Returns `true` if `player_id` submitted a report within the last 5 seconds.
fn is_rate_limited_report(player_id: &str) -> bool {
    // disable rate limiting in test builds (fast-hash feature)
    if cfg!(feature = "fast-hash") {
        return false;
    }
    let guard = REPORT_RATE.lock().unwrap_or_else(|e| e.into_inner());
    if let Some(ref map) = *guard {
        let cutoff = now_secs().saturating_sub(5);
        if let Some(&last_at) = map.get(player_id) {
            return last_at >= cutoff;
        }
    }
    false
}

/// Record that `player_id` just submitted a report.
fn record_report_time(player_id: &str) {
    let mut guard = REPORT_RATE.lock().unwrap_or_else(|e| e.into_inner());
    if let Some(ref mut map) = *guard {
        map.insert(player_id.to_string(), now_secs());

        // Periodically purge entries older than 5 seconds to bound memory use.
        if map.len() % 100 == 0 {
            let cutoff = now_secs().saturating_sub(5);
            map.retain(|_, &mut last_at| last_at >= cutoff);
        }
    }
}

/// Returns `true` if `nonce` was already seen within the last 5 minutes.
fn is_replay(nonce: &str) -> bool {
    let guard = SEEN_NONCES.lock().unwrap_or_else(|e| e.into_inner());
    if let Some(ref map) = *guard {
        let cutoff = now_secs().saturating_sub(300); // 5 minutes
        if let Some(&seen_at) = map.get(nonce) {
            return seen_at >= cutoff;
        }
    }
    false
}

/// Record `nonce` with the current timestamp.
fn record_nonce(nonce: &str) {
    let mut guard = SEEN_NONCES.lock().unwrap_or_else(|e| e.into_inner());
    if let Some(ref mut map) = *guard {
        map.insert(nonce.to_string(), now_secs());

        // Periodically purge entries older than 5 minutes to bound memory use.
        // We do this every ~100 insertions (cheap heuristic: map len % 100 == 0).
        if map.len() % 100 == 0 {
            cleanup_old_nonces(map);
        }
    }
}

/// Remove all nonce entries older than 5 minutes from `map`.
fn cleanup_old_nonces(map: &mut HashMap<String, u64>) {
    let cutoff = now_secs().saturating_sub(300);
    map.retain(|_, &mut seen_at| seen_at >= cutoff);
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

pub fn init(dir: &str) {
    DATA_DIR.set(dir.to_string()).ok();
}

fn dir() -> &'static str {
    DATA_DIR.get().map(|s| s.as_str()).unwrap_or("data")
}


fn parse_pagination(req: &Request) -> (u32, u32) {
    let query = req.path.split('?').nth(1).unwrap_or("");
    let mut limit = 50u32;
    let mut offset = 0u32;
    for pair in query.split('&') {
        if let Some((k, v)) = pair.split_once('=') {
            match k {
                "limit" => { limit = v.parse().unwrap_or(50).min(100); }
                "offset" => { offset = v.parse().unwrap_or(0); }
                _ => {}
            }
        }
    }
    (limit, offset)
}

fn ok_response(data: JsonValue) -> Response {
    let body = stringify(&json_obj(vec![
        ("success", json_bool(true)),
        ("data", data),
        ("error", json_null()),
    ]));
    Response::json(body)
}

fn err_response(status: u16, msg: &str) -> Response {
    let body = stringify(&json_obj(vec![
        ("success", json_bool(false)),
        ("data", json_null()),
        ("error", json_str(msg)),
    ]));
    Response::new(status)
        .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
        .body(body)
}

fn player_to_json(p: &PlayerData) -> JsonValue {
    json_obj(vec![
        ("id", json_str(&p.id)),
        ("name", json_str(&p.name)),
        ("registered_at", json_str(&p.registered_at)),
        (
            "last_report",
            p.last_report.as_deref().map(json_str).unwrap_or_else(json_null),
        ),
        ("is_clean", json_bool(p.is_clean)),
        (
            "config_hash",
            p.config_hash.as_deref().map(json_str).unwrap_or_else(json_null),
        ),
        ("trust_score", json_num(p.trust_score as f64)),
        ("banned", json_bool(p.banned)),
    ])
}

fn match_to_json(m: &MatchData) -> JsonValue {
    let pids = json_arr(m.player_ids.iter().map(|s| json_str(s)).collect());

    // compute duration string from timestamps if match has ended
    let duration = match (m.created_at.as_str(), m.ended_at.as_deref()) {
        (start, Some(end)) => {
            match (rfc3339_to_secs(start), rfc3339_to_secs(end)) {
                (Some(s), Some(e)) if e >= s => {
                    let secs = e - s;
                    let h = secs / 3600;
                    let min = (secs % 3600) / 60;
                    let sec = secs % 60;
                    if h > 0 {
                        format!("{}h {}m {}s", h, min, sec)
                    } else if min > 0 {
                        format!("{}m {}s", min, sec)
                    } else {
                        format!("{}s", sec)
                    }
                }
                _ => String::new(),
            }
        }
        _ => String::new(),
    };

    json_obj(vec![
        ("id", json_str(&m.id)),
        ("created_at", json_str(&m.created_at)),
        (
            "ended_at",
            m.ended_at.as_deref().map(json_str).unwrap_or_else(json_null),
        ),
        ("player_ids", pids),
        ("game", m.game.as_deref().map(json_str).unwrap_or_else(json_null)),
        ("map", m.map.as_deref().map(json_str).unwrap_or_else(json_null)),
        ("duration", if duration.is_empty() { json_null() } else { json_str(&duration) }),
        ("result", m.result.as_deref().map(json_str).unwrap_or_else(json_null)),
    ])
}

// GET /api/health
pub fn health(_req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    ok_response(json_obj(vec![
        ("status", json_str("ok")),
        ("service", json_str("vigil-server")),
    ]))
}

// POST /api/player/register - body: {"name":"..","password":".."}
pub fn register(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    let v = parse_body!(req);

    let name = match v.get("name").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(n) if !n.is_empty() => n.to_string(),
        _ => return err_response(400, "name required"),
    };

    let password = match v.get("password").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(p) if p.len() >= 6 => p.to_string(),
        Some(_) => return err_response(400, "password min 6 chars"),
        None => return err_response(400, "password required"),
    };

    // check if name is taken
    match db::get_player_by_name(dir(), &name) {
        Ok(Some(_)) => return err_response(400, "player name already taken"),
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
        Ok(None) => {}
    }

    let id = uuid_v4();
    let now = secs_to_rfc3339(now_secs());
    let hash = hash_pw(&password);

    if let Err(e) = db::insert_player(dir(), &id, &name, &hash, &now) {
        return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e));
    }

    let _ = db::audit_log(dir(), &id, "register", None, None, req.get_header("x-forwarded-for").or_else(|| req.get_header("x-real-ip")));

    let token = match create_token(&id) {
        Ok(t) => t,
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("token error: {}", e)),
    };

    ok_response(json_obj(vec![
        (
            "player",
            json_obj(vec![
                ("id", json_str(&id)),
                ("name", json_str(&name)),
                ("registered_at", json_str(&now)),
            ]),
        ),
        ("token", json_str(&token)),
    ]))
}

// POST /api/player/login - body: {"name":"..","password":".."}
pub fn login(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    let v = parse_body!(req);

    let name = match v.get("name").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(n) => n.to_string(),
        None => return err_response(400, "name required"),
    };

    let password = match v.get("password").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(p) => p.to_string(),
        None => return err_response(400, "password required"),
    };

    let (player, hash) = match db::get_player_by_name(dir(), &name) {
        Ok(Some(pair)) => pair,
        Ok(None) => return err_response(401, "invalid credentials"),
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    };

    if !verify_pw(&password, &hash) {
        return err_response(401, "invalid credentials");
    }

    let token = match create_token(&player.id) {
        Ok(t) => t,
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("token error: {}", e)),
    };

    ok_response(json_obj(vec![
        ("player", player_to_json(&player)),
        ("token", json_str(&token)),
    ]))
}

// GET /api/player/{id} - requires JWT auth
pub fn get_player(req: &Request, params: Params) -> Response {
    require_auth!(req);

    let id = match params.get("id") {
        Some(id) => id.to_string(),
        None => return err_response(400, "missing id"),
    };

    match db::get_player(dir(), &id) {
        Ok(Some(p)) => ok_response(player_to_json(&p)),
        Ok(None) => err_response(404, "player not found"),
        Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    }
}

// GET /api/player/{id}/status - requires JWT auth
pub fn player_status(req: &Request, params: Params) -> Response {
    require_auth!(req);

    let id = match params.get("id") {
        Some(id) => id.to_string(),
        None => return err_response(400, "missing id"),
    };

    let player = match db::get_player(dir(), &id) {
        Ok(Some(p)) => p,
        Ok(None) => return err_response(404, "player not found"),
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    };

    // check if last report is within 30 seconds of now
    let verified = player
        .last_report
        .as_deref()
        .and_then(rfc3339_to_secs)
        .map(|t| now_secs().saturating_sub(t) < 30)
        .unwrap_or(false);

    let expected_hash = match db::get_config(dir(), "expected_config_hash") {
        Ok(h) => h,
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    };

    let config_hash_match = match (&player.config_hash, &expected_hash) {
        (Some(ph), Some(eh)) => ph == eh,
        _ => false,
    };

    ok_response(json_obj(vec![
        ("player_id", json_str(&player.id)),
        ("player_name", json_str(&player.name)),
        ("verified", json_bool(verified)),
        ("is_clean", json_bool(player.is_clean)),
        (
            "last_report",
            player.last_report.as_deref().map(json_str).unwrap_or_else(json_null),
        ),
        ("config_hash_match", json_bool(config_hash_match)),
    ]))
}

// POST /api/report - requires JWT auth, body is full ScanReport JSON
// player_id from JWT, not request body
pub fn receive_report(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    let player_id = require_auth!(req);

    // Per-player rate limit: 1 report per 5 seconds
    if is_rate_limited_report(&player_id) {
        return err_response(429, "too many reports, try again later");
    }

    let v = parse_body!(req);

    // --- Replay protection: nonce check ---
    // Nonce is optional for backwards compatibility; if present it must be
    // unseen in the last 5 minutes.
    let nonce = v.get("nonce").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("");
    if !nonce.is_empty() {
        if is_replay(nonce) {
            return err_response(409, "duplicate report (replay detected)");
        }
        record_nonce(nonce);
    }

    // ignore player_id from body — always use the authenticated identity

    let timestamp = match v.get("timestamp").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(t) => t.to_string(),
        None => secs_to_rfc3339(now_secs()),
    };

    // --- Timestamp window check ---
    // Reject reports whose timestamp deviates more than 60 s from server time.
    // This prevents an attacker from replaying stale reports that lack a nonce.
    if let Some(report_secs) = rfc3339_to_secs(&timestamp) {
        let server_secs = now_secs();
        let drift = (server_secs as i64 - report_secs as i64).unsigned_abs();
        if drift > 60 {
            return err_response(400, "report timestamp too far from server time");
        }
    }

    let config_hash = v
        .get("config_hash")
        .and_then(|x| x.as_str())
        .unwrap_or("")
        .to_string();

    // determine if player is clean from this report
    let suspicious_empty = v
        .get("suspicious_processes")
        .and_then(|x| x.as_array())
        .map(|a| a.is_empty())
        .unwrap_or(true);

    let cheats_empty = v
        .get("cheat_matches")
        .and_then(|x| x.as_array())
        .map(|a| a.is_empty())
        .unwrap_or(true);

    let sandbox_empty = v
        .get("sandbox_detected")
        .and_then(|x| x.as_array())
        .map(|a| a.is_empty())
        .unwrap_or(true);

    let file_ok = v
        .get("file_integrity")
        .and_then(|fi| fi.get("status"))
        .and_then(|x| x.as_str())
        .map(|s| s == "ok")
        .unwrap_or(true);

    let is_clean = suspicious_empty && cheats_empty && sandbox_empty && file_ok;

    // extract new report fields
    let ebpf_active = v.get("ebpf_active").and_then(|x| x.as_bool()).unwrap_or(false);
    let heartbeat_seq = v.get("heartbeat_seq").and_then(|x| x.as_i64()).unwrap_or(0) as u64;
    let mut self_protection_count = v
        .get("self_protection")
        .and_then(|x| x.as_array())
        .map(|a| a.len())
        .unwrap_or(0);
    let clock_drift_ms = v.get("clock_drift_ms").and_then(|x| x.as_i64());

    // config hash match check
    let config_hash_match = match db::get_config(dir(), "expected_config_hash") {
        Ok(Some(expected)) => config_hash == expected,
        _ => true, // no expected hash configured = match
    };

    // client binary hash verification
    let client_hash = v.get("client_hash").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("");
    let client_hash_ok = match db::get_config(dir(), "expected_client_hash") {
        Ok(Some(expected)) => client_hash == expected,
        _ => true,
    };
    if !client_hash_ok {
        self_protection_count += 1;
    }

    // verify challenge response from previous cycle
    let challenge_resp = v.get("challenge_response").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("");
    if let Ok(Some(expected_challenge)) = db::get_config(dir(), &format!("challenge_{}", player_id)) {
        let hostname = v.get("hostname").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("");
        let expected = crate::crypto::sha256_hex(
            format!("{}{}{}{}", expected_challenge, client_hash, hostname, heartbeat_seq).as_bytes(),
        );
        if challenge_resp != expected {
            self_protection_count += 1;
        }
    }

    // compute trust score
    let player = match db::get_player(dir(), &player_id) {
        Ok(Some(p)) => p,
        Ok(None) => return err_response(400, "player not registered"),
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    };

    if player.banned {
        return ok_response(json_obj(vec![
            ("banned", json_bool(true)),
            ("reason", player.ban_reason.as_deref().map(json_str).unwrap_or_else(json_null)),
        ]));
    }

    let report_secs = rfc3339_to_secs(&timestamp).unwrap_or(now_secs());
    let prev_report_secs = player
        .last_report
        .as_deref()
        .and_then(rfc3339_to_secs)
        .unwrap_or(0);

    let trust_input = crate::trust::TrustInput {
        prev_score: player.trust_score,
        prev_heartbeat_seq: player.heartbeat_seq,
        prev_report_secs,
        new_heartbeat_seq: heartbeat_seq,
        new_report_secs: report_secs,
        ebpf_active,
        config_hash_match,
        self_protection_issues: self_protection_count,
        clock_drift_ms,
        cheats_found: !cheats_empty,
        consecutive_clean: player.consecutive_clean,
    };

    let trust_result = crate::trust::compute(&trust_input);

    if trust_result.score <= 20 {
        let _ = db::ban_player(dir(), &player_id, &format!("trust score dropped to {}", trust_result.score));
    }

    match db::update_player_report(
        dir(),
        &player_id,
        &timestamp,
        is_clean,
        &config_hash,
        trust_result.score,
        heartbeat_seq,
        trust_result.consecutive_clean,
    ) {
        Ok(false) => return err_response(400, "player not registered"),
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
        Ok(true) => {}
    }

    // notify player via websocket if trust changed significantly (>= 5 points)
    let trust_delta = (trust_result.score as i16 - player.trust_score as i16).unsigned_abs();
    if trust_delta >= 5 {
        ws::send_to(
            &player_id,
            &stringify(&json_obj(vec![
                ("event", json_str("trust_update")),
                ("trust_score", json_num(trust_result.score as f64)),
                ("previous", json_num(player.trust_score as f64)),
            ])),
        );
    }

    // mark dirty if config hash mismatches
    if !config_hash_match {
        let _ = db::mark_player_dirty(dir(), &player_id);
    }

    // generate new challenge for next cycle
    let new_challenge = crate::crypto::uuid_v4();
    let _ = db::set_config(dir(), &format!("challenge_{}", player_id), &new_challenge);

    // store the raw report
    if let Err(e) = db::insert_report(dir(), &player_id, &timestamp, &req.body) {
        return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e));
    }

    // Record the time this report was accepted for rate limiting future submissions.
    record_report_time(&player_id);

    ok_response(json_obj(vec![
        ("status", json_str("report received")),
        ("trust_score", json_num(trust_result.score as f64)),
        ("challenge", json_str(&new_challenge)),
    ]))
}

// POST /api/match - requires JWT auth, body: {"player_ids":["uuid",..]}
pub fn create_match(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    require_auth!(req);
    let v = parse_body!(req);

    let player_ids: Vec<String> = v
        .get("player_ids")
        .and_then(|x| x.as_array())
        .map(|arr| arr.iter().filter_map(|x| x.as_str()).map(|s| s.to_string()).collect())
        .unwrap_or_default();

    if player_ids.is_empty() {
        return err_response(400, "player_ids required");
    }

    // optional metadata — not required, default to None
    let game = v.get("game").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).map(|s| s.to_string());
    let map = v.get("map").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).map(|s| s.to_string());

    // match gate: check all players
    let threshold = match db::get_config(dir(), "match_trust_threshold") {
        Ok(Some(v)) => v.parse::<u8>().unwrap_or(60),
        _ => 60,
    };

    // require all players have reported in the last 60 seconds
    let now = now_secs();
    let max_report_age = 60;

    let mut rejected = Vec::new();
    for pid in &player_ids {
        match db::get_player(dir(), pid) {
            Ok(Some(p)) => {
                if p.banned {
                    rejected.push(json_obj(vec![
                        ("player_id", json_str(pid)),
                        ("reason", json_str(&format!("player {} is banned", p.name))),
                    ]));
                } else if p.last_report.is_none() || p.last_report.as_deref()
                    .and_then(rfc3339_to_secs)
                    .map(|t| now.saturating_sub(t) > max_report_age)
                    .unwrap_or(true) {
                    rejected.push(json_obj(vec![
                        ("player_id", json_str(pid)),
                        ("reason", json_str(&format!("player {} has no recent report (vigil not running?)", p.name))),
                    ]));
                } else if p.trust_score < threshold {
                    rejected.push(json_obj(vec![
                        ("player_id", json_str(pid)),
                        ("reason", json_str(&format!(
                            "player {} trust score {} below threshold {}",
                            p.name, p.trust_score, threshold
                        ))),
                    ]));
                }
            }
            Ok(None) => {
                rejected.push(json_obj(vec![
                    ("player_id", json_str(pid)),
                    ("reason", json_str("player not found")),
                ]));
            }
            Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
        }
    }

    if !rejected.is_empty() {
        return err_response(400, &stringify(&json_obj(vec![
            ("message", json_str("match rejected")),
            ("failures", json_arr(rejected)),
        ])));
    }

    let id = uuid_v4();
    let now = secs_to_rfc3339(now_secs());

    if let Err(e) = db::insert_match(dir(), &id, &now, &player_ids, game.as_deref(), map.as_deref()) {
        return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e));
    }

    let m = MatchData {
        id,
        created_at: now,
        ended_at: None,
        player_ids,
        game,
        map,
        result: None,
    };

    ok_response(match_to_json(&m))
}

// POST /api/match/end - requires JWT auth, body: {"match_id":"uuid"}
pub fn end_match_handler(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    require_auth!(req);
    let v = parse_body!(req);

    let match_id = match v.get("match_id").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(id) => id.to_string(),
        None => return err_response(400, "match_id required"),
    };

    let now = secs_to_rfc3339(now_secs());

    match db::end_match(dir(), &match_id, &now) {
        Ok(false) => err_response(404, "match not found"),
        Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
        Ok(true) => ok_response(json_str("match ended")),
    }
}

// GET /api/match/{id}/integrity - requires JWT auth
pub fn match_integrity(req: &Request, params: Params) -> Response {
    require_auth!(req);

    let match_id = match params.get("id") {
        Some(id) => id.to_string(),
        None => return err_response(400, "missing id"),
    };

    let m = match db::get_match(dir(), &match_id) {
        Ok(Some(m)) => m,
        Ok(None) => return err_response(404, "match not found"),
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    };

    let start = &m.created_at;
    // use ended_at or current time as end bound
    let end_owned;
    let end: &str = match &m.ended_at {
        Some(t) => t.as_str(),
        None => {
            end_owned = secs_to_rfc3339(now_secs());
            &end_owned
        }
    };

    let mut player_statuses = Vec::new();
    let mut all_clean = true;

    for pid in &m.player_ids {
        let player = match db::get_player(dir(), pid) {
            Ok(Some(p)) => p,
            _ => PlayerData {
                id: pid.clone(),
                name: "unknown".to_string(),
                registered_at: String::new(),
                last_report: None,
                is_clean: false,
                config_hash: None,
                trust_score: 0,
                heartbeat_seq: 0,
                consecutive_clean: 0,
                banned: false,
                banned_at: None,
                ban_reason: None,
            },
        };
        let player_name = player.name.clone();

        let report_jsons = match db::get_reports_in_range(dir(), pid, start, end) {
            Ok(r) => r,
            Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
        };

        let mut violations = Vec::new();
        let mut is_clean = true;

        for raw in &report_jsons {
            if let Ok(r) = parse(raw) {
                // check suspicious_processes
                if let Some(arr) = r.get("suspicious_processes").and_then(|x| x.as_array()) {
                    for sp in arr {
                        let name = sp.get("name").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("unknown");
                        let reason = sp.get("reason").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("");
                        violations.push(json_str(&format!("suspicious process: {} ({})", name, reason)));
                        is_clean = false;
                    }
                }

                // check cheat_matches
                if let Some(arr) = r.get("cheat_matches").and_then(|x| x.as_array()) {
                    for cm in arr {
                        let name = cm.get("name").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("unknown");
                        let cat = cm.get("category").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("");
                        violations.push(json_str(&format!("cheat detected: {} [{}]", name, cat)));
                        is_clean = false;
                    }
                }

                // check sandbox_detected
                if let Some(arr) = r.get("sandbox_detected").and_then(|x| x.as_array())
                    && !arr.is_empty() {
                        let items: Vec<&str> = arr.iter().filter_map(|x| x.as_str()).collect();
                        violations.push(json_str(&format!("sandbox: {:?}", items)));
                        is_clean = false;
                    }

                // check file_integrity
                if let Some(fi) = r.get("file_integrity") {
                    let status = fi.get("status").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("ok");
                    if status != "ok" {
                        let modified = fi.get("modified").and_then(|x| x.as_array()).map(|a| a.len()).unwrap_or(0);
                        let added = fi.get("added").and_then(|x| x.as_array()).map(|a| a.len()).unwrap_or(0);
                        let removed = fi.get("removed").and_then(|x| x.as_array()).map(|a| a.len()).unwrap_or(0);
                        violations.push(json_str(&format!(
                            "file integrity: {} modified, {} added, {} removed",
                            modified, added, removed
                        )));
                        is_clean = false;
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        if player.banned {
            violations.push(json_str("player is banned"));
            is_clean = false;
        }

        if report_jsons.is_empty() {
            violations.push(json_str("no reports received during match"));
            is_clean = false;
        }

        if !is_clean {
            all_clean = false;
        }

        player_statuses.push(json_obj(vec![
            ("player_id", json_str(pid)),
            ("player_name", json_str(&player_name)),
            ("reports_during_match", json_num(report_jsons.len() as f64)),
            ("is_clean", json_bool(is_clean)),
            ("violations", json_arr(violations)),
        ]));
    }

    ok_response(json_obj(vec![
        ("match_id", json_str(&match_id)),
        ("players", json_arr(player_statuses)),
        ("all_clean", json_bool(all_clean)),
    ]))
}

// POST /api/admin/config - requires admin key, body is raw config text
pub fn set_config(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    require_admin!(req);

    let hash = sha256_hex(req.body.as_bytes());

    if let Err(e) = db::set_config(dir(), "expected_config_hash", &hash) {
        return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e));
    }

    ok_response(json_obj(vec![("config_hash", json_str(&hash))]))
}

// GET /api/players - requires admin key
pub fn list_players_handler(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    require_admin!(req);

    let (limit, offset) = parse_pagination(req);
    match db::list_players_paged(dir(), limit, offset) {
        Ok(players) => {
            let arr = json_arr(players.iter().map(player_to_json).collect());
            ok_response(arr)
        }
        Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    }
}

// GET /api/whitelist - auth required, returns whitelist entries for client fetch
pub fn get_whitelist(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    require_auth!(req);

    match db::list_whitelist(dir()) {
        Ok(entries) => {
            let arr = json_arr(
                entries
                    .iter()
                    .map(|e| {
                        json_obj(vec![
                            ("pattern", json_str(&e.pattern)),
                            ("reason", json_str(&e.reason)),
                            ("added_by", json_str(&e.added_by)),
                            ("added_at", json_str(&e.added_at)),
                        ])
                    })
                    .collect(),
            );
            ok_response(arr)
        }
        Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    }
}

// POST /api/admin/whitelist - admin adds entry, body: {"pattern":"..","reason":".."}
pub fn add_whitelist(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    require_admin!(req);
    let v = parse_body!(req);

    let pattern = match v.get("pattern").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(p) if !p.is_empty() => p.to_string(),
        _ => return err_response(400, "pattern required"),
    };

    let reason = v
        .get("reason")
        .and_then(|x| x.as_str())
        .unwrap_or("")
        .to_string();

    let now = secs_to_rfc3339(now_secs());

    if let Err(e) = db::add_whitelist_entry(dir(), &pattern, &reason, "admin", &now) {
        return err_response(400, &e);
    }

    ok_response(json_str("whitelist entry added"))
}

// POST /api/admin/whitelist/remove - admin removes entry, body: {"pattern":".."}
pub fn remove_whitelist(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    require_admin!(req);
    let v = parse_body!(req);

    let pattern = match v.get("pattern").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(p) => p.to_string(),
        None => return err_response(400, "pattern required"),
    };

    match db::remove_whitelist_entry(dir(), &pattern) {
        Ok(true) => ok_response(json_str("whitelist entry removed")),
        Ok(false) => err_response(404, "whitelist entry not found"),
        Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    }
}

// POST /api/admin/ban - body: {"player_id":"..","reason":".."}
pub fn admin_ban(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    require_admin!(req);
    let v = parse_body!(req);

    let player_id = match v.get("player_id").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(id) => id.to_string(),
        None => return err_response(400, "player_id required"),
    };

    let reason = v
        .get("reason")
        .and_then(|x| x.as_str())
        .unwrap_or("banned by admin")
        .to_string();

    match db::ban_player(dir(), &player_id, &reason) {
        Ok(true) => {
            // notify banned player via websocket
            ws::send_to(
                &player_id,
                &stringify(&json_obj(vec![
                    ("event", json_str("banned")),
                    ("reason", json_str(&reason)),
                ])),
            );
            ok_response(json_str("player banned"))
        }
        Ok(false) => err_response(404, "player not found"),
        Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    }
}

// POST /api/admin/unban - body: {"player_id":".."}
pub fn admin_unban(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    require_admin!(req);
    let v = parse_body!(req);

    let player_id = match v.get("player_id").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(id) => id.to_string(),
        None => return err_response(400, "player_id required"),
    };

    match db::unban_player(dir(), &player_id) {
        Ok(true) => ok_response(json_str("player unbanned")),
        Ok(false) => err_response(404, "player not found"),
        Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    }
}

fn party_to_json(p: &PartyData) -> JsonValue {
    json_obj(vec![
        ("id", json_str(&p.id)),
        ("leader", json_str(&p.leader)),
        ("members", json_arr(p.members.iter().map(|s| json_str(s)).collect())),
        ("invited", json_arr(p.invited.iter().map(|s| json_str(s)).collect())),
        ("game", p.game.as_deref().map(json_str).unwrap_or_else(json_null)),
        ("created_at", json_str(&p.created_at)),
    ])
}

// POST /api/friends/add - body: {"friend_name":".."}
pub fn add_friend_handler(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    let player_id = require_auth!(req);
    let v = parse_body!(req);

    let friend_name = match v.get("friend_name").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(n) if !n.is_empty() => n.to_string(),
        _ => return err_response(400, "friend_name required"),
    };

    let (friend, _) = match db::get_player_by_name(dir(), &friend_name) {
        Ok(Some(pair)) => pair,
        Ok(None) => return err_response(404, "player not found"),
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    };

    if friend.id == player_id {
        return err_response(400, "cannot add yourself");
    }

    if let Err(e) = db::add_friend(dir(), &player_id, &friend.id) {
        return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e));
    }

    ok_response(json_str("friend added"))
}

// POST /api/friends/remove - body: {"friend_id":".."}
pub fn remove_friend_handler(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    let player_id = require_auth!(req);
    let v = parse_body!(req);

    let friend_id = match v.get("friend_id").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(id) if !id.is_empty() => id.to_string(),
        _ => return err_response(400, "friend_id required"),
    };

    if let Err(e) = db::remove_friend(dir(), &player_id, &friend_id) {
        return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e));
    }

    ok_response(json_str("friend removed"))
}

// GET /api/friends - returns friends with player data
pub fn list_friends_handler(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    let player_id = require_auth!(req);

    let (limit, offset) = parse_pagination(req);
    let friend_ids = match db::get_friends_paged(dir(), &player_id, limit, offset) {
        Ok(f) => f,
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    };

    let mut friends = Vec::new();
    for fid in &friend_ids {
        match db::get_player(dir(), fid) {
            Ok(Some(p)) => friends.push(player_to_json(&p)),
            Ok(None) => {}
            Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
        }
    }

    ok_response(json_arr(friends))
}

// POST /api/party/create
pub fn create_party_handler(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    let player_id = require_auth!(req);

    // check player is not already in a party
    match db::get_player_party(dir(), &player_id) {
        Ok(Some(_)) => return err_response(400, "already in a party"),
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
        Ok(None) => {}
    }

    match db::create_party(dir(), &player_id) {
        Ok(id) => {
            match db::get_party(dir(), &id) {
                Ok(Some(p)) => ok_response(party_to_json(&p)),
                Ok(None) => err_response(500, "party created but not found"),
                Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
            }
        }
        Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    }
}

// POST /api/party/invite - body: {"player_id":".."}
pub fn invite_party_handler(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    let player_id = require_auth!(req);
    let v = parse_body!(req);

    let invite_id = match v.get("player_id").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(id) if !id.is_empty() => id.to_string(),
        _ => return err_response(400, "player_id required"),
    };

    let party = match db::get_player_party(dir(), &player_id) {
        Ok(Some(p)) => p,
        Ok(None) => return err_response(400, "not in a party"),
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    };

    if party.leader != player_id {
        return err_response(403, "only leader can invite");
    }

    if let Err(e) = db::invite_to_party(dir(), &party.id, &invite_id) {
        return err_response(400, &e);
    }

    // notify invited player via websocket
    ws::send_to(
        &invite_id,
        &stringify(&json_obj(vec![
            ("event", json_str("party_invite")),
            ("party_id", json_str(&party.id)),
            ("invited_by", json_str(&player_id)),
        ])),
    );

    ok_response(json_str("player invited"))
}

// POST /api/party/join - body: {"party_id":".."}
pub fn join_party_handler(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    let player_id = require_auth!(req);
    let v = parse_body!(req);

    let party_id = match v.get("party_id").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(id) if !id.is_empty() => id.to_string(),
        _ => return err_response(400, "party_id required"),
    };

    if let Err(e) = db::join_party(dir(), &party_id, &player_id) {
        return err_response(400, &e);
    }

    match db::get_party(dir(), &party_id) {
        Ok(Some(p)) => ok_response(party_to_json(&p)),
        Ok(None) => err_response(404, "party not found"),
        Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    }
}

    let player_id = require_auth!(req);

    let party = match db::get_player_party(dir(), &player_id) {
        Ok(Some(p)) => p,
        Ok(None) => return err_response(400, "not in a party"),
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    };

    if let Err(e) = db::leave_party(dir(), &party.id, &player_id) {
        return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e));
    }

    ok_response(json_str("left party"))
}

        Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    }
}

// POST /api/queue/join - body: {"game":"cs2","party_id":".."}
pub fn join_queue_handler(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    let player_id = require_auth!(req);
    let v = parse_body!(req);

    let game = match v.get("game").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(g) if !g.is_empty() => g.to_string(),
        _ => return err_response(400, "game required"),
    };

    let party_id = v.get("party_id").and_then(|x| x.as_str());

    if let Err(e) = db::join_queue(dir(), &player_id, party_id, &game) {
        return err_response(400, &e);
    }

    // try to form a match (default 10 players, configurable via match_size)
    let match_size = match db::get_config(dir(), "match_size") {
        Ok(Some(v)) => v.parse::<usize>().unwrap_or(10),
        _ => 10,
    };

    if let Ok(Some((match_id, matched_players))) = db::try_matchmake(dir(), &game, match_size) {
        // notify all matched players via websocket
        let msg = stringify(&json_obj(vec![
            ("event", json_str("match_found")),
            ("match_id", json_str(&match_id)),
        ]));
        for pid in &matched_players {
            ws::send_to(pid, &msg);
        }

        return ok_response(json_obj(vec![
            ("status", json_str("match_found")),
            ("match_id", json_str(&match_id)),
        ]));
    }

    ok_response(json_str("joined queue"))
}

// POST /api/queue/leave
pub fn leave_queue_handler(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    let player_id = require_auth!(req);

    if let Err(e) = db::leave_queue(dir(), &player_id) {
        return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e));
    }

    ok_response(json_str("left queue"))
}

// GET /api/queue/status
pub fn queue_status_handler(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    let player_id = require_auth!(req);

    let (limit, offset) = parse_pagination(req);
    let queue = match db::get_queue_paged(dir(), limit, offset) {
        Ok(q) => q,
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    };

    let position = match db::get_queue_position(dir(), &player_id) {
        Ok(p) => p,
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    };

    ok_response(json_obj(vec![
        ("total", json_num(queue.len() as f64)),
        ("position", position.map(|p| json_num(p as f64)).unwrap_or_else(json_null)),
    ]))
}

// POST /api/servers/register - body: {"name":"..","address":"..","game":"..","max_players":16}
pub fn register_server_handler(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    require_auth!(req);
    let v = parse_body!(req);

    let name = match v.get("name").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(n) if !n.is_empty() => n.to_string(),
        _ => return err_response(400, "name required"),
    };

    let address = match v.get("address").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(a) if !a.is_empty() => a.to_string(),
        _ => return err_response(400, "address required"),
    };

    let game = match v.get("game").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(g) if !g.is_empty() => g.to_string(),
        _ => return err_response(400, "game required"),
    };

    let max_players = v.get("max_players").and_then(|x| x.as_i64()).unwrap_or(16) as u32;

    match db::register_server(dir(), &name, &address, &game, max_players) {
        Ok(id) => ok_response(json_obj(vec![
            ("id", json_str(&id)),
            ("name", json_str(&name)),
            ("address", json_str(&address)),
            ("game", json_str(&game)),
            ("max_players", json_num(max_players as f64)),
        ])),
        Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    }
}

// GET /api/servers
pub fn list_servers_handler(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    require_auth!(req);

    let (limit, offset) = parse_pagination(req);

    // count active players: players in matches that have not yet ended
    let current_players = db::count_active_players(dir()).unwrap_or(0);

    match db::list_servers_paged(dir(), limit, offset) {
        Ok(servers) => {
            let arr = json_arr(servers.iter().map(|s| {
                // distribute active players across servers proportionally for now —
                // since matches have no server_id linkage, we report the global
                // active player count on every server entry so the GUI shows a
                // non-zero number rather than hardcoded 0
                json_obj(vec![
                    ("id", json_str(&s.id)),
                    ("name", json_str(&s.name)),
                    ("address", json_str(&s.address)),
                    ("game", json_str(&s.game)),
                    ("max_players", json_num(s.max_players as f64)),
                    ("current_players", json_num(current_players.min(s.max_players) as f64)),
                    ("created_at", json_str(&s.created_at)),
                ])
            }).collect());
            ok_response(arr)
        }
        Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    }
}

// GET /api/player/{id}/profile - compose from existing data
pub fn player_profile_handler(req: &Request, params: Params) -> Response {
    require_auth!(req);

    let id = match params.get("id") {
        Some(id) => id.to_string(),
        None => return err_response(400, "missing id"),
    };

    let player = match db::get_player(dir(), &id) {
        Ok(Some(p)) => p,
        Ok(None) => return err_response(404, "player not found"),
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    };

    let match_count = match db::count_player_matches(dir(), &id) {
        Ok(c) => c as usize,
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    };

    let friends = match db::get_friends(dir(), &id) {
        Ok(f) => f,
        Err(e) => return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    };

    ok_response(json_obj(vec![
        ("player", player_to_json(&player)),
        ("match_count", json_num(match_count as f64)),
        ("friend_count", json_num(friends.len() as f64)),
    ]))
}

// GET /api/player/{id}/matches - filter matches containing player
pub fn player_matches_handler(req: &Request, params: Params) -> Response {
    require_auth!(req);

    let id = match params.get("id") {
        Some(id) => id.to_string(),
        None => return err_response(400, "missing id"),
    };

    let (limit, offset) = parse_pagination(req);
    match db::get_player_matches(dir(), &id, limit, offset) {
        Ok(matches) => {
            let arr = json_arr(matches.iter().map(match_to_json).collect());
            ok_response(arr)
        }
        Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    }
}

// POST /api/admin/appeal/resolve - body: {"appeal_id":"..","status":"accepted|rejected"}
pub fn resolve_appeal_handler(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    require_admin!(req);
    let v = parse_body!(req);

    let appeal_id = match v.get("appeal_id").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(id) => id.to_string(),
        None => return err_response(400, "appeal_id required"),
    };

    let status = match v.get("status").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
        Some(s) if s == "accepted" || s == "rejected" => s.to_string(),
        _ => return err_response(400, "status must be accepted or rejected"),
    };

    if status == "accepted"
        && let Ok(appeals) = db::list_appeals(dir())
        && let Some(a) = appeals.iter().find(|a| a.id == appeal_id)
    {
        let _ = db::unban_player(dir(), &a.player_id);
    }

    match db::resolve_appeal(dir(), &appeal_id, &status) {
        Ok(true) => ok_response(json_str("appeal resolved")),
        Ok(false) => err_response(404, "appeal not found"),
        Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    }
}

// GET /api/cheat-signatures - auth required, returns cheat signature text for client fetch
pub fn get_cheat_signatures(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    require_auth!(req);

    match db::get_config(dir(), "cheat_signatures") {
        Ok(Some(sigs)) => ok_response(json_str(&sigs)),
        Ok(None) => ok_response(json_str("")),
        Err(e) => err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e)),
    }
}

// POST /api/admin/cheat-signatures - admin sets cheat signatures
// body: raw text in hash:name:category:description format, one per line
pub fn set_cheat_signatures(req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
    require_admin!(req);

    // body can be raw text or {"signatures":"..."}
    let text = if let Ok(v) = parse(&req.body)
        && let Some(s) = v.get("signatures").and_then(|x| x.as_str())
    {
        s.to_string()
    } else {
        req.body.clone()
    };

    if let Err(e) = db::set_config(dir(), "cheat_signatures", &text) {
        return err_response(500, &format!("db error: {}", e));
    }

    // count entries for feedback
    let count = text.lines().filter(|l| !l.trim().is_empty() && !l.starts_with('#')).count();
    ok_response(json_obj(vec![
        ("stored", json_num(count as f64)),
    ]))
}
```

`crates/vigil-server/src/http.rs`:

```rs
use std::io::{BufRead, BufReader, Read, Write};
use std::net::TcpStream;
use std::time::Duration;

pub struct Request {
    pub method: String,
    pub path: String,
    pub headers: Vec<(String, String)>,
    pub body: String,
}

pub struct Response {
    pub status: u16,
    pub status_text: String,
    pub headers: Vec<(String, String)>,
    pub body: String,
    pub body_raw: Option<Vec<u8>>,
}

impl Request {
    // reads and parses an HTTP/1.1 request from a tcp stream
    // sets a 5 second read timeout so we dont hang on slow clients
    pub fn parse(stream: &mut TcpStream) -> Result<Request, String> {
        stream
            .set_read_timeout(Some(Duration::from_secs(5)))
            .map_err(|e| format!("timeout setup failed: {}", e))?;

        let mut reader = BufReader::new(stream);

        // read request line: GET /path HTTP/1.1
        let mut req_line = String::new();
        reader
            .read_line(&mut req_line)
            .map_err(|e| format!("failed to read request line: {}", e))?;

        let req_line = req_line.trim();
        if req_line.is_empty() {
            return Err("empty request line".to_string());
        }

        let parts: Vec<&str> = req_line.splitn(3, ' ').collect();
        if parts.len() < 3 {
            return Err(format!("malformed request line: {}", req_line));
        }

        let method = parts[0].to_string();
        let path = parts[1].to_string();
        // parts[2] is HTTP/1.1, we dont care about the version

        // read headers until empty line
        let mut headers = Vec::new();
        let mut header_count = 0usize;
        loop {
            let mut line = String::new();
            reader
                .read_line(&mut line)
                .map_err(|e| format!("failed to read header: {}", e))?;

            // #8: reject oversized header lines
            if line.len() > 8192 {
                return Err("header line too long (max 8192 bytes)".to_string());
            }

            let trimmed = line.trim();
            if trimmed.is_empty() {
                break;
            }

            // #8: reject requests with too many headers
            header_count += 1;
            if header_count > 100 {
                return Err("too many headers (max 100)".to_string());
            }

            // split on first colon
            if let Some(pos) = trimmed.find(':') {
                let key = trimmed[..pos].trim().to_string();
                let val = trimmed[pos + 1..].trim().to_string();

                // #7: reject transfer-encoding to prevent HTTP request smuggling
                if key.eq_ignore_ascii_case("transfer-encoding") {
                    return Err("transfer-encoding not supported".to_string());
                }

                headers.push((key, val));
            }
        }

        // read body if content-length is present
        let mut body = String::new();
        let content_len = headers
            .iter()
            .find(|(k, _)| k.eq_ignore_ascii_case("content-length"))
            .and_then(|(_, v)| v.parse::<usize>().ok())
            .unwrap_or(0);

        // reject payloads over 1MB
        if content_len > 1_048_576 {
            return Err("request body too large (max 1MB)".to_string());
        }

        if content_len > 0 {
            let mut buf = vec![0u8; content_len];
            reader
                .read_exact(&mut buf)
                .map_err(|e| format!("failed to read body: {}", e))?;
            body = String::from_utf8(buf).map_err(|e| format!("body not utf8: {}", e))?;
        }

        Ok(Request {
            method,
            path,
            headers,
            body,
        })
    }

    // case-insensitive header lookup
    pub fn get_header(&self, name: &str) -> Option<&str> {
        self.headers
            .iter()
            .find(|(k, _)| k.eq_ignore_ascii_case(name))
            .map(|(_, v)| v.as_str())
    }
}

impl Response {
    // creates a response with the right status text for common codes
    pub fn new(status: u16) -> Response {
        let status_text = match status {
            200 => "OK",
            201 => "Created",
            204 => "No Content",
            400 => "Bad Request",
            401 => "Unauthorized",
            403 => "Forbidden",
            404 => "Not Found",
            405 => "Method Not Allowed",
            500 => "Internal Server Error",
            _ => "Unknown",
        }
        .to_string();

        Response {
            status,
            status_text,
            headers: Vec::new(),
            body: String::new(),
            body_raw: None,
        }
    }

    // builder - add a header
    pub fn header(mut self, key: &str, val: &str) -> Self {
        self.headers.push((key.to_string(), val.to_string()));
        self
    }

    // builder - set the body
    pub fn body(mut self, body: String) -> Self {
        self.body = body;
        self
    }

    // builder - set raw binary body (use for binary files to avoid UTF-8 corruption)
    pub fn body_bytes(mut self, bytes: Vec<u8>) -> Self {
        self.body_raw = Some(bytes);
        self
    }

    // shortcut for a 200 json response
    pub fn json(body: String) -> Response {
        Response::new(200)
            .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
            .body(body)
    }

    // writes the full http response to the stream
    pub fn write_to(&self, stream: &mut TcpStream) -> std::io::Result<()> {
        // status line
        let mut out = format!("HTTP/1.1 {} {}\r\n", self.status, self.status_text);

        // collect headers, add content-length if body is present
        for (k, v) in &self.headers {
            out.push_str(&format!("{}: {}\r\n", k, v));
        }

        // always send content-length so the client knows when to stop reading
        let has_cl = self
            .headers
            .iter()
            .any(|(k, _)| k.eq_ignore_ascii_case("content-length"));
        if !has_cl {
            let len = if let Some(raw) = &self.body_raw {
                raw.len()
            } else {
                self.body.len()
            };
            out.push_str(&format!("Content-Length: {}\r\n", len));
        }

        // end of headers
        out.push_str("\r\n");

        // write headers, then body - keep raw bytes separate to avoid UTF-8 corruption
        stream.write_all(out.as_bytes())?;
        if let Some(raw) = &self.body_raw {
            stream.write_all(raw)?;
        } else {
            stream.write_all(self.body.as_bytes())?;
        }
        stream.flush()
    }
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn response_new_200_ok() {
        let r = Response::new(200);
        assert_eq!(r.status, 200);
        assert_eq!(r.status_text, "OK");
        assert!(r.headers.is_empty());
        assert!(r.body.is_empty());
    }

    #[test]
    fn response_new_201_created() {
        let r = Response::new(201);
        assert_eq!(r.status_text, "Created");
    }

    #[test]
    fn response_new_204_no_content() {
        let r = Response::new(204);
        assert_eq!(r.status_text, "No Content");
    }

    #[test]
    fn response_new_400_bad_request() {
        let r = Response::new(400);
        assert_eq!(r.status_text, "Bad Request");
    }

    #[test]
    fn response_new_401_unauthorized() {
        let r = Response::new(401);
        assert_eq!(r.status_text, "Unauthorized");
    }

    #[test]
    fn response_new_403_forbidden() {
        let r = Response::new(403);
        assert_eq!(r.status_text, "Forbidden");
    }

    #[test]
    fn response_new_404_not_found() {
        let r = Response::new(404);
        assert_eq!(r.status_text, "Not Found");
    }

    #[test]
    fn response_new_405_method_not_allowed() {
        let r = Response::new(405);
        assert_eq!(r.status_text, "Method Not Allowed");
    }

    #[test]
    fn response_new_500_internal_server_error() {
        let r = Response::new(500);
        assert_eq!(r.status_text, "Internal Server Error");
    }

    #[test]
    fn response_new_unknown_status() {
        let r = Response::new(418);
        assert_eq!(r.status_text, "Unknown");
    }

    #[test]
    fn response_json_sets_content_type_and_status() {
        let r = Response::json(r#"{"ok":true}"#.to_string());
        assert_eq!(r.status, 200);
        assert_eq!(r.status_text, "OK");
        assert_eq!(r.body, r#"{"ok":true}"#);

        let ct = r.headers.iter().find(|(k, _)| k == "Content-Type");
        assert!(ct.is_some());
        assert_eq!(ct.unwrap().1, "application/json");
    }

    #[test]
    fn response_header_builder_adds_headers() {
        let r = Response::new(200)
            .header("X-Custom", "value1")
            .header("X-Other", "value2");

        assert_eq!(r.headers.len(), 2);
        assert_eq!(r.headers[0], ("X-Custom".to_string(), "value1".to_string()));
        assert_eq!(r.headers[1], ("X-Other".to_string(), "value2".to_string()));
    }

    #[test]
    fn response_body_builder_sets_body() {
        let r = Response::new(200).body("hello world".to_string());
        assert_eq!(r.body, "hello world");
    }

    #[test]
    fn response_full_builder_chain() {
        let r = Response::new(201)
            .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
            .header("X-Request-Id", "abc")
            .body(r#"{"id":"abc"}"#.to_string());

        assert_eq!(r.status, 201);
        assert_eq!(r.status_text, "Created");
        assert_eq!(r.headers.len(), 2);
        assert_eq!(r.body, r#"{"id":"abc"}"#);
    }

    #[test]
    fn request_get_header_case_insensitive() {
        let req = Request {
            method: "GET".to_string(),
            path: "/test".to_string(),
            headers: vec![
                ("Content-Type".to_string(), "application/json".to_string()),
                ("Authorization".to_string(), "Bearer tok123".to_string()),
            ],
            body: String::new(),
        };

        assert_eq!(req.get_header("content-type"), Some("application/json"));
        assert_eq!(req.get_header("CONTENT-TYPE"), Some("application/json"));
        assert_eq!(req.get_header("Content-Type"), Some("application/json"));
        assert_eq!(req.get_header("authorization"), Some("Bearer tok123"));
        assert_eq!(req.get_header("X-Missing"), None);
    }

    #[test]
    fn request_get_header_returns_none_when_empty() {
        let req = Request {
            method: "GET".to_string(),
            path: "/".to_string(),
            headers: vec![],
            body: String::new(),
        };
        assert_eq!(req.get_header("Anything"), None);
    }
}
```

```rs
use vigil_server::{db, handlers, router, ws};

fn main() {
    let data_dir = std::env::var("VIGIL_DATA").unwrap_or_else(|_| "data".to_string());

    db::init_db(&data_dir);
    handlers::init(&data_dir);
    handlers::init_nonces();
    ws::init();

    let mut r = router::Router::new();

    // public routes
    r.get("/api/health", handlers::health);
    r.post("/api/player/register", handlers::register);
    r.post("/api/player/login", handlers::login);

    // auth routes
    r.get("/api/player/{id}", handlers::get_player);
    r.get("/api/player/{id}/status", handlers::player_status);
    r.post("/api/report", handlers::receive_report);
    r.post("/api/match", handlers::create_match);
    r.post("/api/match/end", handlers::end_match_handler);
    r.get("/api/match/{id}/integrity", handlers::match_integrity);

    // whitelist routes
    r.get("/api/whitelist", handlers::get_whitelist);
    r.post("/api/admin/whitelist", handlers::add_whitelist);
    r.post("/api/admin/whitelist/remove", handlers::remove_whitelist);

    // friends routes
    r.post("/api/friends/add", handlers::add_friend_handler);
    r.post("/api/friends/remove", handlers::remove_friend_handler);
    r.get("/api/friends", handlers::list_friends_handler);

    // party routes
    r.post("/api/party/create", handlers::create_party_handler);
    r.post("/api/party/invite", handlers::invite_party_handler);
    r.post("/api/party/join", handlers::join_party_handler);
    r.post("/api/party/leave", handlers::leave_party_handler);
    r.get("/api/party", handlers::get_party_handler);

    // queue routes
    r.post("/api/queue/join", handlers::join_queue_handler);
    r.post("/api/queue/leave", handlers::leave_queue_handler);
    r.get("/api/queue/status", handlers::queue_status_handler);

    // server browser routes
    r.post("/api/servers/register", handlers::register_server_handler);
    r.get("/api/servers", handlers::list_servers_handler);

    // profile & history routes
    r.get("/api/player/{id}/profile", handlers::player_profile_handler);
    r.get("/api/player/{id}/matches", handlers::player_matches_handler);

    // admin routes
    r.post("/api/admin/config", handlers::set_config);
    r.post("/api/admin/ban", handlers::admin_ban);
    r.post("/api/admin/unban", handlers::admin_unban);
    r.get("/api/players", handlers::list_players_handler);
    r.get("/api/matches", handlers::list_matches_handler);

    // appeal routes
    r.post("/api/appeal", handlers::submit_appeal_handler);
    r.get("/api/admin/appeals", handlers::list_appeals_handler);
    r.post("/api/admin/appeal/resolve", handlers::resolve_appeal_handler);

    // cheat signature routes
    r.get("/api/cheat-signatures", handlers::get_cheat_signatures);
    r.post("/api/admin/cheat-signatures", handlers::set_cheat_signatures);

    let addr = std::env::var("VIGIL_ADDR").unwrap_or_else(|_| "0.0.0.0:3000".to_string());

    router::serve(&addr, r);
}
```
