`crates/vigil-server/src/router.rs`:

```rs
use std::collections::HashMap;
use std::fs;
use std::net::TcpListener;
use std::sync::atomic::{AtomicBool, AtomicUsize, Ordering};
use std::sync::{Arc, Mutex};
use std::thread;
use std::time::{Instant, Duration};

static RUNNING: AtomicBool = AtomicBool::new(true);
// counts connections currently being handled by worker threads
static ACTIVE_CONNECTIONS: AtomicUsize = AtomicUsize::new(0);

unsafe extern "C" fn handle_signal(_sig: i32) {
    RUNNING.store(false, Ordering::SeqCst);
}

fn setup_signals() {
    unsafe extern "C" {
        fn signal(sig: i32, handler: usize) -> usize;
    }
    unsafe {
        signal(2, handle_signal as *const () as usize);  // SIGINT
        signal(15, handle_signal as *const () as usize); // SIGTERM
    }
}

use crate::http::{Request, Response};

// tracks request timestamps per IP for rate limiting
struct RateLimiter {
    requests: Mutex<HashMap<String, Vec<Instant>>>,
}

impl RateLimiter {
    fn new() -> Self {
        RateLimiter {
            requests: Mutex::new(HashMap::new()),
        }
    }

    // returns true if request is allowed, false if rate limited
    // max_requests per window duration
    fn check(&self, ip: &str, max_requests: usize, window: Duration) -> bool {
        let mut map = self.requests.lock().unwrap();
        let now = Instant::now();

        // purge stale IPs every 100 checks
        if map.len() > 100 {
            map.retain(|_, timestamps| {
                timestamps.retain(|t| now.duration_since(*t) < window);
                !timestamps.is_empty()
            });
        }

        let entries = map.entry(ip.to_string()).or_default();
        entries.retain(|t| now.duration_since(*t) < window);

        if entries.len() >= max_requests {
            return false;
        }

        entries.push(now);
        true
    }
}

// handler function signature - takes a request and extracted path params
pub type Handler = fn(&Request, Params) -> Response;

// extracted path parameters from url matching
#[derive(Default)]
pub struct Params {
    pairs: Vec<(String, String)>,
}

impl Params {
    pub fn new() -> Self { Self::default() }

    pub fn from_pairs(pairs: Vec<(String, String)>) -> Self {
        Params { pairs }
    }

    pub fn get(&self, key: &str) -> Option<&str> {
        self.pairs
            .iter()
            .find(|(k, _)| k == key)
            .map(|(_, v)| v.as_str())
    }
}

// a registered route with its parsed path segments
struct Route {
    method: String,
    segments: Vec<Segment>,
    handler: Handler,
}

// a path segment is either a literal match or a named param capture
enum Segment {
    Literal(String),
    Param(String),
}

#[derive(Default)]
pub struct Router {
    routes: Vec<Route>,
}

impl Router {
    pub fn new() -> Self { Self::default() }

    // register a GET route
    pub fn get(&mut self, path: &str, handler: Handler) {
        self.add("GET", path, handler);
    }

    // register a POST route
    pub fn post(&mut self, path: &str, handler: Handler) {
        self.add("POST", path, handler);
    }

    // parses the path into segments and stores the route
    fn add(&mut self, method: &str, path: &str, handler: Handler) {
        let segments = parse_segments(path);
        self.routes.push(Route {
            method: method.to_string(),
            segments,
            handler,
        });
    }

    // finds the matching route for a method+path, returns handler and extracted params
    pub fn resolve(&self, method: &str, path: &str) -> Option<(Handler, Params)> {
        let parts: Vec<&str> = path.split('/').filter(|s| !s.is_empty()).collect();

        for route in &self.routes {
            if !route.method.eq_ignore_ascii_case(method) {
                continue;
            }

            if route.segments.len() != parts.len() {
                continue;
            }

            let mut pairs = Vec::new();
            let mut matched = true;

            for (seg, part) in route.segments.iter().zip(parts.iter()) {
                match seg {
                    Segment::Literal(lit) => {
                        if lit != part {
                            matched = false;
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                    Segment::Param(name) => {
                        pairs.push((name.clone(), part.to_string()));
                    }
                }
            }

            if matched {
                return Some((route.handler, Params { pairs }));
            }
        }

        None
    }
}

// parses "/api/player/{id}" into [Literal("api"), Literal("player"), Param("id")]
fn parse_segments(path: &str) -> Vec<Segment> {
    path.split('/')
        .filter(|s| !s.is_empty())
        .map(|s| {
            if s.starts_with('{') && s.ends_with('}') {
                Segment::Param(s[1..s.len() - 1].to_string())
            } else {
                Segment::Literal(s.to_string())
            }
        })
        .collect()
}

// adds cors headers to every response
// VIGIL_CORS_ORIGIN must be set explicitly - no wildcard default
fn add_cors(res: &mut Response) {
    let origin = std::env::var("VIGIL_CORS_ORIGIN").unwrap_or_default();
    if origin.is_empty() {
        return;
    }
    res.headers
        .push(("Access-Control-Allow-Origin".to_string(), origin));
    res.headers.push((
        "Access-Control-Allow-Methods".to_string(),
        "GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, OPTIONS".to_string(),
    ));
    res.headers.push((
        "Access-Control-Allow-Headers".to_string(),
        "Content-Type, Authorization, X-Admin-Key".to_string(),
    ));
}

// serves a static file from the public/ directory
// paths without a file extension get index.html (SPA support)
fn serve_static(path: &str) -> Response {
    // filter path segments to prevent traversal (....// → ../ bypass)
    let segments: Vec<&str> = path
        .split('/')
        .filter(|s| !s.is_empty() && *s != "." && *s != "..")
        .collect();
    let clean = segments.join("/");

    // pick the filesystem path
    let fs_path = if clean.is_empty() || !clean.contains('.') {
        "public/index.html".to_string()
    } else {
        format!("public/{}", clean)
    };

    // canonicalize and verify the resolved path is inside public/
    let public_dir = match std::fs::canonicalize("public") {
        Ok(p) => p,
        Err(_) => {
            return Response::new(404)
                .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
                .body("{\"error\":\"not found\"}".to_string());
        }
    };

    let resolved = match std::fs::canonicalize(&fs_path) {
        Ok(p) => p,
        Err(_) => {
            // fallback to index.html for SPA deep links
            match fs::read("public/index.html") {
                Ok(b) => {
                    return Response::new(200)
                        .header("Content-Type", "text/html")
                        .body_bytes(b);
                }
                Err(_) => {
                    return Response::new(404)
                        .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
                        .body("{\"error\":\"not found\"}".to_string());
                }
            }
        }
    };

    if !resolved.starts_with(&public_dir) {
        return Response::new(403)
            .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
            .body("{\"error\":\"forbidden\"}".to_string());
    }

    let content = match fs::read(&fs_path) {
        Ok(b) => b,
        Err(_) => {
            return Response::new(404)
                .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
                .body("{\"error\":\"not found\"}".to_string());
        }
    };

    let content_type = mime_type(&fs_path);

    Response::new(200)
        .header("Content-Type", content_type)
        .body_bytes(content)
}

// returns content-type based on file extension
fn mime_type(path: &str) -> &'static str {
    if path.ends_with(".html") {
        "text/html; charset=utf-8"
    } else if path.ends_with(".js") {
        "application/javascript"
    } else if path.ends_with(".css") {
        "text/css"
    } else if path.ends_with(".json") {
        "application/json"
    } else if path.ends_with(".png") {
        "image/png"
    } else if path.ends_with(".svg") {
        "image/svg+xml"
    } else if path.ends_with(".ico") {
        "image/x-icon"
    } else if path.ends_with(".woff2") {
        "font/woff2"
    } else if path.ends_with(".woff") {
        "font/woff"
    } else {
        "application/octet-stream"
    }
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;
    use crate::http::{Request, Response};

    // dummy handlers for testing
    fn handler_a(_req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
        Response::new(200).body("handler_a".to_string())
    }

    fn handler_b(_req: &Request, _params: Params) -> Response {
        Response::new(200).body("handler_b".to_string())
    }

    fn handler_c(_req: &Request, params: Params) -> Response {
        let id = params.get("id").unwrap_or("none");
        Response::new(200).body(format!("id={}", id))
    }

    #[test]
    fn resolve_matches_exact_get_path() {
        let mut router = Router::new();
        router.get("/api/health", handler_a);

        let result = router.resolve("GET", "/api/health");
        assert!(result.is_some());
        let (handler, _params) = result.unwrap();
        let req = Request {
            method: "GET".to_string(),
            path: "/api/health".to_string(),
            headers: vec![],
            body: String::new(),
        };
        let resp = handler(&req, Params { pairs: vec![] });
        assert_eq!(resp.body, "handler_a");
    }

    #[test]
    fn resolve_matches_exact_post_path() {
        let mut router = Router::new();
        router.post("/api/report", handler_b);

        let result = router.resolve("POST", "/api/report");
        assert!(result.is_some());
    }

    #[test]
    fn resolve_distinguishes_get_from_post() {
        let mut router = Router::new();
        router.get("/api/data", handler_a);
        router.post("/api/data", handler_b);

        // GET should match handler_a
        let (handler, _) = router.resolve("GET", "/api/data").unwrap();
        let req = Request {
            method: "GET".to_string(),
            path: "/api/data".to_string(),
            headers: vec![],
            body: String::new(),
        };
        let resp = handler(&req, Params { pairs: vec![] });
        assert_eq!(resp.body, "handler_a");

        // POST should match handler_b
        let (handler, _) = router.resolve("POST", "/api/data").unwrap();
        let resp = handler(&req, Params { pairs: vec![] });
        assert_eq!(resp.body, "handler_b");
    }

    #[test]
    fn resolve_extracts_single_path_param() {
        let mut router = Router::new();
        router.get("/api/player/{id}", handler_c);

        let (_, params) = router.resolve("GET", "/api/player/abc-123").unwrap();
        assert_eq!(params.get("id"), Some("abc-123"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn resolve_extracts_multiple_path_params() {
        let mut router = Router::new();
        router.get("/api/{resource}/{id}", handler_a);

        let (_, params) = router.resolve("GET", "/api/player/42").unwrap();
        assert_eq!(params.get("resource"), Some("player"));
        assert_eq!(params.get("id"), Some("42"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn resolve_param_at_different_positions() {
        let mut router = Router::new();
        router.get("/api/match/{id}/integrity", handler_a);

        let (_, params) = router.resolve("GET", "/api/match/m-001/integrity").unwrap();
        assert_eq!(params.get("id"), Some("m-001"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn resolve_returns_none_for_unregistered_path() {
        let mut router = Router::new();
        router.get("/api/health", handler_a);

        assert!(router.resolve("GET", "/api/nonexistent").is_none());
    }

    #[test]
    fn resolve_returns_none_for_wrong_method() {
        let mut router = Router::new();
        router.get("/api/health", handler_a);

        assert!(router.resolve("POST", "/api/health").is_none());
        assert!(router.resolve("DELETE", "/api/health").is_none());
    }

    #[test]
    fn resolve_returns_none_for_wrong_segment_count() {
        let mut router = Router::new();
        router.get("/api/player/{id}", handler_a);

        // too few segments
        assert!(router.resolve("GET", "/api/player").is_none());
        // too many segments
        assert!(router.resolve("GET", "/api/player/123/extra").is_none());
    }

    #[test]
    fn resolve_returns_none_for_partial_literal_mismatch() {
        let mut router = Router::new();
        router.get("/api/player/{id}", handler_a);

        // "players" != "player"
        assert!(router.resolve("GET", "/api/players/123").is_none());
    }

    #[test]
    fn resolve_method_is_case_insensitive() {
        let mut router = Router::new();
        router.get("/api/health", handler_a);

        assert!(router.resolve("get", "/api/health").is_some());
        assert!(router.resolve("Get", "/api/health").is_some());
    }

    #[test]
    fn params_get_returns_none_for_missing_key() {
        let params = Params { pairs: vec![("id".to_string(), "42".to_string())] };
        assert_eq!(params.get("id"), Some("42"));
        assert_eq!(params.get("name"), None);
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_segments_handles_empty_and_root() {
        let router = Router::new();
        // empty router should return None for root path
        assert!(router.resolve("GET", "/").is_none());
    }
}

// starts the server - binds to addr, spawns a thread pool, dispatches requests
pub fn serve(addr: &str, router: Router) {
    setup_signals();
    let listener = TcpListener::bind(addr).expect("failed to bind");
    listener.set_nonblocking(true).expect("failed to set nonblocking");
    println!("vigil server listening on {}", addr);

    let router = Arc::new(router);
    let limiter = Arc::new(RateLimiter::new());

    let thread_count: usize = std::env::var("VIGIL_THREADS")
        .ok()
        .and_then(|v| v.parse().ok())
        .unwrap_or(8);

    let (tx, rx) = std::sync::mpsc::channel::<std::net::TcpStream>();
    let rx = Arc::new(std::sync::Mutex::new(rx));

    for _ in 0..thread_count {
        let rx = Arc::clone(&rx);
        let router = Arc::clone(&router);
        let limiter = Arc::clone(&limiter);

        thread::spawn(move || loop {
            // grab next connection from the channel
            let mut stream = match rx.lock().unwrap().recv() {
                Ok(s) => s,
                Err(_) => break, // channel closed, shut down
            };

            // track this connection for graceful drain
            ACTIVE_CONNECTIONS.fetch_add(1, Ordering::SeqCst);

            // parse the request
            let req = match Request::parse(&mut stream) {
                Ok(r) => r,
                Err(_) => {
                    ACTIVE_CONNECTIONS.fetch_sub(1, Ordering::SeqCst);
                    continue; // bad request, just drop it
                }
            };

            // handle OPTIONS preflight
            if req.method.eq_ignore_ascii_case("OPTIONS") {
                let mut res = Response::new(204);
                add_cors(&mut res);
                let _ = res.write_to(&mut stream);
                ACTIVE_CONNECTIONS.fetch_sub(1, Ordering::SeqCst);
                continue;
            }

            // websocket upgrade on /api/ws
            if req.path.starts_with("/api/ws")
                && let Ok(player_id) = crate::auth::check_auth(&req)
                    && crate::ws::try_upgrade(&req, &mut stream, &player_id) {
                        // ws loop owns the stream from here; decrement now
                        ACTIVE_CONNECTIONS.fetch_sub(1, Ordering::SeqCst);
                        continue;
                    }

            // strip query string for routing - only match on path
            let path = req.path.split('?').next().unwrap_or(&req.path);

            // rate limit login and register (5 per minute)
            let rate_limited_paths = [
                "/api/player/login", "/api/player/register",
                "/api/queue/join", "/api/queue/leave",
                "/api/party/create", "/api/party/invite", "/api/party/join", "/api/party/leave",
                "/api/friends/add", "/api/friends/remove",
            ];
            if rate_limited_paths.contains(&path) {
                let ip = stream.peer_addr()
                    .map(|a| a.ip().to_string())
                    .unwrap_or_else(|_| "unknown".to_string());
                if !limiter.check(&ip, 5, Duration::from_secs(60)) {
                    let mut res = Response::new(429)
                        .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
                        .body("{\"success\":false,\"data\":null,\"error\":\"too many requests\"}".to_string());
                    add_cors(&mut res);
                    let _ = res.write_to(&mut stream);
                    ACTIVE_CONNECTIONS.fetch_sub(1, Ordering::SeqCst);
                    continue;
                }
            }

            // find handler or try static file, then 404
            let mut res = match router.resolve(&req.method, path) {
                Some((handler, params)) => handler(&req, params),
                None if req.method.eq_ignore_ascii_case("GET") => serve_static(path),
                None => Response::new(404)
                    .header("Content-Type", "application/json")
                    .body("{\"error\":\"not found\"}".to_string()),
            };

            add_cors(&mut res);

            let ip = stream.peer_addr().map(|a| a.to_string()).unwrap_or_else(|_| "?".into());
            eprintln!("{} {} {} {}", ip, req.method, path, res.status);

            let _ = res.write_to(&mut stream);

            ACTIVE_CONNECTIONS.fetch_sub(1, Ordering::SeqCst);
        });
    }

    // accept loop - checks RUNNING flag for graceful shutdown
    while RUNNING.load(Ordering::SeqCst) {
        match listener.accept() {
            Ok((s, _)) => {
                let _ = tx.send(s);
            }
            Err(ref e) if e.kind() == std::io::ErrorKind::WouldBlock => {
                std::thread::sleep(Duration::from_millis(50));
            }
            Err(e) => {
                eprintln!("accept error: {}", e);
            }
        }
    }

    // stop accepting new connections by dropping the sender;
    // workers drain their queued items then break on recv() error
    drop(tx);

    // drain phase: wait up to 5 seconds for in-flight connections to finish
    let active = ACTIVE_CONNECTIONS.load(Ordering::SeqCst);
    if active > 0 {
        println!("shutting down... waiting for {} connection(s) to finish", active);
    }

    let drain_deadline = Instant::now() + Duration::from_secs(5);
    loop {
        let remaining = ACTIVE_CONNECTIONS.load(Ordering::SeqCst);
        if remaining == 0 {
            break;
        }
        if Instant::now() >= drain_deadline {
            println!("drain timeout: {} connection(s) still active, forcing exit", remaining);
            break;
        }
        thread::sleep(Duration::from_millis(50));
    }

    println!("vigil server shut down cleanly");
}
```

`crates/vigil-server/src/sqlite.rs`:

```rs
#![allow(dead_code)]
// minimal sqlite3 FFI wrapper - links to system libsqlite3

use std::ffi::CString;
use std::os::raw::{c_char, c_int, c_void};
use std::ptr;

const SQLITE_OK: c_int = 0;
const SQLITE_ROW: c_int = 100;
const SQLITE_DONE: c_int = 101;

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn sqlite3_open(filename: *const c_char, db: *mut *mut c_void) -> c_int;
    fn sqlite3_close(db: *mut c_void) -> c_int;
    fn sqlite3_prepare_v2(
        db: *mut c_void,
        sql: *const c_char,
        nbyte: c_int,
        stmt: *mut *mut c_void,
        tail: *mut *const c_char,
    ) -> c_int;
    fn sqlite3_step(stmt: *mut c_void) -> c_int;
    fn sqlite3_finalize(stmt: *mut c_void) -> c_int;
    fn sqlite3_column_count(stmt: *mut c_void) -> c_int;
    fn sqlite3_column_text(stmt: *mut c_void, col: c_int) -> *const c_char;
    fn sqlite3_column_int64(stmt: *mut c_void, col: c_int) -> i64;
    fn sqlite3_bind_text(
        stmt: *mut c_void,
        idx: c_int,
        val: *const c_char,
        n: c_int,
        destructor: isize,
    ) -> c_int;
    fn sqlite3_bind_int64(stmt: *mut c_void, idx: c_int, val: i64) -> c_int;
    fn sqlite3_errmsg(db: *mut c_void) -> *const c_char;
    fn sqlite3_last_insert_rowid(db: *mut c_void) -> i64;
    fn sqlite3_changes(db: *mut c_void) -> c_int;
}

const SQLITE_TRANSIENT: isize = -1;

pub struct Db {
    handle: *mut c_void,
}

// sqlite3 is safe to use from multiple threads with serialized mode (default)
unsafe impl Send for Db {}
unsafe impl Sync for Db {}

impl Db {
    pub fn open(path: &str) -> Result<Self, String> {
        let c_path = CString::new(path).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
        let mut handle: *mut c_void = ptr::null_mut();
        let rc = unsafe { sqlite3_open(c_path.as_ptr(), &mut handle) };
        if rc != SQLITE_OK {
            let msg = Self::errmsg_raw(handle);
            return Err(format!("sqlite3_open failed: {}", msg));
        }
        // enable WAL mode for better concurrent reads
        let db = Db { handle };
        db.execute("PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL")?;
        db.execute("PRAGMA foreign_keys=ON")?;
        Ok(db)
    }

    fn errmsg_raw(handle: *mut c_void) -> String {
        if handle.is_null() {
            return "null db handle".to_string();
        }
        unsafe {
            let ptr = sqlite3_errmsg(handle);
            if ptr.is_null() {
                "unknown error".to_string()
            } else {
                std::ffi::CStr::from_ptr(ptr).to_string_lossy().to_string()
            }
        }
    }

    fn errmsg(&self) -> String {
        Self::errmsg_raw(self.handle)
    }

    // execute a statement with no results (CREATE, INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE)
    pub fn execute(&self, sql: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
        let c_sql = CString::new(sql).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
        let mut stmt: *mut c_void = ptr::null_mut();
        let rc = unsafe {
            sqlite3_prepare_v2(self.handle, c_sql.as_ptr(), -1, &mut stmt, ptr::null_mut())
        };
        if rc != SQLITE_OK {
            return Err(format!("prepare failed: {}", self.errmsg()));
        }
        let rc = unsafe { sqlite3_step(stmt) };
        unsafe { sqlite3_finalize(stmt) };
        if rc != SQLITE_DONE && rc != SQLITE_ROW {
            return Err(format!("step failed: {}", self.errmsg()));
        }
        Ok(())
    }

    // execute with string parameters (?1, ?2, ...)
    pub fn execute_params(&self, sql: &str, params: &[&str]) -> Result<(), String> {
        let c_sql = CString::new(sql).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
        let mut stmt: *mut c_void = ptr::null_mut();
        let rc = unsafe {
            sqlite3_prepare_v2(self.handle, c_sql.as_ptr(), -1, &mut stmt, ptr::null_mut())
        };
        if rc != SQLITE_OK {
            return Err(format!("prepare failed: {}", self.errmsg()));
        }

        for (i, param) in params.iter().enumerate() {
            let c_param = CString::new(*param).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
            unsafe {
                sqlite3_bind_text(stmt, (i + 1) as c_int, c_param.as_ptr(), -1, SQLITE_TRANSIENT);
            }
        }

        let rc = unsafe { sqlite3_step(stmt) };
        unsafe { sqlite3_finalize(stmt) };
        if rc != SQLITE_DONE && rc != SQLITE_ROW {
            return Err(format!("step failed: {}", self.errmsg()));
        }
        Ok(())
    }

    // query returning rows as Vec<Vec<String>>
    pub fn query(&self, sql: &str, params: &[&str]) -> Result<Vec<Vec<String>>, String> {
        let c_sql = CString::new(sql).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
        let mut stmt: *mut c_void = ptr::null_mut();
        let rc = unsafe {
            sqlite3_prepare_v2(self.handle, c_sql.as_ptr(), -1, &mut stmt, ptr::null_mut())
        };
        if rc != SQLITE_OK {
            return Err(format!("prepare failed: {}", self.errmsg()));
        }

        for (i, param) in params.iter().enumerate() {
            let c_param = CString::new(*param).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
            unsafe {
                sqlite3_bind_text(stmt, (i + 1) as c_int, c_param.as_ptr(), -1, SQLITE_TRANSIENT);
            }
        }

        let col_count = unsafe { sqlite3_column_count(stmt) };
        let mut rows = vec![];

        loop {
            let rc = unsafe { sqlite3_step(stmt) };
            if rc == SQLITE_DONE {
                break;
            }
            if rc != SQLITE_ROW {
                unsafe { sqlite3_finalize(stmt) };
                return Err(format!("step failed: {}", self.errmsg()));
            }

            let mut row = vec![];
            for col in 0..col_count {
                let ptr = unsafe { sqlite3_column_text(stmt, col) };
                let val = if ptr.is_null() {
                    String::new()
                } else {
                    unsafe { std::ffi::CStr::from_ptr(ptr).to_string_lossy().to_string() }
                };
                row.push(val);
            }
            rows.push(row);
        }

        unsafe { sqlite3_finalize(stmt) };
        Ok(rows)
    }

    // returns number of rows changed by last INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE
    pub fn changes(&self) -> i32 {
        unsafe { sqlite3_changes(self.handle) }
    }
}

impl Drop for Db {
    fn drop(&mut self) {
        if !self.handle.is_null() {
            unsafe { sqlite3_close(self.handle) };
        }
    }
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn open_in_memory() {
        let db = Db::open(":memory:").unwrap();
        db.execute("CREATE TABLE t (id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY, name TEXT)").unwrap();
        db.execute_params("INSERT INTO t (name) VALUES (?1)", &["hello"]).unwrap();
        let rows = db.query("SELECT id, name FROM t", &[]).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(rows.len(), 1);
        assert_eq!(rows[0][1], "hello");
    }

    #[test]
    fn query_with_params() {
        let db = Db::open(":memory:").unwrap();
        db.execute("CREATE TABLE t (k TEXT, v TEXT)").unwrap();
        db.execute_params("INSERT INTO t VALUES (?1, ?2)", &["a", "1"]).unwrap();
        db.execute_params("INSERT INTO t VALUES (?1, ?2)", &["b", "2"]).unwrap();
        let rows = db.query("SELECT v FROM t WHERE k = ?1", &["a"]).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(rows.len(), 1);
        assert_eq!(rows[0][0], "1");
    }

    #[test]
    fn changes_count() {
        let db = Db::open(":memory:").unwrap();
        db.execute("CREATE TABLE t (x TEXT)").unwrap();
        db.execute_params("INSERT INTO t VALUES (?1)", &["one"]).unwrap();
        db.execute_params("INSERT INTO t VALUES (?1)", &["two"]).unwrap();
        db.execute("DELETE FROM t").unwrap();
        assert_eq!(db.changes(), 2);
    }

    #[test]
    fn empty_query() {
        let db = Db::open(":memory:").unwrap();
        db.execute("CREATE TABLE t (x TEXT)").unwrap();
        let rows = db.query("SELECT * FROM t", &[]).unwrap();
        assert!(rows.is_empty());
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil-server/src/trust.rs`:

```rs
// trust score computation, 0 to 100

pub struct TrustInput {
    pub prev_score: u8,
    pub prev_heartbeat_seq: u64,
    pub prev_report_secs: u64,
    pub new_heartbeat_seq: u64,
    pub new_report_secs: u64,
    pub ebpf_active: bool,
    pub config_hash_match: bool,
    pub self_protection_issues: usize,
    pub clock_drift_ms: Option<i64>,
    pub cheats_found: bool,
    pub consecutive_clean: u32,
}

pub struct TrustResult {
    pub score: u8,
    #[allow(dead_code)]
    pub penalties: Vec<String>,
    pub consecutive_clean: u32,
}

pub fn compute(input: &TrustInput) -> TrustResult {
    let mut score = input.prev_score as i32;
    let mut penalties = Vec::new();
    let mut clean = input.consecutive_clean;

    // heartbeat gap (vigil was restarted or killed)
    if input.new_heartbeat_seq > 0 && input.prev_heartbeat_seq > 0 {
        let gap = input.new_heartbeat_seq.saturating_sub(input.prev_heartbeat_seq);
        if gap > 1 {
            let pen = ((gap - 1) * 10).min(50) as i32;
            score -= pen;
            penalties.push(format!("heartbeat gap {} (-{})", gap, pen));
            clean = 0;
        }
    }

    // report timing gap (>30s between reports = vigil was down)
    if input.prev_report_secs > 0 && input.new_report_secs > input.prev_report_secs {
        let gap_secs = input.new_report_secs - input.prev_report_secs;
        if gap_secs > 30 {
            score -= 25;
            penalties.push(format!("report gap {}s (-25)", gap_secs));
            clean = 0;
        }
    }

    // no ebpf
    if !input.ebpf_active {
        score -= 15;
        penalties.push("ebpf not active (-15)".to_string());
        clean = 0;
    }

    // config hash mismatch
    if !input.config_hash_match {
        score -= 20;
        penalties.push("config hash mismatch (-20)".to_string());
        clean = 0;
    }

    // self-protection issues
    if input.self_protection_issues > 0 {
        score -= 30;
        penalties.push(format!("self-protection issues: {} (-30)", input.self_protection_issues));
        clean = 0;
    }

    // clock drift
    if let Some(drift) = input.clock_drift_ms
        && drift.abs() > 500 {
            score -= 20;
            penalties.push(format!("clock drift {}ms (-20)", drift));
            clean = 0;
        }

    // cheats found - instant zero, leads to auto-ban
    if input.cheats_found {
        score = 0;
        penalties.push("cheat signatures detected (score=0)".to_string());
        clean = 0;
    }

    // floor at 0
    if score < 0 {
        score = 0;
    }

    // clean streak recovery: 10 consecutive clean reports -> reset to 100
    if penalties.is_empty() {
        clean += 1;
        if clean >= 10 && score < 100 {
            score = 100;
            clean = 0;
        }
    }

    TrustResult {
        score: score as u8,
        penalties,
        consecutive_clean: clean,
    }
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    fn base_input() -> TrustInput {
        TrustInput {
            prev_score: 100,
            prev_heartbeat_seq: 10,
            prev_report_secs: 1000,
            new_heartbeat_seq: 11,
            new_report_secs: 1005,
            ebpf_active: true,
            config_hash_match: true,
            self_protection_issues: 0,
            clock_drift_ms: None,
            cheats_found: false,
            consecutive_clean: 0,
        }
    }

    #[test]
    fn clean_report_no_penalty() {
        let r = compute(&base_input());
        assert_eq!(r.score, 100);
        assert!(r.penalties.is_empty());
        assert_eq!(r.consecutive_clean, 1);
    }

    #[test]
    fn heartbeat_gap_penalty() {
        let mut input = base_input();
        input.new_heartbeat_seq = 15; // gap of 4
        let r = compute(&input);
        assert_eq!(r.score, 60); // 100 - 40
        assert_eq!(r.penalties.len(), 1);
    }

    #[test]
    fn no_ebpf_penalty() {
        let mut input = base_input();
        input.ebpf_active = false;
        let r = compute(&input);
        assert_eq!(r.score, 85);
    }

    #[test]
    fn config_mismatch_penalty() {
        let mut input = base_input();
        input.config_hash_match = false;
        let r = compute(&input);
        assert_eq!(r.score, 80);
    }

    #[test]
    fn self_protection_penalty() {
        let mut input = base_input();
        input.self_protection_issues = 2;
        let r = compute(&input);
        assert_eq!(r.score, 70);
    }

    #[test]
    fn clock_drift_penalty() {
        let mut input = base_input();
        input.clock_drift_ms = Some(1500);
        let r = compute(&input);
        assert_eq!(r.score, 80);
    }

    #[test]
    fn cheats_found_penalty() {
        let mut input = base_input();
        input.cheats_found = true;
        let r = compute(&input);
        assert_eq!(r.score, 0); // cheats = instant zero
    }

    #[test]
    fn multiple_penalties_stack() {
        let mut input = base_input();
        input.ebpf_active = false;
        input.config_hash_match = false;
        input.cheats_found = true;
        let r = compute(&input);
        assert_eq!(r.score, 0); // cheats override everything to zero
    }

    #[test]
    fn score_floors_at_zero() {
        let mut input = base_input();
        input.prev_score = 10;
        input.cheats_found = true;
        input.self_protection_issues = 3;
        let r = compute(&input);
        assert_eq!(r.score, 0);
    }

    #[test]
    fn clean_streak_resets_score() {
        let mut input = base_input();
        input.prev_score = 50;
        input.consecutive_clean = 9; // this will be the 10th
        let r = compute(&input);
        assert_eq!(r.score, 100);
        assert_eq!(r.consecutive_clean, 0);
    }

    #[test]
    fn report_gap_penalty() {
        let mut input = base_input();
        input.new_report_secs = 1060; // 60s gap
        let r = compute(&input);
        assert_eq!(r.score, 75);
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil-server/src/ws.rs`:

```rs
#![allow(dead_code)]
// minimal websocket implementation (RFC 6455)

use std::collections::HashMap;
use std::io::{Read, Write};
use std::net::TcpStream;
use std::sync::{Arc, Mutex};

use crate::crypto::sha1_raw;

const WS_MAGIC: &str = "258EAFA5-E914-47DA-95CA-5AB5D4085731";

// connected clients keyed by player_id
static CLIENTS: Mutex<Option<HashMap<String, Arc<Mutex<TcpStream>>>>> = Mutex::new(None);

pub fn init() {
    *CLIENTS.lock().unwrap() = Some(HashMap::new());
}

// send a message to a specific player (if connected)
pub fn send_to(player_id: &str, msg: &str) {
    let guard = CLIENTS.lock().unwrap();
    if let Some(ref clients) = *guard
        && let Some(stream) = clients.get(player_id)
            && let Ok(mut s) = stream.lock() {
                let _ = write_frame(&mut s, msg);
            }
}

// broadcast to all connected clients
pub fn broadcast(msg: &str) {
    let guard = CLIENTS.lock().unwrap();
    if let Some(ref clients) = *guard {
        for stream in clients.values() {
            if let Ok(mut s) = stream.lock() {
                let _ = write_frame(&mut s, msg);
            }
        }
    }
}

// try to upgrade an HTTP request to websocket
// returns true if upgraded (caller should not send HTTP response)
pub fn try_upgrade(req: &crate::http::Request, stream: &mut TcpStream, player_id: &str) -> bool {
    let upgrade = req.get_header("upgrade").unwrap_or_default();
    if !upgrade.eq_ignore_ascii_case("websocket") {
        return false;
    }

    let key = match req.get_header("sec-websocket-key") {
        Some(k) => k.to_string(),
        None => return false,
    };

    // compute accept hash: base64(sha1(key + magic))
    let accept = compute_accept(&key);

    let response = format!(
        "HTTP/1.1 101 Switching Protocols\r\n\
         Upgrade: websocket\r\n\
         Connection: Upgrade\r\n\
         Sec-WebSocket-Accept: {}\r\n\r\n",
        accept
    );

    if stream.write_all(response.as_bytes()).is_err() {
        return false;
    }

    // register client
    let stream_clone = stream.try_clone().unwrap();
    {
        let mut guard = CLIENTS.lock().unwrap();
        if let Some(ref mut clients) = *guard {
            clients.insert(player_id.to_string(), Arc::new(Mutex::new(stream_clone)));
        }
    }

    // read loop - keep connection alive, handle pings
    let mut buf = [0u8; 4096];
    loop {
        match stream.read(&mut buf) {
            Ok(0) => break,
            Ok(n) => {
                if let Some(frame) = decode_frame(&buf[..n]) {
                    match frame.opcode {
                        // ping -> pong
                        0x9 => { let _ = write_pong(stream, &frame.data); }
                        // close
                        0x8 => break,
                        // text - ignore for now (server push only)
                        _ => {}
                    }
                }
            }
            Err(_) => break,
        }
    }

    // unregister
    {
        let mut guard = CLIENTS.lock().unwrap();
        if let Some(ref mut clients) = *guard {
            clients.remove(player_id);
        }
    }

    true
}

struct Frame {
    opcode: u8,
    data: Vec<u8>,
}

fn decode_frame(buf: &[u8]) -> Option<Frame> {
    if buf.len() < 2 { return None; }
    let opcode = buf[0] & 0x0F;
    let masked = buf[1] & 0x80 != 0;
    let mut len = (buf[1] & 0x7F) as usize;
    let mut offset = 2;

    if len == 126 {
        if buf.len() < 4 { return None; }
        len = ((buf[2] as usize) << 8) | buf[3] as usize;
        offset = 4;
    } else if len == 127 {
        // we dont handle >64k frames
        return None;
    }

    let mask_key = if masked {
        if buf.len() < offset + 4 { return None; }
        let key = [buf[offset], buf[offset+1], buf[offset+2], buf[offset+3]];
        offset += 4;
        Some(key)
    } else {
        None
    };

    if buf.len() < offset + len { return None; }
    let mut data = buf[offset..offset+len].to_vec();

    if let Some(key) = mask_key {
        for (i, byte) in data.iter_mut().enumerate() {
            *byte ^= key[i % 4];
        }
    }

    Some(Frame { opcode, data })
}

fn write_frame(stream: &mut TcpStream, msg: &str) -> std::io::Result<()> {
    let data = msg.as_bytes();
    let mut frame = vec![0x81u8]; // FIN + text opcode

    if data.len() < 126 {
        frame.push(data.len() as u8);
    } else {
        frame.push(126);
        frame.push((data.len() >> 8) as u8);
        frame.push(data.len() as u8);
    }

    frame.extend_from_slice(data);
    stream.write_all(&frame)
}

fn write_pong(stream: &mut TcpStream, data: &[u8]) -> std::io::Result<()> {
    let mut frame = vec![0x8Au8]; // FIN + pong
    frame.push(data.len() as u8);
    frame.extend_from_slice(data);
    stream.write_all(&frame)
}

fn compute_accept(key: &str) -> String {
    let combined = format!("{}{}", key, WS_MAGIC);
    let hash = sha1_raw(combined.as_bytes());
    base64_encode(&hash)
}

fn base64_encode(data: &[u8]) -> String {
    const CHARS: &[u8] = b"ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789+/";
    let mut result = String::new();
    for chunk in data.chunks(3) {
        let b0 = chunk[0] as u32;
        let b1 = if chunk.len() > 1 { chunk[1] as u32 } else { 0 };
        let b2 = if chunk.len() > 2 { chunk[2] as u32 } else { 0 };
        let triple = (b0 << 16) | (b1 << 8) | b2;
        result.push(CHARS[((triple >> 18) & 0x3F) as usize] as char);
        result.push(CHARS[((triple >> 12) & 0x3F) as usize] as char);
        if chunk.len() > 1 { result.push(CHARS[((triple >> 6) & 0x3F) as usize] as char); } else { result.push('='); }
        if chunk.len() > 2 { result.push(CHARS[(triple & 0x3F) as usize] as char); } else { result.push('='); }
    }
    result
}

```

`crates/vigil-server/tests/integration.rs`:

```rs
// Integration tests for vigil-server.
//
// Handler functions are called directly with constructed Request structs —
// no network layer is involved.  Tests that exercise the handler globals
// (DATA_DIR via OnceLock) share a single temp directory initialised once per
// process.  A Mutex serialises those tests so they do not stomp on shared
// state.  Tests that only call db::* directly get their own isolated temp dir.

use std::sync::{Mutex, OnceLock};

use vigil_server::db;
use vigil_server::handlers;
use vigil_server::http::Request;
use vigil_server::json::{parse, JsonValue};
use vigil_server::router::Params;
use vigil_server::ws;

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Shared test infrastructure
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

// Single temp directory used by all handler-level tests.
// handlers::init() uses OnceLock internally so it can only be called once per
// process.  All handler tests that call through the handler globals share this
// DB file.  Because SQLite rejects concurrent writers on the same file, a
// mutex serialises those tests.  db-direct tests use isolated temp dirs and
// do not need the mutex.
static HANDLER_DIR: OnceLock<String> = OnceLock::new();

// Serialises handler tests to avoid SQLite "database is locked" errors caused
// by concurrent writers hitting the shared DB file.  unwrap_or_else recovers
// from a poisoned lock so a single test failure does not block all others.
static HANDLER_LOCK: Mutex<()> = Mutex::new(());

fn handler_lock() -> std::sync::MutexGuard<'static, ()> {
    HANDLER_LOCK.lock().unwrap_or_else(|e| e.into_inner())
}

/// Returns the shared handler data dir, initialising DB + handlers on first call.
fn handler_dir() -> &'static str {
    HANDLER_DIR.get_or_init(|| {
        // Make JWT/admin secrets available to the auth module.  cfg!(test) is
        // false for library code compiled into an integration test binary, so
        // the secrets must come from env vars.
        // SAFETY: this closure runs exactly once via OnceLock; no other thread
        // is reading these env vars at this point.
        unsafe {
            std::env::set_var("VIGIL_JWT_SECRET", "integration-test-secret");
            std::env::set_var("VIGIL_ADMIN_KEY", "test-admin-key");
        }

        let dir = std::env::temp_dir()
            .join(format!("vigil_integration_{}", std::process::id()))
            .to_string_lossy()
            .to_string();
        let _ = std::fs::remove_dir_all(&dir);
        db::init_db(&dir);
        handlers::init(&dir);
        handlers::init_nonces();
        ws::init();
        dir
    })
}

/// Creates a fresh isolated temp dir for db-direct tests.
fn tmp_dir(label: &str) -> String {
    let dir = std::env::temp_dir()
        .join(format!("vigil_int_{}_{}", std::process::id(), label))
        .to_string_lossy()
        .to_string();
    let _ = std::fs::remove_dir_all(&dir);
    dir
}

fn cleanup(dir: &str) {
    let _ = std::fs::remove_dir_all(dir);
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Request helpers
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

fn get(path: &str) -> Request {
    Request {
        method: "GET".to_string(),
        path: path.to_string(),
        headers: vec![],
        body: String::new(),
    }
}

fn get_auth(path: &str, token: &str) -> Request {
    Request {
        method: "GET".to_string(),
        path: path.to_string(),
        headers: vec![("Authorization".to_string(), format!("Bearer {}", token))],
        body: String::new(),
    }
}

fn post_json(path: &str, body: &str, token: Option<&str>) -> Request {
    let mut headers = vec![("Content-Type".to_string(), "application/json".to_string())];
    if let Some(t) = token {
        headers.push(("Authorization".to_string(), format!("Bearer {}", t)));
    }
    Request {
        method: "POST".to_string(),
        path: path.to_string(),
        headers,
        body: body.to_string(),
    }
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Response parsing helpers
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

fn no_params() -> Params {
    Params::new()
}

fn id_param(id: &str) -> Params {
    Params::from_pairs(vec![("id".to_string(), id.to_string())])
}

/// Extract the "data" field from a standard API envelope.
fn data(body: &str) -> JsonValue {
    let v = parse(body).expect("response body is not valid JSON");
    v.get("data").cloned().unwrap_or(JsonValue::Null)
}

/// Extract the "error" string from an API envelope.
fn error_field(body: &str) -> String {
    let v = parse(body).expect("response body is not valid JSON");
    v.get("error")
        .and_then(|e| e.as_str())
        .unwrap_or("")
        .to_string()
}

/// Register a player via the handler and return (player_id, token).
fn register_player(name: &str, password: &str) -> (String, String) {
    let body = format!(r#"{{"name":"{}","password":"{}"}}"#, name, password);
    let req = post_json("/api/player/register", &body, None);
    let resp = handlers::register(&req, no_params());
    assert_eq!(resp.status, 200, "register '{}' failed: {}", name, resp.body);
    let d = data(&resp.body);
    let player_id = d
        .get("player")
        .and_then(|p| p.get("id"))
        .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
        .expect("missing player.id in register response")
        .to_string();
    let token = d
        .get("token")
        .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
        .expect("missing token in register response")
        .to_string();
    (player_id, token)
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Test: GET /api/health
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

#[test]
fn test_health_returns_ok() {
    let _guard = handler_lock();
    handler_dir();

    let req = get("/api/health");
    let resp = handlers::health(&req, no_params());
    assert_eq!(resp.status, 200);
    let d = data(&resp.body);
    assert_eq!(d.get("status").and_then(|v| v.as_str()), Some("ok"));
    assert_eq!(
        d.get("service").and_then(|v| v.as_str()),
        Some("vigil-server")
    );
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Test: Register → Login → Get player profile
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

#[test]
fn test_register_login_get_profile() {

    let _guard = handler_lock();
    handler_dir();

    // --- Register ---
    let (player_id, reg_token) = register_player("alice_int", "password123");
    assert!(!player_id.is_empty());
    assert!(!reg_token.is_empty());

    // --- Login returns a fresh token ---
    let login_req = post_json(
        "/api/player/login",
        r#"{"name":"alice_int","password":"password123"}"#,
        None,
    );
    let login_resp = handlers::login(&login_req, no_params());
    assert_eq!(login_resp.status, 200, "login failed: {}", login_resp.body);
    let login_token = data(&login_resp.body)
        .get("token")
        .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
        .expect("missing token in login response")
        .to_string();
    assert!(!login_token.is_empty());

    // --- Get player by id using the login token ---
    let get_resp = handlers::get_player(
        &get_auth(&format!("/api/player/{}", player_id), &login_token),
        id_param(&player_id),
    );
    assert_eq!(get_resp.status, 200, "get_player failed: {}", get_resp.body);
    let player_data = data(&get_resp.body);
    assert_eq!(
        player_data.get("id").and_then(|v| v.as_str()),
        Some(player_id.as_str())
    );
    assert_eq!(
        player_data.get("name").and_then(|v| v.as_str()),
        Some("alice_int")
    );
    assert_eq!(
        player_data.get("trust_score").and_then(|v| v.as_i64()),
        Some(100)
    );

    // --- Full profile endpoint ---
    let profile_resp = handlers::player_profile_handler(
        &get_auth(
            &format!("/api/player/{}/profile", player_id),
            &login_token,
        ),
        id_param(&player_id),
    );
    assert_eq!(
        profile_resp.status, 200,
        "player_profile failed: {}",
        profile_resp.body
    );
    let profile_data = data(&profile_resp.body);
    assert_eq!(
        profile_data
            .get("player")
            .and_then(|p| p.get("id"))
            .and_then(|v| v.as_str()),
        Some(player_id.as_str())
    );
    assert_eq!(
        profile_data.get("match_count").and_then(|v| v.as_i64()),
        Some(0)
    );

    // --- Wrong password is rejected ---
    let bad_resp = handlers::login(
        &post_json(
            "/api/player/login",
            r#"{"name":"alice_int","password":"wrongpass"}"#,
            None,
        ),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(bad_resp.status, 401);

    // --- Duplicate name is rejected ---
    let dup_resp = handlers::register(
        &post_json(
            "/api/player/register",
            r#"{"name":"alice_int","password":"anotherpass"}"#,
            None,
        ),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(dup_resp.status, 400);
    assert!(
        error_field(&dup_resp.body).contains("already taken"),
        "unexpected error: {}",
        error_field(&dup_resp.body)
    );
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Test: Register → Add friend → List friends → Remove friend
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

#[test]
fn test_friends_flow() {

    let _guard = handler_lock();
    handler_dir();

    let (pid_a, tok_a) = register_player("bob_int", "password123");
    let (pid_b, _tok_b) = register_player("carol_int", "password123");

    // --- Add friend (bob adds carol by name) ---
    let add_resp = handlers::add_friend_handler(
        &post_json(
            "/api/friends/add",
            r#"{"friend_name":"carol_int"}"#,
            Some(&tok_a),
        ),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(add_resp.status, 200, "add_friend failed: {}", add_resp.body);

    // --- List friends — carol should appear ---
    let list_resp = handlers::list_friends_handler(
        &get_auth("/api/friends", &tok_a),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(
        list_resp.status, 200,
        "list_friends failed: {}",
        list_resp.body
    );
    let arr = data(&list_resp.body)
        .as_array()
        .expect("expected friends array")
        .clone();
    assert_eq!(arr.len(), 1);
    assert_eq!(
        arr[0].get("id").and_then(|v| v.as_str()),
        Some(pid_b.as_str())
    );

    // --- Cannot add yourself ---
    let self_resp = handlers::add_friend_handler(
        &post_json(
            "/api/friends/add",
            r#"{"friend_name":"bob_int"}"#,
            Some(&tok_a),
        ),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(self_resp.status, 400);
    assert!(
        error_field(&self_resp.body).contains("yourself"),
        "unexpected error: {}",
        error_field(&self_resp.body)
    );

    // --- Remove friend ---
    let rm_resp = handlers::remove_friend_handler(
        &post_json(
            "/api/friends/remove",
            &format!(r#"{{"friend_id":"{}"}}"#, pid_b),
            Some(&tok_a),
        ),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(rm_resp.status, 200, "remove_friend failed: {}", rm_resp.body);

    // --- List friends again — should be empty ---
    let list2_resp = handlers::list_friends_handler(
        &get_auth("/api/friends", &tok_a),
        no_params(),
    );
    let arr2 = data(&list2_resp.body)
        .as_array()
        .expect("expected array")
        .clone();
    assert_eq!(arr2.len(), 0);

    let _ = pid_a;
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Test: Register → Create party → Get party
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

#[test]
fn test_party_flow() {

    let _guard = handler_lock();
    handler_dir();

    let (pid_leader, tok_leader) = register_player("dave_int", "password123");
    let (pid_member, tok_member) = register_player("eve_int", "password123");

    // --- Create party ---
    let create_resp = handlers::create_party_handler(
        &post_json("/api/party/create", "{}", Some(&tok_leader)),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(
        create_resp.status, 200,
        "create_party failed: {}",
        create_resp.body
    );
    let party = data(&create_resp.body);
    let party_id = party
        .get("id")
        .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
        .expect("missing party id")
        .to_string();
    assert_eq!(
        party.get("leader").and_then(|v| v.as_str()),
        Some(pid_leader.as_str())
    );
    let members = party
        .get("members")
        .and_then(|v| v.as_array())
        .expect("expected members array");
    assert_eq!(members.len(), 1);
    assert_eq!(members[0].as_str(), Some(pid_leader.as_str()));

    // --- Cannot create another party while already in one ---
    let dup_resp = handlers::create_party_handler(
        &post_json("/api/party/create", "{}", Some(&tok_leader)),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(dup_resp.status, 400);
    assert!(
        error_field(&dup_resp.body).contains("already in a party"),
        "unexpected error: {}",
        error_field(&dup_resp.body)
    );

    // --- Get party ---
    let get_resp = handlers::get_party_handler(
        &get_auth("/api/party", &tok_leader),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(
        get_resp.status, 200,
        "get_party failed: {}",
        get_resp.body
    );
    assert_eq!(
        data(&get_resp.body).get("id").and_then(|v| v.as_str()),
        Some(party_id.as_str())
    );

    // --- Invite member ---
    let invite_resp = handlers::invite_party_handler(
        &post_json(
            "/api/party/invite",
            &format!(r#"{{"player_id":"{}"}}"#, pid_member),
            Some(&tok_leader),
        ),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(
        invite_resp.status, 200,
        "invite failed: {}",
        invite_resp.body
    );

    // --- Member joins party ---
    let join_resp = handlers::join_party_handler(
        &post_json(
            "/api/party/join",
            &format!(r#"{{"party_id":"{}"}}"#, party_id),
            Some(&tok_member),
        ),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(
        join_resp.status, 200,
        "join_party failed: {}",
        join_resp.body
    );
    let joined_members = data(&join_resp.body)
        .get("members")
        .and_then(|v| v.as_array())
        .expect("members after join")
        .len();
    assert_eq!(joined_members, 2);

    // --- Member leaves ---
    let leave_member = handlers::leave_party_handler(
        &post_json("/api/party/leave", "{}", Some(&tok_member)),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(
        leave_member.status, 200,
        "member leave failed: {}",
        leave_member.body
    );

    // --- Leader leaves (disbands the party) ---
    let leave_leader = handlers::leave_party_handler(
        &post_json("/api/party/leave", "{}", Some(&tok_leader)),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(
        leave_leader.status, 200,
        "leader leave failed: {}",
        leave_leader.body
    );

    // --- Party no longer accessible ---
    let after_resp = handlers::get_party_handler(
        &get_auth("/api/party", &tok_leader),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(after_resp.status, 404);
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Test: Register → Join queue → Leave queue
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

#[test]
fn test_queue_flow() {

    let _guard = handler_lock();
    handler_dir();

    let (pid, tok) = register_player("frank_int", "password123");

    // --- Join queue ---
    let join_resp = handlers::join_queue_handler(
        &post_json("/api/queue/join", r#"{"game":"cs2"}"#, Some(&tok)),
        no_params(),
    );
    // 200 regardless of whether matchmaking fired immediately
    assert_eq!(
        join_resp.status, 200,
        "join_queue failed: {}",
        join_resp.body
    );
    let join_data = data(&join_resp.body);
    let status_str = join_data.as_str().unwrap_or("");
    let status_obj = join_data
        .get("status")
        .and_then(|v| v.as_str())
        .unwrap_or("");
    assert!(
        status_str == "joined queue" || status_obj == "match_found",
        "unexpected join_queue response: {}",
        join_resp.body
    );

    // Only check queue status / leave if a match was not immediately formed
    if status_str == "joined queue" {
        // --- Queue status shows player in queue ---
        let status_resp = handlers::queue_status_handler(
            &get_auth("/api/queue/status", &tok),
            no_params(),
        );
        assert_eq!(
            status_resp.status, 200,
            "queue_status failed: {}",
            status_resp.body
        );
        let qdata = data(&status_resp.body);
        let total = qdata.get("total").and_then(|v| v.as_i64()).unwrap_or(0);
        assert!(total >= 1, "queue total should be >= 1, got {}", total);
        // position is 0-indexed; first player in queue is at position Some(0)
        let position = qdata.get("position").and_then(|v| v.as_i64());
        assert!(
            position.is_some(),
            "player should have a queue position: {}",
            status_resp.body
        );

        // --- Leave queue ---
        let leave_resp = handlers::leave_queue_handler(
            &post_json("/api/queue/leave", "{}", Some(&tok)),
            no_params(),
        );
        assert_eq!(
            leave_resp.status, 200,
            "leave_queue failed: {}",
            leave_resp.body
        );

        // --- Position is null after leaving ---
        let status2 = handlers::queue_status_handler(
            &get_auth("/api/queue/status", &tok),
            no_params(),
        );
        let qdata2 = data(&status2.body);
        let pos2 = qdata2.get("position");
        assert!(
            pos2.map(|v| v.is_null()).unwrap_or(true),
            "position should be null after leaving queue: {}",
            status2.body
        );
    }

    let _ = pid;
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Test: Register → Report (trust score changes)
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

#[test]
fn test_report_trust_score() {

    let _guard = handler_lock();
    handler_dir();

    let (player_id, token) = register_player("grace_int", "password123");

    // Initial trust score is 100
    let get_resp = handlers::get_player(
        &get_auth(&format!("/api/player/{}", player_id), &token),
        id_param(&player_id),
    );
    assert_eq!(get_resp.status, 200);
    let initial_score = data(&get_resp.body)
        .get("trust_score")
        .and_then(|v| v.as_i64())
        .expect("missing trust_score");
    assert_eq!(initial_score, 100);

    // --- Submit a clean report ---
    // No timestamp field: the server fills in now(), which always passes the
    // 60-second window check.  A unique nonce prevents replay detection.
    let clean_report = format!(
        r#"{{
            "player_id": "{pid}",
            "nonce": "grace-clean-1",
            "config_hash": "abc123",
            "suspicious_processes": [],
            "cheat_matches": [],
            "sandbox_detected": [],
            "file_integrity": {{"status": "ok", "modified": [], "added": [], "removed": []}},
            "ebpf_active": true,
            "heartbeat_seq": 1,
            "self_protection": []
        }}"#,
        pid = player_id
    );
    let report_resp = handlers::receive_report(
        &post_json("/api/report", &clean_report, Some(&token)),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(
        report_resp.status, 200,
        "clean report failed: {}",
        report_resp.body
    );
    let clean_data = data(&report_resp.body);
    assert_eq!(
        clean_data.get("status").and_then(|v| v.as_str()),
        Some("report received")
    );
    let trust_after_clean = clean_data
        .get("trust_score")
        .and_then(|v| v.as_i64())
        .expect("missing trust_score in report response");
    // A clean report should not reduce trust significantly from 100
    assert!(
        trust_after_clean >= 95,
        "trust after clean report should be >= 95, got {}",
        trust_after_clean
    );

    // --- Submit a report with a cheat detection ---
    let cheat_report = format!(
        r#"{{
            "player_id": "{pid}",
            "nonce": "grace-cheat-1",
            "config_hash": "abc123",
            "suspicious_processes": [],
            "cheat_matches": [{{"name":"aimbot","category":"aimassist"}}],
            "sandbox_detected": [],
            "file_integrity": {{"status": "ok", "modified": [], "added": [], "removed": []}},
            "ebpf_active": true,
            "heartbeat_seq": 2,
            "self_protection": []
        }}"#,
        pid = player_id
    );
    let cheat_resp = handlers::receive_report(
        &post_json("/api/report", &cheat_report, Some(&token)),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(
        cheat_resp.status, 200,
        "cheat report failed: {}",
        cheat_resp.body
    );
    let trust_after_cheat = data(&cheat_resp.body)
        .get("trust_score")
        .and_then(|v| v.as_i64())
        .expect("missing trust_score after cheat");
    // Cheat detection must reduce trust
    assert!(
        trust_after_cheat < trust_after_clean,
        "trust should decrease after cheat detection: {} -> {}",
        trust_after_clean,
        trust_after_cheat
    );
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// db-direct: friends are bidirectional and isolated per db
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

#[test]
fn test_db_direct_friends_isolated() {
    let dir = tmp_dir("friends_iso");
    db::init_db(&dir);

    db::insert_player(&dir, "p1", "user1", "hash1", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();
    db::insert_player(&dir, "p2", "user2", "hash2", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();

    // add_friend inserts both directions
    db::add_friend(&dir, "p1", "p2").unwrap();

    let p1_friends = db::get_friends(&dir, "p1").unwrap();
    assert_eq!(p1_friends, vec!["p2".to_string()]);

    // friendship is bidirectional — p2 also sees p1
    let p2_friends = db::get_friends(&dir, "p2").unwrap();
    assert_eq!(p2_friends, vec!["p1".to_string()]);

    // remove_friend deletes both directions
    db::remove_friend(&dir, "p1", "p2").unwrap();
    assert!(db::get_friends(&dir, "p1").unwrap().is_empty());
    assert!(db::get_friends(&dir, "p2").unwrap().is_empty());

    cleanup(&dir);
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// db-direct: party create / invite / join / leave
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

#[test]
fn test_db_direct_party() {
    let dir = tmp_dir("party_direct");
    db::init_db(&dir);

    db::insert_player(&dir, "leader1", "leaderuser", "hash", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();
    db::insert_player(&dir, "mem1", "memberuser", "hash", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();

    let party_id = db::create_party(&dir, "leader1").unwrap();
    assert!(!party_id.is_empty());

    let party = db::get_party(&dir, &party_id)
        .unwrap()
        .expect("party should exist");
    assert_eq!(party.leader, "leader1");
    assert_eq!(party.members, vec!["leader1".to_string()]);

    // invite then join
    db::invite_to_party(&dir, &party_id, "mem1").unwrap();
    db::join_party(&dir, &party_id, "mem1").unwrap();

    let after_join = db::get_party(&dir, &party_id).unwrap().expect("party");
    assert_eq!(after_join.members.len(), 2);
    assert!(after_join.members.contains(&"mem1".to_string()));

    // member leaves — party still exists with only the leader
    db::leave_party(&dir, &party_id, "mem1").unwrap();
    let after_leave = db::get_party(&dir, &party_id).unwrap().expect("party");
    assert_eq!(after_leave.members.len(), 1);

    cleanup(&dir);
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// db-direct: queue join / position / leave
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

#[test]
fn test_db_direct_queue() {
    let dir = tmp_dir("queue_direct");
    db::init_db(&dir);

    db::insert_player(&dir, "q1", "queueuser", "hash", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();

    db::join_queue(&dir, "q1", None, "cs2").unwrap();

    let queue = db::get_queue(&dir).unwrap();
    assert_eq!(queue.len(), 1);
    assert_eq!(queue[0].player_id, "q1");
    assert_eq!(queue[0].game, "cs2");

    // get_queue_position uses .position() — 0-indexed; first entry = Some(0)
    let pos = db::get_queue_position(&dir, "q1").unwrap();
    assert_eq!(pos, Some(0), "first queue entry should be at position 0");

    db::leave_queue(&dir, "q1").unwrap();
    assert!(db::get_queue(&dir).unwrap().is_empty());
    assert!(db::get_queue_position(&dir, "q1").unwrap().is_none());

    cleanup(&dir);
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// db-direct: ban / unban changes player state
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

#[test]
fn test_db_direct_ban_unban() {
    let dir = tmp_dir("ban_direct");
    db::init_db(&dir);

    db::insert_player(&dir, "ban1", "banuser", "hash", "2025-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap();

    let p = db::get_player(&dir, "ban1").unwrap().unwrap();
    assert!(!p.banned);

    db::ban_player(&dir, "ban1", "test ban").unwrap();
    let banned = db::get_player(&dir, "ban1").unwrap().unwrap();
    assert!(banned.banned);
    assert_eq!(banned.ban_reason.as_deref(), Some("test ban"));

    db::unban_player(&dir, "ban1").unwrap();
    let unbanned = db::get_player(&dir, "ban1").unwrap().unwrap();
    assert!(!unbanned.banned);
    assert!(unbanned.ban_reason.is_none());

    cleanup(&dir);
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Test: Replay protection — same nonce is rejected with 409
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

#[test]
fn test_report_replay_rejected() {
    let _guard = handler_lock();
    handler_dir();

    let (player_id, token) = register_player("replay_int", "password123");

    let report = format!(
        r#"{{
            "player_id": "{pid}",
            "nonce": "unique-nonce-replay-test-xyz",
            "config_hash": "abc123",
            "suspicious_processes": [],
            "cheat_matches": [],
            "sandbox_detected": [],
            "file_integrity": {{"status": "ok", "modified": [], "added": [], "removed": []}},
            "ebpf_active": true,
            "heartbeat_seq": 1,
            "self_protection": []
        }}"#,
        pid = player_id
    );

    // First submission must succeed.
    let resp1 = handlers::receive_report(
        &post_json("/api/report", &report, Some(&token)),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(resp1.status, 200, "first report should succeed: {}", resp1.body);

    // Identical report (same nonce) must be rejected as a replay.
    let resp2 = handlers::receive_report(
        &post_json("/api/report", &report, Some(&token)),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(resp2.status, 409, "replay should be rejected with 409: {}", resp2.body);
    assert!(
        error_field(&resp2.body).contains("replay"),
        "error message should mention replay: {}",
        error_field(&resp2.body)
    );
}

#[test]

    let _guard = handler_lock();

    let (player_id, token) = register_player("stale_ts_int", "password123");

            "player_id": "{pid}",
            "timestamp": "2020-06-15T08:00:00Z",
            "config_hash": "abc123",
            "suspicious_processes": [],
            "cheat_matches": [],
            "sandbox_detected": [],
            "file_integrity": {{"status": "ok", "modified": [], "added": [], "removed": []}},
            "ebpf_active": true,
            "heartbeat_seq": 1,
            "self_protection": []
        }}"#,
        pid = player_id
    );

    let resp = handlers::receive_report(
        &post_json("/api/report", &stale_report, Some(&token)),
        no_params(),

    assert!(
        error_field(&resp.body).contains("timestamp"),
        "error message should mention timestamp: {}",
        error_field(&resp.body)
    );
}

            "config_hash": "abc123",
            "suspicious_processes": [],
            "cheat_matches": [],
            "sandbox_detected": [],
            "file_integrity": {{"status": "ok", "modified": [], "added": [], "removed": []}},
            "ebpf_active": true,
            "heartbeat_seq": 1,
            "self_protection": []
        }}"#,
        pid = player_id
    );

        &post_json("/api/report", &report1, Some(&token)),
        no_params(),
    );

        r#"{{
            "player_id": "{pid}",
            "nonce": "rate-limit-nonce-2",
            "config_hash": "abc123",
            "suspicious_processes": [],
            "cheat_matches": [],
            "sandbox_detected": [],
            "file_integrity": {{"status": "ok", "modified": [], "added": [], "removed": []}},
            "ebpf_active": true,
            "heartbeat_seq": 2,
            "self_protection": []
        }}"#,
        pid = player_id
    );
    let resp2 = handlers::receive_report(
        &post_json("/api/report", &report2, Some(&token)),
        no_params(),
    );
    assert_eq!(
        resp2.status, 429,
        "second immediate report should be rate limited: {}",
        resp2.body
    );
    assert!(
        error_field(&resp2.body).contains("too many reports"),
        "error should mention rate limiting: {}",
        error_field(&resp2.body)
    );
}
```

`crates/vigil-tui/src/ipc.rs`:

```rs
// IPC client - talks to vigil daemon via /run/vigil.sock

use std::io::{Read, Write};
use std::os::unix::net::UnixStream;
use std::time::Duration;
use vigil_common::json::{parse, stringify, json_obj, json_str};

const SOCK_PATH: &str = "/run/vigil.sock";

#[derive(Default)]
pub struct DaemonStatus {
    pub running: bool,
    pub trust_score: i32,
    pub ebpf: bool,
    pub profile: String,
    pub scan_count: i64,
    pub banned: bool,
}

fn send_command(cmd: &str) -> Result<String, String> {
    let mut stream = UnixStream::connect(SOCK_PATH)
        .map_err(|e| format!("ipc connect: {}", e))?;
    stream.set_read_timeout(Some(Duration::from_secs(2))).ok();
    stream.set_write_timeout(Some(Duration::from_secs(2))).ok();

    stream.write_all(cmd.as_bytes())
        .map_err(|e| format!("ipc write: {}", e))?;

    let mut buf = [0u8; 4096];
    let n = stream.read(&mut buf)
        .map_err(|e| format!("ipc read: {}", e))?;

    Ok(String::from_utf8_lossy(&buf[..n]).trim().to_string())
}

pub fn get_status() -> DaemonStatus {
    let cmd = stringify(&json_obj(vec![("cmd", json_str("status"))]));
    match send_command(&cmd) {
        Ok(resp) => {
            if let Ok(val) = parse(&resp) {
                DaemonStatus {
                    running: val.get("running").and_then(|v| v.as_bool()).unwrap_or(false),
                    trust_score: val.get("trust_score").and_then(|v| v.as_i64()).unwrap_or(0) as i32,
                    ebpf: val.get("ebpf").and_then(|v| v.as_bool()).unwrap_or(false),
                    profile: val.get("profile").and_then(|v| v.as_str()).unwrap_or("").to_string(),
                    scan_count: val.get("scan_count").and_then(|v| v.as_i64()).unwrap_or(0),
                    banned: val.get("banned").and_then(|v| v.as_bool()).unwrap_or(false),
                }
            } else {
                DaemonStatus { running: true, ..Default::default() }
            }
        }
        Err(_) => DaemonStatus::default(),
    }
}

#[allow(dead_code)]
pub fn set_profile(name: &str) -> Result<(), String> {
    let cmd = stringify(&json_obj(vec![
        ("cmd", json_str("set_profile")),
        ("profile", json_str(name)),
    ]));
    let resp = send_command(&cmd)?;
    let val = parse(&resp).map_err(|e| format!("ipc json: {}", e))?;
    if val.get("status").and_then(|v| v.as_str()) == Some("ok") {
        Ok(())
    } else {
        Err(resp)
    }
}

```

`crates/vigil-tui/src/main.rs`:

```rs
mod ipc;
mod term;
mod ui;

use std::time::{Duration, Instant};

use term::{Key, Screen};
use ui::{AppState, Tab};

fn main() {
    term::enable_raw_mode();

    let mut scr = Screen::new();
    let mut state = AppState::new();
    let mut last_refresh = Instant::now().checked_sub(Duration::from_secs(10)).unwrap_or_else(Instant::now);

    // initial draw
    state.status = ipc::get_status();
    let (w, h) = term::size();
    ui::draw(&mut scr, &state, w, h);

    loop {
        // poll input (non-blocking due to raw mode VTIME=1)
        if let Some(key) = term::read_key() {
            match key {
                Key::Quit | Key::Esc => break,
                Key::Num(1) => state.tab = Tab::Dashboard,
                Key::Num(2) => state.tab = Tab::Protection,
                Key::Num(3) => state.tab = Tab::Logs,
                Key::Num(4) => state.tab = Tab::Settings,
                Key::Tab => state.tab = state.tab.next(),
                _ => {}
            }

            let (w, h) = term::size();
            ui::draw(&mut scr, &state, w, h);
        }

        // refresh status every 3 seconds
        if last_refresh.elapsed() >= Duration::from_secs(3) {
            state.status = ipc::get_status();
            last_refresh = Instant::now();

            let (w, h) = term::size();
            ui::draw(&mut scr, &state, w, h);
        }
    }

    // cleanup
    scr.clear();
    scr.show_cursor();
    scr.flush();
    term::disable_raw_mode();
}

```

`crates/vigil-tui/src/term.rs`:

```rs
// Zero-dep terminal handling: raw mode, size, cursor, ANSI output

use std::io::{self, Read, Write};

// tcgetattr/tcsetattr via libc FFI
#[repr(C)]
#[derive(Clone)]
struct Termios {
    c_iflag: u32,
    c_oflag: u32,
    c_cflag: u32,
    c_lflag: u32,
    c_line: u8,
    c_cc: [u8; 32],
    c_ispeed: u32,
    c_ospeed: u32,
}

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn tcgetattr(fd: i32, termios: *mut Termios) -> i32;
    fn tcsetattr(fd: i32, action: i32, termios: *const Termios) -> i32;
    fn ioctl(fd: i32, request: u64, ...) -> i32;
}

const STDIN_FD: i32 = 0;
const TCSAFLUSH: i32 = 2;
const ICANON: u32 = 0o000002;
const ECHO: u32 = 0o000010;
const ISIG: u32 = 0o000001;
const IXON: u32 = 0o002000;
const ICRNL: u32 = 0o000400;
const OPOST: u32 = 0o000001;
const TIOCGWINSZ: u64 = 0x5413;

#[repr(C)]
struct Winsize {
    ws_row: u16,
    ws_col: u16,
    ws_xpixel: u16,
    ws_ypixel: u16,
}

static mut ORIG_TERMIOS: Option<Termios> = None;

pub fn enable_raw_mode() {
    unsafe {
        let mut raw = std::mem::zeroed::<Termios>();
        tcgetattr(STDIN_FD, &mut raw);
        ORIG_TERMIOS = Some(raw.clone());

        raw.c_iflag &= !(IXON | ICRNL);
        raw.c_oflag &= !OPOST;
        raw.c_lflag &= !(ECHO | ICANON | ISIG);
        // min bytes = 0, timeout = 1 (100ms)
        raw.c_cc[6] = 0; // VMIN
        raw.c_cc[5] = 1; // VTIME

        tcsetattr(STDIN_FD, TCSAFLUSH, &raw);
    }
}

pub fn disable_raw_mode() {
    unsafe {
        if let Some(ref orig) = ORIG_TERMIOS {
            tcsetattr(STDIN_FD, TCSAFLUSH, orig);
        }
    }
}

pub fn size() -> (u16, u16) {
    unsafe {
        let mut ws = std::mem::zeroed::<Winsize>();
        if ioctl(STDIN_FD, TIOCGWINSZ, &mut ws) == 0 && ws.ws_col > 0 {
            (ws.ws_col, ws.ws_row)
        } else {
            (80, 24)
        }
    }
}

pub fn read_key() -> Option<Key> {
    let mut buf = [0u8; 4];
    let stdin = io::stdin();
    let mut handle = stdin.lock();
    match handle.read(&mut buf) {
        Ok(0) => None,
        Ok(1) => match buf[0] {
            b'q' | b'Q' => Some(Key::Quit),
            b'\x1b' => Some(Key::Esc),
            b'1' => Some(Key::Num(1)),
            b'2' => Some(Key::Num(2)),
            b'3' => Some(Key::Num(3)),
            b'4' => Some(Key::Num(4)),
            b'5' => Some(Key::Num(5)),
            b'j' | b'J' => Some(Key::Down),
            b'k' | b'K' => Some(Key::Up),
            b'\n' | b'\r' => Some(Key::Enter),
            b'\t' => Some(Key::Tab),
            _ => None,
        },
        Ok(n) if n >= 3 && buf[0] == b'\x1b' && buf[1] == b'[' => match buf[2] {
            b'A' => Some(Key::Up),
            b'B' => Some(Key::Down),
            b'C' => Some(Key::Right),
            b'D' => Some(Key::Left),
            _ => None,
        },
        _ => None,
    }
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq)]
pub enum Key {
    Quit,
    Esc,
    Up,
    Down,
    Left,
    Right,
    Enter,
    Tab,
    Num(u8),
}

// ANSI helpers
pub struct Screen {
    buf: String,
}

impl Screen {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        Self { buf: String::with_capacity(4096) }
    }

    pub fn clear(&mut self) {
        self.buf.clear();
        self.buf.push_str("\x1b[2J\x1b[H");
    }

    pub fn hide_cursor(&mut self) {
        self.buf.push_str("\x1b[?25l");
    }

    pub fn show_cursor(&mut self) {
        self.buf.push_str("\x1b[?25h");
    }

    pub fn goto(&mut self, x: u16, y: u16) {
        self.buf.push_str(&format!("\x1b[{};{}H", y + 1, x + 1));
    }

    pub fn fg(&mut self, color: Color) {
        self.buf.push_str(color.fg());
    }

    pub fn bg(&mut self, color: Color) {
        self.buf.push_str(color.bg());
    }

    pub fn reset(&mut self) {
        self.buf.push_str("\x1b[0m");
    }

    pub fn bold(&mut self) {
        self.buf.push_str("\x1b[1m");
    }

    pub fn dim(&mut self) {
        self.buf.push_str("\x1b[2m");
    }

    pub fn write(&mut self, s: &str) {
        self.buf.push_str(s);
    }

    #[allow(dead_code)]
    pub fn write_at(&mut self, x: u16, y: u16, s: &str) {
        self.goto(x, y);
        self.buf.push_str(s);
    }

    pub fn hline(&mut self, x: u16, y: u16, ch: char, len: u16) {
        self.goto(x, y);
        for _ in 0..len {
            self.buf.push(ch);
        }
    }

    pub fn flush(&self) {
        let mut stdout = io::stdout().lock();
        let _ = stdout.write_all(self.buf.as_bytes());
        let _ = stdout.flush();
    }
}

#[derive(Clone, Copy)]
#[allow(dead_code)]
pub enum Color {
    Black,
    Red,
    Green,
    Yellow,
    Blue,
    Magenta,
    Cyan,
    White,
    Gray,
    BrightGreen,
    BrightRed,
    BrightYellow,
    Rgb(u8, u8, u8),
}

impl Color {
    pub fn fg(self) -> &'static str {
        match self {
            Color::Black => "\x1b[30m",
            Color::Red => "\x1b[31m",
            Color::Green => "\x1b[32m",
            Color::Yellow => "\x1b[33m",
            Color::Blue => "\x1b[34m",
            Color::Magenta => "\x1b[35m",
            Color::Cyan => "\x1b[36m",
            Color::White => "\x1b[37m",
            Color::Gray => "\x1b[90m",
            Color::BrightGreen => "\x1b[92m",
            Color::BrightRed => "\x1b[91m",
            Color::BrightYellow => "\x1b[93m",
            Color::Rgb(_, _, _) => "\x1b[37m", // fallback
        }
    }

    pub fn bg(self) -> &'static str {
        match self {
            Color::Black => "\x1b[40m",
            Color::Red => "\x1b[41m",
            Color::Green => "\x1b[42m",
            Color::Yellow => "\x1b[43m",
            Color::Blue => "\x1b[44m",
            Color::Magenta => "\x1b[45m",
            Color::Cyan => "\x1b[46m",
            Color::White => "\x1b[47m",
            Color::Gray => "\x1b[100m",
            Color::BrightGreen => "\x1b[102m",
            Color::BrightRed => "\x1b[101m",
            Color::BrightYellow => "\x1b[103m",
            Color::Rgb(_, _, _) => "\x1b[40m",
        }
    }
}
```
