`crates/vigil-tui/src/ui.rs`:

```rs
// TUI rendering — draws the vigil dashboard

use crate::ipc::DaemonStatus;
use crate::term::{Color, Screen};

#[derive(Clone, Copy, PartialEq)]
pub enum Tab {
    Dashboard,
    Protection,
    Logs,
    Settings,
}

impl Tab {
    pub fn label(self) -> &'static str {
        match self {
            Tab::Dashboard => "Dashboard",
            Tab::Protection => "Protection",
            Tab::Logs => "Logs",
            Tab::Settings => "Settings",
        }
    }

    pub fn all() -> &'static [Tab] {
        &[Tab::Dashboard, Tab::Protection, Tab::Logs, Tab::Settings]
    }

    pub fn next(self) -> Tab {
        match self {
            Tab::Dashboard => Tab::Protection,
            Tab::Protection => Tab::Logs,
            Tab::Logs => Tab::Settings,
            Tab::Settings => Tab::Dashboard,
        }
    }
}

pub struct AppState {
    pub tab: Tab,
    pub status: DaemonStatus,
    pub logs: Vec<String>,
    #[allow(dead_code)]
    pub selected: usize,
}

impl AppState {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        Self {
            tab: Tab::Dashboard,
            status: DaemonStatus::default(),
            logs: Vec::new(),
            selected: 0,
        }
    }
}

pub fn draw(scr: &mut Screen, state: &AppState, w: u16, h: u16) {
    scr.clear();
    scr.hide_cursor();

    draw_header(scr, state, w);
    draw_tabs(scr, state, w);

    let content_y = 4;
    let content_h = h.saturating_sub(6);

    match state.tab {
        Tab::Dashboard => draw_dashboard(scr, state, w, content_y, content_h),
        Tab::Protection => draw_protection(scr, state, w, content_y, content_h),
        Tab::Logs => draw_logs(scr, state, w, content_y, content_h),
        Tab::Settings => draw_settings(scr, state, w, content_y, content_h),
    }

    draw_footer(scr, w, h);
    scr.flush();
}

fn draw_header(scr: &mut Screen, state: &AppState, w: u16) {
    scr.goto(0, 0);
    scr.bg(Color::Black);

    // logo
    scr.bold();
    scr.fg(Color::BrightGreen);
    scr.write(" VIGIL ");
    scr.reset();
    scr.fg(Color::Gray);
    scr.write("v0.3.0");

    // status on the right
    let status_str = if state.status.banned {
        "BANNED"
    } else if state.status.running {
        "ACTIVE"
    } else {
        "OFFLINE"
    };

    let status_color = if state.status.banned {
        Color::BrightRed
    } else if state.status.running {
        Color::BrightGreen
    } else {
        Color::Yellow
    };

    let right_start = w.saturating_sub(status_str.len() as u16 + 4);
    scr.goto(right_start, 0);
    scr.fg(status_color);
    scr.bold();
    scr.write(&format!(" {} ", status_str));
    scr.reset();

    // separator
    scr.goto(0, 1);
    scr.fg(Color::Gray);
    scr.hline(0, 1, '─', w);
}

fn draw_tabs(scr: &mut Screen, state: &AppState, _w: u16) {
    scr.goto(1, 2);
    for (i, tab) in Tab::all().iter().enumerate() {
        let num = i + 1;
        if *tab == state.tab {
            scr.fg(Color::Black);
            scr.bg(Color::BrightGreen);
            scr.bold();
            scr.write(&format!(" {} {} ", num, tab.label()));
            scr.reset();
        } else {
            scr.fg(Color::Gray);
            scr.write(&format!(" {} {} ", num, tab.label()));
        }
        scr.write(" ");
    }
    scr.reset();

    scr.fg(Color::Gray);
    scr.hline(0, 3, '─', _w);
}

fn draw_dashboard(scr: &mut Screen, state: &AppState, w: u16, y: u16, _h: u16) {
    let s = &state.status;

    // trust score bar
    let bar_y = y + 1;
    scr.goto(2, bar_y);
    scr.bold();
    scr.fg(Color::White);
    scr.write("Trust Score");
    scr.reset();

    let score = s.trust_score.clamp(0, 100) as u16;
    let bar_w = w.saturating_sub(6).min(60);
    let filled = (bar_w * score) / 100;

    scr.goto(2, bar_y + 1);
    scr.fg(Color::Gray);
    scr.write("[");

    let bar_color = if score >= 80 {
        Color::BrightGreen
    } else if score >= 50 {
        Color::Yellow
    } else {
        Color::BrightRed
    };

    scr.fg(bar_color);
    for _ in 0..filled {
        scr.write("█");
    }
    scr.fg(Color::Gray);
    for _ in filled..bar_w {
        scr.write("░");
    }
    scr.write(&format!("] {}%", score));
    scr.reset();

    // stats grid
    let stats_y = bar_y + 3;
    draw_stat(scr, 2, stats_y, "eBPF", if s.ebpf { "active" } else { "off" }, if s.ebpf { Color::BrightGreen } else { Color::Yellow });
    draw_stat(scr, 22, stats_y, "Profile", if s.profile.is_empty() { "none" } else { &s.profile }, Color::Cyan);
    draw_stat(scr, 42, stats_y, "Scans", &s.scan_count.to_string(), Color::White);

    let stats_y2 = stats_y + 3;
    draw_stat(scr, 2, stats_y2, "Daemon", if s.running { "running" } else { "stopped" }, if s.running { Color::BrightGreen } else { Color::BrightRed });
    draw_stat(scr, 22, stats_y2, "Status", if s.banned { "BANNED" } else { "clean" }, if s.banned { Color::BrightRed } else { Color::BrightGreen });

    // help
    let help_y = stats_y2 + 4;
    scr.goto(2, help_y);
    scr.fg(Color::Gray);
    scr.dim();
    scr.write("Refreshes every 3 seconds. Press 1-4 to switch tabs.");
    scr.reset();
}

fn draw_stat(scr: &mut Screen, x: u16, y: u16, label: &str, value: &str, color: Color) {
    scr.goto(x, y);
    scr.fg(Color::Gray);
    scr.write(label);
    scr.goto(x, y + 1);
    scr.fg(color);
    scr.bold();
    scr.write(value);
    scr.reset();
}

fn draw_protection(scr: &mut Screen, state: &AppState, w: u16, y: u16, _h: u16) {
    let modules = [
        ("eBPF Tracing", state.status.ebpf, "kernel-level syscall monitoring"),
        ("Process Scanner", state.status.running, "/proc enumeration and analysis"),
        ("Self-Protection", state.status.running, "anti-tamper and integrity checks"),
        ("Speedhack Detection", state.status.running, "clock drift monitoring"),
        ("Honeypot Traps", state.status.running, "fanotify-based deception files"),
        ("File Integrity", state.status.running, "inotify game file watching"),
        ("Network Monitor", state.status.running, "socket inode tracking"),
        ("Kernel Log Watch", state.status.running, "/dev/kmsg monitoring"),
    ];

    scr.goto(2, y + 1);
    scr.bold();
    scr.fg(Color::White);
    scr.write("Protection Modules");
    scr.reset();

    for (i, (name, active, desc)) in modules.iter().enumerate() {
        let row_y = y + 3 + (i as u16);
        scr.goto(2, row_y);

        if *active {
            scr.fg(Color::BrightGreen);
            scr.write(" ● ");
        } else {
            scr.fg(Color::BrightRed);
            scr.write(" ○ ");
        }

        scr.fg(Color::White);
        scr.bold();
        scr.write(name);
        scr.reset();

        let desc_x = 28u16.min(w.saturating_sub(40));
        scr.goto(desc_x, row_y);
        scr.fg(Color::Gray);
        scr.dim();
        let max_desc = (w.saturating_sub(desc_x + 2)) as usize;
        if desc.len() > max_desc {
            scr.write(&desc[..max_desc]);
        } else {
            scr.write(desc);
        }
        scr.reset();
    }
}

fn draw_logs(scr: &mut Screen, state: &AppState, w: u16, y: u16, h: u16) {
    scr.goto(2, y + 1);
    scr.bold();
    scr.fg(Color::White);
    scr.write("Recent Logs");
    scr.reset();

    if state.logs.is_empty() {
        scr.goto(2, y + 3);
        scr.fg(Color::Gray);
        scr.dim();
        scr.write("No logs yet. Waiting for daemon activity...");
        scr.reset();
        return;
    }

    let visible = h.saturating_sub(4) as usize;
    let start = state.logs.len().saturating_sub(visible);
    for (i, log) in state.logs[start..].iter().enumerate() {
        let row_y = y + 3 + i as u16;
        if row_y >= y + h {
            break;
        }
        scr.goto(2, row_y);
        scr.fg(Color::Gray);
        let max_w = w.saturating_sub(4) as usize;
        if log.len() > max_w {
            scr.write(&log[..max_w]);
        } else {
            scr.write(log);
        }
    }
    scr.reset();
}

fn draw_settings(scr: &mut Screen, state: &AppState, _w: u16, y: u16, _h: u16) {
    scr.goto(2, y + 1);
    scr.bold();
    scr.fg(Color::White);
    scr.write("Settings");
    scr.reset();

    let items = [
        ("Profile", if state.status.profile.is_empty() { "none" } else { &state.status.profile }),
        ("Daemon Socket", "/run/vigil.sock"),
        ("Config", "/etc/vigil/config.toml"),
        ("Queue Dir", "/var/lib/vigil/queue"),
    ];

    for (i, (label, value)) in items.iter().enumerate() {
        let row_y = y + 3 + (i as u16 * 2);
        scr.goto(2, row_y);
        scr.fg(Color::Gray);
        scr.write(label);
        scr.goto(20, row_y);
        scr.fg(Color::White);
        scr.write(value);
    }
    scr.reset();
}

fn draw_footer(scr: &mut Screen, w: u16, h: u16) {
    scr.fg(Color::Gray);
    scr.hline(0, h - 2, '─', w);

    scr.goto(1, h - 1);
    scr.fg(Color::Gray);
    scr.dim();
    scr.write(" q");
    scr.reset();
    scr.fg(Color::Gray);
    scr.write(" quit  ");
    scr.dim();
    scr.write("1-4");
    scr.reset();
    scr.fg(Color::Gray);
    scr.write(" tabs  ");
    scr.dim();
    scr.write("Tab");
    scr.reset();
    scr.fg(Color::Gray);
    scr.write(" next");
    scr.reset();

    // timestamp right
    let ts = vigil_common::timestamp::now_rfc3339();
    let ts_short = &ts[..19]; // "2026-03-27T01:23:45"
    let right = w.saturating_sub(ts_short.len() as u16 + 2);
    scr.goto(right, h - 1);
    scr.fg(Color::Gray);
    scr.dim();
    scr.write(ts_short);
    scr.reset();
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/bpf/elf.rs`:

```rs
const ELF_MAGIC: [u8; 4] = [0x7f, b'E', b'L', b'F'];

const SHT_PROGBITS: u32 = 1;
const SHT_SYMTAB: u32 = 2;
const SHT_REL: u32 = 9;

pub struct ElfFile<'a> {
    #[allow(dead_code)]
    data: &'a [u8],
    pub sections: Vec<Section<'a>>,
    pub symbols: Vec<Symbol>,
}

pub struct Section<'a> {
    pub name: String,
    pub sh_type: u32,
    pub data: &'a [u8],
    pub sh_info: u32,  // for REL sections: index of section being relocated
    pub sh_link: u32,  // for REL/SYMTAB: index of associated string/symbol table
    pub idx: usize,
}

pub struct Symbol {
    pub name: String,
    pub section_idx: u16,
    #[allow(dead_code)]
    pub value: u64,
}

pub struct Relocation {
    pub offset: u64,
    pub sym_idx: u32,
}

impl<'a> ElfFile<'a> {
    pub fn parse(data: &'a [u8]) -> Result<Self, String> {
        if data.len() < 64 {
            return Err("ELF too small".into());
        }

        // verify magic
        if data[0..4] != ELF_MAGIC {
            return Err("not an ELF file".into());
        }

        // verify ELF64 little-endian
        if data[4] != 2 {
            return Err("not ELF64".into());
        }
        if data[5] != 1 {
            return Err("not little-endian".into());
        }

        // read ELF header fields
        let e_shoff = u64_at(data, 40) as usize;     // section header table offset
        let e_shentsize = u16_at(data, 58) as usize;  // section header entry size
        let e_shnum = u16_at(data, 60) as usize;      // number of section headers
        let e_shstrndx = u16_at(data, 62) as usize;   // section name string table index

        if e_shoff == 0 || e_shnum == 0 {
            return Err("no section headers".into());
        }

        // first pass: read raw section headers
        let mut raw_sections: Vec<RawSectionHeader> = Vec::with_capacity(e_shnum);
        for i in 0..e_shnum {
            let off = e_shoff + i * e_shentsize;
            if off + e_shentsize > data.len() {
                return Err(format!("section header {} out of bounds", i));
            }
            raw_sections.push(RawSectionHeader {
                sh_name: u32_at(data, off),
                sh_type: u32_at(data, off + 4),
                sh_offset: u64_at(data, off + 24) as usize,
                sh_size: u64_at(data, off + 32) as usize,
                sh_link: u32_at(data, off + 40),
                sh_info: u32_at(data, off + 44),
            });
        }

        // get section name string table
        let shstrtab = &raw_sections[e_shstrndx];
        let shstrtab_data = &data[shstrtab.sh_offset..shstrtab.sh_offset + shstrtab.sh_size];

        // build sections with names
        let mut sections = Vec::with_capacity(e_shnum);
        for (i, raw) in raw_sections.iter().enumerate() {
            let name = read_str(shstrtab_data, raw.sh_name as usize);
            let sec_data = if raw.sh_size > 0 && raw.sh_offset + raw.sh_size <= data.len() {
                &data[raw.sh_offset..raw.sh_offset + raw.sh_size]
            } else {
                &[]
            };
            sections.push(Section {
                name,
                sh_type: raw.sh_type,
                data: sec_data,
                sh_info: raw.sh_info,
                sh_link: raw.sh_link,
                idx: i,
            });
        }

        // find symbol table and its string table
        let mut symbols = Vec::new();
        for sec in &sections {
            if sec.sh_type == SHT_SYMTAB {
                let strtab_idx = sec.sh_link as usize;
                let strtab_data = sections[strtab_idx].data;
                let entry_size = 24; // sizeof(Elf64_Sym)
                let count = sec.data.len() / entry_size;

                for i in 0..count {
                    let off = i * entry_size;
                    let st_name = u32_at(sec.data, off) as usize;
                    let st_info = sec.data[off + 4];
                    let st_shndx = u16_at(sec.data, off + 6);
                    let st_value = u64_at(sec.data, off + 8);

                    let _ = st_info; // we don't filter by binding/type

                    symbols.push(Symbol {
                        name: read_str(strtab_data, st_name),
                        section_idx: st_shndx,
                        value: st_value,
                    });
                }
                break; // only one SYMTAB
            }
        }

        Ok(ElfFile {
            data,
            sections,
            symbols,
        })
    }

    // returns (section, attach_point) for BPF program sections
    // e.g. "tracepoint/syscalls/sys_enter_ptrace" -> (section, "syscalls/sys_enter_ptrace")
    // e.g. "kprobe/do_init_module" -> (section, "do_init_module")
    pub fn program_sections(&self) -> Vec<(&Section<'a>, &str)> {
        let mut result = Vec::new();
        for sec in &self.sections {
            if sec.sh_type != SHT_PROGBITS || sec.data.is_empty() {
                continue;
            }
            if sec.name.starts_with("tracepoint/") {
                let attach = &sec.name["tracepoint/".len()..];
                result.push((sec, attach));
            } else if sec.name.starts_with("kprobe/") {
                let attach = &sec.name["kprobe/".len()..];
                result.push((sec, attach));
            }
        }
        result
    }

    // get relocations for a given section index
    pub fn relocations_for(&self, section_idx: usize) -> Vec<Relocation> {
        let mut result = Vec::new();
        for sec in &self.sections {
            if sec.sh_type == SHT_REL && sec.sh_info as usize == section_idx {
                let entry_size = 16; // sizeof(Elf64_Rel)
                let count = sec.data.len() / entry_size;
                for i in 0..count {
                    let off = i * entry_size;
                    let r_offset = u64_at(sec.data, off);
                    let r_info = u64_at(sec.data, off + 8);
                    let sym_idx = (r_info >> 32) as u32;
                    result.push(Relocation {
                        offset: r_offset,
                        sym_idx,
                    });
                }
            }
        }
        result
    }

    // find section by name
    pub fn section_by_name(&self, name: &str) -> Option<&Section<'a>> {
        self.sections.iter().find(|s| s.name == name)
    }
}

struct RawSectionHeader {
    sh_name: u32,
    sh_type: u32,
    sh_offset: usize,
    sh_size: usize,
    sh_link: u32,
    sh_info: u32,
}

// read a null-terminated string from a string table
fn read_str(data: &[u8], offset: usize) -> String {
    if offset >= data.len() {
        return String::new();
    }
    let end = data[offset..]
        .iter()
        .position(|&b| b == 0)
        .unwrap_or(data.len() - offset);
    String::from_utf8_lossy(&data[offset..offset + end]).into_owned()
}

fn u16_at(data: &[u8], off: usize) -> u16 {
    u16::from_le_bytes([data[off], data[off + 1]])
}

fn u32_at(data: &[u8], off: usize) -> u32 {
    u32::from_le_bytes([data[off], data[off + 1], data[off + 2], data[off + 3]])
}

fn u64_at(data: &[u8], off: usize) -> u64 {
    u64::from_le_bytes([
        data[off],
        data[off + 1],
        data[off + 2],
        data[off + 3],
        data[off + 4],
        data[off + 5],
        data[off + 6],
        data[off + 7],
    ])
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn reject_too_small() {
        let data = [0u8; 32];
        assert!(ElfFile::parse(&data).is_err());
    }

    #[test]
    fn reject_bad_magic() {
        let mut data = [0u8; 128];
        data[0] = 0x00; // not 0x7f
        assert!(ElfFile::parse(&data).is_err());
    }

    #[test]
    fn reject_not_elf64() {
        let mut data = [0u8; 128];
        data[0..4].copy_from_slice(&[0x7f, b'E', b'L', b'F']);
        data[4] = 1; // ELF32, not ELF64
        assert!(ElfFile::parse(&data).is_err());
    }

    #[test]
    fn reject_big_endian() {
        let mut data = [0u8; 128];
        data[0..4].copy_from_slice(&[0x7f, b'E', b'L', b'F']);
        data[4] = 2; // ELF64
        data[5] = 2; // big-endian
        assert!(ElfFile::parse(&data).is_err());
    }

    #[test]
    fn u16_at_works() {
        let data = [0x34, 0x12];
        assert_eq!(u16_at(&data, 0), 0x1234);
    }

    #[test]
    fn u32_at_works() {
        let data = [0x78, 0x56, 0x34, 0x12];
        assert_eq!(u32_at(&data, 0), 0x12345678);
    }

    #[test]
    fn u64_at_works() {
        let data = [0x01, 0x02, 0x03, 0x04, 0x05, 0x06, 0x07, 0x08];
        assert_eq!(u64_at(&data, 0), 0x0807060504030201);
    }

    #[test]
    fn read_str_basic() {
        let data = b"hello\0world\0";
        assert_eq!(read_str(data, 0), "hello");
        assert_eq!(read_str(data, 6), "world");
    }

    #[test]
    fn read_str_out_of_bounds() {
        let data = b"test\0";
        assert_eq!(read_str(data, 100), "");
    }

    #[test]
    fn read_str_empty_at_null() {
        let data = b"\0abc";
        assert_eq!(read_str(data, 0), "");
    }
}

```

`crates/vigil/src/bpf/loader.rs`:

```rs
use std::collections::HashMap;
use std::error::Error;
use std::os::fd::RawFd;

use crate::bpf::elf::ElfFile;
use crate::sys;

const BPF_PSEUDO_MAP_FD: u8 = 1;

pub struct BpfLoader {
    pub prog_fds: Vec<RawFd>,
    pub map_fds: HashMap<String, RawFd>,
    pub event_fds: Vec<RawFd>,
}

impl BpfLoader {
    pub fn load(path: &str) -> Result<Self, Box<dyn Error>> {
        let data = std::fs::read(path)?;
        let elf = ElfFile::parse(&data)?;

        let mut map_fds: HashMap<String, RawFd> = HashMap::new();

        let nr_cpus = sys::nr_cpus() as u32;

        // find map symbols and create perf event array maps
        if let Some(maps_sec) = elf.section_by_name("maps").or_else(|| elf.section_by_name(".maps")) {
            for sym in &elf.symbols {
                if sym.section_idx as usize == maps_sec.idx && !sym.name.is_empty() {
                    let fd = sys::bpf_map_create(
                        sys::BPF_MAP_TYPE_PERF_EVENT_ARRAY,
                        4, // key_size (u32 = cpu index)
                        4, // value_size (u32 = fd)
                        nr_cpus,
                    )?;
                    map_fds.insert(sym.name.clone(), fd);
                }
            }
        }

        let mut prog_fds = Vec::new();
        let license = b"GPL\0";

        for (sec, _attach_point) in elf.program_sections() {
            let prog_type = if sec.name.starts_with("tracepoint/") {
                sys::BPF_PROG_TYPE_TRACEPOINT
            } else if sec.name.starts_with("kprobe/") {
                sys::BPF_PROG_TYPE_KPROBE
            } else {
                continue;
            };

            // patch map fds into BPF instructions
            let mut insns = sec.data.to_vec();
            let relocs = elf.relocations_for(sec.idx);

            for reloc in &relocs {
                let sym = &elf.symbols[reloc.sym_idx as usize];
                if let Some(&map_fd) = map_fds.get(&sym.name) {
                    let off = reloc.offset as usize;
                    if off + 8 <= insns.len() {
                        // set src_reg = BPF_PSEUDO_MAP_FD, imm = map_fd
                        insns[off + 1] = (insns[off + 1] & 0x0f) | (BPF_PSEUDO_MAP_FD << 4);
                        insns[off + 4..off + 8].copy_from_slice(&map_fd.to_le_bytes());
                    }
                }
            }

            let mut log_buf = vec![0u8; 4096];
            match sys::bpf_prog_load(prog_type, &insns, license, &mut log_buf) {
                Ok(fd) => prog_fds.push(fd),
                Err(e) => {
                    let log_str = String::from_utf8_lossy(&log_buf);
                    let log_str = log_str.trim_end_matches('\0');
                    return Err(format!(
                        "failed to load BPF program {}: {} (verifier: {})",
                        sec.name, e, log_str
                    ).into());
                }
            }
        }

        Ok(BpfLoader {
            prog_fds,
            map_fds,
            event_fds: Vec::new(),
        })
    }

    pub fn attach_all(&mut self, elf_path: &str) -> Result<(), Box<dyn Error>> {
        let data = std::fs::read(elf_path)?;
        let elf = ElfFile::parse(&data)?;

        let programs = elf.program_sections();

        for (i, (sec, attach_point)) in programs.iter().enumerate() {
            if i >= self.prog_fds.len() {
                break;
            }
            let prog_fd = self.prog_fds[i];

            if sec.name.starts_with("tracepoint/") {
                let event_fd = attach_tracepoint(prog_fd, attach_point)?;
                self.event_fds.push(event_fd);
            } else if sec.name.starts_with("kprobe/") {
                let event_fd = attach_kprobe(prog_fd, attach_point)?;
                self.event_fds.push(event_fd);
            }
        }

        Ok(())
    }

    pub fn get_map_fd(&self, name: &str) -> Option<RawFd> {
        self.map_fds.get(name).copied()
    }
}

impl Drop for BpfLoader {
    // TODO(rmmod-protection): eBPF programs are not kernel modules so rmmod does not apply,
    // but closing these event_fds detaches the kprobes. An adversary with root can forcibly
    // close our fds (e.g. via /proc/PID/fd) to silently disable hooks. Consider pinning
    // programs into the BPF filesystem (/sys/fs/bpf/) so they survive vigil's death, and
    // checking at startup whether a previously pinned program is still active.
    fn drop(&mut self) {
        for &fd in &self.event_fds {
            let _ = sys::sys_ioctl(fd, sys::PERF_EVENT_IOC_DISABLE, 0);
            sys::sys_close(fd);
        }
        for &fd in &self.prog_fds {
            sys::sys_close(fd);
        }
        for &fd in self.map_fds.values() {
            sys::sys_close(fd);
        }
    }
}

fn attach_tracepoint(prog_fd: RawFd, attach_point: &str) -> Result<RawFd, Box<dyn Error>> {
    let parts: Vec<&str> = attach_point.splitn(2, '/').collect();
    if parts.len() != 2 {
        return Err(format!("invalid tracepoint: {}", attach_point).into());
    }
    let category = parts[0];
    let name = parts[1];

    let id = read_tracepoint_id(category, name)?;

    let attr = sys::PerfEventAttr {
        pe_type: sys::PERF_TYPE_TRACEPOINT,
        size: std::mem::size_of::<sys::PerfEventAttr>() as u32,
        config: id,
        sample_period_or_freq: 0,
        sample_type: 0,
        read_format: 0,
        flags: 0,
        wakeup_events_or_watermark: 0,
        bp_type: 0,
        config1: 0,
        config2: 0,
        branch_sample_type: 0,
        sample_regs_user: 0,
        sample_stack_user: 0,
        clockid: 0,
        sample_regs_intr: 0,
        aux_watermark: 0,
        sample_max_stack: 0,
        reserved: 0,
    };

    let event_fd = sys::sys_perf_event_open(&attr, -1, 0, -1, sys::PERF_FLAG_FD_CLOEXEC)?;
    sys::sys_ioctl(event_fd, sys::PERF_EVENT_IOC_SET_BPF, prog_fd as u64)?;
    sys::sys_ioctl(event_fd, sys::PERF_EVENT_IOC_ENABLE, 0)?;

    Ok(event_fd)
}

fn attach_kprobe(prog_fd: RawFd, func_name: &str) -> Result<RawFd, Box<dyn Error>> {
    let event_name = format!("vigil_{}", func_name);

    let probe_def = format!("p:kprobes/{} {}", event_name, func_name);

    let kprobe_path = if std::path::Path::new("/sys/kernel/tracing/kprobe_events").exists() {
        "/sys/kernel/tracing/kprobe_events"
    } else {
        "/sys/kernel/debug/tracing/kprobe_events"
    };

    std::fs::write(kprobe_path, &probe_def)?;

    let id_path = format!(
        "{}/events/kprobes/{}/id",
        if kprobe_path.contains("debug") {
            "/sys/kernel/debug/tracing"
        } else {
            "/sys/kernel/tracing"
        },
        event_name
    );

    let id: u64 = std::fs::read_to_string(&id_path)?
        .trim()
        .parse()
        .map_err(|_| format!("bad kprobe id in {}", id_path))?;

    let attr = sys::PerfEventAttr {
        pe_type: sys::PERF_TYPE_TRACEPOINT,
        size: std::mem::size_of::<sys::PerfEventAttr>() as u32,
        config: id,
        sample_period_or_freq: 0,
        sample_type: 0,
        read_format: 0,
        flags: 0,
        wakeup_events_or_watermark: 0,
        bp_type: 0,
        config1: 0,
        config2: 0,
        branch_sample_type: 0,
        sample_regs_user: 0,
        sample_stack_user: 0,
        clockid: 0,
        sample_regs_intr: 0,
        aux_watermark: 0,
        sample_max_stack: 0,
        reserved: 0,
    };

    let event_fd = sys::sys_perf_event_open(&attr, -1, 0, -1, sys::PERF_FLAG_FD_CLOEXEC)?;

    sys::sys_ioctl(event_fd, sys::PERF_EVENT_IOC_SET_BPF, prog_fd as u64)?;
    sys::sys_ioctl(event_fd, sys::PERF_EVENT_IOC_ENABLE, 0)?;

    Ok(event_fd)
}

fn read_tracepoint_id(category: &str, name: &str) -> Result<u64, Box<dyn Error>> {
    let paths = [
        format!("/sys/kernel/tracing/events/{}/{}/id", category, name),
        format!(
            "/sys/kernel/debug/tracing/events/{}/{}/id",
            category, name
        ),
    ];

    for path in &paths {
        if let Ok(content) = std::fs::read_to_string(path)
            && let Ok(id) = content.trim().parse::<u64>() {
                return Ok(id);
            }
    }

    Err(format!("tracepoint {}/{} not found", category, name).into())
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/bpf/perf.rs`:

```rs
// perf ring buffer reader, one per CPU

use std::os::fd::RawFd;

use crate::sys;

const DATA_HEAD_OFFSET: usize = 0x40;
const DATA_TAIL_OFFSET: usize = 0x48;

#[repr(C)]
struct PerfEventHeader {
    pe_type: u32,
    misc: u16,
    size: u16,
}

const PERF_RECORD_SAMPLE: u32 = 9;
const PERF_RECORD_LOST: u32 = 2;

pub struct PerfBuffer {
    fds: Vec<RawFd>,
    mmaps: Vec<*mut u8>,
    mmap_size: usize,
    data_size: usize,
}

// only accessed from one thread, mmap ptrs valid for lifetime of fds
unsafe impl Send for PerfBuffer {}

impl PerfBuffer {
    // open perf ring buffers for all CPUs and wire them into the BPF map
    pub fn open(map_fd: RawFd) -> Result<Self, Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {
        let nr_cpus = sys::nr_cpus();
        let page_size = sys::page_size();
        let nr_pages = 16; // 16 data pages = 64KB per CPU
        let mmap_size = (1 + nr_pages) * page_size; // 1 metadata page + data pages
        let data_size = nr_pages * page_size;

        let mut fds = Vec::with_capacity(nr_cpus);
        let mut mmaps = Vec::with_capacity(nr_cpus);

        for cpu in 0..nr_cpus {
            let attr = sys::PerfEventAttr {
                pe_type: 1, // PERF_TYPE_SOFTWARE
                size: std::mem::size_of::<sys::PerfEventAttr>() as u32,
                config: sys::PERF_COUNT_SW_BPF_OUTPUT,
                sample_period_or_freq: 1,
                sample_type: sys::PERF_SAMPLE_RAW,
                read_format: 0,
                flags: 0, // will be set by kernel
                wakeup_events_or_watermark: 1,
                bp_type: 0,
                config1: 0,
                config2: 0,
                branch_sample_type: 0,
                sample_regs_user: 0,
                sample_stack_user: 0,
                clockid: 0,
                sample_regs_intr: 0,
                aux_watermark: 0,
                sample_max_stack: 0,
                reserved: 0,
            };

            let fd = sys::sys_perf_event_open(
                &attr,
                -1,          // pid = -1 (all processes)
                cpu as i32,  // cpu
                -1,          // group_fd
                sys::PERF_FLAG_FD_CLOEXEC,
            )?;

            let ptr = sys::sys_mmap(fd, mmap_size)?;
            sys::sys_ioctl(fd, sys::PERF_EVENT_IOC_ENABLE, 0)?;

            let key = (cpu as u32).to_ne_bytes();
            let val = (fd as u32).to_ne_bytes();
            sys::bpf_map_update_elem(map_fd, &key, &val)?;

            fds.push(fd);
            mmaps.push(ptr);
        }

        Ok(PerfBuffer {
            fds,
            mmaps,
            mmap_size,
            data_size,
        })
    }

    pub fn fds(&self) -> &[RawFd] {
        &self.fds
    }

    pub fn read_events<F>(&self, cpu: usize, mut callback: F)
    where
        F: FnMut(&[u8]),
    {
        if cpu >= self.mmaps.len() {
            return;
        }

        let base = self.mmaps[cpu];
        let page_size = sys::page_size();

        let data_head = unsafe {
            let ptr = base.add(DATA_HEAD_OFFSET) as *const u64;
            std::sync::atomic::fence(std::sync::atomic::Ordering::Acquire);
            ptr.read_volatile()
        };

        let data_tail = unsafe {
            let ptr = base.add(DATA_TAIL_OFFSET) as *const u64;
            ptr.read_volatile()
        };

        if data_head == data_tail {
            return; // no new events
        }

        let data_start = base.wrapping_add(page_size);
        let mut tail = data_tail;

        while tail < data_head {
            let offset = (tail as usize) % self.data_size;

            // read event header
            let header = unsafe {
                let ptr = data_start.add(offset) as *const PerfEventHeader;
                ptr.read_unaligned()
            };

            if header.size == 0 {
                break;
            }

            if header.pe_type == PERF_RECORD_LOST {
                // PERF_RECORD_LOST: 8-byte id + 8-byte count follow the header
                let lost_offset = (offset + std::mem::size_of::<PerfEventHeader>()) % self.data_size;
                let lost_count = unsafe {
                    let ptr = data_start.add(lost_offset + 8) as *const u64;
                    ptr.read_unaligned()
                };
                eprintln!("[eBPF] WARNING: {} event(s) dropped from perf ring buffer on cpu {}", lost_count, cpu);
            } else if header.pe_type == PERF_RECORD_SAMPLE {
                let sample_offset = (offset + std::mem::size_of::<PerfEventHeader>()) % self.data_size;
                let sample_size = unsafe {
                    let ptr = data_start.add(sample_offset) as *const u32;
                    ptr.read_unaligned() as usize
                };

                let data_offset = (sample_offset + 4) % self.data_size;

                if data_offset + sample_size <= self.data_size {
                    let slice = unsafe {
                        std::slice::from_raw_parts(data_start.add(data_offset), sample_size)
                    };
                    callback(slice);
                } else {
                    // wraps around ring buffer
                    let mut buf = vec![0u8; sample_size];
                    let first = self.data_size - data_offset;
                    unsafe {
                        std::ptr::copy_nonoverlapping(
                            data_start.add(data_offset),
                            buf.as_mut_ptr(),
                            first,
                        );
                        std::ptr::copy_nonoverlapping(
                            data_start,
                            buf.as_mut_ptr().add(first),
                            sample_size - first,
                        );
                    }
                    callback(&buf);
                }
            }

            tail += header.size as u64;
        }

        unsafe {
            let ptr = base.add(DATA_TAIL_OFFSET) as *mut u64;
            ptr.write_volatile(data_head);
            std::sync::atomic::fence(std::sync::atomic::Ordering::Release);
        }
    }
}

impl Drop for PerfBuffer {
    fn drop(&mut self) {
        for &ptr in &self.mmaps {
            let _ = sys::sys_munmap(ptr, self.mmap_size);
        }
        for &fd in &self.fds {
            let _ = sys::sys_ioctl(fd, sys::PERF_EVENT_IOC_DISABLE, 0);
            sys::sys_close(fd);
        }
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/cli.rs`:

```rs
use std::collections::HashSet;

use crate::config::{
    check_hash, compare_hashes, get_cheat_db, get_config, get_game_dir, get_whitelist,
    load_baseline, save_baseline, scan_game_dir,
};
use crate::network::{get_connections, get_inode};
use crate::process::Suspicious;
use crate::scanner::{
    check_sandbox, get_cross_traces, get_fd, get_map, get_modules, get_process, scan_processes,
};

pub enum Commands {
    Scan,
    Check,
    Status,
    Init,
}

pub fn parse_args() -> Option<Commands> {
    let args: Vec<String> = std::env::args().collect();
    if args.len() < 2 {
        return None;
    }
    match args[1].as_str() {
        "scan" => Some(Commands::Scan),
        "check" => Some(Commands::Check),
        "status" => Some(Commands::Status),
        "init" => Some(Commands::Init),
        "--help" | "-h" => {
            println!("vigil - linux anti-cheat system\n");
            println!("usage: vigil [command]\n");
            println!("commands:");
            println!("  scan    one-time /proc scan");
            println!("  check   compare game files against baseline");
            println!("  status  show configuration and system readiness");
            println!("  init    create /etc/vigil/ with default configs");
            println!("\nno command = run as daemon");
            std::process::exit(0);
        }
        other => {
            eprintln!("unknown command: {}", other);
            eprintln!("run 'vigil --help' for usage");
            std::process::exit(1);
        }
    }
}

pub fn cmd_scan() {
    let whitelist = get_whitelist().unwrap_or_default();
    let cheat_db = get_cheat_db().unwrap_or_default();
    let mut found_maps: HashSet<String> = HashSet::new();

    if let Ok(reasons) = check_sandbox()
        && !reasons.is_empty()
    {
        println!("[ALERT] Sandbox environment detected: {:?}", reasons);
    }

    let pids = match scan_processes() {
        Ok(v) => v,
        Err(e) => {
            eprintln!("Failed to scan /proc: {}", e);
            return;
        }
    };

    let mut procs = vec![];

    for &pid in &pids {
        if let Ok(proc) = get_process(pid, &whitelist) {
            if let Ok(val) = get_map(pid, &mut found_maps, &whitelist)
                && !val.is_empty()
            {
                println!("[ALERT] {:?}", val);
            }

            if let Ok(val) = get_fd(pid)
                && !val.is_empty()
            {
                println!(
                    "[ALERT] Process {}, reading other process memory: {:?}",
                    pid, val
                );
            }

            if let Ok(inodes) = get_inode(pid)
                && !inodes.is_empty()
                && let Ok(connections) = get_connections(&inodes)
            {
                for conn in &connections {
                    println!("[NET] pid {} has connection: {}", pid, conn);
                }
            }

            if let Ok(Some((name, category, desc))) = check_hash(pid, &cheat_db) {
                println!(
                    "[CHEAT] pid {} matched: {} [{}] - {}",
                    pid, name, category, desc
                );
            }

            if proc.is_suspicious() {
                println!("[ALERT] {:?}", proc);
            }

            procs.push(proc);
        }
    }

    let cross_traced = get_cross_traces(&procs);
    for (tracer, targets) in &cross_traced {
        if targets.len() > 1 {
            println!(
                "[ALERT] Tracer pid {} traces multiple processes: {:?}",
                tracer, targets
            );
        }
    }

    if let Ok(modules) = get_modules() {
        for m in &modules {
            println!("[MODULE] {}", m);
        }
    }

    println!("[SCAN] Done. Scanned {} processes.", pids.len());
}

pub fn cmd_check() {
    let config = get_config().ok();
    let game_path = config
        .as_ref()
        .map(|c| c.game.path.clone())
        .or_else(|| get_game_dir().ok());

    let dir = match game_path {
        Some(d) => d,
        None => {
            eprintln!("No game directory configured (config.toml or game_dir.txt)");
            return;
        }
    };

    let baseline_path = "/etc/vigil/game_baseline.txt";

    let baseline = match load_baseline(baseline_path) {
        Ok(bl) => {
            println!("[CHECK] Baseline loaded ({} files)", bl.len());
            bl
        }
        Err(_) => {
            println!("[CHECK] No baseline found, creating...");
            match scan_game_dir(&dir) {
                Ok(hashes) => {
                    let _ = save_baseline(baseline_path, &hashes);
                    println!("[CHECK] Baseline created ({} files)", hashes.len());
                    println!("[CHECK] Run again to compare against this baseline.");
                    return;
                }
                Err(e) => {
                    eprintln!("[CHECK] Failed to scan game dir: {}", e);
                    return;
                }
            }
        }
    };

    let current = match scan_game_dir(&dir) {
        Ok(h) => h,
        Err(e) => {
            eprintln!("[CHECK] Failed to scan game dir: {}", e);
            return;
        }
    };

    let changes = compare_hashes(&baseline, &current);
    if changes.total() == 0 {
        println!("[CHECK] Game integrity OK - no changes since baseline.");
        return;
    }

    for f in &changes.modified {
        println!("[CHECK] MODIFIED: {}", f);
    }
    for f in &changes.added {
        println!("[CHECK] ADDED: {}", f);
    }
    for f in &changes.removed {
        println!("[CHECK] REMOVED: {}", f);
    }
    if changes.is_suspicious() {
        println!("[CHECK] Small targeted change - possible cheat injection.");
    }
    println!(
        "[CHECK] Total changes: {} modified, {} added, {} removed",
        changes.modified.len(),
        changes.added.len(),
        changes.removed.len()
    );
}

pub fn cmd_status() {
    println!("=== Vigil Status ===\n");

    let config = get_config().ok();

    match &config {
        Some(c) => {
            println!("[CONFIG] /etc/vigil/config.toml - OK");
            println!("  game path:  {}", c.game.path);
            println!("  log path:   {}", c.logging.path);
        }
        None => println!("[CONFIG] /etc/vigil/config.toml - not found"),
    }

    match get_whitelist() {
        Ok(w) => println!("[WHITELIST] {} entries loaded", w.len()),
        Err(_) => println!("[WHITELIST] not found (/etc/vigil/whitelist.txt)"),
    }

    match get_cheat_db() {
        Ok(db) => println!("[CHEAT DB] {} signatures loaded", db.len()),
        Err(_) => println!("[CHEAT DB] not found (/etc/vigil/cheat_hashes.txt)"),
    }

    let game_path = config.map(|c| c.game.path).or_else(|| get_game_dir().ok());

    match game_path {
        Some(dir) => {
            println!("[GAME DIR] {}", dir);
            if std::path::Path::new(&dir).is_dir() {
                println!("  directory exists: yes");
            } else {
                println!("  directory exists: no");
            }
        }
        None => println!("[GAME DIR] not configured"),
    }

    let baseline_path = "/etc/vigil/game_baseline.txt";
    match load_baseline(baseline_path) {
        Ok(bl) => println!("[BASELINE] {} files tracked", bl.len()),
        Err(_) => println!("[BASELINE] not found (run `vigil check` to create)"),
    }

    let ebpf_path = "./target/bpfel-unknown-none/release/vigil";
    if std::path::Path::new(ebpf_path).exists() {
        println!("[eBPF] bytecode found");
    } else {
        println!("[eBPF] bytecode not found (build with cargo +nightly)");
    }

    match check_sandbox() {
        Ok(reasons) if !reasons.is_empty() => {
            println!("[SANDBOX] detected: {:?}", reasons);
        }
        Ok(_) => println!("[SANDBOX] not detected"),
        Err(e) => println!("[SANDBOX] check failed: {}", e),
    }

    println!("\n=== Done ===");
}

pub fn cmd_init() {
    let vigil_dir = "/etc/vigil";

    if let Err(e) = std::fs::create_dir_all(vigil_dir) {
        eprintln!(
            "[INIT] Failed to create {}: {} (run with sudo)",
            vigil_dir, e
        );
        return;
    }
    println!("[INIT] {} - OK", vigil_dir);

    let config_path = format!("{}/config.toml", vigil_dir);
    if !std::path::Path::new(&config_path).exists() {
        let config_content = r#"[game]
path = "/home/user/.steam/steam/steamapps/common/GameName"
# profile = "cs2"

[logging]
path = "/var/log/vigil.log"

# Uncomment to enable server reporting
# [server]
# url = "http://localhost:3000"
# player_id = "your-player-name"
# password = "your-password"
"#;
        match std::fs::write(&config_path, config_content) {
            Ok(_) => println!("[INIT] {} - created (edit game path!)", config_path),
            Err(e) => eprintln!("[INIT] {} - failed: {}", config_path, e),
        }
    } else {
        println!("[INIT] {} - already exists", config_path);
    }

    let whitelist_path = format!("{}/whitelist.txt", vigil_dir);
    if !std::path::Path::new(&whitelist_path).exists() {
        let whitelist_content = "# system libraries
/usr/lib/
/usr/lib64/
/lib/
/lib64/
# steam/game libraries
libmozsandbox.so
libgamemodeauto.so
libsteam_api.so
libmangoapp.so
libmangohud.so
# flatpak/snap
/var/lib/flatpak/
/snap/
";
        match std::fs::write(&whitelist_path, whitelist_content) {
            Ok(_) => println!("[INIT] {} - created", whitelist_path),
            Err(e) => eprintln!("[INIT] {} - failed: {}", whitelist_path, e),
        }
    } else {
        println!("[INIT] {} - already exists", whitelist_path);
    }

    let cheat_path = format!("{}/cheat_hashes.txt", vigil_dir);
    if !std::path::Path::new(&cheat_path).exists() {
        let cheat_content = "# known cheat process names
name_only:aimbot:cheat:Generic aimbot process
name_only:wallhack:cheat:Generic wallhack process
name_only:csgo_cheat:cheat:CS cheat process
name_only:memwrite:injection:Memory writer tool
name_only:deadlocked:cheat:deadlocked external cheat
name_only:charlatano:cheat:Charlatano CS2 cheat
name_only:gamesneeze:cheat:GameSneeze CS cheat
name_only:osiris:cheat:Osiris CS cheat
name_only:fuzion:cheat:Fuzion CS cheat
name_only:pyhack:cheat:Python-based game hack
name_only:chams:cheat:Chams/wallhack tool
name_only:triggerbot:cheat:Triggerbot auto-fire
name_only:esp:cheat:ESP overlay hack
name_only:spinbot:cheat:Spinbot anti-aim
name_only:bhop:cheat:Bunny hop automation
# known injection/debug tools used for cheating
name_only:scanmem:injection:Memory scanner (GameConqueror backend)
name_only:gameconqueror:injection:GUI memory scanner/editor
name_only:cheatengine:injection:Cheat Engine
name_only:pince:injection:PINCE memory debugger
name_only:ce-server:injection:Cheat Engine server
";
        match std::fs::write(&cheat_path, cheat_content) {
            Ok(_) => println!("[INIT] {} - created", cheat_path),
            Err(e) => eprintln!("[INIT] {} - failed: {}", cheat_path, e),
        }
    } else {
        println!("[INIT] {} - already exists", cheat_path);
    }

    let log_path = "/var/log/vigil.log";
    if !std::path::Path::new(log_path).exists() {
        match std::fs::write(log_path, "") {
            Ok(_) => println!("[INIT] {} - created", log_path),
            Err(e) => eprintln!("[INIT] {} - failed: {}", log_path, e),
        }
    } else {
        println!("[INIT] {} - already exists", log_path);
    }

    println!("\n[INIT] Done. Edit {} to set your game path.", config_path);
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/client.rs`:

```rs
use crate::http_client;
use crate::json::{parse, json_obj, json_str, stringify};
use crate::report::ScanReport;

pub struct ReportResponse {
    pub banned: bool,
    pub ban_reason: Option<String>,
    pub trust_score: Option<u8>,
    pub challenge: Option<String>,
}

pub fn login(server_url: &str, name: &str, password: &str) -> Result<String, String> {
    let url = format!("{}/api/player/login", server_url);
    let body = stringify(&json_obj(vec![
        ("name", json_str(name)),
        ("password", json_str(password)),
    ]));

    let res = http_client::post_json(&url, &body, None)?;

    if res.status >= 400 {
        return Err(format!("login failed ({}): {}", res.status, res.body));
    }

    let v = parse(&res.body).map_err(|e| format!("bad login response: {}", e))?;
    let data = v.get("data").unwrap_or(&v);

    data.get("token")
        .and_then(|x| x.as_str())
        .map(|s| s.to_string())
        .ok_or_else(|| "no token in login response".to_string())
}

pub fn fetch_cheat_signatures(server_url: &str, token: Option<&str>) -> Result<String, String> {
    let url = format!("{}/api/cheat-signatures", server_url);

    let res = http_client::get(&url, token)?;

    if res.status >= 400 {
        return Err(format!("cheat-signatures fetch failed ({}): {}", res.status, res.body));
    }

    // server returns {"success":true,"data":"hash:name:cat:desc\n..."}
    // extract the raw text from the data field
    let v = parse(&res.body).map_err(|e| format!("bad cheat-signatures response: {}", e))?;
    let data = v.get("data").unwrap_or(&v);

    match data.as_str() {
        Some(s) => Ok(s.to_string()),
        None => Ok(res.body),
    }
}

pub fn send_report(server_url: &str, report: &ScanReport, token: Option<&str>) -> Result<ReportResponse, String> {
    let url = format!("{}/api/report", server_url);
    let body = crate::report::to_json(report);

    let res = http_client::post_json(&url, &body, token)?;

    if res.status >= 400 {
        return Err(format!("server returned {}: {}", res.status, res.body));
    }

    let mut resp = ReportResponse {
        banned: false,
        ban_reason: None,
        trust_score: None,
        challenge: None,
    };

    if let Ok(v) = parse(&res.body) {
        let data = v.get("data").unwrap_or(&v);

        if let Some(b) = data.get("banned").and_then(|x| x.as_bool()) {
            resp.banned = b;
        }
        if let Some(r) = data.get("reason").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
            resp.ban_reason = Some(r.to_string());
        }
        if let Some(s) = data.get("trust_score").and_then(|x| x.as_i64()) {
            resp.trust_score = Some(s as u8);
        }
        if let Some(c) = data.get("challenge").and_then(|x| x.as_str()) {
            resp.challenge = Some(c.to_string());
        }
    }

    Ok(resp)
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/config.rs`:

```rs
use std::collections::HashMap;
use std::fs::OpenOptions;
use std::io::Write;
use std::path::Path;

use crate::crypto::sha256_hex;
use crate::timestamp::now_local_fmt;
use crate::toml_parser::parse_config;

pub use crate::toml_parser::Config;

pub struct CheatEntry {
    pub hash: String,
    pub name: String,
    pub category: String,
    pub description: String,
}

pub enum LogLevel {
    Alert,
    Cheat,
    Net,
    Inotify,
    Info,
}

impl std::fmt::Display for LogLevel {
    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
        match self {
            LogLevel::Alert => write!(f, "[ALERT]"),
            LogLevel::Cheat => write!(f, "[CHEAT]"),
            LogLevel::Net => write!(f, "[NET]"),
            LogLevel::Inotify => write!(f, "[INOTIFY]"),
            LogLevel::Info => write!(f, "[INFO]"),
        }
    }
}

pub fn get_config() -> Result<Config, Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {
    let content = std::fs::read_to_string("/etc/vigil/config.toml")?;
    parse_config(&content).map_err(|e| e.into())
}

pub fn log(level: LogLevel, message: &str, path: &str) -> std::io::Result<()> {
    let time = now_local_fmt();
    let plain = format!("{} {} {}", time, level, message);

    let color = match level {
        LogLevel::Alert => "\x1b[91m",
        LogLevel::Cheat => "\x1b[1;91m",
        LogLevel::Net => "\x1b[36m",
        LogLevel::Inotify => "\x1b[33m",
        LogLevel::Info => "\x1b[32m",
    };
    println!("{}{}\x1b[0m", color, plain);

    let mut f = OpenOptions::new().append(true).create(true).open(path)?;
    writeln!(f, "{}", plain)?;

    Ok(())
}

pub fn get_whitelist() -> std::io::Result<Vec<String>> {
    let content = std::fs::read_to_string("/etc/vigil/whitelist.txt")?;
    let mut res = vec![];
    for line in content.lines() {
        let trimmed = line.trim();
        if !trimmed.is_empty() && !trimmed.starts_with('#') {
            res.push(trimmed.to_string());
        }
    }
    Ok(res)
}

pub fn get_cheat_db() -> std::io::Result<Vec<CheatEntry>> {
    let content = std::fs::read_to_string("/etc/vigil/cheat_hashes.txt")?;
    let mut res = vec![];

    for line in content.lines() {
        let line = line.trim();
        if line.is_empty() || line.starts_with('#') {
            continue;
        }
        let parts: Vec<&str> = line.splitn(4, ':').collect();
        if parts.len() == 4 {
            res.push(CheatEntry {
                hash: parts[0].to_string(),
                name: parts[1].to_string(),
                category: parts[2].to_string(),
                description: parts[3].to_string(),
            });
        }
    }

    Ok(res)
}

pub fn check_hash(
    pid: u64,
    cheat_db: &[CheatEntry],
) -> std::io::Result<Option<(String, String, String)>> {
    let exe_path = format!("/proc/{}/exe", pid);
    let real_path = std::fs::read_link(&exe_path)?;

    let exe_name = real_path.file_name().and_then(|n| n.to_str()).unwrap_or("");

    for entry in cheat_db {
        if entry.hash == "name_only" && exe_name == entry.name {
            return Ok(Some((
                entry.name.clone(),
                entry.category.clone(),
                entry.description.clone(),
            )));
        }
    }

    let has_hash_entries = cheat_db.iter().any(|e| e.hash != "name_only");

    if has_hash_entries {
        let binary = std::fs::read(&real_path)?;
        let hash = sha256_hex(&binary);

        for entry in cheat_db {
            if entry.hash != "name_only" && hash == entry.hash {
                return Ok(Some((
                    entry.name.clone(),
                    entry.category.clone(),
                    entry.description.clone(),
                )));
            }
        }
    }

    Ok(None)
}

pub struct FileChanges {
    pub modified: Vec<String>,
    pub added: Vec<String>,
    pub removed: Vec<String>,
}

impl FileChanges {
    pub fn total(&self) -> usize {
        self.modified.len() + self.added.len() + self.removed.len()
    }

    pub fn is_suspicious(&self) -> bool {
        self.total() > 0 && self.total() <= 2
    }
}

pub fn get_game_dir() -> std::io::Result<String> {
    let content = std::fs::read_to_string("/etc/vigil/game_dir.txt")?;
    Ok(content.trim().to_string())
}

pub fn scan_game_dir(dir: &str) -> std::io::Result<HashMap<String, String>> {
    let mut result = HashMap::new();
    scan_dir_recursive(Path::new(dir), &mut result)?;
    Ok(result)
}

fn scan_dir_recursive(dir: &Path, result: &mut HashMap<String, String>) -> std::io::Result<()> {
    for entry in std::fs::read_dir(dir)? {
        let entry = entry?;
        let path = entry.path();
        if path.is_dir() {
            scan_dir_recursive(&path, result)?;
        } else {
            let bytes = std::fs::read(&path)?;
            let hash = sha256_hex(&bytes);
            result.insert(path.to_string_lossy().to_string(), hash);
        }
    }
    Ok(())
}

pub fn load_baseline(path: &str) -> std::io::Result<HashMap<String, String>> {
    let content = std::fs::read_to_string(path)?;
    let mut result = HashMap::new();
    for line in content.lines() {
        if let Some((hash, file_path)) = line.split_once(':') {
            result.insert(file_path.to_string(), hash.to_string());
        }
    }
    Ok(result)
}

pub fn save_baseline(path: &str, hashes: &HashMap<String, String>) -> std::io::Result<()> {
    let mut content = String::new();
    for (file_path, hash) in hashes {
        content.push_str(&format!("{}:{}\n", hash, file_path));
    }
    std::fs::write(path, content)
}

pub fn compare_hashes(
    baseline: &HashMap<String, String>,
    current: &HashMap<String, String>,
) -> FileChanges {
    let mut modified = vec![];
    let mut added = vec![];
    let mut removed = vec![];

    for (path, hash) in current {
        match baseline.get(path) {
            Some(old_hash) if old_hash != hash => modified.push(path.clone()),
            None => added.push(path.clone()),
            _ => {}
        }
    }

    for path in baseline.keys() {
        if !current.contains_key(path) {
            removed.push(path.clone());
        }
    }

    FileChanges {
        modified,
        added,
        removed,
    }
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn compare_hashes_no_changes() {
        let mut baseline = HashMap::new();
        baseline.insert("/game/a.dll".to_string(), "abc123".to_string());
        baseline.insert("/game/b.dll".to_string(), "def456".to_string());

        let current = baseline.clone();
        let changes = compare_hashes(&baseline, &current);
        assert_eq!(changes.total(), 0);
        assert!(!changes.is_suspicious());
    }

    #[test]
    fn compare_hashes_modified() {
        let mut baseline = HashMap::new();
        baseline.insert("/game/a.dll".to_string(), "abc123".to_string());

        let mut current = HashMap::new();
        current.insert("/game/a.dll".to_string(), "CHANGED".to_string());

        let changes = compare_hashes(&baseline, &current);
        assert_eq!(changes.modified.len(), 1);
        assert_eq!(changes.added.len(), 0);
        assert_eq!(changes.removed.len(), 0);
        assert_eq!(changes.total(), 1);
        assert!(changes.is_suspicious()); // 1 change = suspicious
    }

    #[test]
    fn compare_hashes_added() {
        let baseline = HashMap::new();
        let mut current = HashMap::new();
        current.insert("/game/new.dll".to_string(), "aaa".to_string());

        let changes = compare_hashes(&baseline, &current);
        assert_eq!(changes.added.len(), 1);
        assert_eq!(changes.modified.len(), 0);
        assert_eq!(changes.removed.len(), 0);
    }

    #[test]
    fn compare_hashes_removed() {
        let mut baseline = HashMap::new();
        baseline.insert("/game/old.dll".to_string(), "bbb".to_string());

        let current = HashMap::new();
        let changes = compare_hashes(&baseline, &current);
        assert_eq!(changes.removed.len(), 1);
        assert_eq!(changes.added.len(), 0);
    }

    #[test]
    fn compare_hashes_many_changes_not_suspicious() {
        let mut baseline = HashMap::new();
        for i in 0..10 {
            baseline.insert(format!("/game/{}.dll", i), format!("old{}", i));
        }
        let mut current = HashMap::new();
        for i in 0..10 {
            current.insert(format!("/game/{}.dll", i), format!("new{}", i));
        }

        let changes = compare_hashes(&baseline, &current);
        assert_eq!(changes.total(), 10);
        assert!(!changes.is_suspicious());
    }

    #[test]
    fn file_changes_total() {
        let fc = FileChanges {
            modified: vec!["a".to_string()],
            added: vec!["b".to_string(), "c".to_string()],
            removed: vec![],
        };
        assert_eq!(fc.total(), 3);
    }

    #[test]
    fn load_baseline_roundtrip() {
        let dir = std::env::temp_dir().join("vigil_test_baseline");
        let path = dir.to_str().unwrap();

        let mut hashes = HashMap::new();
        hashes.insert("/game/test.dll".to_string(), "aabbcc".to_string());
        hashes.insert("/game/lib.so".to_string(), "ddeeff".to_string());

        save_baseline(path, &hashes).unwrap();
        let loaded = load_baseline(path).unwrap();

        assert_eq!(loaded.len(), 2);
        assert_eq!(loaded.get("/game/test.dll").unwrap(), "aabbcc");
        assert_eq!(loaded.get("/game/lib.so").unwrap(), "ddeeff");

        let _ = std::fs::remove_file(path);
    }

    #[test]
    fn log_level_display() {
        assert_eq!(format!("{}", LogLevel::Alert), "[ALERT]");
        assert_eq!(format!("{}", LogLevel::Cheat), "[CHEAT]");
        assert_eq!(format!("{}", LogLevel::Net), "[NET]");
        assert_eq!(format!("{}", LogLevel::Inotify), "[INOTIFY]");
        assert_eq!(format!("{}", LogLevel::Info), "[INFO]");
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/crypto.rs`:

```rs
pub use vigil_common::crypto::sha256_hex;
#[cfg(test)]
pub(crate) use vigil_common::crypto::to_hex;

use std::fs::File;
use std::io::Read;

// random bytes from /dev/urandom

#[allow(dead_code)]
pub fn random_bytes(buf: &mut [u8]) {
    let mut f = File::open("/dev/urandom").expect("failed to open /dev/urandom");
    f.read_exact(buf).expect("failed to read /dev/urandom");
}

#[allow(dead_code)]
fn random_bytes_array<const N: usize>() -> [u8; N] {
    let mut buf = [0u8; N];
    random_bytes(&mut buf);
    buf
}

// random uuid v4 (rfc 4122)
#[allow(dead_code)]
pub fn uuid_v4() -> String {
    let mut bytes = random_bytes_array::<16>();

    // set version to 4 (bits 4-7 of byte 6)
    bytes[6] = (bytes[6] & 0x0f) | 0x40;

    // set variant to 10xx (bits 6-7 of byte 8)
    bytes[8] = (bytes[8] & 0x3f) | 0x80;

    format!(
        "{:02x}{:02x}{:02x}{:02x}-{:02x}{:02x}-{:02x}{:02x}-{:02x}{:02x}-{:02x}{:02x}{:02x}{:02x}{:02x}{:02x}",
        bytes[0], bytes[1], bytes[2], bytes[3],
        bytes[4], bytes[5],
        bytes[6], bytes[7],
        bytes[8], bytes[9],
        bytes[10], bytes[11], bytes[12], bytes[13], bytes[14], bytes[15],
    )
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn test_sha256_empty() {
        let hash = sha256_hex(b"");
        assert_eq!(hash, "e3b0c44298fc1c149afbf4c8996fb92427ae41e4649b934ca495991b7852b855");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_sha256_hello() {
        let hash = sha256_hex(b"hello");
        assert_eq!(hash, "2cf24dba5fb0a30e26e83b2ac5b9e29e1b161e5c1fa7425e73043362938b9824");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_sha256_longer() {
        let data = b"The quick brown fox jumps over the lazy dog";
        let hash = sha256_hex(data);
        assert_eq!(hash, "d7a8fbb307d7809469ca9abcb0082e4f8d5651e46d3cdb762d02d0bf37c9e592");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_hex_roundtrip() {
        let data = [0xde, 0xad, 0xbe, 0xef, 0x00, 0xff];
        let hex = to_hex(&data);
        assert_eq!(hex, "deadbeef00ff");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_uuid_v4_format() {
        let id = uuid_v4();
        assert_eq!(id.len(), 36);
        assert_eq!(id.as_bytes()[8], b'-');
        assert_eq!(id.as_bytes()[13], b'-');
        assert_eq!(id.as_bytes()[18], b'-');
        assert_eq!(id.as_bytes()[23], b'-');
        assert_eq!(id.as_bytes()[14], b'4');
        let variant = id.as_bytes()[19];
        assert!(variant == b'8' || variant == b'9' || variant == b'a' || variant == b'b');
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_uuid_v4_unique() {
        let a = uuid_v4();
        let b = uuid_v4();
        assert_ne!(a, b);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_random_bytes() {
        let a = random_bytes_array::<32>();
        let b = random_bytes_array::<32>();
        assert_ne!(a, b);
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/ebpf.rs`:

```rs
use std::os::fd::RawFd;
use std::sync::atomic::Ordering;

use crate::bpf::loader::BpfLoader;
use crate::bpf::perf::PerfBuffer;
use crate::config::{LogLevel, log};
use crate::sys;
use crate::RUNNING;

const BPF_ELF_PATHS: &[&str] = &[
    "/usr/lib/vigil/vigil.ebpf",
    "/etc/vigil/vigil-ebpf",
    "./kernel/ebpf/vigil.bpf.o",
];

pub struct EbpfState {
    loader: BpfLoader,
    perf: Option<PerfBuffer>,
}

fn find_bpf_elf() -> Result<String, Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {
    for path in BPF_ELF_PATHS {
        if std::path::Path::new(path).exists() {
            return Ok(path.to_string());
        }
    }
    Err(format!(
        "BPF ELF not found, searched: {}",
        BPF_ELF_PATHS.join(", ")
    ).into())
}

pub fn start_ebpf() -> Result<EbpfState, Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {
    let elf_path = find_bpf_elf()?;
    let mut loader = BpfLoader::load(&elf_path)?;
    loader.attach_all(&elf_path)?;
    Ok(EbpfState {
        loader,
        perf: None,
    })
}

pub fn get_events(state: &mut EbpfState) -> Result<Vec<RawFd>, Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {
    let map_fd = state
        .loader
        .get_map_fd("EVENTS")
        .ok_or("EVENTS map not found in BPF ELF")?;
    let perf = PerfBuffer::open(map_fd)?;
    let fds = perf.fds().to_vec();
    state.perf = Some(perf);
    Ok(fds)
}

pub fn read_events(state: &mut EbpfState) -> Result<(), Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {
    let perf = state
        .perf
        .take()
        .ok_or("perf buffers not initialized - call get_events first")?;

    std::thread::spawn(move || {
        let log_path = "/var/log/vigil.log".to_string();

        let epfd = match sys::sys_epoll_create() {
            Ok(fd) => fd,
            Err(e) => {
                let _ = log(
                    LogLevel::Alert,
                    &format!("eBPF epoll_create failed: {}", e),
                    &log_path,
                );
                return;
            }
        };

        let perf_fds = perf.fds().to_vec();
        for &fd in &perf_fds {
            let _ = sys::sys_epoll_ctl(epfd, sys::EPOLL_CTL_ADD, fd, sys::EPOLLIN);
        }

        let mut events = [sys::EpollEvent { events: 0, data: 0 }; 32];

        while RUNNING.load(Ordering::SeqCst) {
            let n = match sys::sys_epoll_wait(epfd, &mut events, 200) {
                Ok(n) => n,
                Err(_) => continue,
            };

            for event in &events[..n] {
                let ready_fd = event.data as RawFd;

                for (cpu, &pfd) in perf_fds.iter().enumerate() {
                    if pfd == ready_fd {
                        perf.read_events(cpu, |data| {
                            if data.len() >= 12 {
                                let caller = u32::from_ne_bytes([
                                    data[0], data[1], data[2], data[3],
                                ]);
                                let target = u32::from_ne_bytes([
                                    data[4], data[5], data[6], data[7],
                                ]);
                                let syscall = u32::from_ne_bytes([
                                    data[8], data[9], data[10], data[11],
                                ]);
                                let _ = log(
                                    LogLevel::Alert,
                                    &format!(
                                        "[eBPF] syscall={} caller={} target={}",
                                        syscall, caller, target
                                    ),
                                    &log_path,
                                );
                            }
                        });
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        sys::sys_close(epfd);
    });

    Ok(())
}

```

`crates/vigil/src/error.rs`:

```rs
use std::fmt;

// TODO: migrate existing String errors to DaemonError
#[derive(Debug)]
pub enum DaemonError {
    Io(String),
    Config(String),
    Ebpf(String),
    Ipc(String),
    Report(String),
    Scan(String),
}

impl fmt::Display for DaemonError {
    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> fmt::Result {
        match self {
            Self::Io(m) => write!(f, "io error: {}", m),
            Self::Config(m) => write!(f, "config error: {}", m),
            Self::Ebpf(m) => write!(f, "ebpf error: {}", m),
            Self::Ipc(m) => write!(f, "ipc error: {}", m),
            Self::Report(m) => write!(f, "report error: {}", m),
            Self::Scan(m) => write!(f, "scan error: {}", m),
        }
    }
}

impl From<String> for DaemonError {
    fn from(s: String) -> Self {
        DaemonError::Io(s)
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/honeypot.rs`:

```rs
// honeypot traps for catching cheats that probe the system
//
// the idea: drop bait files in places where cheat tools typically look —
// /dev/shm (shared memory injection), /tmp (throwaway .so loaders),
// and a fake "debug" socket that looks like we left a backdoor open.
// then watch them with fanotify (or inotify as fallback). any access = instant red flag.
//
// fanotify gives us the PID of the accessor — inotify doesn't.
// we need CAP_SYS_ADMIN for fanotify, but vigil runs as root so that's fine.
// if fanotify_init fails, we fall back to inotify silently.

use std::collections::HashMap;
use std::path::PathBuf;

use crate::sys::{InotifyEvent, IN_ACCESS, IN_OPEN, IN_MODIFY, IN_DELETE_SELF, IN_CLOEXEC};

// --- fanotify constants ---
const FAN_CLASS_CONTENT: u32 = 0x04;
const FAN_CLOEXEC: u32 = 0x01;
const FAN_MARK_ADD: u32 = 0x01;
const FAN_OPEN: u64 = 0x20;
const FAN_ACCESS: u64 = 0x01;
const FAN_MODIFY: u64 = 0x02;
const FAN_CLOSE_WRITE: u64 = 0x10;
const O_RDONLY: u32 = 0;

const FAN_EVENT_METADATA_LEN: usize = std::mem::size_of::<FanotifyEventMetadata>();

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn inotify_init1(flags: i32) -> i32;
    fn inotify_add_watch(fd: i32, pathname: *const u8, mask: u32) -> i32;
    fn read(fd: i32, buf: *mut u8, count: usize) -> isize;
    fn close(fd: i32) -> i32;
    fn getpid() -> i32;
    fn unlink(path: *const u8) -> i32;
    fn fanotify_init(flags: u32, event_f_flags: u32) -> i32;
    fn fanotify_mark(fanotify_fd: i32, flags: u32, mask: u64, dirfd: i32, pathname: *const u8) -> i32;
}

#[repr(C)]
struct FanotifyEventMetadata {
    event_len: u32,
    vers: u8,
    reserved: u8,
    metadata_len: u16,
    mask: u64,
    fd: i32,
    pid: i32,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct TrapHit {
    pub trap_path: String,
    pub action: &'static str,
    pub pid: Option<i32>,
    pub process_name: Option<String>,
}

struct Trap {
    path: PathBuf,
    content: Vec<u8>,
}

// bait files we plant on the system
// names are deliberately realistic — they should look like leftover
// debug artifacts or game memory dumps
fn get_traps() -> Vec<Trap> {
    let pid = unsafe { getpid() };

    vec![
        // looks like a game process left shared memory open
        Trap {
            path: PathBuf::from(format!("/dev/shm/.gl_shader_cache_{}", pid)),
            content: make_fake_shm_header(),
        },
        // looks like a preload library ready to be injected
        Trap {
            path: PathBuf::from("/tmp/.libgtk_overlay.so.tmp"),
            content: make_fake_elf_header(),
        },
        // looks like a pid file from a debug session
        Trap {
            path: PathBuf::from("/tmp/.vigil_debug.pid"),
            content: format!("{}\n", pid).into_bytes(),
        },
    ]
}

// minimal ELF header — just enough to make `file` say "ELF 64-bit"
// no actual code, but cheat scanners that look for injectable .so files
// will try to open/mmap it
fn make_fake_elf_header() -> Vec<u8> {
    let mut buf = vec![0u8; 64];
    // ELF magic
    buf[0] = 0x7f;
    buf[1] = b'E';
    buf[2] = b'L';
    buf[3] = b'F';
    buf[4] = 2; // 64-bit
    buf[5] = 1; // little endian
    buf[6] = 1; // ELF version
    buf[16] = 3; // ET_DYN — shared object
    buf
}

// fake shared memory header — looks like a mapped region with
// some plausible-looking pointers. cheat tools scanning /dev/shm
// for game memory will try to read this
fn make_fake_shm_header() -> Vec<u8> {
    let mut buf = vec![0u8; 256];
    // magic that looks like an internal struct header
    buf[0..4].copy_from_slice(b"VRAM");
    // fake "size" field
    buf[8..16].copy_from_slice(&(4096u64).to_le_bytes());
    // fake pointer-looking values in the rest
    // (just ascending addresses, nothing real)
    for i in 0..4 {
        let fake_addr: u64 = 0x7f0000100000 + (i * 0x1000);
        let off = 32 + (i as usize * 8);
        buf[off..off + 8].copy_from_slice(&fake_addr.to_le_bytes());
    }
    buf
}

pub fn plant_traps() -> Result<Vec<PathBuf>, String> {
    let traps = get_traps();
    let mut planted = vec![];

    for trap in &traps {
        if let Err(e) = std::fs::write(&trap.path, &trap.content) {
            // not fatal — /dev/shm might not exist on some systems,
            // or /tmp could be noexec. just skip it
            eprintln!("[HONEYPOT] couldn't plant {}: {}", trap.path.display(), e);
            continue;
        }

        planted.push(trap.path.clone());
    }

    if planted.is_empty() {
        return Err("no traps could be planted".into());
    }

    Ok(planted)
}

pub fn cleanup_traps() {
    for trap in get_traps() {
        let path_c = format!("{}\0", trap.path.display());
        unsafe { unlink(path_c.as_ptr()); }
    }
}

// reads /proc/PID/comm to get the process name
fn get_process_name(pid: i32) -> Option<String> {
    let path = format!("/proc/{}/comm", pid);
    std::fs::read_to_string(path)
        .ok()
        .map(|s| s.trim().to_string())
}

// resolves which trap file an fanotify fd points to by reading /proc/self/fd/N
fn resolve_fd_path(fd: i32) -> Option<String> {
    let link = format!("/proc/self/fd/{}", fd);
    std::fs::read_link(link)
        .ok()
        .map(|p| p.to_string_lossy().to_string())
}

// figures out the action name from fanotify mask bits
fn fan_action(mask: u64) -> &'static str {
    if mask & FAN_MODIFY != 0 {
        "modified"
    } else if mask & FAN_CLOSE_WRITE != 0 {
        "written"
    } else if mask & FAN_OPEN != 0 {
        "opened"
    } else {
        "accessed"
    }
}

// watches planted traps via fanotify (preferred) or inotify (fallback).
// blocks forever, call from a thread.
// sends trap hits through the callback.
pub fn watch_traps(paths: Vec<PathBuf>, mut on_hit: impl FnMut(TrapHit)) {
    // try fanotify first — it gives us the PID of the accessor
    let fan_fd = unsafe { fanotify_init(FAN_CLASS_CONTENT | FAN_CLOEXEC, O_RDONLY) };
    if fan_fd >= 0 {
        watch_traps_fanotify(fan_fd, paths, &mut on_hit);
        return;
    }

    // fallback to inotify
    eprintln!("[HONEYPOT] fanotify_init failed, falling back to inotify (no PID tracking)");
    watch_traps_inotify(paths, &mut on_hit);
}

fn watch_traps_fanotify(fan_fd: i32, paths: Vec<PathBuf>, on_hit: &mut impl FnMut(TrapHit)) {
    let mask = FAN_OPEN | FAN_ACCESS | FAN_MODIFY | FAN_CLOSE_WRITE;

    // build a set of trap paths for quick lookup
    let trap_paths: std::collections::HashSet<String> = paths
        .iter()
        .map(|p| p.to_string_lossy().to_string())
        .collect();

    for path in &paths {
        let path_c = format!("{}\0", path.display());
        let ret = unsafe { fanotify_mark(fan_fd, FAN_MARK_ADD, mask, -1, path_c.as_ptr()) };
        if ret < 0 {
            eprintln!("[HONEYPOT] fanotify_mark failed for {}", path.display());
        }
    }

    let our_pid = unsafe { getpid() };
    let mut buf = vec![0u8; 4096];

    loop {
        let n = unsafe { read(fan_fd, buf.as_mut_ptr(), buf.len()) };
        if n <= 0 {
            break;
        }

        let mut offset = 0usize;
        while offset + FAN_EVENT_METADATA_LEN <= n as usize {
            let event = unsafe { &*(buf.as_ptr().add(offset) as *const FanotifyEventMetadata) };

            if event.event_len < FAN_EVENT_METADATA_LEN as u32 {
                break;
            }

            // skip our own access (vigil writing the trap files)
            if event.pid != our_pid && event.fd >= 0 {
                // resolve which file was accessed via the fd fanotify opened for us
                if let Some(accessed_path) = resolve_fd_path(event.fd)
                    && trap_paths.contains(&accessed_path)
                {
                    let process_name = get_process_name(event.pid);
                    on_hit(TrapHit {
                        trap_path: accessed_path,
                        action: fan_action(event.mask),
                        pid: Some(event.pid),
                        process_name,
                    });
                }
            }

            // fanotify opens the file for us — we must close it
            if event.fd >= 0 {
                unsafe { close(event.fd); }
            }

            offset += event.event_len as usize;
        }
    }

    unsafe { close(fan_fd); }
}

fn watch_traps_inotify(paths: Vec<PathBuf>, on_hit: &mut impl FnMut(TrapHit)) {
    let fd = unsafe { inotify_init1(IN_CLOEXEC) };
    if fd < 0 {
        eprintln!("[HONEYPOT] inotify_init failed, traps are blind");
        return;
    }

    let mask = IN_ACCESS | IN_OPEN | IN_MODIFY | IN_DELETE_SELF;
    let mut wd_map: HashMap<i32, PathBuf> = HashMap::new();

    for path in &paths {
        let path_c = format!("{}\0", path.display());
        let wd = unsafe { inotify_add_watch(fd, path_c.as_ptr(), mask) };
        if wd >= 0 {
            wd_map.insert(wd, path.clone());
        }
    }

    if wd_map.is_empty() {
        unsafe { close(fd); }
        return;
    }

    let mut buf = vec![0u8; 1024];
    loop {
        let n = unsafe { read(fd, buf.as_mut_ptr(), buf.len()) };
        if n <= 0 {
            break;
        }

        let mut offset = 0;
        while offset < n as usize {
            if offset + std::mem::size_of::<InotifyEvent>() > n as usize {
                break;
            }
            let event = unsafe { &*(buf.as_ptr().add(offset) as *const InotifyEvent) };
            let event_size = std::mem::size_of::<InotifyEvent>() + event.len as usize;

            if let Some(path) = wd_map.get(&event.wd) {
                let action = if event.mask & IN_DELETE_SELF != 0 {
                    "deleted"
                } else if event.mask & IN_MODIFY != 0 {
                    "modified"
                } else if event.mask & IN_OPEN != 0 {
                    "opened"
                } else {
                    "accessed"
                };

                on_hit(TrapHit {
                    trap_path: path.to_string_lossy().to_string(),
                    action,
                    pid: None,
                    process_name: None,
                });

                // if someone deleted our trap, replant it on next cycle
                if event.mask & IN_DELETE_SELF != 0
                    && let Some(trap) = get_traps().iter().find(|t| t.path == *path) {
                        let _ = std::fs::write(&trap.path, &trap.content);
                        // re-add the watch
                        let path_c = format!("{}\0", path.display());
                        let new_wd = unsafe { inotify_add_watch(fd, path_c.as_ptr(), mask) };
                        if new_wd >= 0 {
                            wd_map.insert(new_wd, path.clone());
                        }
                    }
            }

            offset += event_size;
        }
    }

    unsafe { close(fd); }
}


#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn fake_elf_has_valid_magic() {
        let elf = make_fake_elf_header();
        assert_eq!(&elf[0..4], &[0x7f, b'E', b'L', b'F']);
        assert_eq!(elf[4], 2); // 64-bit
        assert_eq!(elf[16], 3); // ET_DYN
    }

    #[test]
    fn fake_shm_has_header() {
        let shm = make_fake_shm_header();
        assert_eq!(&shm[0..4], b"VRAM");
        let size = u64::from_le_bytes(shm[8..16].try_into().unwrap());
        assert_eq!(size, 4096);
    }

    #[test]
    fn trap_paths_look_realistic() {
        let traps = get_traps();
        assert!(traps.len() >= 3);
        // should be in common injection directories
        for trap in &traps {
            let p = trap.path.to_string_lossy();
            assert!(
                p.starts_with("/dev/shm") || p.starts_with("/tmp"),
                "trap {} not in expected location",
                p
            );
        }
    }

    #[test]
    fn trap_hit_has_pid_fields() {
        let hit = TrapHit {
            trap_path: "/tmp/test".to_string(),
            action: "opened",
            pid: Some(1234),
            process_name: Some("test_proc".to_string()),
        };
        assert_eq!(hit.pid, Some(1234));
        assert_eq!(hit.process_name.as_deref(), Some("test_proc"));

        // inotify fallback produces None for pid
        let hit_no_pid = TrapHit {
            trap_path: "/tmp/test".to_string(),
            action: "accessed",
            pid: None,
            process_name: None,
        };
        assert!(hit_no_pid.pid.is_none());
    }

    #[test]
    fn fan_action_returns_correct_strings() {
        assert_eq!(fan_action(FAN_MODIFY), "modified");
        assert_eq!(fan_action(FAN_CLOSE_WRITE), "written");
        assert_eq!(fan_action(FAN_OPEN), "opened");
        assert_eq!(fan_action(FAN_ACCESS), "accessed");
    }

    #[test]
    fn fanotify_event_metadata_size() {
        // fanotify_event_metadata is 24 bytes (4+1+1+2+8+4+4)
        assert_eq!(FAN_EVENT_METADATA_LEN, 24);
    }
}
```
