`crates/vigil/src/http_client.rs`:

```rs
use std::io::{BufRead, BufReader, Read, Write};
use std::net::TcpStream;
use std::time::Duration;

pub struct HttpResponse {
    pub status: u16,
    pub body: String,
}

pub fn get(url: &str, token: Option<&str>) -> Result<HttpResponse, String> {
    let (tls, host, port, path) = parse_url(url)?;

    let stream = TcpStream::connect(format!("{}:{}", host, port))
        .map_err(|e| format!("connect failed: {}", e))?;

    stream
        .set_read_timeout(Some(Duration::from_secs(10)))
        .map_err(|e| format!("set_read_timeout failed: {}", e))?;

    let mut req = format!(
        "GET {} HTTP/1.1\r\nHost: {}\r\n",
        path, host
    );

    if let Some(t) = token {
        req.push_str(&format!("Authorization: Bearer {}\r\n", t));
    }

    req.push_str("Connection: close\r\n");
    req.push_str("\r\n");

    #[cfg(feature = "tls")]
    if tls {
        let tls_stream = crate::tls::TlsStream::connect(stream, &host)
            .map_err(|e| format!("tls connect failed: {}", e))?;
        tls_stream.write_all(req.as_bytes())
            .map_err(|e| format!("tls write failed: {}", e))?;
        let data = tls_stream.read_all()
            .map_err(|e| format!("tls read failed: {}", e))?;
        return parse_raw_response(&data);
    }
    #[cfg(not(feature = "tls"))]
    if tls { return Err("https not supported - build with tls feature".into()); }

    let mut stream = stream;
    stream.write_all(req.as_bytes()).map_err(|e| format!("write failed: {}", e))?;
    read_response(&mut stream)
}

pub fn post_json(url: &str, body: &str, token: Option<&str>) -> Result<HttpResponse, String> {
    let (tls, host, port, path) = parse_url(url)?;

    let stream = TcpStream::connect(format!("{}:{}", host, port))
        .map_err(|e| format!("connect failed: {}", e))?;

    stream
        .set_read_timeout(Some(Duration::from_secs(10)))
        .map_err(|e| format!("set_read_timeout failed: {}", e))?;

    let mut req = format!(
        "POST {} HTTP/1.1\r\nHost: {}\r\nContent-Type: application/json\r\nContent-Length: {}\r\n",
        path,
        host,
        body.len()
    );

    if let Some(t) = token {
        req.push_str(&format!("Authorization: Bearer {}\r\n", t));
    }

    req.push_str("Connection: close\r\n");
    req.push_str("\r\n");
    req.push_str(body);

    #[cfg(feature = "tls")]
    if tls {
        let tls_stream = crate::tls::TlsStream::connect(stream, &host)
            .map_err(|e| format!("tls connect failed: {}", e))?;
        tls_stream.write_all(req.as_bytes())
            .map_err(|e| format!("tls write failed: {}", e))?;
        let data = tls_stream.read_all()
            .map_err(|e| format!("tls read failed: {}", e))?;
        return parse_raw_response(&data);
    }
    #[cfg(not(feature = "tls"))]
    if tls { return Err("https not supported - build with tls feature".into()); }

    let mut stream = stream;
    stream.write_all(req.as_bytes()).map_err(|e| format!("write failed: {}", e))?;
    read_response(&mut stream)
}

fn parse_raw_response(data: &[u8]) -> Result<HttpResponse, String> {
    let text = String::from_utf8_lossy(data);
    let header_end = text.find("\r\n\r\n").ok_or("no header/body separator")?;
    let header_part = &text[..header_end];
    let body = text[header_end + 4..].to_string();

    let status_line = header_part.lines().next().ok_or("empty response")?;
    let status = parse_status_line(status_line)?;

    Ok(HttpResponse { status, body })
}

fn parse_url(url: &str) -> Result<(bool, String, u16, String), String> {
    let (tls, rest) = if let Some(r) = url.strip_prefix("https://") {
        (true, r)
    } else if let Some(r) = url.strip_prefix("http://") {
        (false, r)
    } else {
        return Err(format!("unsupported scheme in url: {}", url));
    };

    let (authority, path) = match rest.find('/') {
        Some(i) => (&rest[..i], rest[i..].to_string()),
        None => (rest, "/".to_string()),
    };

    let default_port = if tls { 443 } else { 80 };
    let (host, port) = match authority.find(':') {
        Some(i) => {
            let p = authority[i + 1..]
                .parse::<u16>()
                .map_err(|_| format!("invalid port in url: {}", url))?;
            (authority[..i].to_string(), p)
        }
        None => (authority.to_string(), default_port),
    };

    Ok((tls, host, port, path))
}

fn read_response(stream: &mut TcpStream) -> Result<HttpResponse, String> {
    let mut reader = BufReader::new(stream);

    let mut status_line = String::new();
    reader
        .read_line(&mut status_line)
        .map_err(|e| format!("read status line failed: {}", e))?;

    let status = parse_status_line(&status_line)?;

    let mut content_length: Option<usize> = None;
    loop {
        let mut line = String::new();
        reader
            .read_line(&mut line)
            .map_err(|e| format!("read header failed: {}", e))?;

        let trimmed = line.trim_end_matches(['\r', '\n']);
        if trimmed.is_empty() {
            break;
        }

        let lower = trimmed.to_ascii_lowercase();
        if let Some(val) = lower.strip_prefix("content-length:")
            && let Ok(n) = val.trim().parse::<usize>() {
                content_length = Some(n);
            }
    }

    let body = if let Some(n) = content_length {
        let mut buf = vec![0u8; n];
        reader
            .read_exact(&mut buf)
            .map_err(|e| format!("read body failed: {}", e))?;
        String::from_utf8_lossy(&buf).into_owned()
    } else {
        let mut buf = Vec::new();
        reader
            .read_to_end(&mut buf)
            .map_err(|e| format!("read body to end failed: {}", e))?;
        String::from_utf8_lossy(&buf).into_owned()
    };

    Ok(HttpResponse { status, body })
}

fn parse_status_line(line: &str) -> Result<u16, String> {
    let mut parts = line.splitn(3, ' ');
    let _version = parts.next().ok_or("empty status line")?;
    let code = parts
        .next()
        .ok_or("missing status code")?
        .trim()
        .parse::<u16>()
        .map_err(|_| format!("invalid status code in: {}", line.trim()))?;
    Ok(code)
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn parse_url_full() {
        let (tls, host, port, path) = parse_url("http://localhost:3000/api/report").unwrap();
        assert!(!tls);
        assert_eq!(host, "localhost");
        assert_eq!(port, 3000);
        assert_eq!(path, "/api/report");
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_url_no_port() {
        let (tls, host, port, path) = parse_url("http://example.com/test").unwrap();
        assert!(!tls);
        assert_eq!(host, "example.com");
        assert_eq!(port, 80);
        assert_eq!(path, "/test");
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_url_no_path() {
        let (_, host, port, path) = parse_url("http://host:8080").unwrap();
        assert_eq!(host, "host");
        assert_eq!(port, 8080);
        assert_eq!(path, "/");
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_url_just_host() {
        let (_, host, port, path) = parse_url("http://myserver").unwrap();
        assert_eq!(host, "myserver");
        assert_eq!(port, 80);
        assert_eq!(path, "/");
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_url_https() {
        let (tls, host, port, path) = parse_url("https://example.com/api").unwrap();
        assert!(tls);
        assert_eq!(host, "example.com");
        assert_eq!(port, 443);
        assert_eq!(path, "/api");
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_url_rejects_garbage() {
        assert!(parse_url("not-a-url").is_err());
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_status_200() {
        assert_eq!(parse_status_line("HTTP/1.1 200 OK\r\n").unwrap(), 200);
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_status_404() {
        assert_eq!(parse_status_line("HTTP/1.1 404 Not Found\r\n").unwrap(), 404);
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_status_500() {
        assert_eq!(parse_status_line("HTTP/1.1 500 Internal Server Error").unwrap(), 500);
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_status_empty_fails() {
        assert!(parse_status_line("").is_err());
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_status_no_code_fails() {
        assert!(parse_status_line("HTTP/1.1").is_err());
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/input_monitor.rs`:

```rs
// watches /dev/input/ for new devices appearing at runtime
// new input devices during a game session can indicate injected
// virtual controllers or fake mouse/keyboard for aimbots

use crate::sys::{InotifyEvent, IN_CREATE, IN_CLOEXEC};

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn inotify_init1(flags: i32) -> i32;
    fn inotify_add_watch(fd: i32, pathname: *const u8, mask: u32) -> i32;
    fn read(fd: i32, buf: *mut u8, count: usize) -> isize;
    fn close(fd: i32) -> i32;
}

// blocks forever - call from std::thread::spawn
// calls on_device with the device name (e.g. "event5") when a new input device appears
pub fn watch_input_devices(mut on_device: impl FnMut(&str)) {
    let fd = unsafe { inotify_init1(IN_CLOEXEC) };
    if fd < 0 {
        eprintln!("[INPUT] inotify_init failed");
        return;
    }

    let path = "/dev/input/\0";
    let wd = unsafe { inotify_add_watch(fd, path.as_ptr(), IN_CREATE) };
    if wd < 0 {
        eprintln!("[INPUT] failed to watch /dev/input/");
        unsafe { close(fd); }
        return;
    }

    let mut buf = vec![0u8; 1024];
    loop {
        let n = unsafe { read(fd, buf.as_mut_ptr(), buf.len()) };
        if n <= 0 {
            break;
        }

        let mut offset = 0;
        while offset < n as usize {
            if offset + std::mem::size_of::<InotifyEvent>() > n as usize {
                break;
            }
            let event = unsafe { &*(buf.as_ptr().add(offset) as *const InotifyEvent) };
            let name_len = event.len as usize;

            if name_len > 0 {
                let name_ptr = unsafe {
                    buf.as_ptr().add(offset + std::mem::size_of::<InotifyEvent>())
                };
                let name_bytes = unsafe { std::slice::from_raw_parts(name_ptr, name_len) };
                let end = name_bytes.iter().position(|&b| b == 0).unwrap_or(name_len);
                let name = String::from_utf8_lossy(&name_bytes[..end]);

                if event.mask & IN_CREATE != 0 {
                    on_device(&name);
                }
            }

            offset += std::mem::size_of::<InotifyEvent>() + name_len;
        }
    }

    unsafe { close(fd); }
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/ipc.rs`:

```rs
#![allow(dead_code)]

use std::os::fd::RawFd;
use std::sync::atomic::Ordering;

use crate::json::{json_bool, json_num, json_obj, json_str, parse, stringify};
use crate::RUNNING;

const SOCK_PATH: &str = "/run/vigil.sock";
const AF_UNIX: i32 = 1;
const SOCK_STREAM: i32 = 1;
const SOCK_CLOEXEC: i32 = 0o2000000;

#[repr(C)]
struct SockaddrUn {
    family: u16,
    path: [u8; 108],
}

// SOL_SOCKET and SO_PEERCRED constants for Linux
const SOL_SOCKET: i32 = 1;
const SO_PEERCRED: i32 = 17;

#[repr(C)]
struct UcredRaw {
    pid: i32,
    uid: u32,
    gid: u32,
}

// returns (uid, gid) of the process on the other end of a Unix socket
fn get_peer_cred(fd: RawFd) -> Result<(u32, u32), &'static str> {
    let mut cred = UcredRaw { pid: 0, uid: 0, gid: 0 };
    let mut len = std::mem::size_of::<UcredRaw>() as u32;
    let ret = unsafe {
        getsockopt(
            fd,
            SOL_SOCKET,
            SO_PEERCRED,
            &mut cred as *mut UcredRaw as *mut u8,
            &mut len,
        )
    };
    if ret < 0 {
        return Err("getsockopt(SO_PEERCRED) failed");
    }
    Ok((cred.uid, cred.gid))
}

// returns the effective UID of the running daemon process
fn daemon_uid() -> u32 {
    unsafe { getuid() }
}

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn socket(domain: i32, sock_type: i32, protocol: i32) -> i32;
    fn bind(fd: i32, addr: *const SockaddrUn, len: u32) -> i32;
    fn listen(fd: i32, backlog: i32) -> i32;
    fn accept4(fd: i32, addr: *mut u8, len: *mut u32, flags: i32) -> i32;
    fn write(fd: i32, buf: *const u8, count: usize) -> isize;
    fn read(fd: i32, buf: *mut u8, count: usize) -> isize;
    fn close(fd: i32) -> i32;
    fn unlink(path: *const u8) -> i32;
    fn getsockopt(fd: i32, level: i32, optname: i32, optval: *mut u8, optlen: *mut u32) -> i32;
    fn getuid() -> u32;
}

#[derive(Clone)]
pub struct DaemonState {
    pub trust_score: u8,
    pub ebpf_active: bool,
    pub active_profile: Option<String>,
    pub scan_count: u64,
    pub heartbeat_seq: u64,
    pub banned: bool,
}

pub enum IpcCommand {
    SetProfile(String),
}

use std::sync::Mutex;
static PENDING_COMMANDS: Mutex<Vec<IpcCommand>> = Mutex::new(Vec::new());

pub fn take_commands() -> Vec<IpcCommand> {
    let mut cmds = PENDING_COMMANDS.lock().unwrap();
    std::mem::take(&mut *cmds)
}

fn make_addr() -> SockaddrUn {
    let mut addr = SockaddrUn {
        family: AF_UNIX as u16,
        path: [0u8; 108],
    };
    let bytes = SOCK_PATH.as_bytes();
    addr.path[..bytes.len()].copy_from_slice(bytes);
    addr
}

fn send_response(fd: RawFd, msg: &str) {
    let mut data = msg.to_string();
    data.push('\n');
    unsafe { write(fd, data.as_ptr(), data.len()) };
}

fn handle_command(cmd: &str, state: &DaemonState) -> String {
    let v = match parse(cmd) {
        Ok(v) => v,
        Err(_) => return stringify(&json_obj(vec![("error", json_str("invalid json"))])),
    };

    let action = v.get("cmd").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("");

    match action {
        "status" => stringify(&json_obj(vec![
            ("running", json_bool(true)),
            ("trust_score", json_num(state.trust_score as f64)),
            ("ebpf", json_bool(state.ebpf_active)),
            (
                "profile",
                state
                    .active_profile
                    .as_deref()
                    .map(json_str)
                    .unwrap_or(crate::json::JsonValue::Null),
            ),
            ("scan_count", json_num(state.scan_count as f64)),
            ("heartbeat", json_num(state.heartbeat_seq as f64)),
            ("banned", json_bool(state.banned)),
        ])),
        "ping" => stringify(&json_obj(vec![("pong", json_bool(true))])),
        "set_profile" => {
            let profile = v.get("profile").and_then(|x| x.as_str()).unwrap_or("");
            if profile.is_empty() {
                stringify(&json_obj(vec![("error", json_str("profile required"))]))
            } else {
                PENDING_COMMANDS.lock().unwrap().push(IpcCommand::SetProfile(profile.to_string()));
                stringify(&json_obj(vec![("ok", json_bool(true))]))
            }
        }
        _ => stringify(&json_obj(vec![("error", json_str("unknown command"))])),
    }
}

pub fn start_ipc_listener<F>(state_fn: F)
where
    F: Fn() -> DaemonState + Send + 'static,
{
    std::thread::spawn(move || {
        let mut path_buf = SOCK_PATH.as_bytes().to_vec();
        path_buf.push(0);
        unsafe { unlink(path_buf.as_ptr()) };

        let fd = unsafe { socket(AF_UNIX, SOCK_STREAM | SOCK_CLOEXEC, 0) };
        if fd < 0 {
            eprintln!("[IPC] socket() failed");
            return;
        }

        let addr = make_addr();
        let addr_len = (2 + SOCK_PATH.len()) as u32;

        if unsafe { bind(fd, &addr, addr_len) } < 0 {
            eprintln!("[IPC] bind() failed");
            unsafe { close(fd) };
            return;
        }

        let mode_path = std::ffi::CString::new(SOCK_PATH).unwrap();
        unsafe {
            libc_chmod(mode_path.as_ptr(), 0o660);
        }

        if unsafe { listen(fd, 4) } < 0 {
            eprintln!("[IPC] listen() failed");
            unsafe { close(fd) };
            return;
        }

        let my_uid = daemon_uid();

        while RUNNING.load(Ordering::SeqCst) {
            let client =
                unsafe { accept4(fd, std::ptr::null_mut(), std::ptr::null_mut(), SOCK_CLOEXEC) };
            if client < 0 {
                continue;
            }

            // Verify the connecting process is root (uid 0) or the daemon's own user.
            match get_peer_cred(client) {
                Err(e) => {
                    eprintln!("[IPC] rejected connection: {}", e);
                    unsafe { close(client) };
                    continue;
                }
                Ok((peer_uid, _)) if peer_uid != 0 && peer_uid != my_uid => {
                    eprintln!(
                        "[IPC] rejected connection from uid {} (not root or daemon uid {})",
                        peer_uid, my_uid
                    );
                    let denial =
                        stringify(&json_obj(vec![("error", json_str("permission denied"))]));
                    send_response(client, &denial);
                    unsafe { close(client) };
                    continue;
                }
                Ok(_) => {} // authorised — fall through
            }

            let mut buf = [0u8; 4096];
            let n = unsafe { read(client, buf.as_mut_ptr(), buf.len()) };
            if n > 0 {
                let msg = String::from_utf8_lossy(&buf[..n as usize]);
                let msg = msg.trim();
                let state = state_fn();
                let resp = handle_command(msg, &state);
                send_response(client, &resp);
            }

            unsafe { close(client) };
        }

        unsafe { close(fd) };
        unsafe { unlink(path_buf.as_ptr()) };
    });
}

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn chmod(path: *const i8, mode: u32) -> i32;
}

unsafe fn libc_chmod(path: *const i8, mode: u32) {
    unsafe { chmod(path, mode) };
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn handle_status_command() {
        let state = DaemonState {
            trust_score: 95,
            ebpf_active: true,
            active_profile: Some("cs2".to_string()),
            scan_count: 42,
            heartbeat_seq: 10,
            banned: false,
        };
        let resp = handle_command(r#"{"cmd":"status"}"#, &state);
        let v = parse(&resp).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(v.get("running").unwrap().as_bool().unwrap(), true);
        assert_eq!(v.get("trust_score").unwrap().as_i64().unwrap(), 95);
        assert_eq!(v.get("ebpf").unwrap().as_bool().unwrap(), true);
        assert_eq!(v.get("profile").unwrap().as_str().unwrap(), "cs2");
    }

    #[test]
    fn handle_ping_command() {
        let state = DaemonState {
            trust_score: 100,
            ebpf_active: false,
            active_profile: None,
            scan_count: 0,
            heartbeat_seq: 0,
            banned: false,
        };
        let resp = handle_command(r#"{"cmd":"ping"}"#, &state);
        let v = parse(&resp).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(v.get("pong").unwrap().as_bool().unwrap(), true);
    }

    #[test]
    fn handle_unknown_command() {
        let state = DaemonState {
            trust_score: 100,
            ebpf_active: false,
            active_profile: None,
            scan_count: 0,
            heartbeat_seq: 0,
            banned: false,
        };
        let resp = handle_command(r#"{"cmd":"nope"}"#, &state);
        assert!(resp.contains("unknown command"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn handle_invalid_json() {
        let state = DaemonState {
            trust_score: 100,
            ebpf_active: false,
            active_profile: None,
            scan_count: 0,
            heartbeat_seq: 0,
            banned: false,
        };
        let resp = handle_command("not json", &state);
        assert!(resp.contains("invalid json"));
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/kernel_log.rs`:

```rs
use std::fs::File;
use std::io::{BufRead, BufReader};

#[derive(Debug)]
pub struct Log {
    #[allow(dead_code)]
    priority: u8,
    #[allow(dead_code)]
    number: u32,
    timestamp: u64,
    message: String,
}

impl Log {
    pub fn new(priority: u8, number: u32, timestamp: u64, message: String) -> Self {
        Self {
            priority,
            number,
            timestamp,
            message,
        }
    }

    #[allow(dead_code)]
    pub fn get_priority(&self) -> &u8 {
        &self.priority
    }

    #[allow(dead_code)]
    pub fn get_number(&self) -> &u32 {
        &self.number
    }

    pub fn get_timestamp(&self) -> &u64 {
        &self.timestamp
    }

    pub fn get_message(&self) -> &String {
        &self.message
    }
}

// reads /dev/kmsg, filters priority 3-4, blocks on read
pub fn get_kernel_logs(callback: impl Fn(Log)) -> std::io::Result<()> {
    let f = File::open("/dev/kmsg")?;
    let reader = BufReader::new(f);

    for line in reader.lines() {
        let line = line?;
        let semi_split = line.split(';').collect::<Vec<&str>>();
        if semi_split.len() < 2 {
            continue;
        }
        let comma_split = semi_split[0].split(',').collect::<Vec<&str>>();
        if comma_split.len() < 3 {
            continue;
        }

        let priority = match comma_split[0].parse::<u8>() {
            Ok(p) => p,
            Err(_) => continue,
        };

        if priority == 3 || priority == 4 {
            let number = comma_split[1].parse().unwrap_or(0);
            let timestamp = comma_split[2].parse().unwrap_or(0);
            let log = Log::new(priority, number, timestamp, semi_split[1].into());
            callback(log);
        }
    }

    Ok(())
}

// checks for anti-cheat relevant kernel events
pub fn parse_kernel_log(log: &Log) {
    let msg = log.get_message();
    let ts = log.get_timestamp();

    if msg.contains("loading out-of-tree module") || msg.contains("module verification failed") {
        println!(
            "[KLOG ts={}] Unsigned/out-of-tree module loaded: {}",
            ts,
            msg.trim()
        );
    }

    if msg.contains("Tainted:") || msg.contains("tainting kernel") {
        println!("[KLOG ts={}] Kernel taint changed: {}", ts, msg.trim());
    }

    if msg.contains("segfault at") || msg.contains("general protection fault") {
        println!(
            "[KLOG ts={}] Memory fault (possible injection failure): {}",
            ts,
            msg.trim()
        );
    }

    if msg.contains("BUG: unable to handle page fault") || msg.contains("page_fault") {
        println!("[KLOG ts={}] Kernel page fault: {}", ts, msg.trim());
    }

    if msg.contains("/dev/mem") || msg.contains("/dev/kmem") {
        println!(
            "[KLOG ts={}] Physical memory device access: {}",
            ts,
            msg.trim()
        );
    }

    if msg.contains("DMAR:") || msg.contains("IOMMU") || msg.contains("DMA") {
        println!("[KLOG ts={}] DMA/IOMMU event: {}", ts, msg.trim());
    }

    if msg.contains("new USB device") || msg.contains("usb") && msg.contains("new") {
        println!("[KLOG ts={}] USB device event: {}", ts, msg.trim());
    }

    if msg.contains("livepatch:") {
        println!("[KLOG ts={}] Kernel livepatch detected: {}", ts, msg.trim());
    }

    if (msg.contains("apparmor=") || msg.contains("avc:")) && msg.contains("ptrace") {
        println!("[KLOG ts={}] kprobe/LSM denied ptrace: {}", ts, msg.trim());
    }
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn log_new_and_getters() {
        let log = Log::new(3, 100, 12345, "test message".to_string());
        assert_eq!(*log.get_priority(), 3);
        assert_eq!(*log.get_number(), 100);
        assert_eq!(*log.get_timestamp(), 12345);
        assert_eq!(log.get_message(), "test message");
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_out_of_tree_module() {
        let log = Log::new(
            3,
            1,
            1000,
            " loading out-of-tree module taints kernel".to_string(),
        );
        parse_kernel_log(&log);
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_taint_log() {
        let log = Log::new(3, 2, 2000, " Tainted: G OE".to_string());
        parse_kernel_log(&log);
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_segfault_log() {
        let log = Log::new(3, 3, 3000, " segfault at 0x0 ip 0x7fff rsp 0x0".to_string());
        parse_kernel_log(&log);
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_devmem_log() {
        let log = Log::new(
            3,
            4,
            4000,
            " Program tried to access /dev/mem range".to_string(),
        );
        parse_kernel_log(&log);
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_livepatch_log() {
        let log = Log::new(3, 5, 5000, " livepatch: enabling patch".to_string());
        parse_kernel_log(&log);
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_kprobe_ptrace_log() {
        let log = Log::new(3, 6, 6000, " apparmor= denied ptrace read".to_string());
        parse_kernel_log(&log);
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_clean_log_no_match() {
        let log = Log::new(
            3,
            7,
            7000,
            " normal kernel message nothing special".to_string(),
        );
        parse_kernel_log(&log);
    }
}
```

```rs
use std::collections::HashMap;
use std::collections::HashSet;
use std::sync::atomic::{AtomicBool, Ordering};
use std::sync::{Arc, Mutex};
use std::time::Duration;

use crate::cli::{Commands, cmd_check, cmd_init, cmd_scan, cmd_status, parse_args};
use crate::kernel_log::{get_kernel_logs, parse_kernel_log};
use crate::report::{
    CheatMatch, CrossTrace, FileIntegrity, ModuleChange, NetworkConnection, SuspiciousProcess,
    build_report,
};
use crate::scanner::check_sandbox;
use crate::{
    config::{
        LogLevel, check_hash, compare_hashes, get_cheat_db, get_config, get_game_dir,
        get_whitelist, load_baseline, log, save_baseline, scan_game_dir,
    },
    ebpf::{get_events, read_events, start_ebpf},
    network::{get_connections, get_inode},
    process::Suspicious,

        check_capabilities, check_namespaces, check_overlay_processes, check_rwx_maps,
        check_text_integrity, get_cross_traces, get_fd, get_map, get_modules, get_process,
        get_process_tree, scan_processes, track_maps_changes, validate_launch_chain,
    },
};

mod bpf;
mod cli;
mod error;
pub use error::DaemonError;
mod client;
mod config;
mod crypto;

mod http_client;

static RUNNING: AtomicBool = AtomicBool::new(true);
static RELOAD: AtomicBool = AtomicBool::new(false);

unsafe extern "C" fn handle_sigint(_sig: i32) {
    RUNNING.store(false, Ordering::SeqCst);
}

unsafe extern "C" fn handle_sighup(_sig: i32) {
    RELOAD.store(true, Ordering::SeqCst);
}

fn main() {
    libc_signal(2, handle_sigint as *const () as usize);
    libc_signal(1, handle_sighup as *const () as usize); // SIGHUP = 1

    match parse_args() {
        Some(Commands::Scan) => cmd_scan(),
        Some(Commands::Check) => cmd_check(),
        Some(Commands::Status) => cmd_status(),
        Some(Commands::Init) => cmd_init(),
        None => run_daemon(),
    }
}

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn signal(sig: i32, handler: usize) -> usize;
    fn kill(pid: i32, sig: i32) -> i32;
}

unsafe fn libc_kill(pid: i32, sig: i32) {
    unsafe { kill(pid, sig); }
}

fn libc_signal(sig: i32, handler: usize) {
    unsafe {
        signal(sig, handler);
    }
}

// ── Config & state types ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

/// Everything derived from the config file that the main loop needs.
struct DaemonConfig {
    log_path: String,
    server_url: Option<String>,
    player_id: String,
    game_dir: Option<String>,
    game_baseline: HashMap<String, String>,
    auth_token: Option<String>,
    whitelist: Vec<String>,
    cheat_db: Vec<crate::config::CheatEntry>,
    active_profile: Option<profile::GameProfile>,
}

/// Per-scan collection buffers, reset each iteration.
struct ScanBuffers {
    suspicious: Vec<SuspiciousProcess>,
    cheats: Vec<CheatMatch>,
    connections: Vec<NetworkConnection>,
    modules: Vec<ModuleChange>,
}

// ── Initialisation helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────

/// Load config file, whitelist, cheat DB, profile, server auth, and game
/// baseline.  Returns a `DaemonConfig` ready for use in the main loop.
fn load_daemon_config() -> DaemonConfig {
    let whitelist = get_whitelist().unwrap_or_default();
    let mut cheat_db = get_cheat_db().unwrap_or_default();

    let config = match get_config() {
        Ok(c) => {
            println!("[CONFIG] Loaded /etc/vigil/config.toml");
            Some(c)
        }
        Err(e) => {
            eprintln!("[CONFIG] Failed to load config: {} - using defaults", e);
            None
        }
    };

    let log_path = config
        .as_ref()
        .map(|c| c.logging.path.clone())
        .unwrap_or_else(|| String::from("/var/log/vigil.log"));

    let active_profile = config
        .as_ref()
        .and_then(|c| c.game.profile.as_ref())
        .and_then(|name| {
            let profiles_dir = "/etc/vigil/profiles";
            match profile::find_profile(profiles_dir, name) {
                Some(p) => {
                    println!("[PROFILE] Active: {} ({})", p.name, name);
                    Some(p)
                }
                None => {
                    eprintln!("[PROFILE] Profile '{}' not found in {}", name, profiles_dir);
                    None
                }
            }
        });

    if let Some(ref prof) = active_profile {
        for name in &prof.cheat_names {
            cheat_db.push(crate::config::CheatEntry {
                hash: "name_only".to_string(),
                name: name.clone(),
                category: "cheat".to_string(),
                description: format!("from profile: {}", prof.name),
            });
        }
    }

    let game_path_from_config = config.as_ref().map(|c| c.game.path.clone());

    let server_url = config
        .as_ref()
        .and_then(|c| c.server.as_ref())
        .map(|s| s.url.clone());
    let player_id = config
        .as_ref()
        .and_then(|c| c.server.as_ref())
        .map(|s| s.player_id.clone())
        .unwrap_or_else(|| "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000".to_string());

    let mut auth_token: Option<String> = None;
    if let Some(ref url) = server_url {
        let server_cfg = config.as_ref().and_then(|c| c.server.as_ref());
        let name = server_cfg.map(|s| s.player_id.as_str()).unwrap_or("");
        let password = server_cfg.and_then(|s| s.password.as_deref()).unwrap_or("");

        if !password.is_empty() {
            match client::login(url, name, password) {
                Ok(token) => {
                    let _ = log(LogLevel::Info, "logged in to server", &log_path);
                    auth_token = Some(token);
                }
                Err(e) => {
                    let _ = log(LogLevel::Alert, &format!("server login failed: {}", e), &log_path);
                }
            }
        } else {
            let _ = log(LogLevel::Info, &format!("server reporting enabled (no auth), player_id: {}", player_id), &log_path);
        }
    }

    let (game_dir, game_baseline) = init_game_baseline(&game_path_from_config, &log_path);

    DaemonConfig {
        log_path,
        server_url,
        player_id,
        game_dir,
        game_baseline,
        auth_token,
        whitelist,
        cheat_db,
        active_profile,
    }
}

/// Load or create the game file baseline. Returns `(game_dir, baseline_map)`.
fn init_game_baseline(
    game_path_from_config: &Option<String>,
    log_path: &str,
) -> (Option<String>, HashMap<String, String>) {
    let baseline_path = "/etc/vigil/game_baseline.txt";
    let mut game_baseline: HashMap<String, String> = HashMap::new();
    let mut game_dir: Option<String> = None;

    let dir_result = game_path_from_config
        .clone()
        .ok_or_else(|| std::io::Error::new(std::io::ErrorKind::NotFound, "no config"))
        .or_else(|_| get_game_dir());

    if let Ok(dir) = dir_result {
        match load_baseline(baseline_path) {
            Ok(bl) => {
                let _ = log(
                    LogLevel::Info,
                    &format!("Baseline loaded ({} files)", bl.len()),
                    log_path,
                );
                game_baseline = bl;
            }
            Err(_) => {
                let _ = log(LogLevel::Info, "No baseline found, creating...", log_path);
                if let Ok(hashes) = scan_game_dir(&dir) {
                    let _ = log(
                        LogLevel::Info,
                        &format!("Baseline created ({} files)", hashes.len()),
                        log_path,
                    );
                    let _ = save_baseline(baseline_path, &hashes);
                    game_baseline = hashes;
                }
            }
        }

        if let Ok(current) = scan_game_dir(&dir) {
            let changes = compare_hashes(&game_baseline, &current);
            if changes.total() > 0 {
                for f in &changes.modified {
                    let _ = log(LogLevel::Alert, &format!("Game file MODIFIED: {}", f), log_path);
                }
                for f in &changes.added {
                    let _ = log(LogLevel::Alert, &format!("Game file ADDED: {}", f), log_path);
                }
                for f in &changes.removed {
                    let _ = log(LogLevel::Alert, &format!("Game file REMOVED: {}", f), log_path);
                }
                if changes.is_suspicious() {
                    let _ = log(
                        LogLevel::Cheat,
                        "Small targeted file change detected - possible cheat injection",
                        log_path,
                    );
                }
            } else {
                let _ = log(
                    LogLevel::Info,
                    "Game integrity OK - no changes since baseline",
                    log_path,
                );
            }
        }

        game_dir = Some(dir);
    }

    (game_dir, game_baseline)
}

/// Attempt to load eBPF programs and attach event readers.
/// Returns `(Option<ebpf_handle>, is_active)`.
fn init_ebpf(log_path: &str) -> (Option<crate::ebpf::EbpfState>, bool) {
    match start_ebpf() {
        Ok(mut ebpf) => {
            match get_events(&mut ebpf) {
                Ok(_event_fds) => {
                    if let Err(e) = read_events(&mut ebpf) {
                        let _ = log(LogLevel::Alert, &format!("eBPF event reader failed: {}", e), log_path);
                        (Some(ebpf), false)
                    } else {
                        let _ = log(LogLevel::Info, "eBPF loaded and listening", log_path);
                        (Some(ebpf), true)
                    }
                }
                Err(err) => {
                    let _ = log(LogLevel::Alert, &format!("eBPF get_events failed: {}", err), log_path);
                    (Some(ebpf), false)
                }
            }
        }
        Err(e) => {
            let _ = log(LogLevel::Info, &format!("eBPF not available: {}", e), log_path);
            (None, false)
        }
    }
}

/// Spawn background monitoring threads: inotify watcher, kernel log reader,
/// input device monitor, and honeypot watcher.
fn start_background_threads(
    game_dir: &Option<String>,
    game_baseline: HashMap<String, String>,
    log_path: &str,
) -> Option<Vec<std::path::PathBuf>> {
    if let Some(dir) = game_dir {
        let dir = dir.clone();
        let baseline = game_baseline.clone();
        let inotify_log_path = log_path.to_string();
        std::thread::spawn(move || {
            let _ = log(
                LogLevel::Inotify,
                &format!("Starting watcher for {}", dir),
                &inotify_log_path,
            );
            if let Err(e) = notify::watch_game_dir(dir, baseline) {
                let _ = log(
                    LogLevel::Inotify,
                    &format!("Watcher error: {}", e),
                    &inotify_log_path,
                );
            }
        });
    }

    std::thread::spawn(|| {
        if let Err(e) = get_kernel_logs(|log| parse_kernel_log(&log)) {
            eprintln!("[KLOG] Failed to read /dev/kmsg: {}", e);
        }
    });

    let input_log_path = log_path.to_string();
    std::thread::spawn(move || {
        input_monitor::watch_input_devices(|device| {
            let _ = log(
                LogLevel::Alert,
                &format!("new input device: {}", device),
                &input_log_path,
            );
        });
    });

    // plant honeypot traps
    match honeypot::plant_traps() {
        Ok(paths) => {
            let _ = log(LogLevel::Info, &format!("honeypot: {} traps planted", paths.len()), log_path);
            let log_path_hp = log_path.to_string();
            let paths_clone = paths.clone();
            std::thread::spawn(move || {
                honeypot::watch_traps(paths_clone, |hit| {
                    let who = match (hit.pid, &hit.process_name) {
                        (Some(pid), Some(name)) => format!(" by pid {} ({})", pid, name),
                        (Some(pid), None) => format!(" by pid {}", pid),
                        _ => String::new(),
                    };
                    let _ = log(
                        LogLevel::Cheat,
                        &format!("HONEYPOT: trap {} was {}{} — something is probing the system", hit.trap_path, hit.action, who),
                        &log_path_hp,
                    );
                });
            });
            Some(paths)
        }
        Err(e) => {
            let _ = log(LogLevel::Info, &format!("honeypot: {}", e), log_path);
            None
        }
    }
}

/// Create the shared IPC state and start the IPC listener thread.
fn init_ipc(ebpf_active: bool, active_profile: &Option<profile::GameProfile>) -> Arc<Mutex<ipc::DaemonState>> {
    let ipc_state = Arc::new(Mutex::new(ipc::DaemonState {
        trust_score: 100,
        ebpf_active,
        active_profile: active_profile.as_ref().map(|p| p.name.clone()),
        scan_count: 0,
        heartbeat_seq: 0,
        banned: false,
    }));

    let ipc_state_clone = Arc::clone(&ipc_state);
    ipc::start_ipc_listener(move || {
        ipc_state_clone.lock().unwrap().clone()
    });

    ipc_state
}

// ── Per-iteration helpers ────────────────────────────────────────────────────

/// Handle SIGHUP: reload whitelist, cheat DB, and active profile.
fn reload_if_signaled(
    whitelist: &mut Vec<String>,
    cheat_db: &mut Vec<crate::config::CheatEntry>,
    active_profile: &mut Option<profile::GameProfile>,
    log_path: &str,
) {
    if RELOAD.swap(false, Ordering::SeqCst) {
        let _ = log(LogLevel::Info, "SIGHUP received, reloading config", log_path);
        if let Ok(new_wl) = get_whitelist() { *whitelist = new_wl; }
        if let Ok(new_db) = get_cheat_db() { *cheat_db = new_db; }
        if let Ok(c) = get_config()
            && let Some(ref name) = c.game.profile
            && let Some(p) = profile::find_profile("/etc/vigil/profiles", name)
        {
            *active_profile = Some(p);
        }
    }
}

/// Every 12 heartbeats: refresh whitelist, cheat DB, and optionally pull new
/// signatures from the server.
fn refresh_cheat_db(
    heartbeat_seq: u64,
    whitelist: &mut Vec<String>,
    cheat_db: &mut Vec<crate::config::CheatEntry>,
    active_profile: &Option<profile::GameProfile>,
    server_url: &Option<String>,
    auth_token: Option<&str>,
    log_path: &str,
) {
    if !heartbeat_seq.is_multiple_of(12) {
        return;
    }

    if let Ok(new_wl) = get_whitelist() {
        *whitelist = new_wl;
    }
    if let Ok(mut new_db) = get_cheat_db() {
        merge_profile_cheats(&mut new_db, active_profile);
        *cheat_db = new_db;
    }

    if let Some(url) = server_url {
        match client::fetch_cheat_signatures(url, auth_token) {
            Ok(sigs) if !sigs.is_empty() => {
                if let Err(e) = std::fs::write("/etc/vigil/cheat_hashes.txt", &sigs) {
                    let _ = log(LogLevel::Info, &format!("failed to write cheat_hashes.txt: {}", e), log_path);
                } else {
                    let _ = log(LogLevel::Info, "cheat signatures updated from server", log_path);
                    if let Ok(mut new_db) = get_cheat_db() {
                        merge_profile_cheats(&mut new_db, active_profile);
                        *cheat_db = new_db;
                    }
                }
            }
            Ok(_) => {} // empty response — no signatures configured on server
            Err(e) => {
                let _ = log(LogLevel::Info, &format!("cheat signature fetch: {}", e), log_path);
            }
        }
    }
}

/// Append profile-specific cheat names into a cheat DB vector.
fn merge_profile_cheats(db: &mut Vec<crate::config::CheatEntry>, profile: &Option<profile::GameProfile>) {
    if let Some(p) = profile {
        for name in &p.cheat_names {
            db.push(crate::config::CheatEntry {
                hash: "name_only".to_string(),
                name: name.clone(),
                category: "profile".to_string(),
                description: format!("from {} profile", p.name),
            });
        }
    }
}

/// Run self-tamper checks and clock-skew detection.
/// Returns `(tamper_issues, clock_drift_ms)`.
fn check_tamper_and_clock(
    startup_hash: &str,
    clock_watcher: &mut speedhack::ClockWatcher,
    log_path: &str,
) -> (Vec<String>, Option<i64>) {
    let mut tamper_issues = self_protect::check();
    if !self_protect::check_binary_integrity(startup_hash) {
        tamper_issues.push("vigil binary changed on disk".to_string());
    }
    for issue in &tamper_issues {
        let _ = log(LogLevel::Alert, &format!("TAMPER: {}", issue), log_path);
    }

    let clock_drift_ms = match clock_watcher.check(5000) {
        Some(anomaly) => {
            let _ = log(
                LogLevel::Cheat,
                &format!("clock anomaly: {} ({}ms)", anomaly.kind, anomaly.drift_ms),
                log_path,
            );
            Some(anomaly.drift_ms)
        }
        None => None,
    };

    (tamper_issues, clock_drift_ms)
}

/// Run all checks for a single process (maps, fds, connections, hash, launch
/// chain, injection, capabilities, namespaces, rwx, text integrity).
///
/// Mutates `found`, `found_maps`, `kill_pending`, `seen_connections`, and the
/// `buffers` report vectors.  Returns the `process::Process` value on success.
#[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]
fn scan_single_process(
    pid: u64,
    whitelist: &[String],
    cheat_db: &[crate::config::CheatEntry],
    found: &mut HashSet<u64>,
    found_maps: &mut HashSet<String>,
    kill_pending: &mut HashMap<u64, u8>,
    seen_connections: &mut HashSet<String>,
    maps_baseline: &mut HashMap<u64, HashSet<String>>,
    history: &HashSet<u64>,
    first_run: bool,
    buffers: &mut ScanBuffers,
    log_path: &str,
) -> Option<crate::process::Proc> {
    let proc = get_process(pid, whitelist).ok()?;

    if let Ok(val) = get_map(pid, found_maps, whitelist)
        && !val.is_empty()
    {
        for (path, reason) in &val {
            let _ = log(
                LogLevel::Alert,
                &format!("pid {} suspicious map: {} ({})", pid, path, reason),
                log_path,
            );
            buffers.suspicious.push(SuspiciousProcess {
                pid,
                name: path.clone(),
                reason: reason.clone(),
            });
        }
    }

    if let Ok(val) = get_fd(pid)
        && !val.is_empty()
    {
        let _ = log(
            LogLevel::Alert,
            &format!("pid {} reading other process memory via fd: {:?}", pid, val),
            log_path,
        );
    }

    if let Ok(inodes) = get_inode(pid)
        && !inodes.is_empty()
        && let Ok(connections) = get_connections(&inodes)
    {
        for conn in &connections {
            let key = format!("{}:{}", pid, conn);
            if seen_connections.insert(key) {
                let _ = log(
                    LogLevel::Net,
                    &format!("pid {} has connection: {}", pid, conn),
                    log_path,
                );
            }
            buffers.connections.push(NetworkConnection {
                pid,
                address: conn.clone(),
            });
        }
    }

    if let Ok(Some((name, category, desc))) = check_hash(pid, cheat_db) {
        let _ = log(
            LogLevel::Cheat,
            &format!("pid {} matched: {} [{}] - {}", pid, name, category, desc),
            log_path,
        );
        let strikes = kill_pending.entry(pid).or_insert(0);
        *strikes += 1;
        if *strikes >= 2 {
            unsafe { libc_kill(pid as i32, 9); }
            let _ = log(
                LogLevel::Alert,
                &format!("killed cheat process pid {} (confirmed)", pid),
                log_path,
            );
            kill_pending.remove(&pid);
        } else {
            let _ = log(
                LogLevel::Alert,
                &format!("cheat pid {} flagged, will kill on next scan if still present", pid),
                log_path,
            );
        }
        buffers.cheats.push(CheatMatch {
            pid,
            name: name.clone(),
            category: category.clone(),
            description: desc.clone(),
        });
    }

    if found.contains(&pid) && !proc.is_suspicious() {
        found.remove(&pid);
    }

    if proc.is_suspicious() && !found.contains(&pid) {
        let _ = log(LogLevel::Alert, &format!("suspicious: {}", proc), log_path);
        found.insert(pid);

        let tree = get_process_tree(pid);
        let (valid, chain_desc) = validate_launch_chain(&tree);
        if !valid {
            let _ = log(
                LogLevel::Alert,
                &format!("invalid launch chain for pid {}: {}", pid, chain_desc),
                log_path,
            );
        }
    }

    let injected = track_maps_changes(pid, maps_baseline, whitelist);
    for lib in &injected {
        let _ = log(
            LogLevel::Alert,
            &format!("[INJECTION] pid {} new .so: {}", pid, lib),
            log_path,
        );
        buffers.suspicious.push(SuspiciousProcess {
            pid,
            name: lib.clone(),
            reason: "injected library detected after baseline".to_string(),
        });
    }

    if let Some(cap) = check_capabilities(pid)
        && !proc.to_string().contains("vigil")
    {
        let _ = log(
            LogLevel::Alert,
            &format!("pid {} has {}", pid, cap),
            log_path,
        );
    }

    if let Some(ns_issue) = check_namespaces(pid) {
        let _ = log(
            LogLevel::Alert,
            &format!("pid {} namespace: {}", pid, ns_issue),
            log_path,
        );
    }

    let rwx = check_rwx_maps(pid);
    for mapping in &rwx {
        let _ = log(
            LogLevel::Alert,
            &format!("pid {} rwx mapping: {}", pid, mapping),
            log_path,
        );
    }

    // text integrity check — expensive, only for already-flagged processes
    if found.contains(&pid)
        && let Some(reason) = check_text_integrity(pid)
    {
        let _ = log(
            LogLevel::Cheat,
            &format!("pid {} text integrity: {}", pid, reason),
            log_path,
        );
        buffers.suspicious.push(SuspiciousProcess {
            pid,
            name: proc.to_string(),
            reason,
        });
    }

    if !history.contains(&pid) && !first_run {
        let _ = log(
            LogLevel::Info,
            &format!("new process: {}", proc),
            log_path,
        );
    }

    Some(proc)
}

/// Diff the live kernel module list against `module_history`, log changes, and
/// return a `Vec<ModuleChange>` for the report.
fn check_modules(
    module_history: &mut HashSet<String>,
    first_run: bool,
    log_path: &str,
) -> Vec<ModuleChange> {
    let mut changes = vec![];

    if let Ok(modules) = get_modules() {
        let current: HashSet<String> = modules.into_iter().collect();

        if !first_run {
            for new_mod in current.difference(module_history) {
                let _ = log(
                    LogLevel::Alert,
                    &format!("New kernel module loaded: {}", new_mod),
                    log_path,
                );
                changes.push(ModuleChange { name: new_mod.clone(), action: "loaded".to_string() });
            }
            for dead_mod in module_history.difference(&current) {
                let _ = log(
                    LogLevel::Info,
                    &format!("Kernel module unloaded: {}", dead_mod),
                    log_path,
                );
                changes.push(ModuleChange { name: dead_mod.clone(), action: "unloaded".to_string() });
            }
        }

        *module_history = current;
    }

    changes
}

/// Build a `FileIntegrity` snapshot by comparing the current game directory
/// against the stored baseline.
fn build_file_integrity(
    game_dir: &Option<String>,
    game_baseline: &HashMap<String, String>,
) -> FileIntegrity {
    match game_dir.as_deref() {
        Some(dir) => {
            if let Ok(current) = scan_game_dir(dir) {
                let changes = compare_hashes(game_baseline, &current);
                FileIntegrity {
                    status: if changes.total() == 0 { "ok".to_string() } else { "modified".to_string() },
                    modified: changes.modified,
                    added: changes.added,
                    removed: changes.removed,
                }
            } else {
                FileIntegrity { status: "unknown".to_string(), modified: vec![], added: vec![], removed: vec![] }
            }
        }
        None => FileIntegrity { status: "unconfigured".to_string(), modified: vec![], added: vec![], removed: vec![] },
    }
}

/// Build the scan report and POST it to the server.  Stores any returned
/// challenge into `pending_challenge`.
#[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]
fn send_report(
    cfg: &DaemonConfig,
    buffers: ScanBuffers,
    report_traces: Vec<CrossTrace>,
    tamper_issues: Vec<String>,
    clock_drift_ms: Option<i64>,
    startup_hash: &str,
    heartbeat_seq: u64,
    ebpf_active: bool,
    sandbox_reasons: &[String],
    pending_challenge: &mut Option<String>,
) {
    let url = match cfg.server_url.as_deref() {
        Some(u) => u,
        None => return,
    };

    let integrity = build_file_integrity(&cfg.game_dir, &cfg.game_baseline);

    let scan_report = build_report(
        &cfg.player_id,
        ebpf_active,
        sandbox_reasons,
        buffers.suspicious,
        buffers.cheats,
        report_traces,
        buffers.connections,
        buffers.modules,
        integrity,
        heartbeat_seq,
        tamper_issues,
        clock_drift_ms,
        startup_hash,
        pending_challenge.take().map(|ch| {
            let input = format!("{}{}{}{}", ch, startup_hash, report::get_hostname(), heartbeat_seq);
            crate::crypto::sha256_hex(input.as_bytes())
        }),
    );

    match client::send_report(url, &scan_report, cfg.auth_token.as_deref()) {
        Ok(resp) => {
            if resp.banned {
                let reason = resp.ban_reason.as_deref().unwrap_or("unknown");
                let _ = log(
                    LogLevel::Alert,
                    &format!("player banned by server: {}", reason),
                    &cfg.log_path,
                );
            }
            if let Some(score) = resp.trust_score {
                let level = if score < 50 { LogLevel::Alert } else { LogLevel::Info };
                let _ = log(level, &format!("trust score: {}", score), &cfg.log_path);
            }
            if let Some(ch) = resp.challenge {
                *pending_challenge = Some(ch);
            }
        }
        Err(e) => {
            let _ = log(
                LogLevel::Info,
                &format!("server unreachable, queueing report: {}", e),
                &cfg.log_path,
            );
            let report_json = crate::report::to_json(&scan_report);
            if let Err(qe) = report_queue::enqueue(&report_json, heartbeat_seq) {
                let _ = log(LogLevel::Info, &format!("queue error: {}", qe), &cfg.log_path);
            }
        }
    }
}

// ── Main daemon entry point ──────────────────────────────────────────────────

fn run_daemon() {
    self_protect::harden();
    let startup_hash = self_protect::binary_hash().unwrap_or_default();

    let mut cfg = load_daemon_config();

    let (_active_ebpf, ebpf_active) = init_ebpf(&cfg.log_path);

    let _honeypot_traps = start_background_threads(
        &cfg.game_dir,
        cfg.game_baseline.clone(),
        &cfg.log_path,
    );

    let sandbox_reasons = check_sandbox().unwrap_or_default();
    if !sandbox_reasons.is_empty() {
        let _ = log(
            LogLevel::Alert,
            &format!("sandbox detected: {}", sandbox_reasons.join(", ")),
            &cfg.log_path,
        );
    }

    let ipc_state = init_ipc(ebpf_active, &cfg.active_profile);

    println!(
        r#"


VVVVVVVV           VVVVVVVV iiii                        iiii  lllllll
V::::::V           V::::::Vi::::i                      i::::i l:::::l
V::::::V           V::::::V iiii                        iiii  l:::::l
V::::::V           V::::::V                                   l:::::l
 V:::::V           V:::::Viiiiiii    ggggggggg   gggggiiiiiii  l::::l
  V:::::V         V:::::V i:::::i   g:::::::::ggg::::gi:::::i  l::::l
   V:::::V       V:::::V   i::::i  g:::::::::::::::::g i::::i  l::::l
    V:::::V     V:::::V    i::::i g::::::ggggg::::::gg i::::i  l::::l
     V:::::V   V:::::V     i::::i g:::::g     g:::::g  i::::i  l::::l
      V:::::V V:::::V      i::::i g:::::g     g:::::g  i::::i  l::::l
       V:::::V:::::V       i::::i g:::::g     g:::::g  i::::i  l::::l
        V:::::::::V        i::::i g::::::g    g:::::g  i::::i  l::::l
         V:::::::V        i::::::ig:::::::ggggg:::::g i::::::il::::::l
          V:::::V         i::::::i g::::::::::::::::g i::::::il::::::l
           V:::V          i::::::i  gg::::::::::::::g i::::::il::::::l
            VVV           iiiiiiii    gggggggg::::::g iiiiiiiillllllll
                                              g:::::g
                                  gggggg      g:::::g
                                  g:::::gg   gg:::::g
                                   g::::::ggg:::::::g
                                    gg:::::::::::::g
                                      ggg::::::ggg
                                         gggggg
      "#
    );

    // ── Per-iteration state ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
    let mut history: HashSet<u64> = HashSet::new();
    let mut module_history: HashSet<String> = HashSet::new();
    let mut found: HashSet<u64> = HashSet::new();
    let mut found_maps: HashSet<String> = HashSet::new();
    let mut kill_pending: HashMap<u64, u8> = HashMap::new();
    let mut seen_connections: HashSet<String> = HashSet::new();
    let mut procs = vec![];
    let mut heartbeat_seq: u64 = 0;
    let mut clock_watcher = speedhack::ClockWatcher::new();
    let mut pending_challenge: Option<String> = None;
    let mut maps_baseline: HashMap<u64, HashSet<String>> = HashMap::new();
    let mut first_run = true;

    runtime::block_on(async {
        while RUNNING.load(Ordering::SeqCst) {
            procs.clear();
            heartbeat_seq += 1;

            reload_if_signaled(
                &mut cfg.whitelist,
                &mut cfg.cheat_db,
                &mut cfg.active_profile,
                &cfg.log_path,
            );

            refresh_cheat_db(
                heartbeat_seq,
                &mut cfg.whitelist,
                &mut cfg.cheat_db,
                &cfg.active_profile,
                &cfg.server_url,
                cfg.auth_token.as_deref(),
                &cfg.log_path,
            );

            let (tamper_issues, clock_drift_ms) =
                check_tamper_and_clock(&startup_hash, &mut clock_watcher, &cfg.log_path);

            let mut buffers = ScanBuffers {
                suspicious: vec![],
                cheats: vec![],
                connections: vec![],
                modules: vec![],
            };

            if let Ok(vec) = scan_processes() {
                for &pid in &vec {
                    if let Some(proc) = scan_single_process(
                        pid,
                        &cfg.whitelist,
                        &cfg.cheat_db,
                        &mut found,
                        &mut found_maps,
                        &mut kill_pending,
                        &mut seen_connections,
                        &mut maps_baseline,
                        &history,
                        first_run,
                        &mut buffers,
                        &cfg.log_path,
                    ) {
                        procs.push(proc);
                    }
                }

                let cross_traced = get_cross_traces(&procs);
                let report_traces: Vec<CrossTrace> = cross_traced
                    .iter()
                    .filter(|(_, targets)| targets.len() > 1)
                    .map(|(tracer, targets)| {
                        let _ = log(
                            LogLevel::Alert,
                            &format!(
                                "tracer pid {} attached to {} processes: {}",
                                tracer,
                                targets.len(),
                                targets.iter().map(|p| p.to_string()).collect::<Vec<_>>().join(", ")
                            ),
                            &cfg.log_path,
                        );
                        CrossTrace { tracer_pid: *tracer, targets: targets.clone() }
                    })
                    .collect();

                for (overlay_pid, reason) in check_overlay_processes() {
                    let _ = log(
                        LogLevel::Alert,
                        &format!("pid {} {}", overlay_pid, reason),
                        &cfg.log_path,
                    );
                }

                history = vec.into_iter().collect();

                buffers.modules = check_modules(&mut module_history, first_run, &cfg.log_path);

                send_report(
                    &cfg,
                    buffers,
                    report_traces,
                    tamper_issues,
                    clock_drift_ms,
                    &startup_hash,
                    heartbeat_seq,
                    ebpf_active,
                    &sandbox_reasons,
                    &mut pending_challenge,
                );

                // flush any queued reports from previous offline periods
                if cfg.server_url.is_some() && cfg.auth_token.is_some() {
                    let flushed = report_queue::flush(
                        cfg.server_url.as_deref().unwrap(),
                        cfg.auth_token.as_deref(),
                    );
                    if flushed > 0 {
                        let _ = log(
                            LogLevel::Info,
                            &format!("flushed {} queued reports", flushed),
                            &cfg.log_path,
                        );
                    }
                }
            }

            first_run = false;

            if let Ok(mut state) = ipc_state.lock() {
                state.scan_count = heartbeat_seq;
                state.heartbeat_seq = heartbeat_seq;
                state.ebpf_active = ebpf_active;
            }

            for cmd in ipc::take_commands() {
                match cmd {
                    ipc::IpcCommand::SetProfile(name) => {
                        if let Some(p) = profile::find_profile("/etc/vigil/profiles", &name) {
                            let _ = log(LogLevel::Info, &format!("switched to {}", p.name), &cfg.log_path);
                            cfg.active_profile = Some(p);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            runtime::sleep(Duration::from_secs(5)).await;
        }
    });

    honeypot::cleanup_traps();
    let _ = log(LogLevel::Info, "Vigil stopped (SIGINT)", &cfg.log_path);
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/network.rs`:

```rs
// resolves socket inodes from /proc/PID/fd
pub fn get_inode(pid: u64) -> std::io::Result<Vec<u64>> {
    let path = format!("/proc/{}/fd", pid);
    let dir = std::fs::read_dir(path)?;
    let mut res = vec![];
    for entry in dir {
        let entry = entry?;
        let content = std::fs::read_link(entry.path())?;
        let symlink = content.to_string_lossy();

        if symlink.starts_with("socket:[") {
            let item = symlink.trim_start_matches("socket:[").trim_end_matches("]");
            if item.is_empty() {
                continue;
            }

            if let Ok(num) = item.parse::<u64>() {
                res.push(num);
            }
        }
    }
    Ok(res)
}

// parses /proc/net/tcp, /proc/net/udp, /proc/net/tcp6, /proc/net/udp6
pub fn get_connections(inodes: &[u64]) -> Result<Vec<String>, Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {
    let mut seen = std::collections::HashSet::new();
    let mut res = vec![];

    for (path, proto, ipv6) in [
        ("/proc/net/tcp", "tcp", false),
        ("/proc/net/udp", "udp", false),
        ("/proc/net/tcp6", "tcp6", true),
        ("/proc/net/udp6", "udp6", true),
    ] {
        let content = match std::fs::read_to_string(path) {
            Ok(c) => c,
            Err(_) => continue,
        };
        for line in content.lines() {
            let parts: Vec<&str> = line.split_whitespace().collect();
            if parts.len() < 10 || parts[0] == "sl" {
                continue;
            }
            // skip no-remote connections
            if !ipv6 && parts[2] == "00000000:0000" { continue; }
            if ipv6 && parts[2] == "00000000000000000000000000000000:0000" { continue; }

            let line_inode = match parts[9].parse::<u64>() {
                Ok(i) => i,
                Err(_) => continue,
            };
            if !inodes.contains(&line_inode) { continue; }

            let addr_parts: Vec<&str> = parts[2].split(':').collect();
            if addr_parts.len() != 2 { continue; }

            let port = match u16::from_str_radix(addr_parts[1], 16) {
                Ok(p) => p,
                Err(_) => continue,
            };

            let ip = if ipv6 {
                parse_ipv6_hex(addr_parts[0])
            } else {
                parse_ipv4_hex(addr_parts[0])
            };

            let addr = format!("{}/{}:{}", proto, ip, port);
            if seen.insert(addr.clone()) {
                res.push(addr);
            }
        }
    }

    Ok(res)
}

fn parse_ipv4_hex(hex: &str) -> String {
    let raw = u32::from_str_radix(hex, 16).unwrap_or(0);
    let b = raw.to_le_bytes();
    format!("{}.{}.{}.{}", b[0], b[1], b[2], b[3])
}

fn parse_ipv6_hex(hex: &str) -> String {
    if hex.len() != 32 { return hex.to_string(); }
    // /proc/net/tcp6 stores IPv6 as 4 groups of 8 hex chars, each in host byte order
    let mut groups = [0u32; 4];
    for i in 0..4 {
        groups[i] = u32::from_str_radix(&hex[i*8..(i+1)*8], 16).unwrap_or(0);
    }
    // convert to bytes (little-endian per group, same as ipv4)
    let mut bytes = [0u8; 16];
    for i in 0..4 {
        let b = groups[i].to_le_bytes();
        bytes[i*4..i*4+4].copy_from_slice(&b);
    }
    // check if v4-mapped: bytes 0-7 zero, bytes 8-9 = 0xff
    // (after le conversion from /proc/net/tcp6 format)
    if bytes[0..8] == [0; 8] && bytes[8] == 0xff && bytes[9] == 0xff && bytes[10] == 0 && bytes[11] == 0 {
        return format!("::ffff:{}.{}.{}.{}", bytes[12], bytes[13], bytes[14], bytes[15]);
    }
    // format as compressed ipv6
    let mut segs = [0u16; 8];
    for i in 0..8 {
        segs[i] = u16::from_be_bytes([bytes[i*2], bytes[i*2+1]]);
    }
    let parts: Vec<String> = segs.iter().map(|s| format!("{:x}", s)).collect();
    parts.join(":")
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn parse_ipv4() {
        assert_eq!(parse_ipv4_hex("0100007F"), "127.0.0.1");
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_ipv6_loopback() {
        assert_eq!(parse_ipv6_hex("00000000000000000000000001000000"), "0:0:0:0:0:0:0:1");
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_ipv6_v4mapped() {
        // ::ffff:127.0.0.1
        assert_eq!(parse_ipv6_hex("00000000000000000000FFFF0100007F"), "::ffff:127.0.0.1");
    }

    #[test]
    fn get_connections_doesnt_crash() {
        // just make sure it doesn't panic with empty inodes
        let _ = get_connections(&[]);
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/notify.rs`:

```rs
use std::collections::HashMap;
use std::path::{Path, PathBuf};

use crate::sys::{InotifyEvent, IN_MODIFY, IN_CREATE, IN_DELETE, IN_MOVED_FROM, IN_MOVED_TO, IN_ISDIR, IN_CLOEXEC};

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn inotify_init1(flags: i32) -> i32;
    fn inotify_add_watch(fd: i32, pathname: *const u8, mask: u32) -> i32;
    fn read(fd: i32, buf: *mut u8, count: usize) -> isize;
    fn close(fd: i32) -> i32;
}

// runs in a blocking loop - meant to be called from std::thread::spawn
pub fn watch_game_dir(dir: String, baseline: HashMap<String, String>) -> Result<(), String> {
    let fd = unsafe { inotify_init1(IN_CLOEXEC) };
    if fd < 0 {
        return Err("inotify_init failed".to_string());
    }

    let mut wd_to_path: HashMap<i32, PathBuf> = HashMap::new();
    let mask = IN_MODIFY | IN_CREATE | IN_DELETE | IN_MOVED_FROM | IN_MOVED_TO;

    add_watches_recursive(fd, Path::new(&dir), mask, &mut wd_to_path)?;

    println!("[INOTIFY] Watching {} ({} directories)", dir, wd_to_path.len());

    let mut buf = vec![0u8; 4096];
    loop {
        let n = unsafe { read(fd, buf.as_mut_ptr(), buf.len()) };
        if n <= 0 {
            break;
        }

        let mut offset = 0;
        while offset < n as usize {
            let event = unsafe { &*(buf.as_ptr().add(offset) as *const InotifyEvent) };
            let name_len = event.len as usize;

            let name = if name_len > 0 {
                let name_ptr = unsafe { buf.as_ptr().add(offset + std::mem::size_of::<InotifyEvent>()) };
                let name_bytes = unsafe { std::slice::from_raw_parts(name_ptr, name_len) };
                let end = name_bytes.iter().position(|&b| b == 0).unwrap_or(name_len);
                String::from_utf8_lossy(&name_bytes[..end]).to_string()
            } else {
                offset += std::mem::size_of::<InotifyEvent>();
                continue;
            };

            offset += std::mem::size_of::<InotifyEvent>() + name_len;

            let dir_path = match wd_to_path.get(&event.wd) {
                Some(p) => p.clone(),
                None => continue,
            };

            let full_path = dir_path.join(&name);
            let path_str = full_path.to_string_lossy().to_string();

            if event.mask & IN_ISDIR != 0 {
                if event.mask & (IN_CREATE | IN_MOVED_TO) != 0 {
                    add_watch(fd, &full_path, mask, &mut wd_to_path);
                    println!("[INOTIFY] New directory watched: {}", path_str);
                }
                continue;
            }

            if event.mask & IN_MODIFY != 0 {
                match hash_file(&full_path) {
                    Ok(hash) => {
                        if let Some(baseline_hash) = baseline.get(&path_str) {
                            if *baseline_hash != hash {
                                println!("[INOTIFY] MODIFIED: {} (hash changed)", path_str);
                            }
                        } else {
                            println!("[INOTIFY] MODIFIED: {} (not in baseline)", path_str);
                        }
                    }
                    Err(_) => println!("[INOTIFY] MODIFIED: {} (could not hash)", path_str),
                }
            } else if event.mask & (IN_CREATE | IN_MOVED_TO) != 0 {
                println!("[INOTIFY] ADDED: {}", path_str);
            } else if event.mask & (IN_DELETE | IN_MOVED_FROM) != 0 {
                println!("[INOTIFY] REMOVED: {}", path_str);
            }
        }
    }

    unsafe { close(fd) };
    Ok(())
}

fn add_watch(fd: i32, path: &Path, mask: u32, wd_to_path: &mut HashMap<i32, PathBuf>) {
    let path_str = format!("{}\0", path.display());
    let wd = unsafe { inotify_add_watch(fd, path_str.as_ptr(), mask) };
    if wd >= 0 {
        wd_to_path.insert(wd, path.to_path_buf());
    }
}

fn add_watches_recursive(
    fd: i32,
    dir: &Path,
    mask: u32,
    wd_to_path: &mut HashMap<i32, PathBuf>,
) -> Result<(), String> {
    add_watch(fd, dir, mask, wd_to_path);
    for entry in std::fs::read_dir(dir).map_err(|e| e.to_string())? {
        let entry = entry.map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
        if entry.path().is_dir() {
            add_watches_recursive(fd, &entry.path(), mask, wd_to_path)?;
        }
    }
    Ok(())
}

fn hash_file(path: &Path) -> std::io::Result<String> {
    let bytes = std::fs::read(path)?;
    Ok(crate::crypto::sha256_hex(&bytes))
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/process.rs`:

```rs
pub trait Suspicious {
    fn is_suspicious(&self) -> bool;
}

#[derive(Debug)]
pub struct Proc {
    name: String,
    pid: u64,
    status: ProcessStatus,
    tracer_pid: u64,
    preload_path: Option<String>,
    cmdline: String,
    exe_path: Option<String>,
    ppid: u64,
}

#[derive(Debug)]
pub enum ProcessStatus {
    Running,
    Sleeping,
    Stopped,
    Zombie,
    #[allow(dead_code)]
    Suspicious(String),
}

impl Proc {
    #[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]
    pub fn new(
        name: String,
        pid: u64,
        status: ProcessStatus,
        tracer_pid: u64,
        preload_path: Option<String>,
        cmdline: String,
        exe_path: Option<String>,
        ppid: u64,
    ) -> Self {
        Self {
            name,
            pid,
            status,
            tracer_pid,
            preload_path,
            cmdline,
            exe_path,
            ppid,
        }
    }

    pub fn get_tracer_pid(&self) -> &u64 {
        &self.tracer_pid
    }

    pub fn get_pid(&self) -> &u64 {
        &self.pid
    }

    #[allow(dead_code)]
    pub fn get_ppid(&self) -> &u64 {
        &self.ppid
    }

    #[allow(dead_code)]
    pub fn get_name(&self) -> &str {
        &self.name
    }
}

impl std::fmt::Display for Proc {
    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
        write!(f, "{} (pid={}, ppid={})", self.name, self.pid, self.ppid)?;
        if self.tracer_pid != 0 {
            write!(f, " traced_by={}", self.tracer_pid)?;
        }
        if let Some(ref p) = self.preload_path {
            write!(f, " LD_PRELOAD={}", p)?;
        }
        if let Some(ref p) = self.exe_path {
            write!(f, " exe={}", p)?;
        }
        Ok(())
    }
}

impl Suspicious for Proc {
    fn is_suspicious(&self) -> bool {
        self.name.contains("cheat")
            || self.tracer_pid != 0
            || self.preload_path.is_some()
            || self.cmdline.contains("gdb")
            || self.cmdline.contains("strace")
            || self.cmdline.contains("ltrace")
            || self.cmdline.contains("scanmem")
            || self.cmdline.contains("gameconqueror")
            || self.cmdline.contains("pince")
            || self.name.contains("inject")
            || self.name.contains("hack")
            || self.name.contains("trainer")
            || self.exe_path.is_some()
            || matches!(self.status, ProcessStatus::Suspicious(_))
    }
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    fn make_proc(
        name: &str,
        tracer_pid: u64,
        preload: Option<&str>,
        cmdline: &str,
        exe_path: Option<&str>,
        status: ProcessStatus,
    ) -> Proc {
        Proc::new(
            name.to_string(),
            1234,
            status,
            tracer_pid,
            preload.map(|s| s.to_string()),
            cmdline.to_string(),
            exe_path.map(|s| s.to_string()),
            1,
        )
    }

    #[test]
    fn clean_process_not_suspicious() {
        let p = make_proc("bash", 0, None, "/bin/bash", None, ProcessStatus::Running);
        assert!(!p.is_suspicious());
    }

    #[test]
    fn cheat_name_is_suspicious() {
        let p = make_proc("mycheat", 0, None, "./mycheat", None, ProcessStatus::Running);
        assert!(p.is_suspicious());
    }

    #[test]
    fn tracer_pid_is_suspicious() {
        let p = make_proc("game", 999, None, "/opt/game", None, ProcessStatus::Running);
        assert!(p.is_suspicious());
    }

    #[test]
    fn preload_is_suspicious() {
        let p = make_proc(
            "game",
            0,
            Some("/tmp/hack.so"),
            "/opt/game",
            None,
            ProcessStatus::Running,
        );
        assert!(p.is_suspicious());
    }

    #[test]
    fn gdb_cmdline_is_suspicious() {
        let p = make_proc("gdb", 0, None, "gdb -p 1234", None, ProcessStatus::Running);
        assert!(p.is_suspicious());
    }

    #[test]
    fn strace_cmdline_is_suspicious() {
        let p = make_proc("strace", 0, None, "strace -p 1234", None, ProcessStatus::Running);
        assert!(p.is_suspicious());
    }

    #[test]
    fn exe_from_tmp_is_suspicious() {
        let p = make_proc(
            "hack",
            0,
            None,
            "./hack",
            Some("/tmp/hack"),
            ProcessStatus::Running,
        );
        assert!(p.is_suspicious());
    }

    #[test]
    fn suspicious_status_is_suspicious() {
        let p = make_proc(
            "thing",
            0,
            None,
            "./thing",
            None,
            ProcessStatus::Suspicious("X (unknown)".to_string()),
        );
        assert!(p.is_suspicious());
    }

    #[test]
    fn sleeping_process_not_suspicious() {
        let p = make_proc("sleep", 0, None, "sleep 60", None, ProcessStatus::Sleeping);
        assert!(!p.is_suspicious());
    }

    #[test]
    fn getters_work() {
        let p = make_proc("test", 42, None, "test", None, ProcessStatus::Running);
        assert_eq!(*p.get_pid(), 1234);
        assert_eq!(*p.get_tracer_pid(), 42);
    }

    #[test]
    fn get_ppid_works() {
        let p = Proc::new(
            "child".to_string(), 500, ProcessStatus::Running,
            0, None, "child".to_string(), None, 100,
        );
        assert_eq!(*p.get_ppid(), 100);
        assert_eq!(p.get_name(), "child");
    }
}
```
