`crates/vigil/src/profile.rs`:

```rs
#[derive(Debug)]
#[allow(dead_code)]
pub struct GameProfile {
    pub name: String,
    pub steam_appid: u32,
    pub process_name: String,
    pub install_path: String,
    pub whitelist_processes: Vec<String>,
    pub whitelist_libraries: Vec<String>,
    pub watch_dirs: Vec<String>,
    pub ignore_patterns: Vec<String>,
    pub cheat_names: Vec<String>,
}

pub fn load_profile(path: &str) -> Result<GameProfile, String> {
    let content =
        std::fs::read_to_string(path).map_err(|e| format!("failed to read {}: {}", path, e))?;
    parse_profile(&content)
}

pub fn parse_profile(content: &str) -> Result<GameProfile, String> {
    let mut section = "";

    let mut name: Option<String> = None;
    let mut steam_appid: Option<u32> = None;
    let mut process_name: Option<String> = None;
    let mut install_path: Option<String> = None;
    let mut whitelist_processes: Vec<String> = vec![];
    let mut whitelist_libraries: Vec<String> = vec![];
    let mut watch_dirs: Vec<String> = vec![];
    let mut ignore_patterns: Vec<String> = vec![];
    let mut cheat_names: Vec<String> = vec![];

    for (lineno, raw) in content.lines().enumerate() {
        let line = raw.trim();

        if line.is_empty() || line.starts_with('#') {
            continue;
        }

        if line.starts_with('[') {
            if !line.ends_with(']') {
                return Err(format!("line {}: malformed section: {}", lineno + 1, line));
            }
            section = &line[1..line.len() - 1];
            continue;
        }

        let eq = line
            .find('=')
            .ok_or_else(|| format!("line {}: expected '=' in: {}", lineno + 1, line))?;
        let key = line[..eq].trim();
        let rest = line[eq + 1..].trim();

        match section {
            "game" => match key {
                "name" => name = Some(parse_str(rest, lineno + 1)?),
                "steam_appid" => steam_appid = Some(parse_num(rest, lineno + 1)?),
                "process_name" => process_name = Some(parse_str(rest, lineno + 1)?),
                "install_path" => install_path = Some(parse_str(rest, lineno + 1)?),
                _ => {}
            },
            "whitelist" => match key {
                "processes" => whitelist_processes = parse_array(rest, lineno + 1)?,
                "libraries" => whitelist_libraries = parse_array(rest, lineno + 1)?,
                _ => {}
            },
            "integrity" => match key {
                "watch_dirs" => watch_dirs = parse_array(rest, lineno + 1)?,
                "ignore" => ignore_patterns = parse_array(rest, lineno + 1)?,
                _ => {}
            },
            "detection" => {
                if key == "cheat_names" {
                    cheat_names = parse_array(rest, lineno + 1)?;
                }
            }
            _ => {}
        }
    }

    Ok(GameProfile {
        name: name.ok_or("missing [game] name")?,
        steam_appid: steam_appid.ok_or("missing [game] steam_appid")?,
        process_name: process_name.ok_or("missing [game] process_name")?,
        install_path: install_path.ok_or("missing [game] install_path")?,
        whitelist_processes,
        whitelist_libraries,
        watch_dirs,
        ignore_patterns,
        cheat_names,
    })
}

fn parse_str(val: &str, lineno: usize) -> Result<String, String> {
    if !val.starts_with('"') || !val.ends_with('"') || val.len() < 2 {
        return Err(format!("line {}: expected quoted string: {}", lineno, val));
    }
    Ok(val[1..val.len() - 1].to_string())
}

fn parse_num(val: &str, lineno: usize) -> Result<u32, String> {
    val.parse::<u32>()
        .map_err(|_| format!("line {}: expected number: {}", lineno, val))
}

fn parse_array(val: &str, lineno: usize) -> Result<Vec<String>, String> {
    if !val.starts_with('[') || !val.ends_with(']') {
        return Err(format!("line {}: expected array: {}", lineno, val));
    }
    let inner = val[1..val.len() - 1].trim();
    if inner.is_empty() {
        return Ok(vec![]);
    }

    let mut res = vec![];
    for item in inner.split(',') {
        let item = item.trim();
        if !item.starts_with('"') || !item.ends_with('"') || item.len() < 2 {
            return Err(format!("line {}: bad array element: {}", lineno, item));
        }
        res.push(item[1..item.len() - 1].to_string());
    }
    Ok(res)
}

#[allow(dead_code)]
pub fn list_profiles(dir: &str) -> Vec<String> {
    let entries = match std::fs::read_dir(dir) {
        Ok(e) => e,
        Err(_) => return vec![],
    };

    let mut res = vec![];
    for entry in entries {
        let entry = match entry {
            Ok(e) => e,
            Err(_) => continue,
        };
        let name = entry.file_name();
        let name = name.to_string_lossy();
        if name.ends_with(".toml") {
            res.push(name.trim_end_matches(".toml").to_string());
        }
    }
    res.sort();
    res
}

pub fn find_profile(dir: &str, name: &str) -> Option<GameProfile> {
    let path = format!("{}/{}.toml", dir, name);
    load_profile(&path).ok()
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    const CS2_PROFILE: &str = r#"
[game]
name = "Counter-Strike 2"
steam_appid = 730
process_name = "cs2"
install_path = "steamapps/common/Counter-Strike Global Offensive"

[whitelist]
processes = ["cs2", "steamwebhelper", "steam", "reaper"]
libraries = ["libsteam_api.so", "libSDL2.so"]

[integrity]
watch_dirs = ["game/csgo/bin"]
ignore = ["*.log", "*.txt"]

[detection]
cheat_names = ["deadlocked", "charlatano"]
"#;

    #[test]
    fn parse_valid_profile() {
        let p = parse_profile(CS2_PROFILE).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(p.name, "Counter-Strike 2");
        assert_eq!(p.steam_appid, 730);
        assert_eq!(p.process_name, "cs2");
        assert_eq!(
            p.install_path,
            "steamapps/common/Counter-Strike Global Offensive"
        );
        assert_eq!(
            p.whitelist_processes,
            vec!["cs2", "steamwebhelper", "steam", "reaper"]
        );
        assert_eq!(p.whitelist_libraries, vec!["libsteam_api.so", "libSDL2.so"]);
        assert_eq!(p.watch_dirs, vec!["game/csgo/bin"]);
        assert_eq!(p.ignore_patterns, vec!["*.log", "*.txt"]);
        assert_eq!(p.cheat_names, vec!["deadlocked", "charlatano"]);
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_missing_name() {
        let input = r#"
[game]
steam_appid = 730
process_name = "cs2"
install_path = "steamapps/common/CS"
"#;
        let res = parse_profile(input);
        assert!(res.is_err());
        assert!(res.unwrap_err().contains("name"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_missing_appid() {
        let input = r#"
[game]
name = "Test"
process_name = "test"
install_path = "steamapps/common/Test"
"#;
        let res = parse_profile(input);
        assert!(res.is_err());
        assert!(res.unwrap_err().contains("steam_appid"));
    }

        let input = r#"
[game]
name = "Test"
steam_appid = 100
install_path = "steamapps/common/Test"
"#;
        let res = parse_profile(input);
        assert!(res.is_err());
        assert!(res.unwrap_err().contains("process_name"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn parse_empty_arrays() {
        let input = r#"
[game]
name = "Test"
steam_appid = 100
process_name = "test"
install_path = "test"

[whitelist]
processes = []
libraries = []

[detection]
cheat_names = []
"#;
        let p = parse_profile(input).unwrap();
        assert!(p.whitelist_processes.is_empty());
        assert!(p.whitelist_libraries.is_empty());
        assert!(p.cheat_names.is_empty());
    }

    #[test]

        let input = r#"
# top comment

[game]
# game name
name = "Test"
steam_appid = 100
process_name = "test"

"#;
        let p = parse_profile(input).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(p.name, "Test");
    }

    #[test]

        let input = r#"

name = "Test"
steam_appid = 100
process_name = "test"
install_path = "test"
unknown_key = "whatever"

[unknown_section]
foo = "bar"
"#;
        let p = parse_profile(input).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(p.name, "Test");
    }

    #[test]
    fn list_profiles_from_temp_dir() {
        let dir = std::env::temp_dir().join("vigil_test_profiles");
        let _ = std::fs::create_dir_all(&dir);

        let p1 = dir.join("cs2.toml");
        let p2 = dir.join("deadlock.toml");
        let p3 = dir.join("readme.txt");
        std::fs::write(&p1, "").unwrap();
        std::fs::write(&p2, "").unwrap();
        std::fs::write(&p3, "").unwrap();

        let res = list_profiles(dir.to_str().unwrap());
        assert_eq!(res.len(), 2);
        assert!(res.contains(&"cs2".to_string()));
        assert!(res.contains(&"deadlock".to_string()));

        let _ = std::fs::remove_dir_all(&dir);
    }

    #[test]
    fn list_profiles_nonexistent_dir() {
        let res = list_profiles("/tmp/vigil_nonexistent_dir_12345");
        assert!(res.is_empty());
    }

    #[test]
    fn find_profile_from_temp_dir() {
        let dir = std::env::temp_dir().join("vigil_test_find_profile");
        let _ = std::fs::create_dir_all(&dir);

        let content = r#"[game]
name = "Test Game"
steam_appid = 999
process_name = "testgame"
install_path = "steamapps/common/TestGame"
"#;
        let path = dir.join("testgame.toml");
        std::fs::write(&path, content).unwrap();

        let p = find_profile(dir.to_str().unwrap(), "testgame").unwrap();
        assert_eq!(p.name, "Test Game");
        assert_eq!(p.steam_appid, 999);

        let missing = find_profile(dir.to_str().unwrap(), "nonexistent");
        assert!(missing.is_none());

        let _ = std::fs::remove_dir_all(&dir);
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/report.rs`:

```rs
use crate::crypto::sha256_hex;
use crate::json::{json_arr, json_bool, json_obj, json_str, stringify, JsonValue};
use crate::timestamp::now_rfc3339;

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ScanReport {
    pub player_id: String,
    pub timestamp: String,
    pub hostname: String,
    pub config_hash: String,
    pub ebpf_active: bool,
    pub sandbox_detected: Vec<String>,
    pub suspicious_processes: Vec<SuspiciousProcess>,
    pub cheat_matches: Vec<CheatMatch>,
    pub cross_traces: Vec<CrossTrace>,
    pub network_connections: Vec<NetworkConnection>,
    pub module_changes: Vec<ModuleChange>,
    pub file_integrity: FileIntegrity,
    pub heartbeat_seq: u64,
    pub self_protection: Vec<String>,
    pub clock_drift_ms: Option<i64>,
    pub client_hash: String,
    pub challenge_response: Option<String>,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct SuspiciousProcess {
    pub pid: u64,
    pub name: String,
    pub reason: String,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct CheatMatch {
    pub pid: u64,
    pub name: String,
    pub category: String,
    pub description: String,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct CrossTrace {
    pub tracer_pid: u64,
    pub targets: Vec<u64>,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct NetworkConnection {
    pub pid: u64,
    pub address: String,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ModuleChange {
    pub name: String,
    pub action: String,
}

#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct FileIntegrity {
    pub status: String,
    pub modified: Vec<String>,
    pub added: Vec<String>,
    pub removed: Vec<String>,
}

pub fn get_hostname() -> String {
    std::fs::read_to_string("/etc/hostname")
        .map(|s| s.trim().to_string())
        .unwrap_or_else(|_| "unknown".to_string())
}

pub fn hash_config() -> String {
    match std::fs::read("/etc/vigil/config.toml") {
        Ok(bytes) => sha256_hex(&bytes),
        Err(_) => "no-config".to_string(),
    }
}

#[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]
pub fn build_report(
    player_id: &str,
    ebpf_active: bool,
    sandbox: &[String],
    suspicious: Vec<SuspiciousProcess>,
    cheats: Vec<CheatMatch>,
    traces: Vec<CrossTrace>,
    connections: Vec<NetworkConnection>,
    modules: Vec<ModuleChange>,
    integrity: FileIntegrity,
    heartbeat_seq: u64,
    self_protection: Vec<String>,
    clock_drift_ms: Option<i64>,
    client_hash: &str,
    challenge_response: Option<String>,
) -> ScanReport {
    ScanReport {
        player_id: player_id.to_string(),
        timestamp: now_rfc3339(),
        hostname: get_hostname(),
        config_hash: hash_config(),
        ebpf_active,
        sandbox_detected: sandbox.to_vec(),
        suspicious_processes: suspicious,
        cheat_matches: cheats,
        cross_traces: traces,
        network_connections: connections,
        module_changes: modules,
        file_integrity: integrity,
        heartbeat_seq,
        self_protection,
        clock_drift_ms,
        client_hash: client_hash.to_string(),
        challenge_response,
    }
}

pub fn to_json(report: &ScanReport) -> String {
    let suspicious: Vec<JsonValue> = report
        .suspicious_processes
        .iter()
        .map(|p| {
            json_obj(vec![
                ("pid", JsonValue::Number(p.pid as f64)),
                ("name", json_str(&p.name)),
                ("reason", json_str(&p.reason)),
            ])
        })
        .collect();

    let cheats: Vec<JsonValue> = report
        .cheat_matches
        .iter()
        .map(|c| {
            json_obj(vec![
                ("pid", JsonValue::Number(c.pid as f64)),
                ("name", json_str(&c.name)),
                ("category", json_str(&c.category)),
                ("description", json_str(&c.description)),
            ])
        })
        .collect();

    let traces: Vec<JsonValue> = report
        .cross_traces
        .iter()
        .map(|t| {
            let targets: Vec<JsonValue> = t
                .targets
                .iter()
                .map(|&pid| JsonValue::Number(pid as f64))
                .collect();
            json_obj(vec![
                ("tracer_pid", JsonValue::Number(t.tracer_pid as f64)),
                ("targets", json_arr(targets)),
            ])
        })
        .collect();

    let connections: Vec<JsonValue> = report
        .network_connections
        .iter()
        .map(|c| {
            json_obj(vec![
                ("pid", JsonValue::Number(c.pid as f64)),
                ("address", json_str(&c.address)),
            ])
        })
        .collect();

    let modules: Vec<JsonValue> = report
        .module_changes
        .iter()
        .map(|m| {
            json_obj(vec![
                ("name", json_str(&m.name)),
                ("action", json_str(&m.action)),
            ])
        })
        .collect();

    let sandbox: Vec<JsonValue> = report
        .sandbox_detected
        .iter()
        .map(|s| json_str(s))
        .collect();

    let fi = &report.file_integrity;
    let integrity = json_obj(vec![
        ("status", json_str(&fi.status)),
        (
            "modified",
            json_arr(fi.modified.iter().map(|s| json_str(s)).collect()),
        ),
        (
            "added",
            json_arr(fi.added.iter().map(|s| json_str(s)).collect()),
        ),
        (
            "removed",
            json_arr(fi.removed.iter().map(|s| json_str(s)).collect()),
        ),
    ]);

    let obj = json_obj(vec![
        ("player_id", json_str(&report.player_id)),
        ("timestamp", json_str(&report.timestamp)),
        ("hostname", json_str(&report.hostname)),
        ("config_hash", json_str(&report.config_hash)),
        ("ebpf_active", json_bool(report.ebpf_active)),
        ("sandbox_detected", json_arr(sandbox)),
        ("suspicious_processes", json_arr(suspicious)),
        ("cheat_matches", json_arr(cheats)),
        ("cross_traces", json_arr(traces)),
        ("network_connections", json_arr(connections)),
        ("module_changes", json_arr(modules)),
        ("file_integrity", integrity),
        ("heartbeat_seq", JsonValue::Number(report.heartbeat_seq as f64)),
        (
            "self_protection",
            json_arr(report.self_protection.iter().map(|s| json_str(s)).collect()),
        ),
        (
            "clock_drift_ms",
            match report.clock_drift_ms {
                Some(ms) => JsonValue::Number(ms as f64),
                None => JsonValue::Null,
            },
        ),
        ("client_hash", json_str(&report.client_hash)),
        (
            "challenge_response",
            report.challenge_response.as_deref().map(json_str).unwrap_or(JsonValue::Null),
        ),
    ]);

    stringify(&obj)
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn report_to_json_empty() {
        let report = ScanReport {
            player_id: "test-player".to_string(),

            hostname: "testhost".to_string(),
            config_hash: "abc123".to_string(),
            ebpf_active: false,
            sandbox_detected: vec![],
            suspicious_processes: vec![],
            cheat_matches: vec![],
            cross_traces: vec![],

                status: "ok".to_string(),
                modified: vec![],
                added: vec![],
                removed: vec![],
            },
            heartbeat_seq: 1,
            self_protection: vec![],
            clock_drift_ms: None,
            client_hash: "abc123hash".to_string(),
            challenge_response: None,
        };

        let json = to_json(&report);
        let parsed = parse(&json).unwrap();

        assert_eq!(parsed.get("player_id").unwrap().as_str().unwrap(), "test-player");
        assert_eq!(parsed.get("hostname").unwrap().as_str().unwrap(), "testhost");
        assert_eq!(parsed.get("ebpf_active").unwrap().as_bool().unwrap(), false);
        assert_eq!(parsed.get("suspicious_processes").unwrap().as_array().unwrap().len(), 0);
    }

    #[test]
    fn report_to_json_with_data() {
        let report = ScanReport {
            player_id: "p1".to_string(),
            timestamp: "2026-01-01T00:00:00Z".to_string(),
            hostname: "host".to_string(),
            config_hash: "hash".to_string(),
            ebpf_active: true,
            sandbox_detected: vec!["hypervisor".to_string()],
            suspicious_processes: vec![SuspiciousProcess {
                pid: 123,
                name: "hack".to_string(),
                reason: "cheat name".to_string(),
            }],
            cheat_matches: vec![CheatMatch {
                pid: 456,
                name: "aimbot".to_string(),
                category: "cheat".to_string(),
                description: "aim assist".to_string(),
            }],
            cross_traces: vec![CrossTrace {
                tracer_pid: 789,
                targets: vec![100, 200],
            }],
            network_connections: vec![NetworkConnection {
                pid: 123,
                address: "1.2.3.4:8080".to_string(),
            }],
            module_changes: vec![ModuleChange {
                name: "evil_mod".to_string(),
                action: "loaded".to_string(),
            }],
            file_integrity: FileIntegrity {
                status: "modified".to_string(),
                modified: vec!["game.dll".to_string()],
                added: vec![],
                removed: vec![],
            },
            heartbeat_seq: 42,
            self_protection: vec!["vigil is being traced by pid 999".to_string()],
            clock_drift_ms: Some(750),
            client_hash: "def456hash".to_string(),
            challenge_response: Some("test-response".to_string()),
        };

        let json = to_json(&report);
        let parsed = parse(&json).unwrap();

        assert_eq!(parsed.get("ebpf_active").unwrap().as_bool().unwrap(), true);

        let procs = parsed.get("suspicious_processes").unwrap().as_array().unwrap();
        assert_eq!(procs.len(), 1);
        assert_eq!(procs[0].get("name").unwrap().as_str().unwrap(), "hack");

        let cheats = parsed.get("cheat_matches").unwrap().as_array().unwrap();
        assert_eq!(cheats[0].get("name").unwrap().as_str().unwrap(), "aimbot");

        let traces = parsed.get("cross_traces").unwrap().as_array().unwrap();
        let targets = traces[0].get("targets").unwrap().as_array().unwrap();
        assert_eq!(targets.len(), 2);

        let fi = parsed.get("file_integrity").unwrap();
        assert_eq!(fi.get("status").unwrap().as_str().unwrap(), "modified");
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/report_queue.rs`:

```rs
use std::fs;

const QUEUE_DIR: &str = "/var/lib/vigil/queue";
const QUEUE_DIR_FALLBACK: &str = "/tmp/vigil-queue";
const MAX_QUEUED: usize = 100;

/// Resolve queue dir: prefer /var/lib/vigil/queue, fall back to /tmp/vigil-queue.
fn queue_dir() -> String {
    if fs::create_dir_all(QUEUE_DIR).is_ok() {
        QUEUE_DIR.to_string()
    } else {
        QUEUE_DIR_FALLBACK.to_string()
    }
}

/// Save a report JSON to the queue directory.
/// Filename: <timestamp_secs>_<seq>.json (zero-padded timestamp for sort order)
pub fn enqueue(report_json: &str, seq: u64) -> Result<(), String> {
    let dir = queue_dir();
    fs::create_dir_all(&dir).map_err(|e| format!("queue dir: {}", e))?;

    if count_queued() >= MAX_QUEUED {
        // Drop oldest to make room, then enqueue.
        if let Some(oldest) = list_queued().into_iter().next() {
            let _ = fs::remove_file(&oldest);
        }
    }

    let path = format!("{}/{:010}_{}.json", dir, now_secs(), seq);
    fs::write(&path, report_json).map_err(|e| format!("queue write: {}", e))
}

/// List queued report file paths sorted by name (oldest first).
pub fn list_queued() -> Vec<String> {
    let dir = queue_dir();
    let rd = match fs::read_dir(&dir) {
        Ok(rd) => rd,
        Err(_) => return vec![],
    };

    let mut files: Vec<String> = rd
        .filter_map(|entry| {
            let entry = entry.ok()?;
            let name = entry.file_name();
            let name_str = name.to_string_lossy();
            if name_str.ends_with(".json") {
                Some(entry.path().to_string_lossy().into_owned())
            } else {
                None
            }
        })
        .collect();

    files.sort();
    files
}

/// Try to send all queued reports via HTTP POST.
/// Stops on first failure (server still unreachable).
/// Returns number of reports successfully sent and removed.
pub fn flush(server_url: &str, token: Option<&str>) -> usize {
    let files = list_queued();
    let mut sent = 0;

    for path in files {
        let body = match fs::read_to_string(&path) {
            Ok(b) => b,
            Err(_) => continue,
        };

        let url = format!("{}/api/report", server_url);
        match crate::http_client::post_json(&url, &body, token) {
            Ok(res) if res.status < 400 => {
                let _ = fs::remove_file(&path);
                sent += 1;
            }
            _ => break, // server still down, stop trying
        }
    }

    sent
}

/// Count queued report files.
pub fn count_queued() -> usize {
    list_queued().len()
}

fn now_secs() -> u64 {
    vigil_common::timestamp::now_secs()
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/runtime/executor.rs`:

```rs
// thin wrapper around vigil-common executor + local reactor access for io.rs

use std::cell::RefCell;
use crate::runtime::reactor::Reactor;

thread_local! {
    static LOCAL_REACTOR: RefCell<Option<Reactor>> = const { RefCell::new(None) };
}

pub(crate) fn with_reactor<F, R>(f: F) -> R
where
    F: FnOnce(&mut Reactor) -> R,
{
    LOCAL_REACTOR.with(|r| {
        let mut borrow = r.borrow_mut();
        let reactor = borrow.as_mut().expect("no reactor active");
        f(reactor)
    })
}

/// Adapter: wraps our local reactor so common's executor can poll it
struct ReactorAdapter;

impl vigil_common::runtime::executor::Reactor for ReactorAdapter {
    fn poll(&mut self, timeout_ms: i32) -> usize {
        LOCAL_REACTOR.with(|r| {
            let mut borrow = r.borrow_mut();
            if let Some(reactor) = borrow.as_mut() {
                reactor.poll(timeout_ms)
            } else {
                0
            }
        })
    }
}

pub fn block_on<F>(main: F)
where
    F: std::future::Future<Output = ()>,
{
    let reactor = Reactor::new().expect("failed to create epoll reactor");
    LOCAL_REACTOR.with(|r| { *r.borrow_mut() = Some(reactor); });
    vigil_common::runtime::executor::block_on_with_reactor(main, ReactorAdapter);
    LOCAL_REACTOR.with(|r| { *r.borrow_mut() = None; });
}

```

`crates/vigil/src/runtime/io.rs`:

```rs
use std::future::Future;
use std::os::fd::RawFd;
use std::pin::Pin;
use std::task::{Context, Poll};

use crate::runtime::executor::with_reactor;

struct Readable {
    fd: RawFd,
    registered: bool,
}

impl Future for Readable {
    type Output = std::io::Result<()>;

    fn poll(mut self: Pin<&mut Self>, cx: &mut Context<'_>) -> Poll<Self::Output> {
        if self.registered {
            with_reactor(|r| r.deregister(self.fd));
            Poll::Ready(Ok(()))
        } else {
            self.registered = true;
            with_reactor(|r| r.register(self.fd, cx.waker().clone()));
            Poll::Pending
        }
    }
}

impl Drop for Readable {
    fn drop(&mut self) {
        if self.registered {
            with_reactor(|r| r.deregister(self.fd));
        }
    }
}

// wait until fd has data to read
pub fn readable(fd: RawFd) -> impl Future<Output = std::io::Result<()>> {
    Readable {
        fd,
        registered: false,
    }
}

```

`crates/vigil/src/runtime/reactor.rs`:

```rs
use std::collections::HashMap;
use std::os::fd::RawFd;
use std::task::Waker;

use crate::sys::{self, EpollEvent, EPOLLIN, EPOLL_CTL_ADD, EPOLL_CTL_DEL};

pub struct Reactor {
    epoll_fd: RawFd,
    interests: HashMap<RawFd, Waker>,
}

impl Reactor {
    pub fn new() -> std::io::Result<Self> {
        let epoll_fd = sys::sys_epoll_create()?;
        Ok(Reactor {
            epoll_fd,
            interests: HashMap::new(),
        })
    }

    // register interest in a fd becoming readable
    pub fn register(&mut self, fd: RawFd, waker: Waker) {
        if !self.interests.contains_key(&fd) {
            let _ = sys::sys_epoll_ctl(self.epoll_fd, EPOLL_CTL_ADD, fd, EPOLLIN);
        }
        self.interests.insert(fd, waker);
    }

    // remove interest in a fd
    pub fn deregister(&mut self, fd: RawFd) {
        if self.interests.remove(&fd).is_some() {
            let _ = sys::sys_epoll_ctl(self.epoll_fd, EPOLL_CTL_DEL, fd, 0);
        }
    }

    // poll for ready fds, wake corresponding tasks
    // returns number of events processed
    pub fn poll(&mut self, timeout_ms: i32) -> usize {
        let mut events = [EpollEvent { events: 0, data: 0 }; 32];
        let n = match sys::sys_epoll_wait(self.epoll_fd, &mut events, timeout_ms) {
            Ok(n) => n,
            Err(_) => return 0,
        };

        for event in &events[..n] {
            let fd = event.data as RawFd;
            if let Some(waker) = self.interests.get(&fd) {
                waker.wake_by_ref();
            }
        }

        n
    }
}

impl Drop for Reactor {
    fn drop(&mut self) {
        sys::sys_close(self.epoll_fd);
    }
}

```

`crates/vigil/src/runtime/time.rs`:

```rs
use std::time::Duration;

use crate::runtime::io::readable;
use crate::sys;

pub async fn sleep(duration: Duration) {
    let fd = match sys::sys_timerfd_create() {
        Ok(fd) => fd,
        Err(_) => {
            // fallback: blocking sleep if timerfd fails
            std::thread::sleep(duration);
            return;
        }
    };

    let secs = duration.as_secs();
    let nanos = duration.subsec_nanos() as u64;

    if sys::sys_timerfd_settime(fd, secs, nanos).is_err() {
        sys::sys_close(fd);
        std::thread::sleep(duration);
        return;
    }

    let _ = readable(fd).await;

    // drain the timerfd
    let mut buf = [0u8; 8];
    let _ = sys::sys_read(fd, &mut buf);

    sys::sys_close(fd);
}

```

`crates/vigil/src/scanner.rs`:

```rs
use crate::crypto::sha256_hex;
use crate::process::{Proc, ProcessStatus};
use std::collections::{HashMap, HashSet};

pub fn scan_processes() -> std::io::Result<Vec<u64>> {
    let mut res = vec![];
    for entry in std::fs::read_dir("/proc/")? {
        let entry = entry?;
        let os_name = entry.file_name();
        let name = os_name.to_str();

        if let Some(val) = name
            && let Ok(pid) = val.parse::<u64>()
        {
            res.push(pid);
        }
    }

    Ok(res)
}

pub fn get_process(pid: u64, whitelist: &[String]) -> std::io::Result<Proc> {
    let mut name = String::new();
    let mut tracer_pid: u64 = 0;
    let mut ppid: u64 = 0;
    let mut status = ProcessStatus::Suspicious(String::from("Status not found"));

    let path = format!("/proc/{}/status", pid);
    let content = std::fs::read_to_string(path)?;

    for line in content.lines() {
        if let Some((key, value)) = line.split_once(':') {
            let value = value.trim();

            match key {
                "Name" => name = value.to_string(),
                "State" => {
                    status = match value.chars().next() {
                        Some('R') => ProcessStatus::Running,
                        Some('S') | Some('D') | Some('I') => ProcessStatus::Sleeping,
                        Some('T') | Some('t') => ProcessStatus::Stopped,
                        Some('Z') => ProcessStatus::Zombie,
                        _ => ProcessStatus::Suspicious(value.to_string()),
                    }
                }
                "TracerPid" => {
                    if let Ok(num) = value.parse::<u64>() {
                        tracer_pid = num;
                    }
                }
                "PPid" => {
                    if let Ok(num) = value.parse::<u64>() {
                        ppid = num;
                    }
                }
                _ => {}
            }
        }
    }

    let preload_path = check_preload(pid, whitelist)?;
    let cmdline = get_cmdline(pid)?;
    let exe_path = get_exe(pid, whitelist)?;

    Ok(Proc::new(
        name,
        pid,
        status,
        tracer_pid,
        preload_path,
        cmdline,
        exe_path,
        ppid,
    ))
}

pub fn get_map(
    pid: u64,
    found_maps: &mut HashSet<String>,
    whitelist: &[String],
) -> std::io::Result<Vec<(String, String)>> {
    let mut res = vec![];
    let path = format!("/proc/{}/maps", pid);
    let content = std::fs::read_to_string(path)?;
    for line in content.lines() {
        if !line.contains(".so") {
            continue;
        }
        let parts: Vec<&str> = line.split_whitespace().collect();
        if let Some(path) = parts.last()
            && !found_maps.contains(*path)
        {
            if whitelist
                .iter()
                .any(|whitelist_item| path.contains(whitelist_item))
            {
                found_maps.insert(path.to_string());
                continue;
            }
            if parts[1].contains("w") && parts[1].contains("x") {
                res.push((
                    path.to_string(),
                    String::from("Process has w and x rights at the same time"),
                ));
            }
            if path.contains("/tmp/") || path.contains("/dev/shm/") {
                res.push((
                    path.to_string(),
                    String::from("library loaded from suspicious dir"),
                ));
            } else if path.contains("/home/") {
                // skip known safe paths inside /home/
                let safe_home_paths = [
                    "/.rustup/", "/.cargo/", "/.local/share/", "/.local/lib/",
                    "/node_modules/", "/.nvm/", "/.pyenv/", "/.config/",
                    "/target/debug/deps/", "/target/release/deps/",
                ];
                if !safe_home_paths.iter().any(|p| path.contains(p)) {
                    res.push((
                        path.to_string(),
                        String::from("library loaded from home dir"),
                    ));
                }
            }
            found_maps.insert(path.to_string());
        }
    }

    Ok(res)
}

pub fn check_preload(pid: u64, whitelist: &[String]) -> std::io::Result<Option<String>> {
    let suspicious_vars = ["LD_PRELOAD", "LD_AUDIT", "LD_LIBRARY_PATH"];
    let path = format!("/proc/{}/environ", pid);
    let content = std::fs::read_to_string(path)?;
    for part in content.split('\0') {
        if let Some((key, value)) = part.split_once("=")
            && suspicious_vars.contains(&key)
        {
            let is_whitelisted = whitelist
                .iter()
                .any(|whitelist_item| value.contains(whitelist_item));

            if !is_whitelisted {
                return Ok(Some(format!("{}={}", key, value)));
            }
        }
    }

    Ok(None)
}

pub fn get_cmdline(pid: u64) -> std::io::Result<String> {
    let path = format!("/proc/{}/cmdline", pid);
    let content = std::fs::read_to_string(path)?;
    Ok(content.replace('\0', " "))
}

pub fn get_exe(pid: u64, whitelist: &[String]) -> std::io::Result<Option<String>> {
    let path = format!("/proc/{}/exe", pid);
    let content = std::fs::read_link(path)?;
    let res = content.to_string_lossy().to_string();

    // always whitelist vigil itself
    if res.contains("/vigil") && (res.contains("/target/") || res.contains("/etc/vigil")) {
        return Ok(None);
    }

    let is_whitelisted = whitelist
        .iter()
        .any(|whitelist_item| res.contains(whitelist_item));

    if !is_whitelisted
        && (res.contains("/tmp/") || res.contains("/dev/shm/"))
    {
        return Ok(Some(res));
    }

    // /home/ is only suspicious for unknown binaries not in common tool paths
    if !is_whitelisted && res.contains("/home/") {
        // skip known dev tools and standard locations
        let safe_home_paths = [
            "/.rustup/", "/.cargo/", "/.local/share/", "/.local/bin/",
            "/node_modules/", "/.nvm/", "/.pyenv/", "/.config/",
        ];
        if !safe_home_paths.iter().any(|p| res.contains(p)) {
            return Ok(Some(res));
        }
    }

    Ok(None)
}

pub fn get_fd(pid: u64) -> std::io::Result<Vec<u64>> {
    let path = format!("/proc/{}/fd", pid);
    let dir = std::fs::read_dir(path)?;
    let mut res = vec![];
    for entry in dir {
        let entry = entry?;
        let content = std::fs::read_link(entry.path())?;
        let symlink = content.to_string_lossy();

        if symlink.starts_with("/proc/") && symlink.ends_with("/mem") {
            for item in symlink.split('/') {
                if item.is_empty() {
                    continue;
                }

                if let Ok(num) = item.parse::<u64>()
                    && num != pid
                {
                    res.push(num);
                }
            }
        }
    }
    Ok(res)
}

pub fn get_modules() -> std::io::Result<Vec<String>> {
    let content = std::fs::read_to_string("/proc/modules")?;
    let mut res = vec![];

    for line in content.lines() {
        let parts: Vec<&str> = line.split_whitespace().collect();

        res.push(parts[0].to_string());
    }

    Ok(res)
}

pub fn get_cross_traces(procs: &[Proc]) -> HashMap<u64, Vec<u64>> {
    let mut res: HashMap<u64, Vec<u64>> = HashMap::new();

    for p in procs {
        let tracer_pid: u64 = *p.get_tracer_pid();
        let pid: u64 = *p.get_pid();

        if tracer_pid != 0 {
            res.entry(tracer_pid).or_default().push(pid);
        }
    }

    res
}

pub fn get_process_tree(pid: u64) -> Vec<(u64, String)> {
    let mut chain = vec![];
    let mut current = pid;

    for _ in 0..64 {
        let path = format!("/proc/{}/status", current);
        let content = match std::fs::read_to_string(&path) {
            Ok(c) => c,
            Err(_) => break,
        };

        let mut name = String::new();
        let mut ppid: u64 = 0;

        for line in content.lines() {
            if let Some((key, value)) = line.split_once(':') {
                let value = value.trim();
                match key {
                    "Name" => name = value.to_string(),
                    "PPid" => {
                        if let Ok(num) = value.parse::<u64>() {
                            ppid = num;
                        }
                    }
                    _ => {}
                }
            }
        }

        chain.push((current, name));

        if current <= 1 {
            break;
        }
        current = ppid;
    }

    chain
}

// known launchers: steam, reaper, lutris, wine, bash, zsh, systemd
pub fn validate_launch_chain(tree: &[(u64, String)]) -> (bool, String) {
    let known = [
        "steam", "reaper", "lutris", "wine", "wine64", "wineserver",
        "bash", "zsh", "sh", "fish", "systemd", "init", "gameoverlayui",
        "pressure-vessel", "proton", "python", "python3",
    ];

    let chain_desc: String = tree
        .iter()
        .map(|(pid, name)| format!("{}({})", name, pid))
        .collect::<Vec<_>>()
        .join(" -> ");

    let valid = tree.iter().all(|(_, name)| {
        let lower = name.to_lowercase();
        known.iter().any(|k| lower.contains(k))
    });

    (valid, chain_desc)
}

pub fn track_maps_changes(
    pid: u64,
    baseline: &mut HashMap<u64, HashSet<String>>,
    whitelist: &[String],
) -> Vec<String> {
    let path = format!("/proc/{}/maps", pid);
    let content = match std::fs::read_to_string(&path) {
        Ok(c) => c,
        Err(_) => return vec![],
    };

    let mut current_libs: HashSet<String> = HashSet::new();
    for line in content.lines() {
        if !line.contains(".so") {
            continue;
        }
        let parts: Vec<&str> = line.split_whitespace().collect();
        if let Some(lib_path) = parts.last()
            && lib_path.contains('/') {
                current_libs.insert(lib_path.to_string());
            }
    }

    let entry = baseline.entry(pid);
    match entry {
        std::collections::hash_map::Entry::Vacant(e) => {
            e.insert(current_libs);
            vec![]
        }
        std::collections::hash_map::Entry::Occupied(mut e) => {
            let known = e.get();
            let mut new_libs = vec![];
            for lib in &current_libs {
                if !known.contains(lib) {
                    let is_whitelisted = whitelist
                        .iter()
                        .any(|w| lib.contains(w));
                    if !is_whitelisted {
                        new_libs.push(lib.clone());
                    }
                }
            }
            e.get_mut().extend(current_libs);
            new_libs
        }
    }
}

pub fn check_capabilities(pid: u64) -> Option<String> {
    let path = format!("/proc/{}/status", pid);
    let content = std::fs::read_to_string(path).ok()?;

    for line in content.lines() {
        if let Some((key, value)) = line.split_once(':')
            && key.trim() == "CapEff"
        {
            let hex = value.trim().trim_start_matches("0x");
            if let Ok(caps) = u64::from_str_radix(hex, 16) {
                // CAP_SYS_PTRACE = bit 19
                if caps & (1 << 19) != 0 {
                    return Some("CAP_SYS_PTRACE".to_string());
                }
            }
        }
    }

    None
}

pub fn check_overlay_processes() -> Vec<(u64, String)> {
    let mut res = vec![];
    let overlay_names = ["overlay", "esp", "crosshair"];

    let pids = match scan_processes() {
        Ok(p) => p,
        Err(_) => return res,
    };

    for pid in pids {
        let fd_path = format!("/proc/{}/fd", pid);
        let has_dri = match std::fs::read_dir(&fd_path) {
            Ok(dir) => dir.filter_map(|e| e.ok()).any(|entry| {
                std::fs::read_link(entry.path())
                    .map(|target| target.to_string_lossy().contains("/dev/dri/"))
                    .unwrap_or(false)
            }),
            Err(_) => false,
        };

        if !has_dri {
            continue;
        }

        let comm_path = format!("/proc/{}/comm", pid);
        let name = std::fs::read_to_string(comm_path)
            .unwrap_or_default()
            .trim()
            .to_lowercase();

        if overlay_names.iter().any(|n| name.contains(n)) {
            res.push((pid, format!("overlay process: {}", name)));
        }
    }

    res
}

pub fn check_namespaces(pid: u64) -> Option<String> {
    let self_ns = std::fs::read_link("/proc/self/ns/pid").ok()?;
    let target_ns = std::fs::read_link(format!("/proc/{}/ns/pid", pid)).ok()?;

    if self_ns != target_ns {
        return Some("different pid namespace".to_string());
    }

    None
}

pub fn check_rwx_maps(pid: u64) -> Vec<String> {
    let path = format!("/proc/{}/maps", pid);
    let content = match std::fs::read_to_string(&path) {
        Ok(c) => c,
        Err(_) => return vec![],
    };

    let mut res = vec![];
    for line in content.lines() {
        let parts: Vec<&str> = line.split_whitespace().collect();
        if parts.len() < 2 {
            continue;
        }
        let perms = parts[1];
        // look for rwxp on anonymous mappings (no path or [heap]/[stack])
        if perms.contains('r') && perms.contains('w') && perms.contains('x') {
            let mapping = parts.last().unwrap_or(&"");
            // skip known safe .so mappings - those are caught by get_map
            if !mapping.contains(".so") {
                res.push(format!("{} {}", parts[0], perms));
            }
        }
    }

    res
}

pub fn check_sandbox() -> std::io::Result<Vec<String>> {
    let mut res = vec![];
    let vm_modules = ["vboxguest", "vmw_balloon", "virtio", "hyperv"];
    let vm_names = [
        "VirtualBox",
        "VMware",
        "QEMU",
        "KVM",
        "Bochs",
        "Hyper-V",
        "Parallels",
        "Xen",
        "BHYVE",
        "innotek",
    ];

    let product_name = std::fs::read_to_string("/sys/class/dmi/id/product_name")?
        .trim()
        .to_lowercase();
    let cpuifo = std::fs::read_to_string("/proc/cpuinfo")?;

    for line in cpuifo.lines() {
        if let Some((key, value)) = line.split_once(":")
            && (key.trim().starts_with("flags") && value.contains("hypervisor"))
        {
            res.push(String::from("hypervisor"));
        }
    }

    for &name in &vm_names {
        if product_name.contains(&name.to_lowercase()) {
            res.push(name.to_string());
        }
    }
    if let Ok(modules) = get_modules() {
        for m in &modules {
            if vm_modules.iter().any(|vm| m.contains(vm)) {
                res.push(m.to_string());
            }
        }
    }

    if std::fs::read_to_string("/.dockerenv").is_ok() {
        res.push(String::from("/.dockerenv"));
    }

    if let Ok(cgroup) = std::fs::read_to_string("/proc/1/cgroup") {
        for line in cgroup.lines() {
            if line.starts_with("docker") || line.starts_with("lxc") {
                res.push(line.to_string());
            }
        }
    }

    Ok(res)
}

// checks if the executable .text section in memory matches the binary on disk.
// if a cheat has patched code in memory (e.g. NOP-ing out anti-cheat calls),
// the hashes will differ. returns Some(reason) if tampered, None if clean or unreadable.
pub fn check_text_integrity(pid: u64) -> Option<String> {
    // get the exe path from /proc/PID/exe
    let exe_link = format!("/proc/{}/exe", pid);
    let exe_path = std::fs::read_link(&exe_link).ok()?;
    let exe_str = exe_path.to_string_lossy();

    // skip deleted or special entries
    if exe_str.contains("(deleted)") || exe_str.starts_with('[') {
        return None;
    }

    // read /proc/PID/maps and find the first r-xp mapping that points to the exe (not a .so)
    let maps_path = format!("/proc/{}/maps", pid);
    let maps_content = std::fs::read_to_string(&maps_path).ok()?;

    let mut text_start: u64 = 0;
    let mut text_end: u64 = 0;
    let mut file_offset: u64 = 0;
    let mut found = false;

    for line in maps_content.lines() {
        let parts: Vec<&str> = line.split_whitespace().collect();
        if parts.len() < 6 {
            continue;
        }

        let perms = parts[1];
        let mapped_path = parts[5];

        // look for r-xp (read+execute, private) mapping of the exe itself
        if perms != "r-xp" {
            continue;
        }

        // the mapped path must match the exe — skip .so files and anonymous mappings
        if !mapped_path.contains('/') || mapped_path.contains(".so") {
            continue;
        }

        // canonicalize both paths for comparison
        let mapped_canonical = std::fs::canonicalize(mapped_path).ok();
        let exe_canonical = std::fs::canonicalize(&exe_path).ok();

        if mapped_canonical != exe_canonical {
            continue;
        }

        // parse address range: "start-end"
        if let Some((start_hex, end_hex)) = parts[0].split_once('-') {
            text_start = u64::from_str_radix(start_hex, 16).ok()?;
            text_end = u64::from_str_radix(end_hex, 16).ok()?;
        }

        // parse file offset (third field in maps)
        file_offset = u64::from_str_radix(parts[2], 16).ok()?;
        found = true;
        break;
    }

    if !found || text_end <= text_start {
        return None;
    }

    let region_size = (text_end - text_start) as usize;

    // cap at 4MB to avoid blowing up on huge mappings
    if region_size > 4 * 1024 * 1024 {
        return None;
    }

    // read the mapped region from /proc/PID/mem
    let mem_path = format!("/proc/{}/mem", pid);
    let mem_data = read_proc_mem(&mem_path, text_start, region_size)?;

    // read the same offset from the binary on disk
    let disk_data = read_file_region(&exe_str, file_offset, region_size)?;

    let mem_hash = sha256_hex(&mem_data);
    let disk_hash = sha256_hex(&disk_data);

    if mem_hash != disk_hash {
        Some("code section modified in memory".to_string())
    } else {
        None
    }
}

// reads `size` bytes from a file at `offset` using seek
fn read_proc_mem(path: &str, offset: u64, size: usize) -> Option<Vec<u8>> {
    use std::io::{Read, Seek, SeekFrom};
    let mut f = std::fs::File::open(path).ok()?;
    f.seek(SeekFrom::Start(offset)).ok()?;
    let mut buf = vec![0u8; size];
    f.read_exact(&mut buf).ok()?;
    Some(buf)
}

fn read_file_region(path: &str, offset: u64, size: usize) -> Option<Vec<u8>> {
    use std::io::{Read, Seek, SeekFrom};
    let mut f = std::fs::File::open(path).ok()?;
    f.seek(SeekFrom::Start(offset)).ok()?;
    let mut buf = vec![0u8; size];
    f.read_exact(&mut buf).ok()?;
    Some(buf)
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn cross_traces_empty() {
        let procs: Vec<Proc> = vec![];
        let result = get_cross_traces(&procs);
        assert!(result.is_empty());
    }

    #[test]
    fn cross_traces_no_tracers() {
        let procs = vec![
            Proc::new("bash".into(), 1, ProcessStatus::Running, 0, None, "bash".into(), None, 0),
            Proc::new("vim".into(), 2, ProcessStatus::Running, 0, None, "vim".into(), None, 1),
        ];
        let result = get_cross_traces(&procs);
        assert!(result.is_empty());
    }

    #[test]
    fn cross_traces_single_tracer_multiple_targets() {
        let procs = vec![
            Proc::new("game".into(), 100, ProcessStatus::Running, 999, None, "game".into(), None, 1),
            Proc::new("game2".into(), 200, ProcessStatus::Running, 999, None, "game2".into(), None, 1),
        ];
        let result = get_cross_traces(&procs);
        assert_eq!(result.len(), 1);
        let targets = result.get(&999).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(targets.len(), 2);
        assert!(targets.contains(&100));
        assert!(targets.contains(&200));
    }

    #[test]
    fn cross_traces_multiple_tracers() {
        let procs = vec![
            Proc::new("a".into(), 10, ProcessStatus::Running, 1, None, "a".into(), None, 0),
            Proc::new("b".into(), 20, ProcessStatus::Running, 2, None, "b".into(), None, 0),
            Proc::new("c".into(), 30, ProcessStatus::Running, 1, None, "c".into(), None, 0),
        ];
        let result = get_cross_traces(&procs);
        assert_eq!(result.len(), 2);
        assert_eq!(result.get(&1).unwrap().len(), 2);
        assert_eq!(result.get(&2).unwrap().len(), 1);
    }

    #[test]
    fn get_process_tree_returns_self() {
        let tree = get_process_tree(1);
        assert!(!tree.is_empty());
        assert_eq!(tree[0].0, 1);
    }

    #[test]
    fn get_process_tree_handles_nonexistent_pid() {
        let tree = get_process_tree(999999999);
        assert!(tree.is_empty());
    }

    #[test]
    fn get_process_tree_current_process() {
        let pid = std::process::id() as u64;
        let tree = get_process_tree(pid);
        assert!(!tree.is_empty());
        assert_eq!(tree[0].0, pid);
        let last = tree.last().unwrap();
        assert!(last.0 <= 1 || tree.len() >= 2);
    }

    #[test]
    fn validate_launch_chain_known_chain() {
        let chain = vec![
            (1000, "cs2".to_string()),
            (999, "reaper".to_string()),
            (500, "steam".to_string()),
            (1, "systemd".to_string()),
        ];
        let (valid, desc) = validate_launch_chain(&chain);
        assert!(!valid);
        assert!(desc.contains("cs2"));
        assert!(desc.contains("steam"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn validate_launch_chain_all_known() {
        let chain = vec![
            (100, "bash".to_string()),
            (1, "systemd".to_string()),
        ];
        let (valid, desc) = validate_launch_chain(&chain);
        assert!(valid);
        assert!(desc.contains("bash"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn validate_launch_chain_empty() {
        let (valid, desc) = validate_launch_chain(&[]);
        assert!(valid);
        assert!(desc.is_empty());
    }

    #[test]
    fn validate_launch_chain_unknown_process() {
        let chain = vec![
            (100, "suspicious_loader".to_string()),
            (50, "bash".to_string()),
            (1, "systemd".to_string()),
        ];
        let (valid, _desc) = validate_launch_chain(&chain);
        assert!(!valid);
    }

    #[test]
    fn track_maps_changes_first_call_returns_empty() {
        let mut baseline: HashMap<u64, HashSet<String>> = HashMap::new();
        let pid = std::process::id() as u64;
        let result = track_maps_changes(pid, &mut baseline, &[]);
        assert!(result.is_empty());
        assert!(baseline.contains_key(&pid));
    }

    #[test]
    fn track_maps_changes_no_change_returns_empty() {
        let mut baseline: HashMap<u64, HashSet<String>> = HashMap::new();
        let pid = std::process::id() as u64;
        track_maps_changes(pid, &mut baseline, &[]);
        let result = track_maps_changes(pid, &mut baseline, &[]);
        assert!(result.is_empty());
    }

    #[test]
    fn track_maps_changes_nonexistent_pid() {
        let mut baseline: HashMap<u64, HashSet<String>> = HashMap::new();
        let result = track_maps_changes(999999999, &mut baseline, &[]);
        assert!(result.is_empty());
        assert!(!baseline.contains_key(&999999999));
    }

    #[test]
    fn check_capabilities_current_process() {
        // just verify it doesn't panic - result depends on caps
        let pid = std::process::id() as u64;
        let _ = check_capabilities(pid);
    }

    #[test]
    fn check_capabilities_nonexistent_pid() {
        assert!(check_capabilities(999999999).is_none());
    }

    #[test]
    fn check_overlay_processes_runs() {
        // shouldn't panic, may or may not find anything
        let _ = check_overlay_processes();
    }

    #[test]
    fn check_namespaces_self() {
        let pid = std::process::id() as u64;
        // same process = same namespace
        assert!(check_namespaces(pid).is_none());
    }

    #[test]
    fn check_namespaces_nonexistent_pid() {
        assert!(check_namespaces(999999999).is_none());
    }

    #[test]
    fn check_rwx_maps_current_process() {
        let pid = std::process::id() as u64;
        // just verify it runs without panic
        let _ = check_rwx_maps(pid);
    }

    #[test]
    fn check_rwx_maps_nonexistent_pid() {
        let res = check_rwx_maps(999999999);
        assert!(res.is_empty());
    }

    #[test]
    fn track_maps_changes_detects_injection() {
        let mut baseline: HashMap<u64, HashSet<String>> = HashMap::new();
        let mut known = HashSet::new();
        known.insert("/usr/lib/libc.so.6".to_string());
        baseline.insert(42, known);

        let result = track_maps_changes(42, &mut baseline, &[]);
        assert!(result.is_empty());
    }

    #[test]
    fn check_text_integrity_current_process() {
        // run on ourselves — our .text should match disk (no one is patching us)
        let pid = std::process::id() as u64;
        let result = check_text_integrity(pid);
        // should be None (clean) or None (couldn't read — either is fine, no panic)
        assert!(result.is_none(), "vigil's own .text should match disk, got: {:?}", result);
    }

    #[test]
    fn check_text_integrity_nonexistent_pid() {
        let result = check_text_integrity(999999999);
        assert!(result.is_none());
    }

    #[test]
    fn read_proc_mem_self() {
        // verify we can read our own memory without crashing
        let pid = std::process::id() as u64;
        let maps = std::fs::read_to_string(format!("/proc/{}/maps", pid));
        assert!(maps.is_ok());
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/self_protect.rs`:

```rs
use crate::crypto::sha256_hex;
use std::os::unix::fs::MetadataExt;

const PR_SET_DUMPABLE: i32 = 4;
const PR_SET_NO_NEW_PRIVS: i32 = 38;

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn prctl(option: i32, ...) -> i32;
}

pub fn harden() {
    unsafe {
        prctl(PR_SET_DUMPABLE, 0i64);
        prctl(PR_SET_NO_NEW_PRIVS, 1i64, 0i64, 0i64, 0i64);
    }
}

pub fn check() -> Vec<String> {
    let mut issues = Vec::new();

    if let Some(tracer) = check_tracer() {
        issues.push(format!("vigil is being traced by pid {}", tracer));
    }

    if !is_running_as_root() {
        issues.push("vigil is not running as root".to_string());
    }

    check_permissions(&mut issues);

    issues
}

pub fn binary_hash() -> Option<String> {
    let exe = std::fs::read_link("/proc/self/exe").ok()?;
    let data = std::fs::read(exe).ok()?;
    Some(sha256_hex(&data))
}

pub fn check_binary_integrity(startup_hash: &str) -> bool {
    match binary_hash() {
        Some(current) => current == startup_hash,
        None => false,
    }
}

fn check_tracer() -> Option<u64> {
    let status = std::fs::read_to_string("/proc/self/status").ok()?;
    for line in status.lines() {
        if let Some((key, value)) = line.split_once(':')
            && key == "TracerPid" {
                let pid = value.trim().parse::<u64>().ok()?;
                if pid != 0 {
                    return Some(pid);
                }
            }
    }
    None
}

fn is_running_as_root() -> bool {
    let status = match std::fs::read_to_string("/proc/self/status") {
        Ok(s) => s,
        Err(_) => return false,
    };
    for line in status.lines() {
        if let Some((key, value)) = line.split_once(':')
            && key == "Uid" {
                let uid = value.split_whitespace().next().unwrap_or("65534");
                return uid == "0";
            }
    }
    false
}

fn check_permissions(issues: &mut Vec<String>) {
    let paths = [
        "/etc/vigil",
        "/etc/vigil/config.toml",
        "/etc/vigil/whitelist.txt",
        "/etc/vigil/cheat_hashes.txt",
    ];

    for path in &paths {
        if let Ok(meta) = std::fs::metadata(path) {
            let uid = meta.uid();
            if uid != 0 {
                issues.push(format!("{} not owned by root (uid={})", path, uid));
            }
            let mode = meta.mode();
            if mode & 0o002 != 0 {
                issues.push(format!("{} is world-writable (mode={:o})", path, mode));
            }
        }
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/speedhack.rs`:

```rs
const CLOCK_REALTIME: i32 = 0;
const CLOCK_MONOTONIC: i32 = 1;

#[repr(C)]
struct Timespec {
    tv_sec: i64,
    tv_nsec: i64,
}

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn clock_gettime(clk_id: i32, tp: *mut Timespec) -> i32;
}

fn get_time(clock: i32) -> i64 {
    let mut ts = Timespec {
        tv_sec: 0,
        tv_nsec: 0,
    };
    unsafe { clock_gettime(clock, &mut ts) };
    ts.tv_sec * 1000 + ts.tv_nsec / 1_000_000
}

pub struct ClockWatcher {
    initial_delta_ms: i64,
    last_monotonic_ms: i64,
}

impl ClockWatcher {
    pub fn new() -> Self {
        let mono = get_time(CLOCK_MONOTONIC);
        let real = get_time(CLOCK_REALTIME);
        ClockWatcher {
            initial_delta_ms: real - mono,
            last_monotonic_ms: mono,
        }
    }

    // returns drift in ms if clock drift >500ms or scan cycle timing is way off
    pub fn check(&mut self, expected_interval_ms: i64) -> Option<ClockAnomaly> {
        let mono = get_time(CLOCK_MONOTONIC);
        let real = get_time(CLOCK_REALTIME);

        let current_delta = real - mono;
        let drift_ms = (current_delta - self.initial_delta_ms).abs();

        let elapsed = mono - self.last_monotonic_ms;
        self.last_monotonic_ms = mono;

        let timing_off = (elapsed - expected_interval_ms).abs();

        if drift_ms > 500 {
            return Some(ClockAnomaly {
                drift_ms,
                kind: "clock drift between MONOTONIC and REALTIME".to_string(),
            });
        }

        // 2s tolerance, first check will be off
        if timing_off > 2000 && elapsed > 0 {
            return Some(ClockAnomaly {
                drift_ms: timing_off,
                kind: format!(
                    "scan cycle took {}ms (expected ~{}ms)",
                    elapsed, expected_interval_ms
                ),
            });
        }

        None
    }
}

pub struct ClockAnomaly {
    pub drift_ms: i64,
    pub kind: String,
}

```

`crates/vigil/src/sys.rs`:

```rs
use std::io;
use std::os::fd::RawFd;

pub const EPOLLIN: u32 = 0x001;
pub const EPOLL_CTL_ADD: i32 = 1;
pub const EPOLL_CTL_DEL: i32 = 2;

#[repr(C, packed)]
#[derive(Copy, Clone)]
pub struct EpollEvent {
    pub events: u32,
    pub data: u64,
}

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn epoll_create1(flags: i32) -> i32;
    fn epoll_ctl(epfd: i32, op: i32, fd: i32, event: *mut EpollEvent) -> i32;
    fn epoll_wait(epfd: i32, events: *mut EpollEvent, maxevents: i32, timeout: i32) -> i32;
}

pub fn sys_epoll_create() -> io::Result<RawFd> {
    let fd = unsafe { epoll_create1(0) };
    if fd < 0 {
        Err(io::Error::last_os_error())
    } else {
        Ok(fd)
    }
}

pub fn sys_epoll_ctl(epfd: RawFd, op: i32, fd: RawFd, events: u32) -> io::Result<()> {
    let mut ev = EpollEvent {
        events,
        data: fd as u64,
    };
    let ret = unsafe { epoll_ctl(epfd, op, fd, &mut ev) };
    if ret < 0 {
        Err(io::Error::last_os_error())
    } else {
        Ok(())
    }
}

pub fn sys_epoll_wait(epfd: RawFd, buf: &mut [EpollEvent], timeout_ms: i32) -> io::Result<usize> {
    let ret = unsafe { epoll_wait(epfd, buf.as_mut_ptr(), buf.len() as i32, timeout_ms) };
    if ret < 0 {
        Err(io::Error::last_os_error())
    } else {
        Ok(ret as usize)
    }
}

pub const CLOCK_MONOTONIC: i32 = 1;
pub const TFD_NONBLOCK: i32 = 0o4000;
pub const TFD_CLOEXEC: i32 = 0o2000000;

#[repr(C)]
pub struct Timespec {
    pub tv_sec: i64,
    pub tv_nsec: i64,
}

#[repr(C)]
pub struct ItimerSpec {
    pub it_interval: Timespec,
    pub it_value: Timespec,
}

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn timerfd_create(clockid: i32, flags: i32) -> i32;
    fn timerfd_settime(fd: i32, flags: i32, new: *const ItimerSpec, old: *mut ItimerSpec) -> i32;
}

pub fn sys_timerfd_create() -> io::Result<RawFd> {
    let fd = unsafe { timerfd_create(CLOCK_MONOTONIC, TFD_NONBLOCK | TFD_CLOEXEC) };
    if fd < 0 {
        Err(io::Error::last_os_error())
    } else {
        Ok(fd)
    }
}

pub fn sys_timerfd_settime(fd: RawFd, secs: u64, nanos: u64) -> io::Result<()> {
    let spec = ItimerSpec {
        it_interval: Timespec {
            tv_sec: 0,
            tv_nsec: 0,
        },
        it_value: Timespec {
            tv_sec: secs as i64,
            tv_nsec: nanos as i64,
        },
    };
    let ret = unsafe { timerfd_settime(fd, 0, &spec, std::ptr::null_mut()) };
    if ret < 0 {
        Err(io::Error::last_os_error())
    } else {
        Ok(())
    }
}

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn close(fd: i32) -> i32;
    fn read(fd: i32, buf: *mut u8, count: usize) -> isize;
}

pub fn sys_close(fd: RawFd) {
    unsafe {
        close(fd);
    }
}

pub fn sys_read(fd: RawFd, buf: &mut [u8]) -> io::Result<usize> {
    let ret = unsafe { read(fd, buf.as_mut_ptr(), buf.len()) };
    if ret < 0 {
        Err(io::Error::last_os_error())
    } else {
        Ok(ret as usize)
    }
}

pub const SYS_BPF: i64 = 321;

pub const BPF_MAP_CREATE: u32 = 0;
pub const BPF_PROG_LOAD: u32 = 5;
pub const BPF_MAP_UPDATE_ELEM: u32 = 2;

pub const BPF_MAP_TYPE_PERF_EVENT_ARRAY: u32 = 4;
pub const BPF_PROG_TYPE_TRACEPOINT: u32 = 5;
pub const BPF_PROG_TYPE_KPROBE: u32 = 2;

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn syscall(num: i64, ...) -> i64;
}

pub fn sys_bpf(cmd: u32, attr: &[u8]) -> io::Result<i64> {
    let ret = unsafe { syscall(SYS_BPF, cmd as i64, attr.as_ptr() as i64, attr.len() as i64) };
    if ret < 0 {
        Err(io::Error::last_os_error())
    } else {
        Ok(ret)
    }
}

pub fn bpf_map_create(
    map_type: u32,
    key_size: u32,
    value_size: u32,
    max_entries: u32,
) -> io::Result<RawFd> {
    let mut attr = [0u8; 64];
    attr[0..4].copy_from_slice(&map_type.to_ne_bytes());
    attr[4..8].copy_from_slice(&key_size.to_ne_bytes());
    attr[8..12].copy_from_slice(&value_size.to_ne_bytes());
    attr[12..16].copy_from_slice(&max_entries.to_ne_bytes());
    sys_bpf(BPF_MAP_CREATE, &attr).map(|fd| fd as RawFd)
}

pub fn bpf_prog_load(
    prog_type: u32,
    insns: &[u8],
    license: &[u8],
    log_buf: &mut [u8],
) -> io::Result<RawFd> {
    let insn_cnt = (insns.len() / 8) as u32;
    let mut attr = [0u8; 128];
    attr[0..4].copy_from_slice(&prog_type.to_ne_bytes());
    attr[4..8].copy_from_slice(&insn_cnt.to_ne_bytes());
    attr[8..16].copy_from_slice(&(insns.as_ptr() as u64).to_ne_bytes());
    attr[16..24].copy_from_slice(&(license.as_ptr() as u64).to_ne_bytes());
    if !log_buf.is_empty() {
        attr[24..28].copy_from_slice(&1u32.to_ne_bytes());
    }
    attr[28..32].copy_from_slice(&(log_buf.len() as u32).to_ne_bytes());
    attr[32..40].copy_from_slice(&(log_buf.as_mut_ptr() as u64).to_ne_bytes());

    sys_bpf(BPF_PROG_LOAD, &attr).map(|fd| fd as RawFd)
}

pub fn bpf_map_update_elem(map_fd: RawFd, key: &[u8], value: &[u8]) -> io::Result<()> {
    let mut attr = [0u8; 64];
    attr[0..4].copy_from_slice(&(map_fd as u32).to_ne_bytes());
    attr[8..16].copy_from_slice(&(key.as_ptr() as u64).to_ne_bytes());
    attr[16..24].copy_from_slice(&(value.as_ptr() as u64).to_ne_bytes());
    sys_bpf(BPF_MAP_UPDATE_ELEM, &attr)?;
    Ok(())
}

pub const SYS_PERF_EVENT_OPEN: i64 = 298;

pub const PERF_TYPE_TRACEPOINT: u32 = 2;
pub const PERF_COUNT_SW_BPF_OUTPUT: u64 = 10;
pub const PERF_SAMPLE_RAW: u64 = 1 << 10;
pub const PERF_FLAG_FD_CLOEXEC: u64 = 8;

#[repr(C)]
pub struct PerfEventAttr {
    pub pe_type: u32,
    pub size: u32,
    pub config: u64,
    pub sample_period_or_freq: u64,
    pub sample_type: u64,
    pub read_format: u64,
    pub flags: u64,
    pub wakeup_events_or_watermark: u32,
    pub bp_type: u32,
    pub config1: u64,
    pub config2: u64,
    pub branch_sample_type: u64,
    pub sample_regs_user: u64,
    pub sample_stack_user: u32,
    pub clockid: i32,
    pub sample_regs_intr: u64,
    pub aux_watermark: u32,
    pub sample_max_stack: u16,
    pub reserved: u16,
}

pub fn sys_perf_event_open(
    attr: &PerfEventAttr,
    pid: i32,
    cpu: i32,
    group_fd: i32,
    flags: u64,
) -> io::Result<RawFd> {
    let ret = unsafe {
        syscall(
            SYS_PERF_EVENT_OPEN,
            attr as *const PerfEventAttr as i64,
            pid as i64,
            cpu as i64,
            group_fd as i64,
            flags as i64,
        )
    };
    if ret < 0 {
        Err(io::Error::last_os_error())
    } else {
        Ok(ret as RawFd)
    }
}

pub const PERF_EVENT_IOC_ENABLE: u64 = 0x2400;
pub const PERF_EVENT_IOC_SET_BPF: u64 = 0x40042408;
pub const PERF_EVENT_IOC_DISABLE: u64 = 0x2401;

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn ioctl(fd: i32, request: u64, ...) -> i32;
}

pub fn sys_ioctl(fd: RawFd, request: u64, arg: u64) -> io::Result<()> {
    let ret = unsafe { ioctl(fd, request, arg as i64) };
    if ret < 0 {
        Err(io::Error::last_os_error())
    } else {
        Ok(())
    }
}

pub const PROT_READ: i32 = 1;
pub const PROT_WRITE: i32 = 2;
pub const MAP_SHARED: i32 = 1;

unsafe extern "C" {
    fn mmap(addr: *mut u8, len: usize, prot: i32, flags: i32, fd: i32, offset: i64) -> *mut u8;
    fn munmap(addr: *mut u8, len: usize) -> i32;
}

pub fn sys_mmap(fd: RawFd, len: usize) -> io::Result<*mut u8> {
    let ptr = unsafe {
        mmap(
            std::ptr::null_mut(),
            len,
            PROT_READ | PROT_WRITE,
            MAP_SHARED,
            fd,
            0,
        )
    };
    if ptr == usize::MAX as *mut u8 {
        // MAP_FAILED = (void*)-1
        Err(io::Error::last_os_error())
    } else {
        Ok(ptr)
    }
}

pub fn sys_munmap(ptr: *mut u8, len: usize) -> io::Result<()> {
    let ret = unsafe { munmap(ptr, len) };
    if ret < 0 {
        Err(io::Error::last_os_error())
    } else {
        Ok(())
    }
}

pub fn nr_cpus() -> usize {
    std::fs::read_to_string("/sys/devices/system/cpu/possible")
        .ok()
        .and_then(|s| {
            // format: "0-N" or "0"
            let s = s.trim();
            if let Some((_start, end)) = s.split_once('-') {
                end.parse::<usize>().ok().map(|n| n + 1)
            } else {
                s.parse::<usize>().ok().map(|n| n + 1)
            }
        })
        .unwrap_or(1)
}

#[allow(dead_code)]
unsafe extern "C" {
    fn sysconf(name: i32) -> i64;
}

pub fn page_size() -> usize {
    // _SC_PAGESIZE = 30 on Linux x86-64 (unistd.h)
    const SC_PAGESIZE: i32 = 30;
    let ret = unsafe { sysconf(SC_PAGESIZE) };
    if ret > 0 {
        ret as usize
    } else {
        4096 // fallback if sysconf fails
    }
}

// --- inotify ---

pub const IN_CREATE: u32     = 0x00000100;
pub const IN_DELETE: u32     = 0x00000200;
pub const IN_DELETE_SELF: u32= 0x00000400;
pub const IN_ISDIR: u32      = 0x40000000;
pub const IN_CLOEXEC: i32    = 0o2000000;

#[repr(C)]
pub struct InotifyEvent {
    pub wd: i32,
    pub mask: u32,
    pub cookie: u32,
    pub len: u32,
```

`crates/vigil/src/timestamp.rs`:

```rs
// Re-export the canonical implementations from vigil-common.
pub use vigil_common::timestamp::{now_rfc3339, rfc3339_to_secs, secs_to_rfc3339 as unix_to_rfc3339};

use vigil_common::timestamp::now_secs;

/// Returns the current time formatted as a local-style string (UTC):
/// "2024-01-15 10:30:00"
pub fn now_local_fmt() -> String {
    let s = unix_to_rfc3339(now_secs());
    // "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z" → "2024-01-15 10:30:00"
    s.trim_end_matches('Z').replacen('T', " ", 1)
}

/// Parse an RFC3339 UTC string to unix seconds.  Returns `Err` with a
/// descriptive message on failure (wraps `rfc3339_to_secs`).
#[allow(dead_code)]
pub fn rfc3339_to_unix(s: &str) -> Result<u64, String> {
    rfc3339_to_secs(s).ok_or_else(|| format!("invalid rfc3339 timestamp: {}", s))
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn test_epoch() {
        assert_eq!(unix_to_rfc3339(0), "1970-01-01T00:00:00Z");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_known_date() {
        assert_eq!(unix_to_rfc3339(1704067200), "2024-01-01T00:00:00Z");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_known_datetime() {
        assert_eq!(unix_to_rfc3339(1705314600), "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_leap_year_feb29() {
        assert_eq!(unix_to_rfc3339(1709164800), "2024-02-29T00:00:00Z");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_rfc3339_roundtrip() {
        let ts = 1704067200u64;
        let s = unix_to_rfc3339(ts);
        assert_eq!(rfc3339_to_unix(&s).unwrap(), ts);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_rfc3339_plus_offset() {
        assert_eq!(
            rfc3339_to_unix("2024-01-01T00:00:00+00:00").unwrap(),
            1704067200
        );
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_rfc3339_z() {
        assert_eq!(rfc3339_to_unix("2024-01-01T00:00:00Z").unwrap(), 1704067200);
    }
}
```

`crates/vigil/src/tls.rs`:

```rs
use std::io;
use std::net::TcpStream;
use std::os::raw::{c_int, c_long, c_void};
use std::os::unix::io::AsRawFd;

unsafe extern "C" {
    // OpenSSL 3.x API
    fn TLS_client_method() -> *const c_void;
    fn SSL_CTX_new(method: *const c_void) -> *mut c_void;
    fn SSL_CTX_free(ctx: *mut c_void);
    fn SSL_CTX_set_default_verify_paths(ctx: *mut c_void) -> c_int;
    fn SSL_new(ctx: *mut c_void) -> *mut c_void;
    fn SSL_free(ssl: *mut c_void);
    fn SSL_set_fd(ssl: *mut c_void, fd: c_int) -> c_int;
    fn SSL_connect(ssl: *mut c_void) -> c_int;
    fn SSL_read(ssl: *mut c_void, buf: *mut u8, num: c_int) -> c_int;
    fn SSL_write(ssl: *mut c_void, buf: *const u8, num: c_int) -> c_int;
    // SSL_set_tlsext_host_name is a macro, actual function is SSL_ctrl
    fn SSL_ctrl(ssl: *mut c_void, cmd: c_int, larg: c_long, parg: *mut c_void) -> c_long;
    fn SSL_CTX_set_verify(ctx: *mut c_void, mode: c_int, callback: *const c_void);
    fn SSL_set1_host(ssl: *mut c_void, hostname: *const u8) -> c_int;
    fn SSL_get_verify_result(ssl: *const c_void) -> c_long;
}

const SSL_CTRL_SET_TLSEXT_HOSTNAME: c_int = 55;
const TLSEXT_NAMETYPE_HOST_NAME: c_long = 0;

fn ssl_set_hostname(ssl: *mut c_void, name: &str) {
    let c_name = std::ffi::CString::new(name).unwrap();
    unsafe {
        SSL_ctrl(ssl, SSL_CTRL_SET_TLSEXT_HOSTNAME, TLSEXT_NAMETYPE_HOST_NAME, c_name.as_ptr() as *mut c_void);
    }
}

pub struct TlsStream {
    ssl: *mut c_void,
    ctx: *mut c_void,
    _tcp: TcpStream,
}

unsafe impl Send for TlsStream {}

impl TlsStream {
    pub fn connect(stream: TcpStream, host: &str) -> Result<Self, String> {
        let ctx = unsafe { SSL_CTX_new(TLS_client_method()) };
        if ctx.is_null() {
            return Err("SSL_CTX_new failed".to_string());
        }
        unsafe { SSL_CTX_set_default_verify_paths(ctx) };
        // verify server certificate
        unsafe { SSL_CTX_set_verify(ctx, 1, std::ptr::null()) }; // SSL_VERIFY_PEER = 1

        let ssl = unsafe { SSL_new(ctx) };
        if ssl.is_null() {
            unsafe { SSL_CTX_free(ctx) };
            return Err("SSL_new failed".to_string());
        }

        ssl_set_hostname(ssl, host);
        // hostname verification
        let c_host = std::ffi::CString::new(host).map_err(|e| e.to_string())?;
        unsafe { SSL_set1_host(ssl, c_host.as_ptr() as *const u8) };
        unsafe { SSL_set_fd(ssl, stream.as_raw_fd()) };

        let ret = unsafe { SSL_connect(ssl) };
        if ret != 1 {
            unsafe { SSL_free(ssl); SSL_CTX_free(ctx) };
            return Err(format!("SSL_connect failed: {}", ret));
        }

        // check cert verification result
        let verify_result = unsafe { SSL_get_verify_result(ssl) };
        if verify_result != 0 { // X509_V_OK = 0
            unsafe { SSL_free(ssl); SSL_CTX_free(ctx) };
            return Err(format!("certificate verification failed: {}", verify_result));
        }

        Ok(TlsStream { ssl, ctx, _tcp: stream })
    }

    pub fn write_all(&self, data: &[u8]) -> io::Result<()> {
        let mut written = 0;
        while written < data.len() {
            let n = unsafe {
                SSL_write(self.ssl, data[written..].as_ptr(), (data.len() - written) as c_int)
            };
            if n <= 0 {
                return Err(io::Error::other("SSL_write failed"));
            }
            written += n as usize;
        }
        Ok(())
    }

    pub fn read_all(&self) -> io::Result<Vec<u8>> {
        let mut result = Vec::new();
        let mut buf = [0u8; 4096];
        loop {
            let n = unsafe { SSL_read(self.ssl, buf.as_mut_ptr(), buf.len() as c_int) };
            if n <= 0 { break; }
            result.extend_from_slice(&buf[..n as usize]);
        }
        Ok(result)
    }
}

impl Drop for TlsStream {
    fn drop(&mut self) {
        unsafe {
            SSL_free(self.ssl);
            SSL_CTX_free(self.ctx);
        }
    }
}

```

`crates/vigil/src/toml_parser.rs`:

```rs
// minimal toml parser for the vigil config format
// only handles [sections] and key = "quoted string" assignments

#[derive(Debug)]
pub struct Config {
    pub game: GameConfig,
    pub logging: LogConfig,
    pub server: Option<ServerConfig>,
}

#[derive(Debug)]
pub struct GameConfig {
    pub path: String,
    pub profile: Option<String>,
}

#[derive(Debug)]
pub struct LogConfig {
    pub path: String,
}

#[derive(Debug)]
pub struct ServerConfig {
    pub url: String,
    pub player_id: String,
    pub password: Option<String>,
}

pub fn parse_config(content: &str) -> Result<Config, String> {
    let mut section = "";

    let mut game_path: Option<String> = None;
    let mut game_profile: Option<String> = None;
    let mut log_path: Option<String> = None;
    let mut server_url: Option<String> = None;
    let mut server_player_id: Option<String> = None;
    let mut server_password: Option<String> = None;

    for (lineno, raw) in content.lines().enumerate() {
        let line = raw.trim();

        if line.is_empty() || line.starts_with('#') {
            continue;
        }

        if line.starts_with('[') {
            if !line.ends_with(']') {
                return Err(format!(
                    "line {}: malformed section header: {}",
                    lineno + 1,
                    line
                ));
            }
            section = &line[1..line.len() - 1];
            continue;
        }

        let (key, val) = parse_kv(line, lineno + 1)?;

        if section == "game" && key == "path" {
            game_path = Some(val);
        } else if section == "game" && key == "profile" {
            game_profile = Some(val);
        } else if section == "logging" && key == "path" {
            log_path = Some(val);
        } else if section == "server" {
            if key == "url" {
                server_url = Some(val);
            } else if key == "player_id" {
                server_player_id = Some(val);
            } else if key == "password" {
                server_password = Some(val);
            }
        }
    }

    let game_path = game_path.ok_or("missing [game] path")?;
    let log_path = log_path.ok_or("missing [logging] path")?;

    let server = match (server_url, server_player_id) {
        (Some(url), Some(player_id)) => Some(ServerConfig {
            url,
            player_id,
            password: server_password,
        }),
        (None, None) => None,
        (Some(_), None) => return Err("missing server.player_id".to_string()),
        (None, Some(_)) => return Err("missing server.url".to_string()),
    };

    Ok(Config {
        game: GameConfig {
            path: game_path,
            profile: game_profile,
        },
        logging: LogConfig { path: log_path },
        server,
    })
}

// parse a single "key = \"value\"" line
fn parse_kv(line: &str, lineno: usize) -> Result<(&str, String), String> {
    let eq = line
        .find('=')
        .ok_or_else(|| format!("line {}: expected '=' in: {}", lineno, line))?;

    let key = line[..eq].trim();
    let rest = line[eq + 1..].trim();

    if !rest.starts_with('"') || !rest.ends_with('"') || rest.len() < 2 {
        return Err(format!(
            "line {}: value must be a quoted string: {}",
            lineno, rest
        ));
    }

    let inner = &rest[1..rest.len() - 1];
    Ok((key, inner.to_string()))
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    const FULL_CONFIG: &str = r#"
[game]
path = "/home/user/.steam/steam/steamapps/common/GameName"

[logging]
path = "/var/log/vigil.log"

[server]
url = "http://localhost:3000"
player_id = "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000"
"#;

    const NO_SERVER_CONFIG: &str = r#"
# vigil config without server block

[game]
path = "/opt/game"

[logging]
path = "/tmp/vigil.log"
"#;

    #[test]
    fn test_full_config() {
        let cfg = parse_config(FULL_CONFIG).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(
            cfg.game.path,
            "/home/user/.steam/steam/steamapps/common/GameName"
        );
        assert_eq!(cfg.logging.path, "/var/log/vigil.log");
        let srv = cfg.server.unwrap();
        assert_eq!(srv.url, "http://localhost:3000");
        assert_eq!(srv.player_id, "00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_no_server() {
        let cfg = parse_config(NO_SERVER_CONFIG).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(cfg.game.path, "/opt/game");
        assert_eq!(cfg.logging.path, "/tmp/vigil.log");
        assert!(cfg.server.is_none());
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_missing_game_path() {
        let input = "[logging]\npath = \"/tmp/vigil.log\"\n";
        let res = parse_config(input);
        assert!(res.is_err());
        assert!(res.unwrap_err().contains("game"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_missing_log_path() {
        let input = "[game]\npath = \"/opt/game\"\n";
        let res = parse_config(input);
        assert!(res.is_err());
        assert!(res.unwrap_err().contains("logging"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_partial_server_missing_player_id() {
        let input = "[game]\npath = \"/opt/game\"\n[logging]\npath = \"/tmp/v.log\"\n[server]\nurl = \"http://localhost:3000\"\n";
        let res = parse_config(input);
        assert!(res.is_err());
        assert!(res.unwrap_err().contains("player_id"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_comments_and_blank_lines() {
        let input = "# top comment\n\n[game]\n# inline comment\npath = \"/opt/game\"\n\n[logging]\npath = \"/tmp/vigil.log\"\n";
        let cfg = parse_config(input).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(cfg.game.path, "/opt/game");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_unknown_keys_ignored() {
        let input = "[game]\npath = \"/opt/game\"\nunknown = \"value\"\n[logging]\npath = \"/tmp/vigil.log\"\n";
        let cfg = parse_config(input).unwrap();
        assert_eq!(cfg.game.path, "/opt/game");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_unquoted_value_error() {
        let input = "[game]\npath = /opt/game\n[logging]\npath = \"/tmp/v.log\"\n";
        let res = parse_config(input);
        assert!(res.is_err());
        assert!(res.unwrap_err().contains("quoted string"));
    }
}
```

`dist/nginx/vigil.conf`:

```conf
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name vigil.example.com;
    return 301 https://$host$request_uri;
}

server {
    listen 443 ssl http2;
    server_name vigil.example.com;

    ssl_certificate /etc/letsencrypt/live/vigil.example.com/fullchain.pem;
    ssl_certificate_key /etc/letsencrypt/live/vigil.example.com/privkey.pem;

    # security headers
    add_header X-Frame-Options DENY;
    add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff;
    add_header Strict-Transport-Security "max-age=31536000; includeSubDomains" always;

    # request size limit (match vigil-server's 1MB)
    client_max_body_size 1m;

    location / {
        proxy_pass http://127.0.0.1:3000;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
    }
}
```
